rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog gi rnam thar skal bzang dad pa'i shing rta 'dren byed/ p. 21rnam thar skal bzang dad pa'i shing rta 'dren byed kyi 'phros zur 'debs mdzes rgyan/
p. 179rnam thar yang rgyan nor bu'i phra bkod/ p. 209rnam thar spel rgyan nor bu'i do shal/ p. 267rnam thar mtshar rgyan/ p. 288zhen pa rang grol gyi lhug par brjod pa'i
gtam skal bzang dad pa'i shing rta 'dren byed/

shre ya se stu/rig vc: rigsgnas kun gyi ngo mtshar blta ba dang//legs bshad dga' ston 'gyed la gus pa'i blo//dman pa'i spyod las grol ba'i rtogs brjod phreng//mchog tu dang
ba vc: dad parnams kyis bsten bya yin//gang yang 'di na thog mtha' dbus spangs dri bral gdod ma'i dbyings las ma g.yos thog mar A yig rnam kun 'god// nanda bde stong dga'
bzhi'i dbyings// mukta ye nas grol ba ste// wa ra mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'o// A nanta mukta wa ra// sAdhuHrtag par gnas//dpal ldan kun gzhi'i zhing sa las 'thon vc: thon'gro
kun dga' bskyed tshul khrims gsar pa'i 'dab stong can//'jig rten las snang nyon mongs 'dam rdzab 'ching vc: mching ba las grol mchog tu nges vc: yid'byung cher ldan pa//blo
gsal 'dus pa'i rgya mtsho'i dbus der mdo dang rgyud sde'i nges gsang 'chad mkhas bsngags par 'os//mang thos gsung rab kun gyi khur lci ba//rnam dpyod rab dga'i myos
bum cher mtho zhing//'khor tshogs sred pa'i zhags las grol byed pa'i//brtse ldan gnyis 'thung mchog gis dge byas bzhin//rang rang ngo bo'i chos kun gsal ba dang//rnam mang

tha snyad 'chad la dga' dang bcas//zab lam re re yis kyang grol ba ster//gsal ba'i spobs pa mchog kyang rnyed pa lags//dam pa kun gyi gsung gi rnga bo che//skal bzang rab dga'i
dbyug gus bskul ba las//zhen pa rang grol mchog gis brjod pa'i gtam//gang gis thos pa don dang bcas par 'gyur//'dir 'khor ba'i byings las yongs su ma brgal ba'i bdag
cag so so skye bo'i rang 'tshang gi cha/ brdzun sgrib dang bral ba'i brjod pa'i sgo cung zad gleng ba ni/ de'ang thog ma med pa'i dus sngon gyi skyes pa'i rabs kyi phreng
ba rnams su/ nyam nga ba'i 'khor ba'i rgya mtsho kun rtog gi rlabs brgya kun tu 'khrugs pa/ dug gsum gyi klongs dang/ las kyi chu srin gyis bstams shing/ nye bar len pa'i
phung pa'i rta gdong gis yongs su skor ba'i nang du bying ba'i gnas tshul gyi cha shas ma lus pa ni sgrib med gzigs pa'i ye shes kyi spyod yul can dag gis ji lta ji snyed
du mkhyen pa las/ bdag lta'i sems can ma rig pa stug po'i mun pa'i khung bur gnas pa'i rang rgyud pa dag gis/ blun mos khyo ngo mi mtshon pa bzhin dpag par mi nus pas/
mi chos bla ma dang 'brel ba'i nyes ltung gi las mi zad pa ci'i phyir lhur len/ shes ldan dag/ thog ma med pa'i 'khor ba nas bsags pa'i las nyon gyi khur cung zad kyang
ma bri bar/ chos la brten pa'i las sgrib 'bad med de sgrub pa ni gnyen po'i sman dug tu 'gyur ba dang cis te mi 'tshungs/ 'on kyang 'dir pha ma'i nyer len gyis skye ba yongs
su gzung ba/ gzhon nu'i kun spyod da lta'i ye shes la gsal ba/

bstan rim rnams la zhugs te bslab pa'i gnas rjes su mnos pa/ thos pa'i rtsol bas sngar goms pa'i bag chags kyi mthu cung zad sad pa/ bsam pa las byung ba'i shes rab kyi sgo
ngang gis bye ba/ rgyud ma lus pa'i rdo rje'i gnas dbang don lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes nye bar bstsal nas/ de nyid snga phyir bar gsum du mnos pa'i khrid tshul brgya rtsa
brgyad kyis sargar phye ste rang gzhan gyi re ba yid bzhin du bskong ba'i las snang gi 'char tshul sgro skur dang bral ba/ yun ring du 'grogs pa'i grogs dag dpang du
gyur ba che long tsam zhig smos na/ sngon gyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen bka' gdams pa dag gi gsung sgros na/snga ma gang byas rang gi lus la ltos//phyi ma gar 'gro rang gi sems
la dris//zhes gsungs pa 'di glo ba la 'jen par byung bas/ don de nyid la bsams pa na/ da lta dngos su thob cing ma nyams pa'i dal 'byor 'khor lo bzhi ldan gyi rten khyad
par can 'di'i rgyu dri ma med pa'i tshul khrims kyi brtul zhugs la nan tan du bgyid pa po de nyid kyi smon lam dag pa'i legs byas kyis bskrun te/ 'dir skye ba yongs su
gzung ba'i yul ni mnga' ris smad kyi sa'i ljongs/ gnyag ston shAkya mu ne'i rigs brgyud 'dzin pa'i/ yab rje dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa brgyad/ yum nyi shu rtsa gnyis bzhes pa'i
tshe lhums su zhugs par snang la/ skabs der ska rags nas byang sems rin po che spyan drangs/ rgyal ba tshe dpag tu med pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du/ mas dbang bskur ba
lan grangs dpag tu med pa mnos pa'i mthar/ nam zhig mngal 'dzin pa'i zla ba rdzogs nas/ rab byung zhes pa me mo yos kyi lo'i hor zla bcu pa'i tshes nyi shu lnga/

gza' lhag pa/ skar ma me bzhi/ 'phrod kun dga'/ sbyor ba mdza' bo rnams 'jom pa la/ shag ma khang rnying pa de nyid du bde bar btsas ces gleng la/ dus der skyed mos tshal gyi
ldum ra na me tog rgya men sum thog re re zhing yang kha dog mi gcig pa/ thog steng ma de'i ze'u 'bru'i dbus na 'dab ma ljang ser rgyangs kyis 'thon pa zhig 'khrungs pa/
gser khang gi rten rnams kyi drung du phul bas/ zla ba phyed tsam gyi bar du ma rnyings par thub pa de dus kyi skye bo kun la mngon sum du gyur/ de nas zla ba 'ga' zhig
lon pa na/ rwa ston chos rje'i drung du ming zhu ba la phyin pas/ byis pa 'di sgrol ma 'bum ther btsugs pa'i rjes rang la skyes byung pas ming sgrol ma 'bum du thogs/ btsun
pa'i bag chags bzang po 'dug pas chos sgor chug ces lung bstan gnang zhing/ snga phyir ma dang lhan du rgyal ba tshe dpag tu med pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang lan
grangs du ma dang/ sgrol ma dkar mo/ rta mgrin lcags ral can/ phyag rdor u tsarya rnams kyi bka' lung thob zer/de nas lo bzhi tsam gyi bar du byang sems rin po che bar
chad kyis mi brdzi bar bya ba'i ched du bka' rjes gnang du ma gnang ba tho ro tsam dran/ khyad par drung pa chos rje pas thugs dam zab mo'i skyabs 'og tu g.yel ba med pa'i
bka' drin bstsal zhing/ skabs su tshe dbang/ sgrol dkar gur mgon gyi bka' bsgo yang yang gnang/lo bzhi tsam lon pa na/ phu phag dgon pa mjal du phyin pa'i lam/ byams gling
gi mdun du sleb pa na/ a li a li yi na yi na zer zhing/ dgon pa'i grwa khang rnams mthong bas bag chags sad pa'i blo nyams mang po byung/

dbu rtse'i thad du sleb nas kyang rta mthen/ nga ltad mo blta dgos pa 'dug byas shing/ rgyun ring du bsdad pas da lta yang gsal po dran gyi 'dug/ byis pa'i dus yul du sdod
pa'i ring la/ khye'u rtse grogs mang po dang bcas te chos khri brtsigs pa la bsdad nas/ khong rnams chos nyan gyi tshul du byas/ ngas chos bshad pa yin/ khyed rnams nyon
byas pa rgyus yod pa'i mi da dung yang yod/ de dus kyi chos khri la'ang yun ring po'i bar du nga rang dung dpun rnams kyis 'dzin tshugs bgyis/ de dag gi bar skabs rnams su
yang yang grib rkyen la brten pa'i na ba glo bur ba du mas gtses pas nyer len gyi rkyen byas/ yab yum gyis kyang chos sgor 'jug pa'i mthun rkyen yang dag pa'i bka' drin
stsal te// lo de nyid la skyabs gsum dang/ phyi lo sa ga'i dus chen stengs su yongs rdzogs dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa drung pa chos rje las thob/ skabs der mdo sde skyes rabs
las klog thar byas pas/ tshig phal cher blo la zin nas/ ja gral la bstsol med du bskyar bas/ na tshod phra mo la de ltar du byung pas yum dgyes pa che ste thams cad ma
bu yod pa mang po yod de/ nga'i bu 'di 'dra yod pa su la yang med/ mngal du chags pa nas deng sang gi bar gyi dge mtshan 'di rnams la bltas na gzhan dang mi mnyam pa cig
yong nges pa yin gsung ba'ang dran/ de lo tsog ge'i nad pa mang 'dug pas/ a mas ming sring kun la bsrung skud mdogs kyi 'dug pa la/ nga rang gi dgos skal de rtsed mo'i rnam
pas kha phye ste bltas pas/ sran ma 'bru dgu 'dug pa zos pas/ de nub man shin tu na ba byung ste/ 'tsho byed kyi 'phul sman stobs

bskyed de byin pas/ 'brum bu shin tu 'thug pa phyir 'thon/ lus kyi phyi thams cad rnam dag tu song ba/ de dang gos 'byar nas gyon mi stub pa la/ mon dar gyi gzan bcos te sha
la sbyar ba na yang/ skabs rer ma sangs na sha la 'byar yong ba tsam byung/ der mas lhag par brtse bas/ nyin mtshan med ma bral bar nad g.yog gnang/ dus phyis bsam pas
nga'i a ma des/ de dus nad g.yog rkyen du 'byor ba byas pa gcig pu'i drin yang 'khor ba med/ nga gcig pu la brtse bar ma zad/ spyir yang a ma de'i dge blo dang/ rang bzhin
bzang ngan/ gtong ba'i sgo gang la bsams kyang/ bud med phal las 'das pa rang gcig gi yid ches yang yang skye ba byung//skabs der drung pa chos rjes yang yang du phebs
pa na/ sems spro ba dang gus pa chen po skyes te/ ma las blangs pa dang/ thabs mkhas kyi 'du byas nas/ nyin re bzhin gsol ja zhu ba/ sku la 'dud pa/ tha na na bza' la gnas
pa'i sa rdul phra mo sogs phyir gsol ba/ rgyang ring po nas bsu ba/ skyel ba sogs gzhan gyis slob pa la ma ltos par/ rang shar du byung ba'i kun tu spyod pa des thugs phrogs
te/ byis pa khyod chung chung nas dad pa che zhing/ chos kyi rigs sad pa/ shes rab dang ldan pa cig 'dug ces bsngags pa yang yang gnang zhing/ nged la ja mang po rang
byin pa'i sbyin bdag yin gsung ba sogs dgyes pa'i rnam 'gyur mang po mdzad/ dus der yab yum gyi pho brang de nyid du klog sogs bslab sbyangs kyi gnas phra mo tshegs med
du shes/lo drug pa la sde pa sku mched drung du lo gsar la mjal du phyin pas/ 'phral shes kyi tshig rnams

bzhugs gral gyi dbus su gtsang sing ba/ spobs pa zhum pa med par gzengs mtho zhing brjod pa dag par bton pas/ dpon po rgan po'i bu 'di ngo mtshar che gsung gzengs bstod dang
bcas pa'i gnang sbyin bsam gyis mi khyab pa stsal/de nas lo bdun lon pa na/ drung pa chos rje pa'i drung du bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed dmar po lha lnga'i rdul tshon
gyi dkyil 'khor du bcug nas/ rigs brtag pa'i me tog gtso bos bzhes pa'i dbang las/ gsang mtshan dpal zhe sdang rnam par dag pa'i rdo rje zhes gdags par mdzad de/ skye ba
'di la sngags kyi dkyil 'khor du zhugs shing/ dbang nod pa'i thog ma yang 'di yin no//de lo dgon pa'i dge 'dun rnams la zhen pa bzhi bral gyi khrid gnang ba'i khrid rar
zhugs te zla chos cig dmigs khrid zhib par nyan pas/ chos kyi rkang zhen pas ma bcings pa'i chags med du 'dug snyam pa/ cis kyang dgos med kyi blo rtsa bral/ gang la'ang
snying po mi 'dug snyam pa'i yid ches/ zer sgra la ma ltos pa nang nas go ba byung ste/ phyis khrid gang zhus kyang chags med kyi nges 'byung de dus 'dra ba'i rngo thogs
pa gtan ma byung zhing/ brgyud pa'i phyag bzhes kyi srol mi 'dug pa ma gtogs dri med rig pa'i rang 'tshang grung pa de dus nas gcer mthong du byung 'dug ste/ yun ring po'i
bar du ngo shes pa dang nges shes skyes pa ni ma byung mod/ phyis ngo sprod mdzub btsugs su mdzad pa dag gi bsnyems med du ston par mdzad nas/ sngar gyi de nyid las gsal
bzhag gi blang dor spu rtse tsam yang mi 'dug ste/ zhen pa bzhi bral 'di khri thob pa thams cad kyi thog ma yin no//'di'i rtsa

tshig/tshe 'di la zhen na chos pa min//'khor ba la zhen na nges 'byung min//bdag don la zhen na byang sems min//'dzin pa byung na blta ba min//ces pa 'di yang yang 'gro 'dug
gi skabs lhang lhang smras pa da lta'i dran yul na yang 'dug cing/ a ma/ spun zla tha na bran khol tshun gyi'ang blo la tshig de 'jags 'dug/ de dus skad phra mo gling bu
ltar snyan pa cig yod pas/ rje btsun grags pa'i zhen pa bzhi bral gyi rtog mgur rnams dgongs mchod skabs 'gol dus yab yum thams cad gdan 'dzom pa'i spyan sngar nyin re
bzhin lan dgos pa la/ a phyi bgres mo cig yod pa de nges 'byung dang/ dad pa bla lhag tu 'khrungs pa'i spyan chab mang po bsil ba rang gnang ba dran/ nga rang yang chung
chung gi dus nges 'byung gi sems kyis drangs pa'i phyag mchod 'bul ba la spro zhing/ rten gsum gang na bzhugs pa'i sar mchod gshom dang/ dkar me lha bshos/ dbyar dus me tog
sogs gtsang zhing/ bkod pas tho ba'i tshogs bsog pa'i mdun pa la rang gis mi khrel/ sngon gyi gom pa mthu brtas pa'i dbang gis blang dor gyi gnas phra rags kun la bzo
med shugs 'byung du spyod pa'i brtul zhugs dpa' ma zhums pa/ gang la yang 'jigs pa med pa'i blo rtsal gyi 'char sgo su rung rung gis nan tur du bco mi thub pa cig de dus
yod/ skabs shed du yab kyis bka' zhal nas/ dus tshes bzang po yod zer ba cig gi nyin/ chos rje drung btsun pa la bsdus pa brtsi ba'i dus/ khong gi gsung nas/ khyed shes rab
che zhing thugs bag chags bsad pa cig 'dug pas/ sa dkar chos can nas brtsi ba de 'dra mi

byed/ mkhas nyams kyi rten 'brel legs sa nas 'bul dgos pas/ sangs rgyas pa'i rgyu yin na shes rab ma yin pa phud sogs de dus ngag slob byas pa'i bsdus sbyor rnams go rim phra
mo tsam gyi tshig zur yang ma brjed pa da lta'i bar du gnas/ de lo nas gzhung chen rnams 'dzin pa'i dbu btsugs te/ thog mar sa skya pa'i mos zhen byas/ sdom rig gnyis
blo la btsud pa'i tshe'ang/ zhogs re la gzhung shog re tsam gzung zhing/ bshar sbyang ha cang ma byas kyang nam yin du gtsang zhing ma 'dres par thon pa'i ngang nas/ drung
pa chos rje la 'phrag snon phul bas/ re shig des 'dzin gzhan shol la/ gzhung gnyis po brgya tshar re lce thog nas bshor du chug gsung ba'i bka' bstsal slob dpon pa la gnang
ba ji lta ba bzhin du bsgrubs rjes/ dpe cha'i yig spyi tshun gsal po blo la shar nas/ mig btsums te gzhung gi rkang pa re re nas lugs ldog tu bton pa de shog 'debs re
re gnyis gnyis la 'thogs thug med par thon pa byung ste/ de dus kyi dpe bsnon grogs ldan pa da lta yang shin tu mang bar yod/ de mtshams phar tshad 'dul mngon/ byams chos
lhag ma bzhi/ spyod 'jug bshes spring sogs blo la zin rjes/ drung pa chos rje la 'phrag bsnon 'bul ba dang/ gzhung re re yang brgya tshar du bshor ba gong bzhin byas/
pha ma 'byor ldan gyi drin las/ rnam 'grel gyi zho 'thung ston mo/ tshad 'bras mar khu/ gzhung rdzogs ston mo/ phar phyin gyi skabs ston sogs kyis/ slob dpon/ grwa pa/ dpe
'dzin rogs kun tshim par byas shing/ skabs der/ paN chen rin po che byams pa gling pa des phag dkar shes rab gsal byed kyi zhal

gzigs pa yin zer ba'i grags pa 'dug cing/ rig pa'i gnas lnga la phul du byung ba'i mkhyen pa mnga' ba/ ri mo yang spyan gyis gzigs pa la ma ltos par/ sku rgyab ru rtsol med
'dri ba mngon sum du gnang ba thos shing mthong bas mos par byung/ 'di lta bu'i mkhyen rab kyi rgyun bdag la 'phos na snyam/ phag dkar gyi byin rlabs cig gnang dgos zhus
pas/ drung pa sku na gzhon nu nas thugs rdzogs che ba'i snyan pa yang yang thos pas ya mtshan che/ da bstan pa la phan pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po gcig gi khur bzhes
gnang dgos gsung zhing/ dges pa dang bcas te byin rlabs zab nas gnang/ de dus lce'i steng du ghi hu waM gi lanydza'i hriH 'dri ba sogs blo rno ba'i cho ga'i legs byas
yang mdzad kyi 'dug pa nges/ de'i rjes su slob dpon kong ka sbyin gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs kyi rgya gzhung de rje rang gis phyag bris su sum bid mdzad de gnang zhing/
bla ma 'dis bdag la thugs dkar ba'i cha'i bka' drin nam du yang mi 'khor ba lta bu yod/ de dus shes rab chen po rang cig byed dgos bsam te/ byang sems rin po che la/ shes
rab 'phel ba'i lha rigs 'jam dkar/ dbyangs can ma/ mi g.yo ba/ sher phyin dkar mo rnams kyi bsgrub skor zhus shing/ drung pa chos rje'i spyan sngar/ a ra pa tsa/ smra seng/
'jam dkar bstan pa'i 'khor lo/ gang blo ma'i bstod sgrub/ 'jam dbyangs rnon po rnams kyi sgrub skor nos/ de'i dbyar lo phu phag bskyed tshal du lha chung chung de rnams
kyis mngon rtogs dang 'brel ba'i zlas brjod la 'grus pa dang/ nyi zla gza' 'dzin byung ngo cog la lha so so la

brten pa'i ma Sha'i sbyor ba mang du byas shing/ phag dkar/ 'jam dkar dbyangs can ma sogs la ba gzhon dkar mo'i 'o mas 'phul ba dang/ sher phyin dkar mo la ma bslad pa'i sing
bus 'phul ba sogs rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i lag len ma 'khrul bar bskyangs pas/ dus ding sang sba bar ma nus pa'i blo gros kyi rtsal mngon sum du gsal ba 'di yin/ da lta
rgyu 'bras la yid mi ches/ lag len la blo mi gtad/ lha bsgom la dang ma chags par/ dngos grub thob par 'dod pa rnams byed ma btsir bas mar khu lta bu'o/ de lo phu phag
bskyed tshal du mkhan chen rin po che dang mjal/ bla mchod gong ma tog nas brgyud pa'i bstod pa chos kyi rgyal po'i 'don thabs dang bcas pa/ sha wa ra ser mo'i rjes gnang/
dmar nag gnyis kyi bsgom lung dang bcas pa thob/ de'i dgun drung pa chos rje la/ thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid/ rten 'brel snying po/ skyid sdug lam 'khyer/ sum pa lo
tsa'i snyan brgyud/ blo sbyong dpal ye ma ste rgyal sras khrid drug gi phyag chen lhan cig skyes sbyor ma gtogs/ gzhan gong smos lnga'i dmigs khrid snga phyir rgyal sras
bka' 'bum bzlas pa lan bdun lung smin par thob/ bsnyung gnas dang blo sbyong la rgyal sras bu bzhi ka'i rgyud pa'i chu bo bla ma 'di la bzhugs pa kun thob pas tshim par byung/
gsung las kyang/ rgyal sras chos rdzong pa nas brgyud pa'i phyag chen/ rgya ma ba yon tan 'od kyi yig char 'khod pa cig 'dug pa 'di ma 'ongs pa na khyod kyis thob par
gyis/ des rgyal sras khrid drug tshang ba yin zhes nan tan mdzad pa snying la bzhag/ yang de skabs mdo sde dkon brtsegs/ mdo sil bu

bcu bdun/ mdo me tog bsil ma/ mdzangs blun/ bka' bsdams zhung drug/ ka ma la shI la'i bsgom rim thog mtha' bar gsum// jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsa/ po to ba'i dpe chos rin
spungs/ de'i dmigs sgrom gyi gzer bu hor bka' bzhi pas bsgrigs pa'i dpe don ngo sprod mdzub btsugs kyi khrid/ rgyab chos su lung rin dpungs/ gtab rgyud rin dpungs dang bcas
pa/ chig lam ring mo/ lce bsgom pas sgrigs pa'i bka' gdams thor bu ba/ be'u bum sngon po/ snar thang mkhan chen grags don pa nas brgyud pa'i skyes bu gsum gyi khrid/
srid zhi mnyam nyid/ dbu ma chen po bdag pas gzhan gces te rtsa ba'i khrid bzhi/ mdo ting nge 'dzin rgyal po bsgom bya/ thub pa la brten pa'i zhi gnas sems 'dzin/ mi g.yo
ba bla med kyi rgyud kyi bsgom bya/ gtum po me bsrungs/ sgrol ma las sna tshogs pa'i rgyud kyi bsgom bya/ mngon shes lung ston/ za ma tog bkod pa'i bsgom bya/ snying rje
mkha' khyab te bka' bsdams lha bzhi'i zab khrid/ rgya bod kyi blo sbyong yod do cog kun gyi tshig don 'dums pa/ sems dpal gzhon nu rgyal mchog pas mdzad pa'i blo sbyong
legs bshad kun 'dus nang ltar bsgom don gyi dmigs pa zhib par stsal zhing/ de dang 'brel bar jo bo'i lam yig chen mo/ 'brom/ nag tsho/ lung a me phyag sor ba rnams kyis mdzad
pa'i rnam thar/ mtshon cha 'khor lo/ rma bya dug 'joms/ dgyer bsgom rdo rje'i glu/ sems dpa'i rim pa/ lam khyer chos bco brgyad/ gtsug gi nor bu te/ rgya gzhung 'di
rnams dang 'brel ba'i blo sbyong yig sna brgya drug cu re bgrangs kyi bshad lung/

rje mus chen gyis mdzad pa'i spyod khri che chung gnyis kyi steng nas/ do lugs kyi nyams len khrigs bkod/ stong phrag brgya pa/ byams chos sde lnga/ de dag gi bsgom khrid/
'jam bsdud bzang gsum sogs lung brjod las 'das pa nyin re bzhin yul nas dgon par bsnyags te/ chos thun gcig la yang snga phyi med par thob cing/ 'di'i skabs byang sems rin
po che ma yang/ a ma dang lhan du spyan ras gzigs 'gro 'dul gyi dbang/ rgyal po bka' 'bum gyi lung/ sems nyid ngal gso dang/ zhi byed utpa la'i 'dab drug gi bsgom chos/
dam pa sangs rgyas kyi ding ri brgyad cu ma grags pa'i ngo sprod mang po dang/ gtsang smyon pas bsgrigs pa'i mi la'i rnam thar mgur 'bum/ snga phyi lo re bzhin rgyun ma
chad pa'i tshe dbang/ chos skyong gi bka' bsgo sogs grangs su btab nas brgya phrag long nges yod/ byang sems rin po ches dus 'khor mar kun mkhyen don yod dpal dang/ paN chen
chos rje'i bsngags pa kho na brjod cing/ yab sras gnyis kyi rnam thar dang/ zhal bkod 'ba' zhig gsung ba rna bar 'jags pas/ de dus phyogs zhen gyi pho rgyus che bar byung/
lo bcu 'gro ba la slar drung pa chos rje'i spyan sngar dbyar bar ma rab byung dang/ lo de'i zla ba dgu pa la dge tshul zhus/ dge bsnyen sdom brgyad rtsa 'grel/ kA ra
vc: kA rikA lnga bcu pa/ sum brgya pa rtsa 'grel rnams kyi lung stsal/ rab tu byung phyin chad pha ma'i khyim du gnas par mi rung pas dgon par shog gsung/ dgun de nas dbus
gtsang la nam 'gro/ drung pa chos rje'i zhal drung las skad cig kyang ma bral bar bsdad/ bu ston chos 'byung drung btsun

bzang brtan pas zhus pa'i zhar chos la gnang zhing/ khyod shes rab che bar 'dug pa 'di lta bu'i bstan pa la srid zhu che ba'i sems la nges shes brtan po phyogs rer ma song
ba'i blo rgya bskyed dgos gsung ba deng sang yang sems la gsal bar 'dug/ sman bla'i mdo brgyad brgya pa/ mkhan chen bo dhi satwa'i cho ga 'bring po/ mchims kyi mdo bshad
chen mo/ jo gdan grags gzhon gyi chog bsgrigs/ gnas brtan phyag mchod/ don zhabs lha lnga dang dpa' bo gcig pa'i rigs gtad/ a mo gha pA sha'i rtogs pa/ de nyid bcu drug gi
cho ga sogs phyogs 'di'i rgya bod kyi lugs ma tsang ba med pa/ gzhan yang sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang/ rgya mtshor ma 'dus pa'i zur bka' rnam par dag pa ji snyed pa'i rjes
gnang/ yig lung yang stsal/ nang sel gyi phyag len phan tshun la yang nan tan du sbyor bar mdzad cing/ khyad par phyogs 'dir kun rig gi cho ga 'di kho na dgos pa la/
dbang tsam yang ma thob par chog bral du 'jug pa sogs dar la ma smin par 'dug pas/ 'di la 'khrig chud pa'i phyag rgya phra mo yan chad la brnyas par ma song ba'i bslab sbyangs
yang dag bgyis ces bka' gnang zhing/ kun rig gi dbang/ sbyong rgyud la mchan bshad zhib mo/ gzhan phan skor gsum gyi lung/ cho ga'i phyag khrid mthong ba brgyud pa'i
bka' drin la 'god par mdzad rjes/ lo gsum gyi dgun zla ba bzhi re'i bar lam 'bras chos thun shin tu che ba/ nyi tshod tsam la yang snga phyi med pa'i gaNDi sgras bskul
nas/ bar chad kyi mtshan ma cung zad kyang med par mthar phyin pa kho na'i sgo nas bzlas pa lan gsum du thos pas/ dmigs

pa'i spyod mtshams rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum gyi/ rgyas pa na brgyad cu rtsa dgu 'bring po gsum/ bsdus pa dgur byed pa'i nang sel/ de dag gi lung sbyor ngos 'dzin tshig zur tsam
yang ma brjed par/ phyis rang gis gzhan la 'chad pa na yang de nyid kho na spod pa las zin bris sogs kyi dpe 'dzin la ma ltos par byung/ rjes su 'dren pa gzhan dag las
bzlas pa lan du mar zhus pa'i tshe yang/ sngar ma thob pa'i yig cha'i lung gsar 'phel tsam/ spyi bshad kyi dgag sgrub du ma la yid ches skyes pa'i spobs pa gong 'phel las/
rgyu lam gyi skabs bden gnyis gzugs rnam du slong ba/ lam khrid dngos kyi tshe gong ma'i gsung snying dag la phyis 'byung gi zer sgra gang gis yang ma slad pa'i bsgom
don brjen pa/ don thob kyi tshig gcig ma chad/ dgos med kyi 'bru gcig ma lhag pa'i ston tshul thun bzhi'i chu bo dus khor mor nyi tshod sor gang la sngags phyi ma mchis
pa thugs nyams su bdar ba'i bka' babs yid ches des sems 'phrogs te/ lam srol 'byed pa po rnal 'byor dbang phyug nyid dang mjal yang som nyi gsal ba'i zhus tig skrag rtse
tshad kyang dri rgyu mi snang la/ lo re bzhin yang lung yig sna drug cu sna gcig kyang ma chad pa'i steng du/ snga ma la gzhung bshad gsung bgros ma/ yig chung bdun/ bla
ma'i rnam thar zhib mo rnam dag/ bar ston zin bris/ dmar gyis mdzad pa'i lung sbyar rnams sbyor ba'i bshad lung/ bar ma la gzhung bshad man ngag mdzod/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul
khrims kyi mchan bcas/ brgyud pa'i rnam thar ngo mtshar snang ba/ khrid yig sbas don gsal ba sogs/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pas mdzad do

cog ma lus pa lhan du bsgrigs pa'i bshad lung/ rjes ma khyed dpun dbus gtsang la 'gro ba'i rdzong chos yin gsung/ snang gsum skabs zab mo mdo lnga/ lam 'bras chos 'byung gis
mtshon pa'i lung rgyun yod do cog zhib rgyas dang bcas pa'i lam 'bras shin tu smin par thob/ slar dge 'dun nyung bsdus la/ tog rtse ba'i bsam mi khyab/ Dom bhi ba'i lhan
cig skyes grub/ mtsho skyes kyi zab pa'i tshul dgu/ klu sgrub kyi mchod rten drung thob/ nag po spyod pa'i gtum mo lam rdzogs/ nag po ba'i yon po srong ba/ intra bo dhi'i
phyag rgya lam/ ngag gi dbang phyug gi yi ge med pa ste/ lam skor phyi ma brgyad kyi khrid/ rgya bod kyi yig lung mtha' dag byin rlabs sgo gnyis/ sgo drug chos 'grel du
grags pa/ shanti pa'i mdo rgyud bsre ba/ rin chen rdo rje/ dznyA na shrI/ sher 'byung blo gros rnams kyis ting nge 'dzin sems/ 'byung ba lus 'khrugs/ phyi rol gdon gyis
bar chad bsrung ba ste bar gsum sel du grags pa/ ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa'i gnyug ma dran gsal/ nA ro pa'i phyag rgya chen po sdug bsngal gsum sel rnams kyi bshad lung
kyang bstsal/ mdor na 'brog mi lo tsA ba chos kyi rgya mtsho de nyid la bka' babs pa'i lam 'bras/ lam skor zhar byung gi gdams pa rnams tshang bar thos shing/ gsung las
kyang kyai rdor bka' babs phyi ma rnams la gtso che'i chos sna sum cu dgu yid ches kyi gnas su yod pa ltar/ man ngag lugs la sa chen yab sras gsum gyi lhan cig tu bsgrigs
pa'i dkar chag tu thebs pa/ yig sna drug cu mig ltar gces par bskyangs dgos ces 'doms pa'i don la phyis dpyad pa na/ rje btsun chen

pos yi ger 'god pa la 'di dag las mang nyung logs su sbas pa'i dpe yod re kan zhes gtsigs chen pos g.yar dam du legs par bzhes pa 'di las/ phyogs 'di'i lo rgyus tshad ma dang/
smra ba po 'di las lhag pa'i bla ma tshad ma yang rnyed pa dka' ba'i phyir/ dkar chag tu thebs pa ji snyed dag gi lam srol 'di'i lus ma tshang ba med cing/ yan lag yongs
su rdzogs par yid ma ches na/ slob brgyud so so'i yi ge rigs mtha' dag ma 'tshogs na/ lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa rdzogs par ma thob pa'i 'khrul rtog gi spros pa'i g.yeng
bas/ lam gyi rkang stor ba la 'tshogs chas su nam yang mi bya ste/ 'di ni nges pa'i snying gtam yang dag pa'o//de ltar zab rgyas kyi gdams pa zhu dus/ a ma drin can des/
thog mar tshugs ston/ bar du sems bskyed kyi skabs/ mthar chos kyi grol ston rnams chos nyan dang bcas pa'i der 'dus thams cad la mang ja bsnyen bkur/ rje'i drung du rin
po che'i maNDal/ na bza' cha tshang ba/ gya nom pa'i 'bul ba yang lo re bzhin bgyis/ de mthar bdag chen blo gros pa nas brgyud pa'i gur zhal gyi bka' rjes gnang/ lung
man ngag/ phyag len zhal shes che mo yang thugs rjes gzung/ de nas rang lo bcu gsum lon pa la dbus gtsang du slob gnyer la chas pa'i skabs der/ a la a phyi rnams/ drung pa
chos rdze vc: rjepa la skyang/ byang sems rin po che ngos la mos zhen che ba tsam yod pa'i bag chags kyis/ ska rags sgrub phug tu rkang gtad phyin/ zhag bdun tsam gyi bar
la/ phyag na rdo rje 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i dbang/ rdo rje tshe'i sgrub thabs/ khro mo'i rnam thar dpag bsam 'khri shing

dang/ khro phu ba'i man ngag brgya rtsa'i lung/ snying po don gsum gyi khrid rdzong chos su nyan/ slar yang drung pa chos rje'i zhabs pad la btud de/ tshe dbang/ sgrol dkar/
rnam rgyal 'joms/ chos skyong gi bka' bsgo sogs lam gyi rkyen sel la dmigs pa'i chos bka' de rnams nyin re bzhin stsal nas/ nang par shar phyogs la thegs pa'i do nub srod
kyi ja gral la spyi 'grogs slob gnyer ba kun la yang dag pa'i bka' bkod thugs tshas ma dor ba zhib rgyas su gnang zhing/ khyad par bdag la khyod na tshod shin tu phra
ba yin yang da lta gzhung chen 'di tsam yod pas slob gnyer yang cha mthun yong ba'i re ba yod/ mdor na bslab sbyangs kyi yon tan che chung gang shes kyang rgyud zhi zhing
dul ba la gnas dgos/ sems dang chos su ma 'dres na yon tan gyis mi phan pa'i gtam rgyud/ sngar bka' gdams kyi chos mang du thob pa'i tshe thos pa'i de dag ma brjed pa dang/
khyad par thos pas dregs nas bslab pa la khyad sod byas na/ ngan song du skyes tshe thos pas mi phan par/ zla ba sgron mes zhus pa'i mdo las/ji snyed chos kyi rnam pas
byang chub kyang//thos pas rgyags te tshul khrims mi bsrung na//tshul khrims 'chal pas ngan 'gror de 'gro ste//de la thos pa mang pos skyob mi nus/ tshig bcad 'di snying
la yang yang zhog/ mi lus rnyed/ tshul khrims rnam par dag pa bsrungs/ theg pa chen po'i chos la thos bsam byed rgyu yod pa bsod nams bsags pa yin/ nged na tshod rgas pa
tshun dbus gtsang du sdod rgyu yong ba dka'/ gang sdod ring le lor ma song ba'i 'bad pa gyis/ spyir da lan brtag pa tshun 'tshub cing/ bar chad kyi sgo

che bar 'dug pas/ phyogs bcu mun sel sogs thun pod rnams klog pa dang/ lam la yang kha don/ phyi gtor nang gtong rnams ma chag par gyis/ thub pa dgongs gsal nas gsungs pa'i
phyogs gar 'gro'i sangs rgyas rnams la skyabs 'gro gsol btab phreng skor re tsam yid rtse gcig pas bsgrubs/ dus dang gnas skabs kun tu rkyen bde sdug ci byung yang chos
kyi dgos pa ma shor ba gal che/ 'di nam 'chir 'chang ba'i zhal ta'i dngos gzhi yin no// ces brtse bas rjes su gdams pa'i rdo rje'i gsung 'di dag ni/ dred po chos rgyus mkhan
bdag la gnas skabs thams cad du dran pa tsam gyis chos min gyi snang ba btsan thabs su bzlog pa'i yid ches kyis ngo bo mthar thug pa'i bka' drin 'khor ba med pa'i byin
chen po nam du'ang mi brjed pa'i gzer bu ther zug tu gnas te/ zab mo mtshal mgo ma'i gegs sel ltar/ dgos dus yig ngor lus pa ma yin pa'i/ dran chog lam gyi go char dngos
su rtol ba 'di nyid yin/ dus der 'bral bar mi spobs pa'i gdung shugs ngang nas ci bya tol med pa'i yus kyis zhabs spyi bor bkod pa tsam la sems kyi rten po byas/ mig chu
rgyun mi 'chad par 'dzag bzhin du shar phyogs la yong/ byis pa'i blo tshod dang sbyar ba'i bla ma'i mos gus rang blos mi khrel ba tsam de dus skyes 'dug/ zla phyed song
ba'i lam du/ las stod sman khab pa'i nyer 'tshe la brten yid 'byung che bar byung yang/ yongs dus kyi ma 'ongs lung bstan dran/ zhe sdang mngon gyur ba spu rtse tsam yang
ma skyes/ de nas rim gyis dpal ldan sa skyar sleb/ lha khang chen mo steng shod/ bzhi thog/ sgo rum/ bla brang

shar sogs kyi rten gsum gnas mjal la zla phyed zhib len byas/ kha 'u'i brag rdzong du kun spangs rin po che la/ dpal mgon thim pa'i brag sgo de nyid du zhal bzhi pa'i rjes
gnang zhus pas/ ti se/ bsil ba tshal sogs chos skyong gi gnas rnams nas mgon po 'khor bcas ling ling 'byon pa'i snang ba/ ye shes dbab ring la gsal bar byung zhing/ dbang
bka' rjes gnang zhus so cog la de 'dra'i zil yong mi dran/ phyis rang gi slob ma dam tshig can 'ga' re la rjes gnang byed dus/ rang rgyud la sngar gyi myong ba de ji lta
ba lan 'ga' re gsal bar byung/de nas zla ba gnyis pa'i dang po'i tshes la chos grwa gser mdog can du sleb pa'i dpyid chos nas slob gnyer btsugs/ slob dpon rin po che'i zhal
mnga' vc: snganas nyin re bzhin thun mong zin thun dang/ bsdus sbyor rtsi ba rgyun ldan du byas/ de lo spyi chos la sdom gsum Tikka nyid kyis mdzad pa'i steng nas bshad
lung/ gser thur/ bya pa dris lan sogs gnas 'di'i yig cha rdzogs par byung/ zhogs pa sngar mnga' ris su gzung ba'i phar tshad sdom rig sogs kyi gzhung brjed gso'i rnam
pas blta rtog byas dus/ rang yul du brgya tshar mang po'i bshar sbyangs smin pa'i nus pas tshig phyed la yang 'khrul med gzhung gnon pa mi non pa tsam byung ba des slob dpon
rin po che dgyes pa rab kyi mthar phyin te/ a la 'byon lam sar sbyang 'bru cig ma mdzad pa la/ gtsang zhing ma 'dres par gzhung chen 'di rnams thogs med du thon pa mi
brjed pa'i gzungs thob pa yang rang du 'dug go gsung/ bdag cag rnams la gsar chos su tshe dbang grub rgyal ma/ seng ge gdong

can/ 'jam dkar/ dbyangs can ma/ mi g.yo ba dkar po/ rnam sras ser chen/ rnam sras dkar po/ rnam sras drag po rnams kyi rjes gnang rnams gnang/ dbyar chos 'brum bu'i rtser bas
chos ra'i spros pa bcad/ nang mtshams bsdams/ gung tshigs stengs su slob dpon mkhas pa'i zhal las/ sngon paN chen rin po che la chos rje blo gros rgyal mtshan pas gsan
dus/ nged rang gis skyor mgo byas pa'i gsung rgyun ji lta ba la tshig phyed kyang 'khrul med yin gsung ba'i rtags rigs tshang bar btang zhing/ phyis ri zhing na de dus kyi
phyag dpe dngos mthong bas ji ltar gsung ba bzhin du 'dug pas shin tu ngo mtshar che ba'i yid ches slar yang skyes/ dus der nged yun la nye thung du dgong ja gral stengs
su/ snyan ngag dpag bsam 'khri shing gi yal 'dab gsum bzhi re'i lung ma chad par rdzogs par bstsal/ ston chos kyi dbu btsugs tsam/ rig gter rang grol vc: 'grel?zin du
nye ba na/ a jo la 'brum bus btab/ glo bur e waM du nad gros byas phyin/ der chos rje ngor chen drung du tshe dbang/ sgrol dkar/ chos skyong gi bka' bsgo tsam bla ma gong
ma'i dbang khang du mnos nas/ nad bsrungs la dmigs sna tshogs yum gyi sgom lung zhus/ grangs bsnyen rdzogs par byas/ rang 'grel gyi mjug tshang bar blo la tshud rjes/ dgon
nang phal cher 'brum bus khyab pa la brten/ yang dgon rtser bros/ der sngar lhan du yongs pa'i grwa pa slob gnyer ba sha stag nyi shu rtsa gynis yod pa la/ a jos sna grangs
bcu dgu gum/ nged rang gsum lus pa'i snang tshul de la brten/ nyin mtshan 'khor mar skye bas sa la mi chags pa lta bu blo rtser yun

ring po sgyur/ zla ba brgyad pa de rang du mtshams bsdams nas bsdad/ skabs der tshe 'di blos ma thongs pa'i mi rngun gyi khengs grags phra mos sems bskul/ slob gnyer gyi mjug
'thud pa'i mdun pas/ don bdun cu/ yan lag rgyas bshad/ spyi ma thal rnams blo 'dzin byas/ bla ma kham pa'i ngag slob kyis bsdus sbyor mang ba brtsams/ ston chag dus/ slob
dpon rin po ches yang dben du phebs/ zhag bdun tsam gdan chags nas/ zhal mkhyen gyi rnam pas nged la phyag rtags gnang ba kun gyi nang na/ mtshan nyid pa skam po la bsgom
med/ sangs mi rgya gsung ba'i bka' bkyon yang yang gnang byung bas/ da lan mtshan nyid pa'i bsgom chos shig 'bul dgos gsung/ btsan kha bo che'i lugs theg chen rgyud
bla ma'i khrid dang/ sa tshab nas brgyud pa'i dbu ma lta khrid/ kA ma la shI la'i bsgom rim dril don chos rje rong ston gyis mdzad pa rnams la lung bshad/ thugs dgyes pa'i
zhal 'phros mo rgyus mang po dang spel nas gnang bas thang chad pa bsos pa lta bu zhig byung/ dus der ba lu me tog sa nas brgyud pa'i ril bu'i lung zhus te bsnyen tshad
zhag nyer gcig bar chad med par bgyis/ de nas zla phyed tsam nas 'brum bu'i thag chod/ kun spangs rje phebs zer ba thos pas yid mgu/ slar dgon par skyes/ slob gnyer cha
mthun tsam gyi ngang nas kun spangs rin po che la 'dod chos mang bar thob/ de dus gnang ba'i lam 'bras la ma zhugs/ bka' las chos rje mchog grub pa dang nged gnyis bdag chen
rin po che la lam 'bras zla ba bco brgyad lhan du zhus pa'i mched grogs yin/ khyed rang gis khong ba'i drung du

lam 'bras tshar gsum thob 'dug pa/ cha lag rnams rdzogs par ster gsung/ rgyud lam bdag med phyi nang/ lcags ri'i khongs mi 'da' ba'i zab chos bzhi/ tshar gsum khug pa/ brda
tshig brgyud/ brda don gsal ba/ mgon rkyang/ sgrub pa lung sbyin sogs ma lus par thugs la btags/ mon rdzong pa zla ba rgyal mtshan nas brgyud pa'i lam 'bras zhwa ma lugs
kyang thob/ tshe dbang lugs gnyis/ sgrol dkar 'byung po 'dul byed/ chos skyong che chung/ pu tra'i zur bka'/ dur khrid vc: khrodbdag po/ dkar bdud lcam dral/ dmar po skor
gsum/ dmar mo skor gsum/ gza' bsrungs thos pa don ldan/ bka' gdams thig le'i dbang/ de'i bsgom khrid zhal shes snyug la paN chen gyis mdzad pa/ tshe khrid/ smar khrid mdzub
btsugs/ phag mo sor mo/ kurma pA da'i byin rlabs khrid bcas/ su kha chos drug/ mgon po'i dpe lung tshang bar zhus shing/ mgon po'i nang khrid kyi phyed tsam du sleb
dus/ slob dpon nam rin pa glo bur du gshegs pas rkyen byas/ khrid sham la lung tsam yang ma gnang ba 'phro can du lus// bsrung 'khor brag rdzong ma zhal shes kyis rgyan pa/
khyad par dpal mgon zhal gyi bsrung bzlog snyan brgyud zla ba gcig gi bar gsung ngag las 'bru gcig ma nyams par nyan cing khong du chud/ de mtshams glang thang nas sangs
rgyas dbon rin po che phebs pa dang mjal bas/ khyed na ning bar dgug yun ring zhing 'brum bu'i rtser bas snyugs bud yod gsung/ mas bu gcig la bgyi bas dper mi mtshon pa'i
thugs rjes gzung/ dpyid chos la dbu ma/ dbyar 'dul ba'i spyi chos gnang ba'i chos gaN dang lhan du

snga phyi sor gang med pa/ bya rgod phung po'i chos khri gdal ba der gzhung shog gcig kyang ma chad par nyan/ zur chos paN chen rin po che'i rnam thar pad dkar phreng ba/ dbyangs
can ma'i skor tshang ba/ phyag rdor gos sngon can/ rnam sras rigs brgyad kyi rjes gnang rnams thob/ gnang chags kyis bkra shis brtsegs par ja bur bzhes spro/ dpe cha/
bris sku/ phyag phreng sogs nyer mkho'i gnang sbyin/ yid shes bcags pa'i sems khrid thabs mkhas lan gcig lan gnyis ma yin pa kho nas drangs te/ sngar gyi skyo shas ngang
gis srabs/ 'tshang 'bru'i bkas slob gnyer ma nan bskul mdzad pa de nyid layid ches skye/ chos rar phar phyin/ sdom gsum/ 'dul ba rnams kyi gtong chos sgo du ma zhal slob
len pa/ dpyil vc: spyilbur zhogs rgyugs phar phyin dka' 'grel/ bzhed tshul rgya mtsho'i rlabs phreng/ sbyor Tika gnad kyi sgron me/ skabs lnga pa yan gyi thal ngag dbang
po rdo rje rnams zin mtshams/ slob dpon rin po che'i dgongs pa mthar thug tu 'dug pas nang du lung chos snying po 'dzin pa'i dbu btsugs/ Tikka gtong chos pa byin dang
lhan du rong Tika gi rgyugs len dang/ logs su 'jug sgo gsum pa'i gzhung chos gnang ba la mi nyag byang chub dpal bas rab sgang du gtong myong 'dug pas skyor ba'i grogs ldan
bgyis/ nam zla dus bzhi khor mor nyin gcig kyang chad pa med pa'i bslabs sbyangs shin tu 'phel bar yod pa'i skabs nas mkhan slob dang bcas pa'i dge 'dun mgron khang du
mtshan brjod la thegs shul/ chos mdzad 'dzims pas rgyugs bsnon pa byas/ nyin

re la 'dul ba'i bslab bya'i shog bu gsum re gzung/ nyin gung snyan ngag gi phyi mo/ rtse thang pa sangs rgyas lhun grub/ drung yig chos rgyal/ chos mdzad nam rgyal rnams kyi
mchod yar zhig phran bu 'ga' zhig bltas pas/ tshigs bcad rkang chag tho re ba tsam shes pa byung ba'i 'phros sangs rgyas dbon chen pa'i snyan du dgongs 'dug pas/ nyin cig
padma rkang gtad du 'bod pa la gnang byung/ bkra shis brtsegs par sleb 'phral/ drung pa snyan ngag cig la thugs mdun yod na 'di ltar mdzad dgos gsung/ snyan ngag me long
la 'jug pa'i sgo dang/ don 'grel paN chen rin po ches mdzad pa de gnyis kyi lung tsam stsal/ don rgyan gyi dpe/ gung thang pa bde blo/ spang lo/ bo dong thams cad mkhyen
pa/ dpal mkha' spyod dbang po/ sgra pa saM gha shrI/ paN chen rin po ches thub pa la bstod pa'i rab byed/ de rnams kyi dpe lag tu stsal/ rje nyid kyi dbu bdag gi mgo la
reg nas/ ma snying nas 'bod dod byangs can ma//ma ltar brtse ba gang gi yid//yid dam bzhin du rjes zung la//la 'or mkhas pa'i spobs pa stsol//ces gsung phra lhang lhang
ba rna bar son pas/ zol dang cam bu ma yin par mi shes mun pa'i cha nges par sel ba'i rjes dpag skye ba byung/ der ja gral la yang yang gleng bgros byung bas/ snyan ngag
phul byung dgongs pa'i rnam cha shar 'dug/ da 'di dag gi tshig don la shes rab zhib pos dpyad na bstan pa spyi'i gnad don dgongs yod pa yin gsung/ paN chen rin po ches mdzad
pa'i dam pa tog dkar gyi bzlos gar/ sa ra ha/ lU nag dril gsum/ rgyan drug/ yon tan 'od/

bI ru pa/ zla ba grags pa rnams kyi rtogs brjod/ gangs can gyi rgyan drug/ sa paN la kun las khyad par du bsngags pa/ byams pa'i dkar chag/ chos 'khor gyi deb gter mdzangs
pa dga' byed/ sdeb sbyor me tog chun po'i don 'grel/ smra sgo mtshon cha'i Tikka'i lung rnams phal cher dgongs ja'i steng du thob/ dus de tsa na bstan pa yar ldan du 'dug
pas grwa dpung yang 'phel rgyas che zhing/ snyoms chung la yongs kyi brtse ba/ phan tshun bslab sbyangs kho na'i 'gran dang/ grub mtha'i tshig zur nang sel bag tsam la mkhas
pa nang rtsod pa'i brjod gleng cung zad las/ 'jig rten lab ris kyi rjes mi spyod/ 'thab rtsod kyang 'khon 'dzin dang bral ba sgyu ma'i gar mkhan gyi rol rtsed lta bur
ston pa/ myos 'gyur/ phyi dro'i kha zas sogs la ngo tsha dang 'dzem bag che ba'i kun spyod ma log par yod grwa sar sdod rin tshogs pa rgya mtsho lta bu'i dbus nas 'khos
med kyi btsun chung bdag la slob dpon mkhas pas thugs kyi brtse ba mi mnyams pa'i bka' drin chen pos/ spyan gyi 'bras bu ltar 'tsho bar mdzad de/ nam mjal yang slob gnyer
gyi bskyed ci byung dri mal kho na gnang ba dang/ sku mdun na dge bshes che phra su yod dang 'bel gtam gyi sleng slong mdzad/ dal bar bsdad na phangs pa lta bu'i brtse
gdung gnang/ skabs der grwa tshang du sdom gsum rab dbye'i sngags sdom gyi dbu nas gzhung skyur gnang ba la/ de thad kyi TIkka bstan pa'i sgron me rang gi tshig rigs tshang
ba dbugs theng gcig la bshar bas/ dge 'dun tshogs pa thams cad kyang thugs ha las shing/ nye ba 'ga' res khong rang gi thugs rab kyi 'khyongs

'dug pas 'phral slob gnyer ma nus kyang chog pa 'dug/ 'o skol gyi mi tshe ril po 'di kho na la bshar sbyang byas kyang 'di 'dra'i byang ba gang la yong zer/ khyad par mchod
yar gyi rtsom pa'i rjes su 'brengs pa'i krig krig lta bu ma yin par ngag las gang thon rtsom nyams gzhan pas thon pa'i ngang nas/ bla ma brgyud pa nas brtsams/ bka' drin
can gyi slob dpon la thug gi bar mchod yar rgyas par phul bas/ der 'dus thams cad shin tu dgyes pa byung/ de dus lo bco lnga'i ngo gsar brtsam yin/ de nub grwa tshang chen
mor mkhas pa lu gu gdong pas gsol ja gnang/ gzengs bstod kyi che bstod mang po mdzad/ mtshan nyid kyi slob gnyer 'di mus kyi mus kyi dbyar gnam dros pa 'dra ba cig gi
ngang nas dgongs yong bas/ ngang thung gi gtugs gtugs gnang na gtan mi bstub/ chos skad kyi gzhi things 'dug pa/ mnga' ris nas spyan 'dren gyi bar chad ma byung ba gcig pus
chog pa 'dug/ da lan 'dir spyan drangs pa'i zhu ba'i snying po/ sngar paN chen rin po che nyid la ma gsan pa'i lhag phyis chos rje rin po che kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa
la bka' 'bum gyi zhabs tshang bar zhus/ rang re'i drung nas la bzhugs pa de'i lung rdzogs pa cig gsan thub na 'phral gyi dpe sna re tsam dgongs pa'i thugs bskyed las/ 'di
khag che zhing bstan pa'i rgyun la phan pa yin gsung ba'i bslab bya nan tan mdzad pas snying dga' spro che bar byung/ phyir sngags sor nged rang dpun khang gsar ba'i grwa
khang na sdod dus/ de'i mdun na khong pa bzhugs 'dug pa mthong ba tsam gyis dpun gnyis ka tshe gcig pa'i dad mos skyes/ snang

chags kyis skam ja sbyor re tsam 'bul ba dang/ phyag ris su bkyon pa'i bsdus sbyor gyi gnang sbyin len pa la 'dzem bag med par yang yang phyin pa'i skabs/ 'brum bu'i stabs
kyis mtshams bsdams pas 'grul chad/ de min ci la thug kyang zur slob tu bsten snyam pa gzhan rkyen la ma ltos par nged rang spun gnyis ka'i shes rgyud la gros btab pa ltar
lhan du byung/ phyis dge ba'i bshes gnyen cig gshegs pa thos pa'i gtam la 'di las yid skyo ba dang/ sha 'bras pa yong ma dran te/ skye ba snga ma'i 'brel pa tshe rab cig
gis bsdus pa 'dra/ da lta yang rnam pa'i yul na wal wal/ dran pa'i yul na sal sal/ rig pa'i rnam 'gyur gyi 'khrab na kho 'dra ba zhig dgos/ sdug gshis ngan la byed spyod
tsog pa ya pho'i spre'u 'dra ba la g.yas ci yod snyam pa rtsol med du gnang chags kyis 'char/ skabs shed cig ja gral la slob dpon rin po che'i zhal snga nas/ chos rje rin
po che kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa'i gdan sa mdzad pa'i 'phros gtam gleng blangs zhig la/ bsod de yong du spyod de'i dpe'i/ bka' chen bco brgyad kyi TIka gzhung tshig 'bru
phyed ma 'khrul bar ljags thog nas 'don pa dang/ nyin zhag phrug gcig la dkyil 'khor mi 'dra ba bdun cu rtsa gnyis kyi zhal 'byed pa'i rnal 'byor la nan tan myur mdzad
pa la yon tan med pa'i mthong dang/ rje de lo rta las mi bzhugs pa thugs kyis mkhyen te/ gdan sar phebs pa'i nyin rang nas bka' bstsal thog mar gnang ba la yid ches spu tsam
med/ sa 'dir paN chen rin po che'i bstan pa'i rgyun la dgongs bka' 'bum gyi lung tshang ba zhig yong la re ba'i dus ma chad par

gsung ba la/ na maH gu ru bhye'i gdags gzhi byas pa la sogs smin pa 'dra/ da gang las kyang bka' 'bum gyi lung 'di ma chad na khyad che gsung ba la/ sngar gyi snying gtam skul
'debs de dran nas/ 'don lung rdzogs pa zhig gi thugs rje gnang dgos zhus/ zhal gyi yang bzhes te/ rong chen/ kun mkhyen don yod dpal gnyis kyi rnam thar/ dbu ma'i byung
tshul lta khrid chen mo/ tshul gnyis rnam 'byed rtsa 'grel/ rngog lo chen po'i rnam thar bstod pa/ springs yig bdud rtsi'i thigs pa'i rnam 'grel/ sman bla'i bris vc: drislan/
bzang spyod/ byams smon/ sher snying/ blo sbyong tshig rkang brgyad ma rnams kyi tshig 'grel/ mkhas pa 'jug sgo'i Twikka vc: TIkkadang dris lan/ bde ba can gyi zhing
bkod smon lam/ smon lam bdun cu pa'i don 'grel/ mtshan brjod Twikka vc: TIkka/ gsang 'dus dang bde mchog rnam bshad/ chos phran brgya rtsa rnams kyi bshad lung rim gyis
thob/ lo ngo gsum po de mdo phyogs kyi nan tan cha mthun yod pa'i skabs/ sdod sa lcang gdong rin po che'i dpyil bu na yod dus/ phar phyin spyi don gsung rgyun/ bshor grogs
la dge slong dol bu nub re bzhin grwa khang nas nam tshad brgyad cha tsam la yong ba'i skabs zhig gi rmi lam du/ nged gnyis dgon pa'i mdun na bang 'gran byed kyi 'dug
pa la/ khong g.yangs la shor ba'i rkyen byas rmi lam zin/ drung pa chos rje'i drung du thal phyin/ zhal ta cig zhu 'dod la sgo phye bas gnyid sad 'phral smras pas/ slob
dpon pas dgongs ni gu'i dbu 'dzugs pa'i nyin/ deng sang thugs gnyer dus bsgom khrid gsan skabs min kyang/ mnal lam rang zin 'dug pa tshun khrid la

phebs pa legs gsung zla chos cig zhus/ skabs shed drung nas yon rin pa dang lhan du phag mo brda bzhi'i dbang/ do ha skor gsum/ par bu ba'i Twaikka vc: TIkkasa dpyad/ lo rgyus
sgrung 'grel zhib bshad/ do khrid dang bcas pa zhus/ bdag rang rkyang bu la slar sgo lo'i gtum mo po ldum pa la gsan pa de yang bstsal/ mnga' ris la 'gro dus rdzong chos/
gang blo ma'i bstod bsgrub kyi rjes gnang rten 'brel bsgrigs/ 'phral yul du dngos dang brgyud pa'i bka' lung brtse bas byon pa'i grangs kyang dpag par mi nus pa'i tshod
tsam yod cing/ yul la ldog dus dngos su bka' bstsal 'doms pa la/ da res las brgya'i bshad pa/ mdo rtsa'i gtong chos gnyis ka'i dge 'dun bsdu ba'i gaNDi'i thad na 'dug
pas phrin las rgya chen po yong nges/ sngar nged kyi mthong snang ma drung pa gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sku me dpung gi dbus na bzhugs pa'i gsal snang brdzun med du byung
bas/ 'di la yi dam gyi gtso bo gnang ba zhu/ phyis 'byon pa zhig byung na bsal pa yongs su rdzogs pa yin na'ang/ yar phyogs mdzad pa rgya ches pas thon pa dka' gsung ba'i
nges gsal mngon sum du gdams/ chos grwa chen po nas btegs pa'i nyin/ bkra shis lhun por zhag sa byas/ lha'i btsun pa blo bzang bstan pa'i zhal snga nas sngar 'khyung ltar
dpe med pa'i thugs tshad bskyangs/ lam gyi nyer mkho mtha' dag gis re ba yid bzhin sbyor bar mdzad de/ byang ngam rings su bde bar phyin/ der zla ba drug bsdad pa'i skabs
khang gsar du khams gsum gyi 'dren pa gling kha ba chen po mjal ba la phyin/ lha babs kyi dus bzang po la dgyes pa'i

'dzum zhal gsal bar mthong/ de nas gzung ste zla ba phyed gnyis bar zhabs pad bsten chos bka' thog ma lU i pa'i lugs kyi bde mchog gi dbang/ kha che paN chen nas brgyud pa'i
bde mchog dkar po'i byin rlabs dpyal a mo gha'i yig cha'i steng nas rdzogs rim dmigs khrid/ chos rje rong ston gyis paN chen shAkya shrI las dngos su gsan pa'i bde mchog
dkar po'i tshe sgrub/ dpa' bo dur khrod bdag po'i rjes gnang/ de dag dang 'brel ba'i lung rnams smin par thob/ der chos rje ngor chen blo vc: globor spyan drangs pa'i phebs
lam byang la sgyur/ rje yab sras zhal mjal ba'i legs tshogs gnang ba'i skabs/ shar nas kyi dpon slob rnams la tshe dbang/ rgyu lam/ lam zab/ bir bsrungs/ rnal 'byor
ma rnams rdzong chos su gnang ba kun lhan cig thob/ khyad par rang la dpe med pa'i thugs rjes/ bdud rtsi ril bu'i gnang sbyin/ lung bstan bslab bya yang dag pas yid lhag
par tshim/ 'brel tshad don ldan gyi mos gus snying nas skyes/ slar bsnyen rdzogs don gnyer la yong 'dod rgyu mtshan phul bas/ bka' ma khrol ba/ de nas ring por ma lon par
bde ba can du gshegs pa la dgongs par 'dug pa/ bsams pas dus gsum gzigs pa'i yid ches rnyed/ sngar e waM du zhal ma mjal ba nas gsol ba btab pas/ rmi lam du 'dod rgyal gyi
rjes gnang nod pa'i dus kyi sku'i rnam pa ji lta ba bzhin 'char sgo ma 'dzol ba som nyi bral ba'i lam la bkod/ der zhabs la phyag byas yid 'phreng ba'i ngang nas rje'i
phyag phyir bkra shis/ lam bde bar zla ba bcu gcig pa'i bcu bzhi la blo vc: globo nang du phebs/ bco lnga'i nyi

shar nas bsu ba gya nom pa'i bkod pas rim par spyan drangs pa'i dus/ drung pa chos rje dang mjal bas lus sems la byin rlabs zhugs/ nges shes kyi mtshan ma brtan po byung/ de
'phral paN chen byams pa gling pa dang yang mjal/ dgyes pa chen pos brtse bar bsdams/ de nyin ka mkhan chen rin po che'i zhal gyi dkyil 'khor yang mthong ste bsam pa yid
bzhin du 'grub/ bcings pa blod pa ltar de nub rang gi khyim du phyin/ a ma dang mjal blo lhag par bde bar byung/ de lo smon thang du dgun ngo rje yab sras kyis rgyur/ lam
'bras sbags nas gsung pa'i chos grwar zhugs/ gsung rgyun yid la ci 'jags byas/ rgyud kyi tshul bzhi'i phyi rnam/ ljon shing gnyis kyi bzur 'debs skyar chos su gnang ba'i
zin thun 'dzin pa snga phyir chos thun tha dad nyan pa sogs nyi rangs pa sdod rgyu skar cig kyang med cing/ srod nas mtshan ma phyed par sgron me'i 'od la brten/ rgyud
sde spyi rnam/ mngon rtogs ljon shing gnyis kyi shog bu gsum gsum blo la gzung/ mtshan thog thag shar sbyang byas pas/ yum gyi dgongs pa la/ gung tsigs dam po byas// de
nas mtshan yal shar sbyang byed pa 'di 'dra la rlung yang langs nyen yod/ snying yang rje bar 'dug ces bzhes spro mang po bcos nas/ nga rang gi sring mo chung shos des skyel
du yong gi 'dug na'ang/ khyim sun 'byin pa'i nyes byas su song dogs cung zad kyang ma zos/ ngas shar sbyang gi skad dum cig bcag la bsdad kyis/ khyod rang zo la/ a ma'i
rtsar ngas zos song zhus byas zhag mang po bstud pas skabs skabs mun thum pa lus 'khyor ba tsam byung na'ang/

sos dal ma byas par skor ba dang chu 'thor ba sogs gnyid sang ba'i thabs bsten/ dus de'i snying rus la sus kyang 'gran du med pa'i tshul dpang po dang bcas pa kho na yin/ de
skabs paN chen byams pa gling pa yang lam 'bras gsan pa la thab btegs te smon thang nyid du phebs yod pas/ nyin re bzhin thun mtshams su rgyud gdams ngag gi 'bel gtam nyi
rtser zhus pas/ mtha' chod pa'i bshad pa yig ngo la ma ltos pa kho nas/ ma go ba'i gnas thams cad 'grol bar mdzad de/ 'di la ci skad gsung snyam dri gtugs phul ba thams
cad la sngon gyi grub mtha' smra ba rnams 'di'i skabs su 'di ltar bzhed/ kho 'di ltar bsam gsung ba sogs legs par bshad pa'i gtam gyis gang ma go ba de nyid la dpyis phyin
pa'i bshad pa mtha' 'khyongs pa stsal bas yid mgu ba thob pa'i bka' drin mdzad cing/ rgyud tshul bzhi'i bshad pa'i chos mtshams dang/ snang gsum grol ba dus mnyam du
mdzad/ sems bskyed skabs kyi skye bo dad can stong phrag 'dus pa'i dbus/ dgos skal gyi byang chub tu nges pa'i blo kha tsam min par skyes/ slob ma rjes 'dzin zhus/ bsags
sbyangs skabs de lo rgyu dus la zla ba phyed gnyis tsam 'gor ba'i bar/ drung pa chos rje'i drung du sngar zhal mjal tsam las/ shar nas sleb 'phral chos tshugs pa'i stabs
nas nub re tsam gsol ja zhu ba la phyin dus rgyud gnyan po nyan pa la nub yan byar mi stub/ bsags sbyangs skabs 'dir shog gsung ba'i bka' bzhin de bar dgon par mtshams se
byas snga phyi dpe 'dzin/ yig brgya/ maNDal sogs thun ma chag pa'i dge sbyor 'grus pa dang/ nyin gung kha

sku mdun du gsol rting ma'i steng du shar phyogs kyi skad bya gleng mol zhu ba/ slob gnyer ji ltar byung gi zhib spyod dris mal/ drung btsun pas gtso mdzad dang 'brel gtam
kho na gnang/ dgong ja'i steng gsum chos thun mi 'chag stsal ba'i thog mar khyed rang gi dbus gtsang nas zhu yig tu yang bkod/ gsol ba btab pa'i 'dod chos 'di bgyi gsung/
gshed dmar gyi rnal 'byor bzhi khrid/ rnam rtog 'od gsal/ bdud rtsi'i byin rlabs/ rang byin rlabs/ 'khor lo'i byin rlabs/ 'pho ba'i byin rlabs/ bdud rtsi 'od 'chang ma'i
rnal 'byor rnams/ rje yab sras gnyis ka la bka' mi bzhugs pas gsol ba 'debs mi mang ba byung stabs gsang nas bsdams/ sngar khrid dpal mo lugs/ jo bo'i gsung la yol sgom
chos dbang gi zin tho sdebs pa byang sems zla rgyal lugs/ zhang skyi tsha 'od chen gyi khrid yig/ byang chub bzang po lugs/ skyes mchog 'bar ra ba'i yig cha la brten pa ste
dmar khrid sgo gsum yang thos/ rta mgrin lcags ral can gyi byin rlabs sgrub skor/ chos skyong che chung gi bka' sgo dam gzhag thun mong ma yin pa'i nges gsang yang stsal
mtshams/ slar smon thang du rje yab sras so so'i rgyud dang sngags mal gnyis ka'i chos zhu la bsnyags sngar bzhin nyin mtshan rgyun ma chad pa'i bslab sbyangs snying non
pa byas/ rgyud la gong mchan dag ldan gyi skyar cag mtha' chod zhib len kho na chos thun re re nas/ mdang gi tshig de ring ma bzlos/ don thob kyi babs rgyun 'brel ba'i
bshad pa go bde gzung sla ba sha stag gnang bas drod pa chen po skyes/ bsam mno khor mor btang ba'i the

tshom thams cad/ paN chen byams pa gling pa yang rgyud bsan kyin yod pas zhus tig le lor ma songs ba/ tha na tshig gi zur tsam la dpyad pa dgongs pa yang dkar rtags btab/ chos
thun grol mtshams sa kha li'i kha phye nas mdzub btsugs su yig ngo spyan lam du phul nas dag byed zhus pas/ dgyes te 'phags 'od kyi lo rgyus yang yang gsung/ chos sgug
skabs bgros gleng byung ba kun gyi kha 'dzin bshags 'debs thams cad kyang paN chen pa nyid kyis mdzad/ AH lar nang du de la 'dug zer ba yin gsung bslab bya mdzad pa'i grangs
mi dpogs pa tsam yod de/ chu la dbyug pa rgyab pa bzhin rjes med la ma btang/ de dus ngas 'di zhus/ rjes 'di gsungs phreng ba la bgrang rgyu yod/ rgyud mchod zhu mi
yang gnang chags kyis ma chad pa bzang 'gran 'ba' zhig byung/ 'phral dpe skyor ba la brjod pa bde zhing mdun pa ma log pa'i brtson 'grus la mkhan rin po che yang lhag par
mnyes/ nyin re bzhin thugs rtsis ji che bka' drin bskyangs/ dus der gtso bor snyen bkur gyi zhabs tog sgrub yul rje ngor chen pa dpon slob byes pa rnams kho na la bgyis
rjes kyang thugs rje tshad med pas spyan du bcug kyang mi tsha ba'i dpes lam gyi cha lag rnams kyang bdag gcig pu kho na la rdzogs par gnang/ phyi bskyed rim skabs bdag
med pa'i phyi dkyil rdul tshon la/ gsang dbang gi sngon 'gror nang dkyil sindhu ra la brten pa'i byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ma chad pa/ rgyu lam skabs aShTa/ yig brgya'i zlas
lung thad sor sbyor ba/ lam dus rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum/ lam dus gso chog/ lam zab phyi nang/ bla ma rin

'byung/ bir bsrung sgo gnyis/ rnam 'joms bir lugs/ dbang gong ma/ lam sbas bshad/ brda don gsal ba/ brda tshig brgyud/ sgrub pa lung sbyin/ mgon rkyang la thug gi bar dbang
bka' byin rlabs cha lag de rnams kyang thad so de dang de kho nar phyag bzhes la yang zor mi mdzad pa mthong ba brgyud pa'i bka' srol ji lta ba bzhin rgyu skar 'char ba'i
go rim ltar ma log par stsal/ de dang lhan du yig sna drug cus mtshon pa'i lung bsam gyis mi khyab pa tshogs chos su spyi 'gror 'dems pa de dag dang/ man ngag phra mo lhan
du bsgrigs pa'i pod dmar ma/ mgon po'i ser po/ dmar po skor gsum gyi yig cha rnams kyi lung zur chos su gnang/ lugs gnyis ka'i mdzad pa rgyun mi 'chad kyis thugs lhag
par g.yengs pa'i skabs der yang/ bdag la mas bu la brtse ba ltar/ rab gnas sbyin sreg/ sa cho ga sgrub mchod/ gtor sgrub/ bskang gso/ zung 'jug/ drug cu pa/ gdon grol/ bum
gter sogs bla ma gong ma'i phyag bzhes yod do cog la mdzub krid vc: khridnan chag/ sha lpags rus gsum la thim 'gro ba lta bu'i mgo 'dren phu dur mdzad/ sde pa rnams la
gnang ba'i phyag phyir rje nyid kyis dgongs pas spyad/ nga rang gis gsol ba 'debs ma dgongs par/ dge legs kyi dkyil 'khor gsum gyi dbang/ 'dod rgyal/ ku ru kulle/ tshogs
bdag/ mgon po lcam dral lha brgyad rnams kyi rjes gnang thob/ der rgyud dang man ngag bar chad med par mthar phyin pa'i skabs/ chos kyi grol ston la rje yab sras kyis gtso
mdzad/ sde pa sku ngo tha dad/ mi chen kun 'dus pa'i skabs der/ nga dang rab 'byams pa blo

gros rgya mtsho gnyis sdom gsum gyi sa rnams bgrod par bya ba'am/ zhes pa'i gzhung 'di'i bshad pa nged la gyis gsung ba'i bka' lung byung bas/ spyi 'gror sngar blo la yod pa'i
TIkka bstan pa'i sgron me'i tshig sbyor ji lta ba'i steng/ sa lam bgrod lugs/ ljon shing bdag med bstod 'grel sogs nas kha bskang zhib bshad byas pas/ rang gi bsod nams
kyi dgos skal ma brten/ rngo thogs zhing 'gros glengs yang bag chags 'dril ba/ mchod yar la thug gi bar rang gzhan gyi bsam pa rdzogs pa rang cig byung ba des/ mkhan rin
po che dgyes pa rab kyi mthar phyin par gyur zhing/ gral la bzhugs pa'i rje ngor pa/ paN chen byams gling pa sogs thams cad kyi gsung cig gi gzengs bstod dang/ shes rab
la 'gran zla med pa'i grags de kho nas chod/ bzhugs gral de nyid kyi stengs su rje yab sras gnyis ka la rgyud man ngag gi chos yon so so nas 'bul ba'i skabs der/ rang gi
ngos skal rgyud kyi bka' drin gso ba gser zho gsum gyis sna grangs pa'i bcu gsum tshan zhig dang/ man ngag gi yon du gser srang gsum rnams phul/ lugs gnyis ka yar dpe la
'gran pa'i mig rkyen bzang po 'bad med du byung/ bkra shis kyi legs tshogs de dag gi mthar/ sa kha'i dus chen steng du rje ngor chen yab sras la mkhan slob zhus/ drung
pa chos rje pas gsang ston gnang/ grib tshong kha bskong gi dge 'dun bcu phrag gcig gi dbus su/ nyin mtshan gyi cha las gung tshigs ma yol ba/ grib tshod skyes bu gcig dang
rkang pa gnyis la bab pa na/ tshangs par spyod pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i sdom pa thob/ mkhan slob dge

'dun dang bcas pa la bsnyen bkur 'bul 'gyed bzang po bsgrubs/ de nyin 'grub sbyor yod pas/ drung pa chos rje'i gdan sar mnga' gsol mdzad de/ chos rje rnam pa gsum kas phyag
nas lhan du gnang zhing/ de dus re zhing du tshes lnga'i dus chen gtso bo la yong dgos nan bskyed byung ba la/ sha tsha'i nye sbyor ba 'ga' zhig na re/ sngar mdzad pa med
pa la/ da res tshogs shin tu che ba yong bas/ sngon blo char na gtan mi bstub pas/ smon thang pa'i sde pa rnams kyi gdung rabs zhig kyang gzigs dgos/ yas gtam gyi dpe cha
yang nan tan yang dag pa gnang dgos zhes bskul ma yang yang bgyid pa la/ mi chos kyi gdung rabs la slob gnyer byed pa rang blos cog pa dka' ba 'dra zhes zol gyi lan btab/
dus la bab pa na/ dpon sa gdung brgyud na rims re re nas lugs gnyis kyi bya ba ci dang ci mdzad pa de dag/ snyan par bsngags pa'i phreng bar spel ba/ gtsang zhing ma
'dres pa'i tshig sbyor rgyas pa ngang ba'i skad dang/ bung ba'i dbyangs ltar rjes su bsgrags pas tshogs pa thams cad mgu ba skyes/ de'i sang snga bar kha sang gral na yod
pa'i slob dpon 'ga' zhig yongs nas/ drung gis kha sang gnang ba'i yas gtam de'i dpe cha g.yar pa gnang dgos zer ba la/ ngas kha nas gang thon byas pa ma gtogs dpe cha med
byas pas/ bden bsam pa mi 'dug/ 'on kyang de nyin yas gtam btang ba phyogs go'i rnam pa rgyas 'bring bsdus gsum mdo skabs dang sbyar/ dgon par bsngo ba byed dgos nyin re
la lan bzlas pa du mar dgos pa'i re re la yang mi 'dra ba'i rnam dpyad kyi khyad par re re sbyar ba'i byed tshig phun

sum tshogs pa chos snang la brten spel bas/ mang du thos pa'i drang srong chen po gnas brtan bzang po brtan pa thugs lhag par nges shes 'drongs pa'i zol ma yin pa gzengs bstod
dngos dang brgyud par stsol bar mdzad/ skabs der drung pa chos rje pa'i bka' las kyang bsngo ba 'di rang gzhan gyi legs byas thams cad spel ba'i gser 'gyur gyi rtsi'i
sman mchog yin/ de la mi zad pa'i spobs pa'i sgos 'dus pa'i dge 'dun/ skye bo tha mal pa yang yid 'khrul thub pa'i ngag bzang po rtsol med du lhug par byung ba ngo mtshar
che/ snga ma'i bsags pa dang yi dam gyi thugs rje'i mthu las rang ngo'i khengs sems kyis bcings na/ nga rgyal gyi bdud 'jug nyen che 'ong gsung/ dus skabs der gdan sa'i
khur blangs pa'i dga' ston rnam gzhag la bzhugs khrir 'khod pa'i thog ma'i gnang sbyin/ drung pa chos rjes snam chos ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan tshul khrims kyi dri gsung
lhag par 'phro ba/ rgyun dan du dam tshig gi rten byar mdzad pa'i rgya dril/ khyad par rgyud sde bdun cu rtsa gnyis kyis lde mig gtad pa'i rmi lam byung/ rgyud bshad la
'gro don rgya che ba'i rten 'brel bsgrigs pa yin gsung/ rgyud gsum gyi glegs bam/ 'dren pa dam pa nyid kyis rwa ston chos rje'i sgrang chen la rgyu mdzad/ dam tshig glegs
bam du byin gyis brlabs pa yang bstsal/ de mtshams rje bla ma yab sras so so'i mos gus kyi rten du na bza'/ gnang sbyin bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ sde pa dpon slob tha dad
kyis bkra shis legs byas gya nom pa rgyun ma chad pas zla phyed bar dgon par thogs/ de bar rje yab sras gnyis ka brnyel bso'i rnam pas sku mtshams

gnang ba grol mtshams rje ngor chen gyi thugs kyi dgongs pa yongs su bskangs nas/ chos kyi srid la mnga' gsol gnang ba'i phyag phyir bdag kyang bkra shis/ mkhan rin po che
nyid kyi bka' 'bum gser ma pod bzhi ma'i bshad lung/ phag mo zhal gnyis ma/ don grub ma/ dbu bcad ma rnams kyis byin rlabs/ phag mo gzhung drug/ de'i don 'grel/ dpyal pa'i
yig rnying ma lus pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston gyis mdzad pa'i 'dul ba'i gleng 'bum/ kun rig gi rtsod spongs gnam lcags 'khor lo/ 'jam dbyangs chos rjes mdzad pa'i mtha'
spyod zhib rgyas/ man ngag gces bsdus cha gnyis/ phra mo nyi shu rtsa lnga/ rdo rje gdan pa'i chos drug pa ri ba'i gser chos bcu gsum/ sgrol dkar gyi sgrub skor/ lo
chen ma Ni ka'i khyad chos ma lus pa/ legs ldan mched gsum gyi rjes gnang rnams gnang mtshams/ rje ngor chen drung kun mkhyen chen po'i bka' 'bum lung don gnyer ba 'ga' la
gnang ba'i skabs/ shar nas byon pa'i chos rje rkyang thur ba sogs la/ dgra gdong 'jigs gsum/ gshed dmar lha lnga dang bcu gsum ma/ 'jam dpal gsang ldan/ gzungs chen grwa
lnga/ spyan ras gzigs lha mangs/ gdugs dkar can/ rigs gsum spyi dbang/ a ra pa tsa lha lnga/ mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu/ gza' yum zur bka' rnams kyi dbang/ 'jam rdor/ bde mchog
mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho/ bshed dmar bcu gsum ma rnams kyi rgya gzhung mtha' dag gi lung stsol bar mdzad pa'i chos thun phan tshun ma chag par nyan pa dang/ sngar byis pa'i
dus kyi bla ma/ byang sems rin po che ska rags gnas a mas khyim du spyan drangs

'dug pa la/ nyin re bzhin bka' gdams glegs bam gyi lung/ rje yab sras kyi thugs dam ma grol gsung tshang bar zhus/ de nas dpon slob lhan du skyes mdun gyi dgon gnas su rgyud
gsum gyi 'chad bshad tsam gyis chos thun ma chags ngos/ gtso bor yab sras thugs phab pa'i gsung 'phros 'ba' zhig gis dus 'da' bar mdzad/ phyis bsam pas de dus kyi gsung
rnams ma 'ongs pa'i gnas sgrib med du gzigs pa'i lung bstan kho nar 'dug na'ang/ nged rang 'khor bas bcings pa'i mkhan po'i ming btags des dbyar gnas kyi gtso bo la 'bod
mi des drag gis bskul nas yongs/ dbyar snga ma nas khas blangs/ chos rje pa'i bzhugs khri'i steng de nyid nas snga phyi'i chos thun ma chag par paN chen chos rje'i bslab
bya chen mo/ gleng 'bum dang sbyar lung sde bzhi lag tu bzhag pa lta bu'i zab bshad byas/ don bsdur drung nas rin po che'i gsung rgyun bslab bya zin thun du spar/ snga chos
la mdo rtsa'i dka' 'grel nyi ma'i shing rta dang/ rgongs chos la las rgyavc: brgya'i Tikka zla ba'i shing rta ba dan dkar po'i rnga dbyangs su grags pa de gnyis kyi lung
tsam bklags/ gzhi gsum cho ga bdud rtsi'i rol mtsho'i phyag len 'khrul med du 'doms pa'i slob dpon mkhas pa'i drung du sgro 'dogs bcad/ yid ches chan bur btab pa'i sngon
bsu yod pa de ji lta bar/ dus bzang dang so so thar pa'i mdo 'don pa rnams bstan pa'i mig rgyan la phan pa'i gsal dag snyan gsum ldan pas/ shes ldan skye bo ngang gis
yid 'jug pa'i legs byas spel/ dbyar gnas ring drung pa chos rje'i drung nas/ bka' 'bum pod bzhi ma'i lung gnang zhing/

'di gal che ba yin gsung dbang bzhi ngo sprod kyi lag bcangs/ dbang bzhi bslab pa gsum ldan gyi dmigs pa/ sbas bshad thugs rdo rje dang/ pho brang lnga'i nyams len/ rlung byor
gyi 'khrul 'khor zhal zhes ma lus pa/ brda don gsal ba'i khrid/ rmi lam sbyong spel gyi gnad 'doms/ chos skyong gi skor/ rje nyid kyis bdag chen blo gros pa la gsan pa
rnams lhug par stsal/ dbyar gyi dgag dbye bgyis/ ljongs rgyu la rje yab sras kyi bka' lung chen gtad gnang nas chos sdings su phyin/ bde mchog dril bu lha lnga/ lwa wa
pa'i lha bcu gsum ma/ bde mchog bong bu'i zhal can gyi dpal sdom pa rnams kyi dbang bkur ba/ bde mchog/ 'jigaya byed kyi sngags btu'i byin rlabs/ chos rje paNDi tas mdzad
pa'i byang chub sems dpa' byams pa dang nor bzang gi rtogs brjod/ lha bla ma ye shes 'od kyi rnam thar/ dpal ldan sa skya la ched du brjod pa dbang po'i nyer 'tsho rnams
kyi lung dang/ rab gnas kyi rgyud/ gsang spyi rgyud/ dpa' bo gcig grub rnams la bshad pa mtha' chod shin tu rgyas pa/ thugs mnyes bzhin pa'i ngang nas sngon gyi lo rgyus
dpag tu med pa dang sbyar gnang bas/ chos thun ji tsam ring ba la sun pa med cing/ grol ba la phang sems che ba sha stag byung/ chos sdings su bzhugs dus/ rje rong pa'i
drung gis 'phral gyi go re men phal mo che yang 'jags par bgyis/ sngar kun spangs rin po che la mgon po'i nang khrid kyi zhabs ma thob pa des mes la rtser bar yod pas/ rje
sangs rgyas rin chen gyis mdzad pa'i yig cha'i steng nas rdzogs par thob/ ston ser slar yab sras lhan du smon thang du phebs/ shar

phyogs kyi dpon slob rnams phyir e waM du thegs pa'i rdzong chos dus 'khor sdom chen/ rnam 'joms ma Ni badzra/ 'jigs byed zhe dgu ma'i stod las smad las kyi dbang go gnyis/
de dag gi yig lung mtha' dag gnang ba'i phyag phyir thob/ rje ngor chen shar phyogs ma thegs khar/ thugs nang bstan gyi bka' bkod/ bdud rtsi ril bu'i gnang sbyin/ rten 'brel
gyi bsgrigs phyogs che ba'i gnas yod gsung/ sngar thob kyang rgyal ba don yod grub par bsgom pa'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ tshar gsum khug pa'i byin rlabs zhar byung man
ngag drug dang bcas pa skyar nas bstsal/ zla med pa'i thugs rjes gzung/ dpal e waM chos ldan nyid du phebs nas yar phyogs 'phros gtam byung res kyis nged rang gi ming nas
'bod par mdzad/ khong la dgos na snying slangs kyang ster nus pa tsam 'dug gsung/ dgyes pa'i bka' lung 'jen pa lan cig ma yin par bstsal/ bla ma'i thugs zin gyis sdug yus
chen po yod/ phyis lo bcu nas jo mjal la yong dus/ yum nas lam mi chags rje drung bsnyags yong bas/ gzhan ngor sku khams shin tu dub pa 'dug/ khyed mes po shi mtshams
pha bsnyags pa khrel ma log pa'i dam tshig yin gsung/ lam dus kyi gso chog gnang dus phyag gser srang gang gi 'bul ba phul/ snyung ba'i stabs na zhabs dbang sogs ni mi gnang
'dug/ dpon po mjal ba'i rjes ma de nyid yin/ sprel lo'i ston de drung pa chos rjes bka' zhal mkhyen gyi tshul du/ na ning bar dbus gtsang phyogs su lo lnga bsdad pa'i
slob gnyer de las/ lo gcig gi nan tan 'dir 'bad pa ngos rngo thogs pa zhig byung/ re zhig

'di'i rgyun 'thud pa'i bslabs sbyangs byed rtsis kho na yin cing/ chos rje byams pa gling pa'i drung nas nged la yang khyed mdo sngags kyi nan tan kho na 'jur dgos pa'i thugs
tsha'i rting bkul yang gnang byung na'ang/ khyod kyis shes na chog pa'i dge bshes kyi 'dzin tshugs ma shor ba'i thos bsam bsgom gsum thun du bcad/ nyin mtshan khor mor
sgrub pa'i dmigs rkyen gang yang ma lobs par/ ma shes kyang chog pa'i bskang gso dang rnga brdungs rna ba rtsed pa'i sbram sil 'di tsam bkag kyang mi khogs/ bsnyen sgrub
bzlas gsum cig ma song ba'i bon khyer 'dis/ bar chad kyi 'jug sgo chen por song dgos 'dug pas/ dgun ngo 'di gzhi bsnyen byed pa'i lugs kyis gsung ba thob phebs shing/ sngar
gser mdog can du kun spangs rin po ches chos skyong gi gtor sgrub bskang gso gnang ba'i phyag phyir lan 'ga' phyin pas/ dbyangs dang chog bsgrigs rnams bcol po blangs
pa ltar/ zur tsam la lon byung ba sems drangs/ byang ngam rings su bsdod rin dang/ yul du yang dbyangs dang rnga brdungs kho na la blo gzhol bas/ mtshan gang rnga brdung
ba yang lan mang du byas/ mchod gtor blo yul las 'das pa bshams/ grogs mi re re gnyis gnyis las med kyang rnga sgras nang thams cad gang ba 'dra ba yong/ khyad par chos
skyong gi bka' bsgo dang/ phrin las zhu ba'i tshe/ mdun na mngon sum du bzhugs yod pa 'dra ba'i bsam pa'i zil dang/ lus nyams ban ma bun ma yong ba yod/ de rang gi rgyun
'jags na/ ming chos skyong gi grub thob tu grags pa'i zog po/ dgra las kyi shi tshad rang gis bsad par

rloms pa'i sdig can/ 'khrul snang la tshad mar 'dzin pa'i log shes can cig yong ba yod de/ mar thar pa'i lam ston des ngan 'gro'i sgo dang gcig pu bkag pa'i drin yang lon pa
med/ de lo drung pa chos rje nyid kyis sgrub khang du nyin re bzhin phebs/ rgyu lam/ 'chag med khyi kha gso bstsal mtshams/ shin tu bcad bya dam pa/ thun mtshams su'ang
mi tshigs gtan mi 'dre ba/ dgos bya'i brda sbyor yod na'ang saM bho ra kho na la brgyud/ g.yog gcig las mi su la yang mi 'phrad pa'i dben pa bsten cing/ de skabs kyi gnang
chags kyis skyabs 'gro'i rting bskul 'tshang 'bru 'ba' zhig gi bka' thos g.yeng ba med par gcun/ zla ngo dgu'i ring la kha gso'i sbyin sreg dang bcas pa bar chad med par
mthar phyin mtshams/ sgrub skra 'bum pa la phyin pas/ drung pa chos rje thugs lhag par dgod pa'i 'dzum zhal dang bcas/ lo tshod dang bstun pa'i snying rus kyang dga' tshad
'dug/ da rdo rje slob dpon chen po'i gnas thob/ rnga brdungs na skabs su bab pa'i dus btol ba yin te/ spyang a pho'i yug sa ltar/ sngar dos drag grags pas da ji ltar
yong ngam gsung/ de ji lta ba bzhin phyis rims kyis spros bcas kyi bya ba la yid mi 'jug pa'i le lor spyod pa zhig byung/ skabs der zhag 'ga' lus gso ba tshun gyi mtshams
ma grol bar gung ja'i skabs sku mdun du jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsa/ lam yig che chung/ so sor thar pa'i mdo/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa'i 'dul ba'i las chog rnams kyi
lung zhu ba sogs zla phyed tsam dben pa bsten mtshams/ mkhan rin po che'i 'bod mi rkang btsugs gnang byung bas/ skyes mdun

dgon sar phyin/ bskyed rdzogs sbrags pa'i gshed dmar spros med kyi khrid/ birwa pa'i gzhung brgyad/ glo bo lo tsA ba'i yig cha mtha' dag/ dol po dbang brtson sogs kyis zin
bris rgyas par thob/ khyad par thub pa dgos gsal/ sdom rig rnam pa gnyis rnams la sa skya paN chen gyi gsung thor bu bas rgyan pa'i zhub 'grel/ 'theb sbyor spyi gnas gnang
zhing/ yang dgos rig gter rang 'grel gyi skyar chos nan chags 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtshos sa paN las dngos su gsan pa'i bshad rgyun thun mong ma yin pa dges par stsal/
de mtshams drag pa nyung bsdus kho na la sa paN gyis dbyig gnyen las dngos su gsan pa'i mdzod kyi bshad rgyun sos ston paN chen nas brgyud pa'i lung bshad/ indra mkha'
spyod/ nA ro mkha' spyod/ mai tri mkha' spyod de sa skya pa'i mchog sgrub pa'i dmar mo skor gsum gyi byin rlabs yag lung so so/ oM gsum ma'i sngags btu/ tshogs mchod
byin rlabs/ sngags kyi de kho na nyid kyi rje btsun grags pa'i yig cha'i zhal shes chos rje paNDitas mdzad pa'i dmigs pa/ rtsa dbu ma'i nyams khrid/ bla ma bsam gtan 'od
zer bas bal po mahnavc: mahAbo dhi la gsan pa'i bde mchog bong zhal ma'i rdzogs rim dmigs phran de nyid mngon brjod bla ma'i rgyud dang sbyar ba'i sgom bya/ mgon po phyag
bzhi pa'i phyi nang gsang gsum gyi rjes gnang dbang bskur/ sgrub skor/ phrin pod/ rgyab rten mgon po sngon byung gi rgyud lung/ rgyud nas bshad pa'i mgon po dkar po'i tshe
sgrub rnams gnang mtshams/ rnam rgyal chos sder dus chos kyi phar tshad/ rong TIka gi gtong chos/ rje rong ston gyis mdzad pa'i

'bum TIka tshang ba'i lung/ de dang 'brel par shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i man ngag bde ba'i 'byung gnas steng dga' ldan lha yul nas brgyud pa/ longs spyod kyi 'byung
gnas 'og klu yul nas brgyud pa/ rig pa'i 'byung gnas shar phyogs bham ga la'i yul nas brgyud pa/ yon tan gyi 'byung gnas lho phyogs bhe ta'i yul nas brgyud pa/ byin rlabs
kyi 'byung gnas nub phyogs o rgyan nas brgyud pa/ ngo mtshar gyi 'byung gnas byang phyogs bi shrA ko Ta tsan dan gyi gling nas brgyud pa'i bka' babs drug po'i snying po'i
don thams cad kyi bcud bsdus nas ston pa'i don khrid yid ches ldan pa thob pa'i rjes/ rang gi dgon par dbyar gnas kyi gtso bo la sngar bzhin phyin/ snga phyi'i gtong chos
sdom gsum/ sa paN nyid kyi rang mchan/ lho dmar gnyis kyis mchan sna srings pa'i steng du/ dmar dang/ sro lung kun smon gyi sa dpyad bcug/ 'dul ba seng ge'i phyogs snga'i
ngos 'dzin gyi gzer btab/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas la zhu phrin/ chag lo/ zhang lo/ glo bo lo tsA ba/ bka' gdams do skor ma/ bka' bsdams vc: gdamsnam mkha' 'bum/ rtogs
ldan rgyan po/ rtogs ldan phru ma sogs/ chos rje sa paN dang/ chos rgyal 'phags pa la sdom gsum rab dbye ma brten nas dris pa'i dris lan ma lus pa phra tshoms bkod de/
sa paN nyid kyis mkhas pa 'jug pa'i sgor ji ltar gsungs pa ltar/blo chen zab cing rgyal che ste//blo dman go bde gzung sla ba//de las zlog na mkhas rmongs kyis//slob ma
dga' ba bskyed mi nus//zhes pa'i man ngag las 'byung ba ltar/ spyi bshad du tshad thub 'grel chen bzhir btags pa/

lha btsun bsam yas pa/ spos khang pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen sga gdong pa chen po/ las chen gzhon nu seng ges mdzad pa bzhi dang/ byang pa dkon mchog grags kyis so
thar byang sems kyi rgyas bshad/ bu ston rin po che'i sa 'bri'i shan 'byed/ yang dgon pa'i sdom gsum zhus lan so/ paN chen 'jigs med grags kyi sdom gsum sgo dbye/ sgra
pa shes rab rin chen dang/ mi nyag chos grags dpal bzang gis TIkka rnams kyis mi 'dra ba'i khyad par so so rnams bshad pa'i rnam grangs su bkod/ paN chen chos rje'i dri ba
brgya rtsa'i lan/ rje rwa ston pa/ bka' bcu pa dpal chen po/ nyi phug pa seng ge bzang po/ chos zom pa shes rab seng ge/ ri ti skyog chos dpal bzang po/ mi nyag chos grags
dpal bzang/ snar thang bka' bzhi pa shes rab tshul khrims/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge/ slob dpon yon tan 'byung gnas rnams kyi dris lan dgu pa dag dang/ dri ba mdzad
pa po nyid kyi ser thur du lan 'debs gnang ba/ phan tshun nang sel phra mo nas shan 'byed pa'i dogs pa'i mtha' chod rgya cher 'grel ba'i chos thun shin tu ring ba srod
tho rangs 'chag med du bshad cing/ tsha ba thon rjes rnam rgyal du sgrub thabs brgya rtsa zhu ba la bsnyags/ dgongs ja steng/ drung pa chos rje'i drung du rgyud gsum gyi
lung zhus/ dbyar gnas grol mtshams dpal mgon byams pa'i gling du/ paN chen rin po che dang mjal bas phyag thal mo thugs kar sbyar/ pha la bu skyes 'dug/ sdom gsum 'chad pa
po mang ste 'di 'dra 'chad mkhan med/ a la ma sa skya paN chen gyi bka' bsrungs yod na phrin las sgrub

ran/ mi rgan shi ba'i shul 'di zung la/ 'di na lag dris rang du byas pa'i man ngag snye mas gtso byas rgya 'grel bco brgyad tsam mchis pa 'di dag la kun chub par mdzad pa zhu/
bstan pa spyi la dgongs pa'i thugs bskyed bzang po/ phyogs re la a ma 'thas pa'i rgya 'bag gi mig ltar 'khrul chags pa cig nges par phyag len la thebs pa rang dgos/ mdo
rgyud thams cad kyi rdo rje'i tshig ma tshang ba med par kha phye ba byang chub sems dpa'i 'grel pa rnams yin/ 'di dag la sbyangs pa mi chung ba bgyis kyang/ da kha rgas
nged kyis 'bul thub pa'i skal ba mi 'dug/ dbus gtsang dag pa'i zhing yin pas/ der dka' tshegs la ma 'dzems par gsan sbyongs mthar phyin gnang dgos/ sa skya pa rang snang
gi chos la rang yul las lhag pa btsal bas mi rnyed cing/ dngos grub kyi rtsa ba rdo rje slob dpon chos rje mchog grub pa nyid la bsnyen pa las lhag pa med pas/ de la sngon
rje btsun grags pas sa paN la gdams pa ltar/ khu bo'i 'du shes las zlog nas sangs rgyas su gzigs pa'i rten 'brel ma log pa 'tshal gsung ba dang bcas chos kyi mdzad pa
mthar phyin pa'i dga' ston yin ces rten khebs bzang bsgrigs shin tu legs pa cig gnang sbyin bstsal/ dbyar smad rnam rgyal chos sder skyas/ lam 'bras cha lag thor tsam zhig
dang/ phyag rdor 'khor chen gyi dbang/ rgyud 'grel bshad dza wa ri'i rgya gzhung bco brgyad kyi lung/ rnal 'byor bzhi ldan gyi dmigs pa/ phur pa sa lugs kyi stod las/
smad las kyi dbang/ smad las rim sogs kyi lung/ bde mchog lU dril nag gsum gyi rgya bod kyi gzhung lung rgyun yod do cog phal che ba/

dmar gyis mdzad pa'i lU i ba'i rnam bshad la skyar chos kyi zin thun rdzogs par skyar cag byas/ rnam sras ser chen zhi drag gi rjes gnang dang 'brel bar/ rdo rje sa 'og gar
mkhan mchog gi rgyud dag las byung ba'i 'gro bzang snying po/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ bu ston yab sras rnams kyi yig cha/ rta bdag so so'i las tshogs dang bcas pa dgyes bzhin
du stsal/ skabs shed byam vc: byamsgling du paN chen rin po che la 'jigs byed sa lugs kyi dbang/ rtog bdun la lugs gnyis kyi mchan bu so so/ 'grel pa phan tshun la brten
pa'i bshad pa/ sngags btu'i byin rlabs/ bla chen chos dpal bzang pa'i yig cha'i steng nas rwa rtse sems 'dzin gyi khrid/ las gshin 'khor bcas kyi rjes gnang/ dug dbang
rma bya rgyas pa/ rwa pod shin tu rgyas pa'i lung rnams zhus/ ston ser brag dkar du kyai rdor DoM bhi lugs/ mtsho skyes lugs/ nag po lugs la/ sku gsung thugs snying po
kyai rdo rje dang bzhir phye ba'i dbang/ gur saM gtso che'i chos sna sum cu dgu'i lung/ bde mchog ma hA mA ya'i dbang/ rgyud chung le'u gsum pa lho mkhar rdo rje snying po'i
'grel pa dang sbyar ba'i bshad pa/ slob dpon ku ku ri pa nyid kyis spros med rgya gzhung ltar snying ka'i dpa' bo 'ga' zhig pa'i rdzogs rim dmigs pa/ sgrub thabs rmongs
pa sgrol ba'i brtag pa/ dkyil chog rim pa gsum pa/ 'phags pa'i mngon dkyil/ bde mchog sangs rgyas thod pa/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro rnams kyi dbang/ rje dbon lha sras gzhon
nu kun bzang dbang phyug pa'i che 'don/ mdo sngags gnyis ka la grwa skor mdzad pa'i dgongs pas/ sngon slob dpon chen po dharmA

rakShi ta'i ched du 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad pa yin gsung/ spyi ljon dag ldan dang bcas pa'i don bsdu chung ngu rnams rtsa rgyud 'phags mchan gyi khongs su sbyar ba'i skyar
chos/ 'phags pa'i yi ge'i steng nas dag pa gsum gyi khrid/ tog gsum skye TIka dang sbyar ba'i bshad pa 'khrul 'khor/ las tshogs so drug gi lag len dmar khrid du 'doms
pa/ rgya ston dang/ lo tsA ba ma Ni ka'i TIkka gnyis la'ang mtha' chod du gnang ba'i dgag sgrub kyi gnas du ma la spobs pa'i snang ba bskyed cing/ 'bri khung dpal 'dzin
gyi sngags kyi sdebs su gri nag po'i so 'debs dug sbral 'bar ba/ gnam lcags urmo sogs kyi 'byin 'jug gi zhal shes snyan brgyud/ skyo lugs kyi rwa rtse sems 'dzin/ mtshan
mo rgyu ba mtshan ma gyen bsgrengs rnams lhan cig bsgrigs pa'i rdzogs rim gyi khrid/ de dang 'brel bar rgyab rten du bskyed rim gyi bshad pa/ 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs/
zhi khro rnam rol/ sems dpa' bsdus pa gnyis la'ang lam bsgrigs/ rang lugs 'gro mgon 'phags pa'i bla ma gnyan rin po che bstan pa'i mtshan nyid ji lta ba bzhin nges gzung
du mdzad nas/ de las gzhan pa'i gnas la/ rje rin po che blo bzang grags pa'i dpal yab sras kyi bzhed pa rnams dgag yul du bzhag pa'i rigs pa'i tsher ma/ rtog ge ba dag gis
bskal brgyar bsams kyang blo'i snang ba la 'char ba ma yin pa'i thal 'gyur gyis mtshon rnon po dpag med stsal ba yang dran shes kyi snod mi brjed gzungs kyi za ma tog nyid
du bzhag pas/ phyis 'bras spungs su rje thams cad mkhyen pa dang mjal ba na/ gleng blangs kyi 'phros la blo yul du

gnas pa rnams phul bas/ ya ya shin tu rmad du byung ri bo dge ldan pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams/ yi dam rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi gleng brjod kho na yin te/ rgya gar gyi slob
dpon chen po mi bskyod pa dang/ gzhon nu zla ba'i brgyud kyi 'grel pa las brtsams pa'i chos skad bzang po/ sngon gyi mkhas pa rwa skyo zhang gsum gyi bzhed pa phan tshun
ma 'dres pa 'di lta bu'i legs bshad sngar ma thos pa ngo mtshar che ces rjes su yi rang ba bstsal/ mdor na gshin rje gshed dmar nag 'jigs gsum la rgyud rgya gzhung gi
thos pa/ bla ma'i man ngag lag len/ rang gi bsnyen sgrub zlas pa rnams kyi sgo nas/ 'di kho na la sbyangs pa 'dra ba zhig byas/ rang gzhan la phan pa'i rmi lam gyi mtshan
ma brtan po 'ga' re la brten/ drug cu pa'i gtor ma'i cho ga gcig gnyis bgyis pa'i skabs kyang/ kho bo nyid rdo rje khro bo chen po khams gsul vc: gsumnote>las rnam par rgyal
ba'i rgyal thabs kyi ya lad rnam par bkra ba'i drag po'i rgyan ched du bdar bas/ klubs pa'i chas su zhugs te gshin rje mthar byed kyi bsnyems pa brtan pos/ bka' gnyan
gyi khro bo'i sprin dang bcas pa'i rdo rje rnam par brtsen pa'i khro bo rol pa chen po'i stabs dang/ bgegs thams cad rnam par rnyed pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang/ chen po'i
gzi byin mngon du bgyis te log par blta ba mtha' dag mthar bar byas pa'i zil gyis gtor ma bsnun pa na/ gnas der 'god pa'i mi thams cad kyang kyi bung zhes byed la/ mig bsdud
mi shes pa ltar had de blta ba dang/ bdag cag gang na 'dug ces gcig gi lag pa la gcig gis 'ju zhing/ gar 'gro'i tol med pa gom pa gya

tshoms su 'dor ba sha stag 'byung bas/ gtor lam gyi phyogs nyin lam gsum bzhi khyab par/ bdud klad 'gems pa'i cha lang drag po'i sgra lta bu rnam dbang ma nyams pa thams cad
kyi spyod yul du gyur pa mngon sum gyi snang ba las ma 'das pa'i chos 'phrul chen po yang thogs med du byung ste/ thams cad dpang por gyur pa'i ngag kho na yin/ de ltar
brag dkar du zab la rgya che ba'i gdams pa de ltar thob te sems tshim nas/ yar lam byams pa gling du zhag 'ga' bsdad pa'i skabs/ paN chen rin po che'i drung nas sngar 'di'i
dmigs pa ma gsan yod pa shas che gsung/ rang byin brlabs kyi dmigs pa nyi shu rtsa dgu/ sam pu Ti'i rgyud dang sbyar nas bstsal zhing/ mi nyag pranydzA dzA la'i zin tho'i
'khor 'das dbyer med kyi dpe zhig la yang dris mal yang dag pa'i sgro 'dogs chod pa'i yid ches khyad par can bskyed par mdzad de/ slar drung pa chos rje'i drung du zla
chos gcig gi ring la mgon po'i man ngag mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje la gsan pa'i gser pod du grags pa'i rje rdo rje 'chang gi dkar chag tu 'khod pa/ me 'bar mar btags
pa'i bdag chen rin po ches phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa/ rwa ston chos rjes paNDi ta grags pa rgyal mtshan la gsan pa'i mal pod du mtshan gsol ba de gsum ka'i steng nas sngar
ma thob pa rnams la lung bstsal mtshams/ khyod kyis bla ma rnam gsum la thob pa'i chos skyong gi bka' rjes gnang lung man ngag rnams yongs su rdzogs pa thob pas sems bde/
mgon po'i bsnyen pa 'di shin tu bar chad sdang bas nged ma shi ba la 'khyol ba zhig dgos pas/ gnang nub man sngar yi dam

gyi skabs las kyang lhag par 'jur ba'i mtshams dam pa rang gal che zhing/ deng sang gi chos rje rnam pa'i phyag bzhes bsrung 'khor la brten nas gnang ba yang yod tshod 'dug
na'ang/ sngar kho bo rang gi bsnyen pa byed dus yi dam gyi bdag skyed sngon du song ba'i/ mdun bskyed la brten nas byas pa ltar lag len ma 'dzol ba gyis gsung/ zhag gnyis
kyi ring la bsnyen pa'i byed lugs zhal shes zhus/ gtor ma'i bca' gzhi/ sdod sa tshun spyan lam du phab nas/ zla ba gnyis la bar chad kyi mtshan ma med par mthar phyin/
der bka' las/ bsnyen pa'i ring mtshan brtags ji ltar byung gsung ba la/ sngar las yid phebs pa tsam las mngon gyur ba gang yang ma byung zhus pas/ da lan gyi rtags rnams
nged la rmi lam du gsal thag chod byung/ rjes sor lab/ da lan sgrub mchod kyi gtso bo gyis/ phrin las rgya che ba'i rten 'brel yod pas/ dkyil 'khor na ning las khru gang
gi cher chug/ rgyud las 'byung khungs kyi bye ma bshad pa ltar spangs/ mthing lo khri srogs bzang mtshon kho nas bris/ spyi mchod dang/ lha so so'i dgos mchod rnams sngar
las nyis 'gyur du spor/ snga phyi'i cho ga'i bar ngag bcad sems 'jur ba gyis/ bdag 'jug gi dkyil 'khor gtso bor bla mar bsgoms pas bla ma la dbang zhus pa dang khyad med
pa yin zhes bka' stsal pa ltar la spu rtse tsam yang ma 'chugs par cho 'phrul gyi ring grub rjes/ slar tshe dpag med dang/ kun rig gi bsnyen pa gyis gsung ba bzhin zla ba
phyed gsum ring shin tu dos drag pa rang byas/ sa kha'i tshes brgyad kyi dge rtsa'i stengs su grol/ de nub gzims chung 'og min du srod la
