gsol ja bzang ba rang gcig gi steng 'das ma 'ongs kyi lung bstan bka' bkod dang/ khyad par bla ma rigs lnga'i bsnyen sgrub las gsum zhib pa zhig gnang/ do zhag khyod 'di kar
yod na bsam pa rdzogs par 'dug te na'ang/ gnangs tshes bcu la 'o skol gnyis ka 'bod mi sleb yong ba 'dra gsung ba'i rjes la sems 'jigs chum pa cig byung/ ci gsung ba yin
nam mi tshe ril po la zhal 'khyal gsung ba ni mi dran snyam/ blo ma bde ba'i rnam pas de nub gnyis tsam yang ma byung/ nang par tsha ba thon rjes gsol ja'i steng zhabs
drung du mjal bas/ sku gzi 'od lang tsovc: tsho'i dpal 'bar zhing/ spyan dkar nag phyed pa blta ba bas mi ngoms pa lta bu gcig 'dug/ 'phros gtam 'bus tsam gnang rjes/ mdangs
gnang ba'i gsung chos la skyar cag nan tan mdzad/ da nga'i gung thun ran/ gro steng du slar 'phrad do gsung/ gsol gro'i steng du yang yan lag bdun pa mdzad rjes dang/
'brel gang yang med par/gung thang pa de bla ma gnyis pa 'tshol//'brom rje khyod ni kho bo gcig pu sems//sbrul gyi lpags pa rje yang sprul mi rje//kho bo 'chi tshul bstan
yang a ti sha//zhes phral gsungs nas gcer gzigs byung bas/ tshugs mi thub pa lta bu'i lus nyams gnan kyang mi non pa tsam zhig byung/ za ba'i mdun pa yang med par drung
rang la blta ba'i ngang nas ja grol/ de'i nang bar skyes mdun dgon par nan bskyed gsol ba btab pa'i bde mchog nag po'i dbang da lan yong gsung/mkhan rin po che'i phyag tho
phebs pa gzigs phul bas//zhal 'dzum mdzad ngas kha sang rang lung bstan pa//da

khyod rang gi yod dgu gos gser ma'i snam sbyar phul/ skyar chags su gsol ba btab pa'i don la/ rje'i thugs rjes gzung ba'i rten 'brel yang yang 'grig pa dka'/ da lta rang song
gsung ba la/ do nub 'phyis pas sang snga bar 'gro zhus nas phyin/ bcu bzhi'i nyin sta gon/ bco lnga la dngos gzhi legs par thob rjes/ dgon par tshes bcu'i nub nas drung
pa chos rje cung zad snyung zer 'bod mi byung/ sku mdun du byin pas/ sku khams cung zad ltem pa'i rnam pa 'dug na'ang/ sku mdangs sngar las kyang ches lhag par gsal bar
'dug pas/ mjal bas blo bde bar byung/ de'i gnangs bcu bdun gyi nyin phyed gung thun mdzad grub mtshams/ spyan ras gzigs zhal bcu gcig pa'i bdag bskyed rdzogs par gnang/
bzlas pa'i na mo ratna trayA ya/ na maH Arya dznyA na sA ga ra bai ro tsa na/ byu ha rA dzA ya zhes pa'i tshig mtshams 'dir/ zhi ba'i dbyings la thugs kyi dang ba stobs su
gyur pa'i zhal 'dzum pa'i mdangs dang bcas bzhin du/ bdag cag rtag 'dzin can rnams skyo ba bskyed pa'i phyir/ sprul pa'i sku chos kyi dbyings su bsdu ba'i mdzad pa tha
ma gces mthong du gyur pa de/ brtse chen yab kyis bor ba'i phru gu tol med nyam ngar lus/ mig mchis ma 'dzag cing gdung rin po che'i zhabs la gtugs te mya ngan gyis yid non
pas smre bzhin gsol ba 'debs pa'i skad cig de nyid la/ shangs bug nas byang sems dkar po'i rgyun sgra dang bcas bzhi thun zhig tu bar ma chad pa'i ltas dang/ ye shes gong
'pho ba'i bseb lam gyis mi slob pa zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang chen po'i sa mngon sum du mdzad

pa'i sgrim med kyi mtshan ma byang chub sems dpa' me tag vc: togzla mdzes ltar/ gzhan du ma 'gyur ma nyams pa'i lang tsho dri zhim po'i ngad ldang ba mthong ba'i rkyen gyis
mi phyed pa'i dad pas snying brlan par gyur te/ sku'i snang ba brtul ma thag nas gzims khang gi thog tu cod pan 'bul ba/ dgung zhag gi mtha' ji srid bar bcom ldan 'das dgyes
pa rdo rje'i ting nge 'dzin gyis/ gdung rin po che dkyil 'khor bdag po de nyid du bskyed pa la/ mgon po de'i thugs gnyis su med pa'i ye shes spyan drangs te/ rgyal ba
rab 'byams kun 'dus pa'i sgyu 'phrul rdo rje'i skur gsal btab nas/ bdun rnam par dag pa dang/ snga phyi sgo brje ba'i mchod pa mar me nyer lnga las mi nyung ba nyin re
bzhin stob pa/ dgung zhag so so la bla ma mchog gi dgongs rdzogs mchod yul mkhan rin po che/ paN chen byams pa gling pa sogs dgon sde'i bla ma so so/ dge 'dun skye bo'i tshogs
dang bcas pa la bsnyen bkur/ gral 'gyed phul du byung ba bsgrub shing/ de skabs dgung zhag gi mtha' ji snyed par sprin dang bral ba'i nam mkha' rdul med cing dag pa
dang/ me tog gi char 'bab pa sogs mthong thos kyis yid brtas par gyur/ rang gis kyang nyin re bzhin sku gdung rin po che'i drung dmigs rten du byas/ dbang blang ba/ bla
mchod 'bul ba/ mngon par 'dul byas pa'i dge ba thams cad mchog gi sems dpa' de nyid kyi spyan lam du yongs su bsngo ba'i tshig don mkhas pa'i rna char 'os pa ja 'debs re'i
rgyun las mi thung ba nyin re bzhin bsgrubs/ sems dag pos yid gzhungs te bgyis pa des/ thugs dam nges

par bskul thub cing yod 'dug/ bdag rang bsngo ba 'bul bar brtsams nas sems mi rtog pa'i ngang du song te/ ci skad byas mi dran par/ tsa na yod pa kun la khyed rnams kyi bltas
dus ci 'dra byung bris pas/ nyin re bzhin gsung gi cha 'di tsam zhig zin bris su 'khod thub na yang yid re ba yongs su rdzogs pa 'dug ste zhes sems dungs pa rang 'dug/
mdor na rang gi stobs kyis ci 'khyud gsol ba btab pa'i rim pa g.yo med par bsgrubs shing/ ye shes kyi sku mngon du mdzad pa'i gdung la/ brnyigs ma'i rnyog pa'i cha ci zhig
'tshal te/ dri ngas pa dang/ myags pa la sogs pa'i rnam pa ci yang med par/ tshul khrims yongs su dag pa'i dri bsung gis khyab pa'i gdung de nyid sa kha'i nyer lnga la
bab pa na zhugs la zhen dgyes pa rdo rje'i cho gas zhi ba las thams cad pa'i zhugs blugs phul/ dri zhim po dang bcas pa'i bud shing bzang pos yud kyis sbyangs te zhag du
mar gsol ba btab/ gdung zhal 'byed pa'i las mngon du bgyis pa na/ sku gdung kha dog sna tshogs pa'i ring bsrel gyis bstams pa'i yid ches des/ ma rung ba'i sems 'chang ba
rnams kyang gus pa'i bsam pa ma sbyor bar mdzad/ sku gdung byin pa tshar btab/ gser gyi na bza' dang bcas dad can la rten skal du 'gyed pa dang/ byin gser 'bum rnal rgyal
mchod rten gyi nang bzhugs bgyis/ rab tu gnas pa'i mnga' gsol legs par phul/ bla ma bsgros po de bzhugs ring khong gi thugs rjes yid bde 'ba' zhig gis 'tsho bar byung yang/

bsams kyang pha bgres po des bsgyur ba'i shul der/ blo skad cig kyang ma chags par/ phugs bya bral zhig la yi dam bcas 'phral a ma drin can de'i sems skogs dogs zol med sdug

nos mtshams/ lo dus dkyil dbyar gnas la 'bod mi byung bas/ nga da lo gtan mi 'gro/ pha des bskyur ba'i sdug shul de sems la gzan byas thag bcad/ dgon sar thugs mi phebs
na 'phred mkhar du dbyar gnas 'dzugs zer nan bskyed byung na'ang/ rtsis btab ma byas pas/ mkhan rin po che'i phyag rtags zhib bkod mdzad nas/ bla ma'i rjes su khrel yod kyi

pa nA ro pas mdzad pa/ tog bdun 'grel pa slob dpon mi bskyod pas mdzad pa/ dgra nag gi 'grel pa dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ rdo rje slob dpon gyi las thams cad tshang bar

lnga/ dril bu gzhung gsum/ nag po gzhung drug rnams kyi rgya gzhung so so la bshad pa rgyas par bgyis pa'i skabs/

spro byung/ bla ma rin po che 'khor bcas la dgongs bzhed ltar/ tshe dbang sogs lam gyi rkyen bsel byin rlabs sgo du ma dang/ rin po che pa nyid la 'bul ba gser gyi maNDal

dzi wa

sogs dzo ki rang snang gi dngos grub kyi rdzas so so'i 'byung sa/ ngos 'dzin byed las dag gi gleng blangs mang du bgyis/ pA ni a gha ma/ dharti a gha ma/ bA yi a gha ma sogs
tshe sgrub kyi rigs dang/ ga dzakarma/ bhi na thaM bha/ ka lassa dza sogs rnal 'byor nang gi/ bi de ki tsu ki tsu dang/ ratna badzra/ kai sha lassa/ tso re banda/ pe Ta
ka/ dzandra/ pU rakka/ a hu TaHa/ tsaNDa li/ pa kal/ o kal/ dzandra sogs sngar ma go ba'i man ngag du ma'i gsang rnyed/ de lo khreng shi ru ba nA tha/ ro ji/ dhu dhu pi/
ces pa'i pir sa dag dzo ki chen po khong dang mjal zhing/ snga phyir dzo ki gdams ngag can du ma dang 'grogs pa'i thog ma/ a sa nA tha'i slob ma bha dra nA tha/ 'dis lo
phyed dang gnyis lhag lhan du 'dug/ de rjes ma hes nA tha'i slob ma bhu dha nA tha/ kha kha nA tha'i slob ma sa dza nA tha/ bikSha nA tha'i slob ma ches ram nA tha/ sru ba
nA tha'i slob ma bha hu na tha/ tir thi nA tha'i slob ma pantha nA tha i tsha nA tha'i slob ma dza Ta nA tha rnams dang/ lo zla ba brgyad dgu 'grogs pas/ gdams ngag gi
gnad cung zad/ 'khrul 'khor gyi byed chings zab mo/ sman sbyor gyi rten 'brel phra mo 'ga' bslabs/ der gnas chen du rgya gar gyi dzo ki der 'dus kyi dbus su ga Na tsakra'i
pU dza'i mchod pa/ na ril gyi 'o ma/ kai la/ ga gon te/ sngar za ma myong ba'i bza' bca' rnam grangs du ma dang/ der 'dus kyi rgyal po/ bram ze rnams kyis/ la du/ ro tri/
ra dzi/ bA dzi/ mA dhu/ so ba ri/ pan gyi 'dab ma sogs kyis mchod/ bram ze rnams kyis shis brjod byas/ shed da tsan dan gyi til la ka dpral bar byin/ ga Na tsakra'i dus/
thog ma dzo ki gzhon pa gnyis kyis

kin dhi ra thogs nas/ gI ta bsgyur/ der rjes/ pir des/ shi ba ka der/ dzwa ki kun gyis satra pur/ zhes brjod pa 'o skol gyi bsngo bar 'dug/ de skabs kho bos rnal 'byor dbang
phyug gi glu/ bI rupang gi dzo ki/ as na se bho ki/ dzo ki ni sang ki na tsho De/ sogs dang/ yang yong grags/ a ti ku ma ri su kha ma na na ri te/rtag tu gzhon nu phru
gu'i lus//bdag med ma dang mi 'brel 'grogs//zer bar snang/ gzhan go bin tsantra'i/ gho re gho re mang gi/ ha mi dza ki pra tes mang gi zer ba dang/ khyad par/ dza brta ri
ghi ta pate bha kru a tre pa tar ho/ a kas gu pa ma gri tsha li tshe sogs kho rang skad ci 'drar smras pas/ der 'tshogs dzo ki thams cad mchi ma 'byin/ nged kyi ming la/
mahna ta pa si tA ra gu ru btags/ khyod lus bod/ sems rgya gar/ kaya

[A:a]sa dag/ angma siddha/ pha la pha la zer zhing/ so so brgya ni dbul bya zhing/ ces bshad pa ji lta ba bzhin du/ mar me bcu gsum bcu gnyis tshar gnyis gnyis phyogs bzhi
la bsgrigs pa'i mtshams bzhir spyi las che ba'i mar me gnyis gnyis kyi phra tshoms bkod pa/ zhal zas dang spos kyang rnam grangs de ltar du bkod pa'i mthar/ dngul bcad gtso
bor gyur pa'i bzed zhal nyer lngas mtha' bskor ba'i nang du/ yon chab kha bsgyur nag po dkyil chog gi rdul tshon skabs/ dkar po'i dkar po sogs nyer lnga bshad pa po sor
kha bsgyur nas bsgrig lugs/ ljang dmar nag ser mchin lcags ngur/ ces bdun tshan du phreng bsgrigs pa'i phyogs bzhir/ rgyud las bshad pa'i rakta'i mchod yon mtshon byed/
padma rA ga'i mdog can bzhi/ kha dog dmar po'i

dmar po rnam grangs su bkod/ mchod pa rnams snga phyir spos/ snod bcad byi dor byed pa'i skabs/ dngul snod rnams la shog phyis yang yang du byas pas/ khong rnams dngul zad
dogs sems las che bar 'dug pa la/ yon chab kyi kha dog legs po byung na bsam pa ma gtogs dngul la phang sems til 'bru tsam yang ma skyes/ me tog rtsi bcud las bsgrubs pa
mtshon bsgyur byas pa dang/ dar sna tshogs la rgyal mtshan gyi gzugs su bcos pa/ rtsa rgyud las/rgyal mtshan dmar dang de bzhin ser//dkar dang nag dang ser skya dang//ces
pa dang mthun pa'i lnga phyogs bzhi'i dbus ma byang shar du bkod pa yang rgyud las/de bzhin gos ni sna tshogs dang//me tog phreng ba du ma dang//bla bre dag dang dar dpyangs
pa'i//mda' dang yol ba shin tu mdzes//ces pa'i dgongs pa/ dkyil 'khor gyi ka ba'i mdun gyi bar snang la pi ta hu'i thag pa la brten pa'i gos du ma sdang 'gel/ me tog
phreng ba'i mtshon don chol ba'i bsgrigs kyi rten mthongs zur 'gem// kyil vc: dkyil'khor gyi steng du bla bre/ dar dpyangs kyi don du ka rgyan dang/ dar yug longs kyi lda
lti/ sbyin sreg gi phyag len skabs ltar dkyil 'khor gyi mthar mda' dra/ dar sum sbrag gi yol ba rnams rgyud mchod du nye bar bshams/ las thams cad pa'i dpal chen po'i mchod
pa/ tshil chen gyis sbags pa'i ga bur gyi mar me/ sha chen dri tshon tsam bsres pa'i gu gul rkyang sbyor gyi reng bu/ sha sna tshogs bag phye dang lhan cig mar la bces
pa'i dzam bu ti ba'i zhal zas kyang rgyud kyi bshad tshod dang mthun par bshams te/ dbang gi mngon par rtogs

pa bdun dang ldan pa'i dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod skabs thog mtha' gnyis su bar chad dang cho ga'i nyams chag kha bskang ba'i zhi ba'i sbyin sreg/ dkyil 'khor zhal 'byed la rgyas
pa'i sbyin sreg rnams ma chad pa/ dge 'dun chas ston/ gzhon nu ma'i mchod pa sogs re re nas bgyi bar 'os pa'i cho ga ma nyams pa/ dkyil 'khor de nyid du lo grangs nyer
lnga'i tshad kyi bdag 'jug blangs rjes sbrel nas snod ldan don gnyer lo grangs dang mnyam pa'i re ba rdzogs par bskang ba'i skabs der// dpal 'byor gyis kyang dus btab kyi
stengs su btol byung/ de nas da lta'i bar la gcig kyang ma bral bar lhan du 'grogs/ dbang gi bya ba rnams legs par grub mtshams/ skyes mdun dgon par yab chos kyi rje'i
drung du/ phyag gser srang gi me tog 'bul du rkang gtad phyin pas/ thugs lhag par dgyes pa'i bka' bstsal bslab bya dpag tu med pa gnang/ khyad par sngar sdom gsum la dbyar
gnas ring bshad pa mthar phyin blo las 'das pa byung ba/ de ji lta ba bzhin cig na ning dbyar chos stengs rig gter ma byas na snyam pa'i yid ma khengs kyang/ da dung na
tshod gzhon nu yin pas phyis kyang sems la zhog gsung ba la/ bdag gis bshad kyang chos nyan rnam pas 'bru gcig kyang mi go mchis pa nas/ sems la yang phan par 'dug snyam
rgyal sras lam bzang tshang bar bgyis lags zhus pas/ de la lung ngan ma zhig las ma byas par dgongs byams gling du nyi ltar chags 'gro yi 'dug zer ba thos/ bos las kha
ta 'jug snyam kyang/ drung pa chos rje pa de gshegs pa nas khyod sems so na mi 'dug pas ma

nus/ yi ge 'di ltos pa skyar gdung brgyud drung du rkang gtad 'bul rgyu'i zhu zhig yin/ 'phags pa'i thugs dam rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i rgya lha 'di dang/ brgyad stong pa'i gsum
bde nyid gser rkyang ma 'di rnams kyang 'bul rgyu yin/ kha ta'i dngos gzhi khyod la rnam par dpyod pa'i shes rab yod pas da dung 'jam dbyangs lo chen snyogs la/ dus 'khor
gsang 'dus/ sgra sogs rig gnas la 'bad pa rang gal che gsung/ de man mjal ba med/ phyis bsams pas zhal chems su 'dug/ de nas slar chos 'phro nag po gzhung drug nag 'bum
dang spel ba'i bshad lung rgyas pa/ bla chos med par bgyis nas/ zab bshad du rdzogs rim rim pa bzhi bzlas pa nyid lan gsum gyis 'khor lo skor te/ gsang ba'i de kho na
nyid du pha rgyud 'dus pa'i lam thams cad zab gsal du bsgrigs nas/ shes bya rgyud sogs su 'grel lugs dang/ o la pa tir gnyis med dgyes pa rdo rje'i gnad snying bo vc: po'khor
'das dbyer med du sdoms na bzhi tshan du sbyar ba'i brgyud rims su ston tshul/ dpyid kyi thig ler ma rgyud bde mchog gi gnas ma lus pa/ dpyid dang thig le zham sbyor
gyi srog rtsar sbyar nas/ rgyud rim thos bsam du gtan la phab/ sngags rim 'khor lo bzhi ldan sgom byar slangs/ ye shes kyi rim pa nyams myong skyes pa'i 'char sgor bshad/
gsang rim dngos ldan dus rnam pa ji ltar ba bzhin du dgongs 'dug/ der spyan chab g.yo bzhin du thugs dam gyi ngang nas shugs 'byung gi gsol 'debs 'dra ma zhig gnang ba'i
ngang ma nyams de bsad 'phral sku 'khris kyi phyag phyi ba kun la gsungs 'dug/ nyi tshod skyur ba'i dus

tsam yin pa 'dra/ nged rang gi rtsa na yod pa kun gyis mig mthun par bya rgod bzhi steng gi thad na lding ba mthong 'dug/ de 'phral rang langs phyin/ de nub dgon par sleb mtshams/
khams shin du dub pa shes pa 'ur langs pa'i ngang nas khong rnams sems phral la bkod pa'i skabs/ nged rang gis smras pa dran tshod ni mi 'dug/ phyis khod rnams sleng
ba la/ nga ci nas kyang ldod 'dod na/ bu mo gtsang ma bzhis gding ba'i sne zung la/ dbus su shAkya thub pa'i sku gcig zhog/ brtan bzhugs kyis/ zon pa de gnyis drung pa
rang byung ba'i brang 'og tu gnon zer ba bzhin byas pas/ de ma thag khams sor chud/ dpus mgo g.yon pa la zug en tsam 'dug pa/ der sdod rin ma chag tshur lam sngar gyi brdabs
sa rang du/ shi skyid kyi gcer nyal thun dmigs zhig byas pas tsher ma bton pa bzhin song/ bla ma rang byung ba dpon slob rnams la ni gu'i byin rlabs bcu gsum tsam mgyogs
khrid lag bcangs mas mtshon pa'i thugs bzhed rdzogs par byas/ slar mtha' dkar du phyin mtshams/ bu'i mchog ba lung snying rje can dang mjal/ lam 'bras ni gu'i skor/
dbang bka' byin rlabs ci bzhed/ gzhung spyi chings rtsom pa mang ba yang byas lhug par phul/ la gsar bar skyel thung byas/ de lo yang bkra dum du phyin lam 'bras na ning
las rgyas pa'i mtha' chod skyar chos yod tsam/ mkhas btsun dbon po chos rje blo gros dbang phyug pas gtso mdzad/ sman khro/ sprin chen sogs nas chos nyan kho na la 'dus
pa'i tshogs la tshar bar byas/ dgun padma yul du phyin mtsho ngubs kyi dben gnas su bsdad/ der bzhugs

kyi sgrub chen 'ga' la ni dgu vc: ni gu?'i mgyogs khrid zhig byas mtshams/ a phyi rgan mo ma dang drin mnyam pa de na tshod kyis gtugs pa'i ngang gis lnga pa'i gnas la gzhol
ba'i mtshan ma brtan po shar nas/ thog mar sems 'khrid pa'i dngos po sbyin pas yid yang yang mgu bar byas rjes/ mngon sul las ma 'das pa'i yid shes kyi bskul blo bur du
mtshams la har 'don byas phyin pas/ dbugs song tsam la sleb/ de dus spyi bo la'ang drod 'dug/ de 'phral mi 'khrugs pa'i dbang bskur/ rjes kyi bya ba rus bu chos skur bsgrub
pa sogs cha tsam gyi sems tshim pa'i dge rtsa yang grub mod/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus mthar 'khor gyi thog ma rgan mo ma mad de gnyis la 'chol snyam yod/ mdor na snga mi bsgags
pa cung zad la brten/ pha ma rigs ldan gyi chos la sbyar/ gzhon nu nas grong pa'i dris ma reg cing/ khyim pa'i kun spyod pa phal pa phra mos kyang ma gos/ byis pa'i rtsed
mo kun kyang sbe skor/ bangs 'phyongs chu rtsed rdo sgor sogs phal pa'i kun spyod gcig lag tu ma blangs/ dbang bkur chos 'chad kyi rnam pa'i bag chags kho nar yod/ khyad
par bcu bdun nas nyer brgyad bar gyi lo skor cig po de la chos zhu/ bsnyen bsgrub kyang du ma yang bgyis mod/ gtso bor thos pa kho na rten pas mi shes pa'i mun pa las
yongs su grol ste/ da lta dbang/ zur bka' rnam par dag pa ka yod la/ lhad ma mchis par rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i dkyil 'khor yongs su rdzogs pa bdun cu don lnga'i
dbang nam bskur dgos kyang/ don spyi'i rnam pas gcig 'gros kun la sbyar ba'i stong zob min/ re re nas bsten pos rgyud 'di la brten/ bod 'gyur

rnams la tshig ris su shar ba'i de dang de thad kyi lung sbyor/ rgyud tshig gtsang sing ba/ rgya 'grel dang sbyar ba'i nges gsang phun sum tshogs pa/ 'gyur khyad sogs spu tsam
gyi nang sel yang ma 'dres pa'i dran pa/ shel bum du chu blugs pa lta bu/ rgya gzhung rnams kyang bstan 'gyur tsam po'i nang de kho na la mur bsubs byas pa la ma yin
pa/ sngon byon gyi mkhas pa chen po dag gis bka' tho mchan bu thebs pa'i yid ches ma kho na la nan tan byas/ tshig 'di thad na mchan 'di yod me long gi gzugs ltar gsal le
ba 'di yin/ gangs can gyi mkhas grub gong ma'i gsung rgyun mtha' yas pa'i mngon dkyil rnams la yang bla ma las thob pa'i dpe nyid kyis tshig ris ma 'chugs pa'i srog rtsa
cho gar byin mi 'dra ba'i khyad par mthong ngo cog bshad pa'i na yams su bkod pa'i dbang gcig ma yin pa kun la sbyar ba'i 'phrul/ gcig shes kun grol rgya mo'i thags kyi
skyes so 'dra ba/ tha dad du gyes shing/ phan tshun ma 'khrug pa lce thog nas bshor ba'i gzigs gsal la phebs pa 'di nyid dang/ bla med nang gi byin rlabs brgyad cu rtsa dgu/
zur ka'i rjes gnang rnam par dag pa brgyar song nges tsam las dbang rdor phreng/ mi tra brgya rtsa/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho/ brgya rtsa lta bu cho ga gcig 'gros kyis kun
grangs nas yig steng nas bklags chog ma yin pa re re yang lo rgyus so so/ rgya gzhung bod gzhung mi 'dra ba'i khyad/ cho ga zhal phyag re re la'ang de 'di la dgongs kyi
'then sbyor 'phrag gnon thub pa/ bsgrub thabs so so'i mchod brjod nas mjug mdzad byang gi bar/ mig gis bltas/ yid kyis gzung/ gzhan la

nam dgos lhag par ster ba'i bsnyen med kun gyis rtogs pa 'di nyid lags/ de tsam gyis blo'i snang ba phra mos ma bcings par/ thos mthar bsgom pa la gzhol ba'i blos/ lo nyer
brgyad lon pa nas/ zhen med blo sna thung ba'i skyo shas kyis bskul/ dpe blta'i spros pa yang rim gyis btang/ sngar thos pa'i chos rnams kyis ro ci myong bgyis/ khyad par
ni gu'i nyams len la blo phyogs par byung bas rang gzhan gyi bsgoms 'debs kyi thog ma 'di la byas/ chos 'chad nyan/ 'gro 'dug za nyal kun gyi skabs sgyu ma rmi lam gyi dran
pa du re ba ma chad pa'i/ las dang po ba'i blo gsar bu'i mdun pa ma log tsam des myong ba'i sne zin tsam byung ste/ paN chen byams pa gling pa sde pa'i sku bsrung la
rab rgyal rtsegs phebs dus rmi lam gzung/ sku mdun du phyin gnas tshul ji lta ba'i mthong snang zhib tu phul bas 'dzol med par thugs chams pa'i phyag rtags gnang ba des mtshon
pa'i 'char sgo cung zad kyis yid drangs/ yengs pa med par nyams len gyi rkang ma khril khril sems gcun pas/ rim gyis blos btang gi bsam pa ngang gi 'phel/ dpe cha/
lha rten/ dgon sde/ grwa pa rnams la zhen log skyes/ mi med kyi ri phug gang dben brtags/ 'jig rten las snang gi mdzes 'chor la gyong ci thogs byas/ sngar bzhin kha nang
log gi bsam mno mtha' spyod btang bas 'phreng chags a ma drin can las log pa til tsam yang ma rnyed pas/ phugs brtse dungs che bar yod kyang/ 'phral zhe gcod kyi gtam kho
na smras/ rig pa'i rgyal po nam du yang dgung kha yan la ma btang bar/ dran pa'i thag pas brtags/ chos kyi srog rtsa nas

bzung ba'i dran 'debs/ cis kyang dgos med/ kha zhe ma 'dzol ba'i nges 'byung bla lhag bye 'phel de nyid la brten/ rmi lam gyi 'char sgo/ rang myong dang 'brel ba'i bag chags
phal pa ma yin pa'i blo 'das kyi snang ba mkha' 'gro ma'i tshogs gral du ga Na tsakra'i pu dza'i dga' ba nyams su myong bas/ rnal 'byor ma'i zhabs dran pa'i rten 'brel
rmad byung dang/ skabs 'gar nyin lam bzhi lngas bar chod pa'i sa/ rang gi slob ma rang 'byung rdo rje'i chos ston gyi tshogs mchod skabs/ der 'dus thams cad kyis gsal bar
mthong ba'i sprul bsgyur gyi gsal snang khyad par can mngon sum gsal mthong/ dgon par lag pa gris phug pa'i rma chen po khrag rgyun mi zad pa yong ba/ de nub rang la mi
dmigs par/ rmen pa'i rjes tsam yang mi snang ba/ lhan du gnas pa'i skye bo thams cad kyis mig shes kyi gcer mthong bsnyen med du gyur pa/ de skabs ni gu tshogs 'khor gyi
dus gcig cho ga'i bya ba rnams grub/ dngos gzhi tshogs la longs spyod pa'i tshe/ shes pa 'ur langs pa'i lus sems kyi 'gyur ba chen po'i zil dang bcas/ mkhar sgong rdo tshad
bre phyed tsam bza' bca' kun la gtor/ dpon slob kun gyis longs spyad pas so rtse ba sogs a 'thas kyi mtshan rtog ci yang med cing/ rjes pho ba na ba/ rdo'i rang tshan
phyir byung ba sogs 'ga' yang med pa/ tshogs kyi 'du ba de na gnas pa'i bskal bzang dam tshig can dag gi rang rgyud la sgyu ma lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin 'phos pa'i yid ches
dang lhan du/ sgrib med du rtogs shing/ yang de skabs nub cig lhag gtor phyir dor ba ma byung ba nang du bzhag pas/ mtshan phyed

yol la khyi lta bu'i dbyibs can/ 'di yin nged rang kun gyis gtan mi shes pa zhig gis/ mis sgo 'byed pa ltar/ bla brang gi sgo/ bar sgo/ nang sgo la thug gi bar gyi sgo rnams
rim par phye nas/ gtor ma lnga tshar du bsgrigs pa'i mtha'i mkha' 'gro spyi gtor dang/ tshogs lhag snod dang bcas pa khyer/ rjes ded kyang ma zin/ nang par snod lam gyi
bzhi mdo nas rnyed pa'i tshul dgon bzhugs thams cad la gsal mthong du gyur pa/ 'phred mkhar gyi na khar gur phub bsdad pa'i skabs/ nub cig rmi lam gyi 'char sgo bud med
kyi khrom dpag tu med 'dus nas/ ga Na tsakra'i mchod pa bgyis pa'i mtshan ma brtan po byung ba'i nang par/ gur 'khris na bu mo gzhon nu zhig gi bskyed man chod kyi lus tshang
ba zhig 'dug pa/ der 'dus thams cad kyis mthong zhing/ slar dur khrod skye mi dngos da lta yang ma shi bar yod/ de nas sne shang gi rong la phyin pas/ rong pa gzhon
nu yul de'i mi su dang yang 'grogs 'dris ngo shes sogs med pa gcig gis/ a bar skyur gsum/ pi pi ling/ sga skya/ ka ko la sogs sman shing gdong nas phab 'phral ka ra lab ta'i
shing lo brlon pa la gril ba gzeb khang dang/ til dang 'bras kyi snye ma ma nyams pa/ snyug ma'i 'bras bu rlon pa phul gang rnams khrom 'dus pa'i dbus su nged la byin/
nged kyis dngos po gang byin yang 'dod pa med par nang par phrad du yong zer/ de nub gar song rjes med la song/ grwa pa tsho bkram yul kun tu btsal bas ma rnyed/ der yul
de'i rgan po rnams na re/ sman 'di dag skye sa dang rang re bzhugs sa 'di'i bar la zla ba phyed dang gnyis nges par yod/

mi rang rgyud pas khyer yongs na 'di 'dra'i so ma ga la yong/ rong pa'i mi tsha mthong na lceb pa tsam byed kyang/ mdangs tshwa/ gos snam ci gnad kyang mig mi blta 'dug/ mi
ma yin nged rang gi yul gyi lha jo bo cen pos drung pa rang la phul ba yin zer zhing/ de nas rang yul bar la rkang 'gros mgyogs pa'i nyin lam gsum yod pa/ bshad nas bang
cen rkang btsugs mngags/ bla ma slob dpon/ dpon pa yab yum kun la sman skyes 'bul du btang/ de dus kyi sman lag na yod pa da lta yang shin tu mang/ der rong mi thams cad
dad pa'i 'ur langs/ chos rje ni nged rang gi lhas kyang mchod pa yin zer snyed pa dpag tu med pa'i bkur bsti byung zhing/ slar log sne shang la bo che'i mdun du sleb tshams
gangs chen po babs/ lam 'phrang dogs pas yar mar la log pa med cing/ sa de rang du bsdad na gangs rgyud kyi nyen chen po yod pas/ 'khor rnams yid khong du chud 'dug pas/

'gril te nged rang gi mgo'i thad rang la 'phar byung ba/ sgyu ma rmi lam gyi rtsis ma shor ba'i ngang nas/ a zhes sgra drag por lhang lhang smras pa/ mig thad kyi bar
snang la a yig dkar po bris pa las gsal ba zhig 'od phyir phir 'dug/ pha bong de mgo'i steng la song dus rlung drang sir ba zhig byung/

de nas ma tshad brdabs song bas dum bu mang por sil gyis zhig song/ der sgyu ma'i rang myong chen po byung bas yid drangs/ nyin rangs mig lta stangs las ma g.yos par yongs/
khong rnams mig la gangs phyid byung dogs g.yag rnga dkris/ gzabs nas yong gin 'dug/ gnas chen chu mig brgya rtsar sleb/ khrus kyi rdzing bu der dpon slob kun gyis khrus
byas pas grang ba'i reg byas rkyen byas/ shes pa 'ur langs pa'i myong ba de dang mtshams/ sngar sbab byung ba'i lo rgyus mkhar che che zer da dung 'jigs 'jigs 'dug/ 'ga'
re sbab de thugs dam gyi skyobs byung ste/ do nub spyan la blta rgyu yong ba med/ zur nas bltas tsa na khro bo lta stangs las skad cig mi 'gyur 'dug/ btsums na zhu snyam
na'ang thugs hur phyungs 'dug pas zhu ma spobs zer/ rtsab rtsab byed cing ja dud sogs kyi'ang spyan la gnod ces sha tsha'i nye gdungs rang 'dug ngas khyed rang gzobs/ nga
sgyu ma'i rnal 'byor pa mig thon kyang sla sgyu ma yin/ zhar kyang rmi lam yin/ 'ong yang las snang yin a'u rtsi byas/ do nub khyed rang 'dir nyol/ nged pa dmigs 'dug pas
nags khrod ya gir cog bu khyer byas/ gcig pur bsdad nas dge sbyor dang sems 'dres pa'i thun ring ba zhig btang nas nyal bsdad/ cho 'phrul gyi klongs blo 'das byung/ de'i

yong gin yod pa la/ su yang ma byung/ ci zer ja mo yang mi gtong yod dam snyam bltas pas rnam pa'ang mi 'dug pas kho tsho'i rtsar phyin

pas/ nged rnams gnyid kri song man mig don 'gro ba tsam gyi zug byung/ skra mdun gyi spyan yang brnyel dgos drung du yong rtsis la zhed drags yong ma nus/ da nang nam langs
nas mthong rgyu med par ma sleb zer/ rang rang gi mal na bre mo phre phre 'dug pas/ de nyin khong rnams la zas ster ba/ rta drel kha phyis thams cad rang la byed pa'i khur
babs/ mdor na brjod pa 'di dag mi gcig dang gnyis min pa yongs kyi gzigs gsal la phebs pa rnams yi ger bris pa yin/ 'dis mtshon pa'i sgyu ma'i 'char tshul/ a 'thas kyi
byis pa rnams dang bag mi 'dra ba'i gtam gyis sgo du ma yod mod/ bris gsal lang/ dus der yang rang gi rang blos ma thongs pa'i 'char 'bru'i 'dzub btsugs thun ma chad pa
byas/ ni gu'i dge sbyor 'di rnams kyi ngo sprod bogs 'don gegs bsel zhu ba'i bla ma zhig 'tshol ba dang/ snyoms chung gi chos 'di sprang po'i dgos skal gyi thar lam du mjal
byung ba 'di la mtha' chod pa'i chos zhu/ dbus gtsang gi bla ma bzang dgu bsten/ sems lhag ma lus pa zhig bgyid cing/ shangs pa bka' rgyud kyi gnas rnams su tshogs 'khor
re'i 'brel pa 'dzud pa la 'gro dgos pa 'dug snyam zhe la bzhag/ 'phral a ma sogs kun la/ nga jo mjal dang chos rje ngor chen/ sa skya bdag chen rab mdzes pa gnyis la rje
drung du ma thob pa'i chos bsham zhu ba la 'gro byas/ yul nas sbrul lo zla ba gnyis pa'i nyer brgyad bla ma'i dus chen la btegs/ lam gyi kun spyod ldum bu ba'i rang snang
skyong zhing/ snang blo bde bar gser mdog can du sleb/ sngar gyi chos grwa lhan cig 'khod pa'i grwa rnying rnams mjal/ ja zhig grangs/

bsgom chen gyi mchod po 'dra ba'i chu la cha bzhag/ mtshan nyid pa skam po la re ba med/ gcig mig gcig la hur hur sgyu ma'i skyes bu nang 'tshogs smra bsam brjod med kyi ltad
mo chen po mthong/ dus der bla brang rgyab kyi bskyed tshal na/ ri ba kun rgyal ba chos rje rin po che'i drung 'dul ba'i lung gsan sa la spyan drangs 'dug pas/ khong sa
'brug pa'i bu chen yin zer bas/ chos 'dra'i rtsad gcod la phyin pas/ nged rang phan tshun mjal ba tsam gyis sngar 'dris kyi mdza' bo ltar thugs dag snang khyad par can
skyes/ 'di ltar sku gzhon nu la mkhyen rab mthar phyin/ sngon gyi smon lam 'bad med du bsad/ sgrub pa nyams len la thugs gzhol ba 'di nged sgrub rgyud pa'i sal du 'dug gsung

gnyis ka'i dpe mthong bas/ de gnang dgos tshul nan bskyed phul kyang stabs bde'i dgongs pa ma lon/ grogs po rnam pa yang snyugs bud dogs zhag bcu las ma bsdad na'ang chos
yon gser gyi maNDal sogs 'bul ba sogs sgo du mas bsnyes pa bsgrubs rjes rgyun bzhes kyi dbu zhwa gos chen la bcos pa'i sku dregs chags pa byin rlabs rten gyi gnang sbyin

zhus/ do nub kyang chibs skyel gnang nas snye thang du sleb/ jo bo'i rten rnams la phyag mchod smon lam btab/ de nas yol rin chen gling gi gong thogs chen rtser karma phrin

du bsnyegs/ sbrul lo zla ba bdun pa'i nyer brgyad la mjal/ de nyin nas dbu btsugs zla ba phyi ma'i nyer bdun bar la o rgyan bsnyen sgrub kyi dmigs pa nyin re bzhin ma chad
pa zhib par stsal/ khrid yig gi lung gsung ma 'dris pas sus mdzad kyi nges pa cher ma rnyed/ zla seng pas mdzad pa'i lugs byas/ sngar lam yig tu bkod kyang/ phyis mthong

chen por btol te/ shar lam lha mdongs su karma spyod khrid/ snyug la rtser rlung sems dbyer med kyi khrid zla phyed tsam re'i bar dmigs pa 'gril bar nos/ phyis mthong

yul/ med rnams su lcag mal tsam gdan chags pa'i skabs der/ grwa pa gtsang la song pa rnams kyang 'gug byung/ dpon slob lhan cig ba de'i la rgyud nas/ gnas chen dpal mtshur

don gyi 'pho ba khyad par can gyi brgyud pa rin po che'i mtha' bral du tshud tsam gyi sgom chung pa zhig stsol ba med du byung/ brgyud pa zhes pa'i tshig bla dag kyang/ dbang
bskur/ rgyud bshad/ man ngag byin pa'i rnam pa lam byed la btags pa ma yin/ 'o na gang gi brgyud pa yin zhe na/ tilli nA ro'i brgyud pa la/ gnyis med ye shes rdo rje
yod/ ces gsungs pas/ brgyud pa rin po che 'di dag ni phas bu la ye shes zhu lugs byas pa'i byang chub sems gnyis su med par rtogs pa'i rang snang thig le nyag gcig/ ye rdzogs
rtsa bral/ gsal bzhag gi dri ma med pa'i sangs rgyas lag bcangs kho na snying la sbyin par mdzad pa ste/ tshig gis na yams kyis don tshol ba'i brgyud pa ma yin/ don

por 'phyos pa/ bzang por sems dpa' 'ga' las/ dad pa can gyi so so skye bo grwa ma nyams pa zhig skal ba mchog tu gyur pa'o//ces pa smra ba 'di nyid zol lam gcam bu ma yin te/

nyid kyis//rigs su nye bar mtshon pa bzhin//zhes pa'i don dang ldan pa'i gnas brdzun med mngon sum gyis gsal ba la/ ma rungs pa'i yid can dag gis bsnyon btags rgyu ci yod/
de ltar ngo sprod zhu ba'i chig bsgril de la zhag bcu gsum dben pa bsten nas slar yang dpal mtshur phu'i gtsug lag khang chen po nyid du/ dad 'dus kyi skye bo du ma la/

dbang lnga/ tshul khrims kyi tshogs kyi slad du bum pa/ gsang ba/ shes rab ye shes/ 'jig rten pa'i dbang bzhi pa rnams grol lam ltar bskul nas/ ye shes kyi tshogs kyi slad
du 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bzhi pa/ gcer mthong du ston pa ye shes rdo rje'i dbang gi chos sgo phye ba'i/ phyi nas maNDal dang yig brgya'i khrid kyis bsags sbyangs tshul
bzhin du bgyis te/ gtum mo'i me dmigs nas khrid mdzad pa na/ dmigs pa kun kyang rnam par mi rtog pa dang gcig/ rnam pa thams cad pa dang gnyis/ lhan cig skyes pa dang gsum

ri mo rnam par bkra ba dang/ de nyid kyang lam gyi srog rtsa/ bla ma chos sku'i mos gus gcig pu pa yid la mi byed pa kho na'i dbyings su 'dril ba dang/ de rtse gcig spros
bral/ ro gcig sgom med sogs rnal 'byor bzhi gsum bcu gnyis su bshad pa'i/ ro gcig chen po tsam nas ni/ phyi rol mu stegs kyi lta bsgom spyod pa thams cad kyang phyag rgya

phag mo phur zhabs can gyi me dbang yang bstsal nas/ rgyal gyi nya la ras phud kyi phyag bzhes bar chad med par mthar phyin te/ zhag lnga bcu rtsa drug gi bar rgyun ma chad

ma gyur pa nyid yin no//deng sang lce bde ba la nyams myong bzlos na mkha' 'gro ma'i bka' chad yong zer gyi 'dug ste/ mkha' 'gro ma la so rnon po yod na gzung bya'i nyan

srang/ sha ra gru kha nas phyin gser mdog can la btang/ nged dpon slob lngas chu byang lam bsrangs phyin pas/ 'u yug dgon pa dkar po na bla ma rin po che phra ri ba bzhugs

po bka' lnga ste dbang bka' nyer lngar mdzad pa'i srol dang/ gnad nye bar bsgrim pa'i bsdus pa la/ chos drug bka' drug dang 'brel ba'i dbang gdams pa zung sbyor gyi phyag

nyid la bka' drug tshang ba'i yid ches ngo sprod/ dmigs chen dmigs phran so sor phye nas/ rtsa ba'i dmigs chen bcu bdun dril te lag bcangs su gtod pa'i gsang lam nyer bsdu'i
bar lung gis rgyan pa/ tshe dbang 'jam dpal nA ga raksha'i rjes gnang/ g.ya' tshan gangs tshan gyi bcud len zur chos su zhus/ gdan thog gcig tu 'dod dgu'i gdams pa lhug
par thob pas sems lhag par tshim zhing bka' drin gyi yon rin po che'i maNDal/ rten khebs bzang bsgrigs gser ma/ dbang bka' so so la dar/ gu gul la sogs pa'i sman gang rung
re phul zhing/ sgyu lus nad kyis rtses pas nyam chung bar yod kyang/ bla lhag gi dad pas bskul/ mi nus bzhin du phyags ltabs pa sogs bla ma dngos la bsten tshul snying
non par bgyis/ ni gu'i khrid brgya rtsa brgyad 'chad pa'i dam bca' phul bas/ rgya sgom chen po'i zhal nas brgya rtsa brgyad kyi mthar dngos grub gyi pha phogs chen po 'byung
zhes pa'i lung bstan gnang/ zhabs spyi bor blangs pa'i gdung shugs kyi ngang nas yong pas/ 'phral bla ma dang bral ba'i skyo shas dang/ phugs lus zungs ngan pa'i stabs
nas dran pa med pa lta bus/ yar blta ba sogs kyi spros pa ma byung bas/ rgya bsgom chen po'i gsung nga ro chen pos bos nas/ chos rje pa nged la mi gzigs sam gsung/ bltas
pas dbu dom gyis g.yob pa mdzad kyi 'dug na'ang/ g.yab lan sogs kyi spros pa ma byung bas/ de'i rten 'brel gyis bla ma bka' drin can de'i zhal phyis nas mthong ba'i skal
ba ma byung/ lus gshed lhag par ngan par yod kyang/ sngar gyi yi dam la brten/ rim gyis

bshangs pa'i gnas rnams mjal/ brtag pa'i lung bstan la yid ches brtan po byung bas rin po che lcags po brtse pa dang yang mjal/ grub rgyal ma'i tshe dbang/ mgon po rgyan gyi
skor/ dur khrod lam khyer/ chos drug dang ga'u ma'i rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi lung tsam zhus/ zhong shong ma'i shar gyi gnas mjal grub rjes/ dkar po brag gi dben gnas dam
par/ mos ldan sangs rgyas rin chen pas gtso mdzad dge 'dun kun gyis dpe med pa'i brtse bas bskyangs/ zhag 'ga' ngal gsos/ 'dod chos re ba rdzogs par byin pa'i skabs der
stag lung sna dkar nas/ bu'i mchog thogs med gsum pas 'bod mi rkang btsugs gnang byung bas sna dkar la 'grims/ slar dkar brag gi yang dben der zla ba 'ga' bsdad pas/ na
ba'i gzhug lus kyis lhag par snar zhing/ dgos med kyi chos 'chad nyin mtshan rgyun mi 'chad pa des shin tu sbyong bar byung/ de nas chos rje rin po che lcang ra ba'i drung
du/ paN chen rin po che'i rnam thar nyid kyis mdzad pa de'i lung chos 'brel du zhus nas/ stag lung sna dkar du zla ba gcig gi bar la rgyal sras khrid drug dang 'brel bar/
sems dpa' chen po dngul chu chos rdzong pa'i bka' 'bum thor bu ba'i bshad lung zhib pa/ dbu sems kyi sems bskyed lugs gnyis/ sngar drung nas rin po che'i drung du nos
pa'i jo bo lugs kyi sgrol ma nyer gcig gi rjes gnang rnams tshogs pa la spyi chos su byas/ chos rje nyid kyi gtso mdzad la dgos chos zab dgu lhug par phul/ gnas 'dir lan
mang du ngal bsos pas yid bde 'phel ba'i sos dul blo chags byung zhing/ rang yul gyi bla

chen songs pa sku mched 'bri khung chos sde sogs kyi chos lugs rgyun chad pa gso ba'i mdun pas/ bya btang chen po chos kyi grags pa las/ dgongs gcig pod lung/ lnga ldan nor
bu'i phreng ba khrid nyan nas rje rin po che chos lung pa la gdams pa zab mo nor bu mthong grol gyi ma bzhi bu bcu bdun tshang par nos mtshams/ sngar gser mdog can nas rten
'brel gyi sgrig phyogs dbu btsugs te byin rlabs zil chen rgyas pa'i lo chen drung du/ zhe la dus kyi 'khor lo skyes rags don grub rnam par dag par bshad pas/ 'di dang
phyi ma byang chub snying po la mthar thug pa'i bar phyi nang gzhan gsum gyi phan bde ma lus pa'i rtsa lag dngos grub thams cad kyi re gnas su gyur pa'i mchog gi rdo rje
slob dpon/ yid kyi 'jug yul gcig tu gtod pa zhig zhu bsam pa byas/ 'phral zhu yig nang du/ dpal mi pham mgon 'jig rten mig 'byed zha lu lo tsA ba'i bka' dam tshig gnyan
po'i rwa ba las mi 'da' ba/ bdag cag rmongs pa'i snang ngor sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyun la dgongs pa gcig gi khrel yod kyi mtshon byed dang sku rags 'di 'bul ces/ dus 'khor
gyi dbang rgyud man ngag zhu ba'i snyan gsan 'bebs pa la sman sdings ri bo rgyas pa'i mgul der/ ming bkra bzang bar 'dug pas kun dga' dpal dbang grogs mched pa brdzangs
pas/ dus gsum la chags thogs mi mnga' ba'i ye shes kyi gzigs pa mkha' khyab kyi ngang nas bka'i cod pan thog mar phebs pa'i tshigs bcad nang na/ rjes don grub rang bzhin
skyed rags bstsal/ ces bsam pa'i gnas dgongs pa'i 'tshang yul nas bton/ gnang sbyin

yang pha lo tsA ba nyid kyis sku la rgyun du bsten pa'i sku rags shin tu rnying ba tshul khrims rnam par dag pa'i dri ngad kyi bsung chags pa'i/ ma log pa'i rten 'brel bzang
po 'bad med des dga' mgu yid drangs nas/ dbyar dus chu che ba'i skabs lam dka' tshegs che ba rang gi dus yin na'ang tshong pa tshong khye mthong bas lus srog thed la 'bor
ba ltar skye ba dang tshe rabs thams cad kyi 'dren pa gcig pu pa de'i drung du bsnyags te/ yar lam drung pa chos rje'i sngon gyi gti gnas dngul chu chos rdzong gi dgon
par nub cig gnas 'brel la nyal ba'i rmi lam gyi 'char sgo ma 'gags pa'i rang myong la/ bdag rang stod g.yogs ras lta bu 'di yin gtan mi mtshon pa shin tu dkar ba zhig 'phur
gos su byas nas nam mkha'i mthongs shin tu mtho ba la lus sems bde snang dang bcas phyin/ ji zhig nas dpag bsam gyi shing yin snyam pa'i sdong po lo 'dab 'bras bus yongs
su rgyan pa'i rtse mo zhig tu sleb/ shing de'i 'bras bu yin snyam pa la kha dog sngon po rnam pa dang rang bzhin du mkhregs shing lci nyams che ba/ phyi gsal nang gsal
gyi rnam pa can zhig lag tu lon/ slar yang byang shar phyogs la 'phur phyin pas spangs shong shig tu son te/ de na kha sarpa Na'i sku rgyu 'di yin mi mtshon pa/ rgyan spangs
pa tshangs par spyod pa'i cha lugs can zhig gis mchog sbyin gyi phyag rgya las 'o ma'i rgyun 'bab pa zhig 'dug pa/ de la kha gtad de 'thung pas shin tu tshims pa'i
snang ba dang bcags gnyid sad pa na/ rmi lam de dag gi don la dpyad pas/ da lan bsam pa bzhin 'grub pa'i bltas khyad par can gyi mtshan ma bzang po rtsol

med shar ba la/ stod g.yogs dkar po gyon 'phur ba rmi ba 'di bsam pa dge ba'i lhag bsam gyis sgrib pa zad pa'i ltas yin snyam/ dpag bsam gyi sdong po rgyud 'grel las gzhan
gyis 'dzol mi 'dug kyang/ de'i 'bras bus rnyed pa 'di da lan man ngag theb pa'i rten 'brel rmad byung du yid ches te/ dbang rgyud gnyis ji ltar thob da res mi shes par 'dug/
'on kyang kha sarpa Na'i sku'i phyag gi 'o rgyun 'thung shing tshims pas bla ma khong pa'i byin rlabs don gyis 'pho ba khyad par can nges par bdag rang gi rgyud la 'jug
par 'dug/ gzims dpyil gyi 'char sgo lha khang ngam/ mchod rten zhig yong thang ba la/ spangs stong de ci'i ltas yin nam snyam snyam pa'i yid dpyod lhug par skyes/ de nas
rgyal sras rin po che dngul chu chos rdzong pa nyid kyi gzim mal sku 'dra'i drung/ spos mar me/ lha bshos snyan dar dang bcas pa'i bkur bsti/ phyag skor ba dpag tu med
pa byas/ sngar jo bo rin po ches chos 'khor lha sar lung bstan pa'i yid ches kyi mtha' thug tu gzung/ 'dod chos zhu ba la rkang gtad 'ongs pa'i mdangs nub kyi rmi lam lung
bstan dang gtan 'dzol med pa'i yid der skyes pa 'di ji bzhin du 'grub par mdzad du gsol snyam pa'i smon lam brgya rtsa yid brtse gcig pas bsgrubs nas phyin pas/ rim gyis

pas/ kha dog dmar ser lbu ba'i phreng ba 'khrigs pa zhig byung ba lhag ma lus pa hob 'thung byas pas rmi lam gyi ngang der ma sad pa la lus nyams shin tu che ba gcig byung

dgu skor thag ring zhing/ chibs med pa sogs sku bsnyel ba blos gtan mi bzod pa 'dug pa re zhig sku ngal bsten pa zhu/ 'dod chos bzhin dgongs par yod na ci dgos 'bul gsung

gin yod tshod 'dug gsung ba la/ lam 'bras las zab pa'i chos med par thag gcod pa la/ chos gzhan gyi zab mi zab sngon la shes dgos/ rmongs zhen dud 'gros kyang shes/

la/ yang gral de'i dge bshes gzhon pa gcig gis nged la sbyor drug dang bsnyen sgrub kyi bar la khyad ji tsam yod 'dir byung pa la/ shes pa hur phyung ba'i skabs yin pas/

tu byung ste/ de dus tshogs lhag dor ba'i sa phyogs yun ring po'i bar snum gyis yongs su sbags pa'i rang bzhin can dang/ ji lta ba'i tshogs bzang ba byung yang rang gi khams
tshod dang bstun che 'bring chung gsum longs spyad pa'i mthar/ lhag kun gtor mar byin gyis rlabs/ ma chags pa'i sbyin gtong lhur len pa la/ skam chags kyi bsam pas chang
bu gcig kyang mi 'khyer ba'i mig ltos bzang po'i phyag len la bkod cing/ tshogs zhu mi bzang ba'i dus sha mar mi khur gnyis long tsam bzhi mdor dpungs pas bya khyi rnams
kyang zhe log/ rnam pa tsam gyis tshim par gyur pa'i tshul yul phyogs kyi lam 'grul ba tshun gyis mig lam du gsal ba de yin/ de ltar shangs chos yongs su rdzogs pa'i
sgo de nyid zla ba dgu pa'i tshes gcig nas/ bcu gcig pa'i bcu bdun gyi ring la bar chad med par mthar phyin pa'i chos kyi grol ston dang/ bcu

bdun mchod pa lhan cig pa'i nyin rangs mang ja bcu gsum sbrel/ chos nyan pa kun la 'bul ba rnam gzhag gya nom pa phyin/ bsngo ba'i skabs bre mo'i tshul du/ sngon bstan pa yar
ldan gyi dus slob mas bla ma la 'bul ba srol du 'dug na'ang/ da dus kyi stabs nas nged bla mas/ slob ma la chos nyan pa'i drin sob tu 'bul ba yin/ nged na ning dbus gtsang
la rkang btsugs phyin pa'i dgos pa shangs chos lhag ma lus pa rdzogs par zhu ba dang/ bka' rgyud shangs pa'i gnas rnams su tshogs 'khor re'i 'brel zhu ba kho na la blo
rtse gtad/ sgrub gnas zhong gshong ma/ srin mo/ lcags po rtse/ rmog cog kun lung/ skyer sgang/ yol bu re gong/ brag chen/ ljags sogs gnas tha dad du tshogs kyi rnam pa
re dang bcas smon lam snying nas btab/ yol phu'i mgon po rang byon la brtag pa zhus pas/ rgya sgom lung bstan pa bzhin zhabs la gtugs/ khyed rnams la byin pa'i chos de rnams
bstan thog gcig tu rdzogs par bstsal skabs der 'brum bu btab/ shin tu bro 'tshal bar gyur kyang bsags sbyang du go bas ma zhum pa'i snying stobs kyis chos sna gcig ma
chad par longs na'ang/ sa byes yul du song 'bul ba tshogs 'khor rgya chen bsgrub rgyu med pas yid nongs par byung nas/ chos kyi sku drin bsob la/ ni gu'i khrid brgya rtsa
brgyad 'chad pa'i dam bca' phul bas/ rgya bsgom chen po'i zhal nas/ khyed ni gu ma dngos dang mjal bas thugs ma tshim par/ nged gang zag so skye la chos nan bskyed dgos
gsung ba gang nas bsams kyang 'jigs par byung kyang/ rmi lam lta bu'i nyams la mgon po 'khor bcas kyis chos rdzogs par

bgyi ces yang yang bskul ba'i mtshan ma brdzun med byung ba dang/ 'di ltar shin du khams dub pa la yang bstan pa dang sems can la dgongs/ nyin mtshan rgyun ma chad par chos
gsan lugs/ bdag las la bkod pa'i phyag brgya 'bul nyin re bzhin gnang ba'i rnam thar mngon sum du mthong ba 'dis yid ches rungs pa'i gting nas skyes/ ci yod kyi gdams pa
lhag ma lus pa bum pa gang byor phyag tu thengs/ chos bdag po la 'phrod pa mi rgan da lta shi yang blo bde/ byes yul gang du shangs chos gnang kyang bar chad med pa'i khag
ngas len/ khrid brgya rtsa'i stengs su dngos grub kyi pha phogs chen po yang yong gsung ba'i bka' lung bzang po dngos su phebs pa yin pas/ khyed rnams yid ches par gyis
ces gnas lugs brjod pas/ der 'dus kyi bdag dpon slob thams cad dga' ba dang skyo ba zung sbrel gyi mchi ma lhug par byung ngo//tshogs de nang du ma Ni dung 'gyur rang rang
gi lce thog nas 'dren pa dang/ gzhan mang po bsnyen bkur bteg te dung 'gyur 'jug mi bcu bdun byung rang gi tshogs gsog pa tsam las ma 'grub pa de la/ khrid kyi mgo rang
la bzang zhing gya nom pa'i ga Na tsakra blo 'das byung ba dang/ lo chen drung du khas blangs pa'i ma Ni dung 'gyur gyi dbu tshugs/ dge bshes sha stag rang 'dus pa'i lam
'bras de yang de nyin ka tshugs tsam bgyis nas bsam pa lhag par rangs pa'i ngang nas nyal ba'i rmi lam du/ bdag sngar 'brum bus na ba'i ri khrod de na 'dug pa'i mdun gyi
nam mkhar rgya sgom ri khrod pa de nyid sku gzi mdangs sngar las kyang che ba/ g.yas g.yon steng 'og thams cad na

bla ma mang po bzhugs pa la/ skyeng sgang pa yin nam snyam pa cig gsal cha che bar byung pa rmi/ phyis 'khrul med du de nyin rab brtan chos lung gi dgon par rgya sgom chen
po zhi ba'i dbyings su gzims 'dug pa tshor bas rmi lam gyi snang ba dran/ bla ma dang sel med pa'i dam tshig gi srog la snying nas yid bde bar byung/ der snang gsum shin
tu rgyas pa zla chos gcig gi bar bla chos med par grub mtshams/ de lo sgyu lus yang gsung ngag pa rang las dbang bskur gtan med pa bgyis/ sngags lam man 'chad rgyu dang smra
rgyu yod do cog labs te/ go ba dang zungs su thebs pa'i rjes ni cig kyang ma dod sgra nam mkha' la dengs/ 'on kyang dus der rang nyid kyi dge sbyor la gsal snang che
ba'i blo bskyed dang/ sngar ma go ba'i chos kyi sgrog mang du khrol/ gnas der dpyid sos bar dben gsum bsten pa'i yang dag 'jog gi rnal 'byor khyad par can la nan tan gyi
snying rus mi chung ba lhur blangs/ rang shong gi sa phug sgo bcad zhig gi nang du gzan rkyang gcig kho na la bsgril nas g.yeng ba med pa'i bsgom bgyis pas/ stong gzugs kyi
'char sgo'i thog mar kun mkhyen mi pham mgon zhal ras brjid chags nya gang ba'i zla ba rgyas pa ltar mthong zhing/ snang ba 'di phyis sman 'byung sding du lo chen dpon
slob lhan cig bzhugs pa'i skabs srod zhig snang ba med pa'i mun pa la lo chen gyi dbu thad tsam gyi bar snang la sngar ji lta ba bzhin bdag gis gsal bar mthong ba dus de
rang du lo chen pa'i snyan du btab bo//de ltar brag stengs su zla ba dgu gdan thog gcig tu skad cig kyang g.yo ba med par bsdad rjes/ lo chen drung du maN

bskul gyi dam bca' phul ba ltar phyogs med kyi 'gro don la dmigs/ chu bzang ba 'dug pas byang phyogs kyi ri khrod spo dmar du phyin/ sa der ba lung snying rje can dpon slob/
dad can gyi skye bo du ma dang bcas dol phyogs nas phebs/ mos ldan gyi slob ma dge slong tshul 'dod pas gtso mdzad sprin chen pa'i dge 'dun mang ba/ drung dpal ldan rin
chen pa dang/ sman khrod pa'i thugs dam pa 'ga' re/ bkra dum pa'i che bsgres drag pa du ma/ dbu legs/ chos lung/ dgon par/ kho la spro/ 'brog phyogs kyi dgon sde so so nas
'dus pa'i chos nyan pa shin tu mang ba la slar yang ni gu'i khrid spyi nye bar dril ba'i 'bring po gzhung bka' nyer lnga dang sbrel/ dmigs pa 'dril zhing 'doms che ba'i
go bde kun gyi snying la 'bab pa 'bad med du byung/ khyad par rgyab rten sgyu ma lam rim rtsa bral la mtha' chod kyi bshad pa skyar chos yod pa byas/ drung ba lung pa sogs
kyis sngar ma gsan pa'i stabs rgyud sde lnga/ bde mchog nag po pa/ phyag bzhi pa'i dbang bzhi rdzogs sogs 'dus pa rnams 'dod chos kyi re ba gang bar bgyis/ phyogs nas
'ongs pa'i mi nag gi skye bo grangs med byung ba la nyin re bzhin tshe dbang/ rgyu 'bras la yid ches pa'i spyi chos thun mi 'chag tu bshad pas sems 'khul/ ma Ni dung 'gyur
'jug mkhan dang rang gi lce thog nas len mi/ drung ba lung pa sogs bla ma rnam pas gzhan la bskul te/ dung 'gyur spel ba'i dam bca'i khur bzhes grangs su btab pas nyi
shu rtsa lnga byung nas slar brag steng rang du log/ don gnyer nyung shas la bka' 'bum pod bzhi ma'i lung/ lam 'bras kyi cha lag

'ga' re bgyis cing ngal bso bsten/ zla phyed tsam bsdad nas rong phyogs kyi 'gro ba skad mi shes dge sdig 'chom par spyod pa dag la snying rjes kun nas blangs/ lho mon gyi
mtshams smad lha khang du grags pa der rkang gtad phyin/ dpon slob bya btang rang sha stag bco lnga tsam rang shong gi cog so la brten/ ldum bu'i snang bde skyong gin/ yul
ljongs che sa ru cag mal tsam dang/ gzhan gdan cig gar phog gi yul chung rnams su ma Ni'i 'gro don dam bca'i khas len srod tho rangs 'tshogs nas 'don pa'i dge bskul sogs
re re nas ma chad pa bgyis/ skad mi shes kyi sems can sngar mi Ni 'dren mi byung na ngan sngags bzla ba yin zer sa mthor rdo mthor gyi rnam rtog can de rnams la/ kho rang
gi skad du rim gyis glengs te/ rgya gar gyi dzo ki rnams gho rag sgo rag smra ba dang/ mo khol rnams kho das kho das/ bram ze rnams ram ram brjod pa dang khyad med nged
bod mi rnams ma Ni pad me bzla ba yin byas pas yid ches nas ngang gis yig drug 'dren mi je mang du 'phel/ zla phyed bsdad ring yul gru chen po de'i skad shes thams cad
kyis 'ur dir dir 'dren pa byung bas/ nged rang dpon slob kyang lhag par sems tshims shing dang spro ba byung na'ang/ sa phyogs de na sha chang ma gtogs za nyan dang spyad
nyan til tsam yang mi 'dug/ ja yang rong chus mi thub par chad nas bskol mi nyan/ phyugs mang bar 'dug kyang 'o ma 'jo ba'i srol med pa/ mar zho dar sogs sgra yang mi grag

gsungs pa'i gnas/ mtshar 'ga' zhes pa'i sa phyogs der zla phyed tsam gyi

ring bsdad/ rong phyogs kyi bla ma chen po songs pa sku mched sogs sku drag dpag med 'dus pa dang/ dol phyogs nas kyang ba lung snying rje can gyis gtso mdzad/ bla ma slob

drug so so'i bka' drug dang khrid drug spel ba'i gdams ngag dbang dang 'grel ba'i yid tshims par bgyis/ gzhan la so so'i zhe 'dod ltar dbang lung nyin mtshan bar ma chad
pa'i chos 'chad le lo med pa dang/ rgyun gyi kha ton sgrol ma brgya rtsa sogs las/ sos dal gyi rnam pa skad cig ma bsten/ der yang ma Ni dung 'gyur rang gi lce thog nas 'don
pa dang/ gzhan yang bskul nas 'jug mi sogs stobs che ba byung mtshams slar log/ rnam rgyal du a ma'i rtsar zla phyed tsam bsdad ring/ brtse lhag gi phan sems chen pos

chen dmigs phran so sor phye nas/ dmigs chen byang chub sgrub lam gzer bu bcu bdun du sdoms/ de nyid cing nyin zhag phrug gcig gi rnal 'byor la phan tshun ma 'dres par

pa'i nad g.yog pa rnams la/ bu chos rje dang ma mjal kyang khong gis byin pa'i gdams ngag brjed pa med/ dbugs 'gro khar khyed rnam pas a zhes sgra che ba vc: cheb?thos nges

'tsho byed pa rnams phyag rtsa yang mi 'dug zer/ chibs khyer spyan 'dren la yongs pa yin/ myur du ma phebs na zhal mi mjal ba yod zer rtsab rtsob 'dug pa la/ ngas rings
na slod yin/ ja cig 'thungs byas bskol bas/ dge slong rnam pa yang da phebs pa drag/ gal srid yum sras ma mjal na ja 'thung gin bzhugs zer gtam yang ngan zer ba la/ rmongs
pa khyed la ci lab kyang go rig mi 'dug/ nga ja ma 'thungs pa'i mi 'gro/ sdug bsngal yod na da gzod gyis byas pa'i rin la ja thon byung/ de nas snyur phyin pas rnam rgyal
gyi gzims chung de na 'dug/ khong rnam pa phebs pa'i dus ma byung zer kha shu shu byed kyi 'dug/ ngas yum gyi dbu bsngas der bsdad sgron me btegs bltas pas zhal ras ser
yal pa cig 'dug/ snying na skam pa cig byung rjes/ lag pa bskyangs thugs kar bzhag pas thugs phir phir 'dug/ de ni gu'i brgyud 'debs gdangs ma zhig skad gzengs phyung
ste gyer bas/ phyi na yod pa kun da 'pho ba btab pa yin zer ngu ci'i ber langs/ lung pa kun tu grong par

thag bcad/ dge slong rnam pas nged kyi tshig la bden zer bcas/ da lo khag len byas pas thams cad kyis khrel khrel byed/ mi shi ba longs na grub thob rang du 'dug zer 'phya
dmog gtong ba byung/ der rgyud 'debs tshar tsam la yum nyid dbu bteg/ nged la gzigs nas bu chos rje phebs sam gsungs/ zhal 'dzum dang bcas sku lang tsho khyad par du 'phags
pa rang gi rnam pa cig ston pa mdzad byung bas skabs der yang rmi lam la nges shes lhug par skyes/ der su med pa'i dben pa zhig la sngar lo chen drung nas da bar gyi ltas
rim par byung ba snyan du btab/ nged bu rnams las phyi thag bsrings/ yun ring du bzhugs pa'i thugs mdun mdzad dgos zhus pas/ sems can skye 'chi la rang dbang ga la yod/
kho mo ma la bzang/ khyed lta bu'i skyes bu dam pa la yang 'khrungs/ da skye ba dang tshe rabs su thugs rjes mi 'dor ba zhu gsung phyag thal mo sbyar/ dbu mdud pa dang
bcas bka' stsal 'byon gyi 'dug pa la/ nged rang bla lhag gi yid ches snying khong nas skyes/ slar thugs rjes khyed kyis 'dzin dgos pa 'dug/ da lan yang sku khams brtas pa'i
legs tshogs spel dgos lags zhus pas/ de nub rang la nang sbyar du sku khams lhag par bde ba/ sngar las kyang sku khams bzang ba byung yang/ zla gcig gi bar sku khams
bcad bya ma zhig pa 'tsho byed rnams kyis yid gso ba'i byug pa re tsam bzhes shing/ bdag la sngar ni gu'i khrid gnyis tsam thob pa da dung nan chags che ba'i zhib len byas
pa zhig dgos gsung/ dbu btsugs/ yang bka' las khong rnam pa nged la kun rig dang mi 'khrugs pa'i dbang 'dra

yang zhus zer gyi 'dug kyang/ bu khyed 'dra skyes nas ma dmyal bar btang na ngo tsha snyam pa'i thugs kyi brjed bso la mi zhu gsung zhal 'dzum 'dzum gnang gin 'dug/ der tshe
dbang/ sgrol dkar/ chos skyong gi gtor dbang sogs nyin rer bzhin ma chag par/ ni gu'i zab khrid kyang rdzogs par phul ba'i mthar/ ga Na tsakra'i pu dza'i gtso mo yum chen
mo nyid la blos dmigs/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs mchod rgyas par bgyis pa/ rang ngo'i bza' btung longs spyod/ snyan grags bde skyid gzhan don phrin las thams cad
kyi rten 'brel do kho nas 'grig cing/ der yum sras thugs phab pa'i 'das ma 'ongs kyi byung tshul/ slad nas kyi smon lam du ma yang phan tshun snying thag pa nas bgyis te/
nged sngar gyi maN bskul yul kha kha so sor btsugs pa rnams la nan cag bgyi ba'i bsam pas/ de lo yang sne shang yul po cher phyin/ sa rong lam 'phrang dog pas dpon slob
kun lhag par sbyong bar byung kyang/ bla ma'i bka' bsgrub pa yin snyam blos longs par byas/ der rong phyogs kyi 'gro ba phal mo che'i sar yi ge drug pa'i chos kyis khyab/
de dus sdod sa bde rtsa brgyad kyi thang yangs shing gcig gi gnas de'i drung rang du chos khri brtsigs/ nyin mtshan khor mor zla gcig tsam/ khrid gcig mjug gcig gis sbrel
ba'i khri thog de rang du ni gu tshar bcu gsum btud rjes/ slar zar phyogs kyi yul kha tha dad du na ning spel ba'i ma Ni dung 'gyur song ba rnams la bsngo ba'i rgyas 'debs
dang/ da dung 'jug mi rnams la nas kyi ster sbyin sogs skul cag 'thems pa'i mtheb rdzis/ sob dang brdzun ma 'dres pa'i nges gsal la

btab/ slar dung 'gyur 'jug mi drug bdun tsam gsar 'phel byung 'tshams/ bar tshigs/ shar ri'i yul gsum sogs sngar ma phyin pa'i sa de rnams su maN bskul kho na'i 'gro don la
rkang gtad nas rang rang so'i 'dod pa ltar dbang lung man ngag/ dpon sa yab yum drung du khral 'chag zhu ba sogs sne sbyor gang legs kyis yid drangs pas/ mgu ba lhag par
skyes/ dung 'gyur 'jug mi bcu gsum lhag tsam dang/ srod tho rangs yul gyi rgan gzhon rnams mgrin gcig par ma Ni bzhi thun re tsam bsgrong ba'i dge rtsa gtan par tshugs/
rang gi dngos su ma slebs pa'i tang skya sogs yul chung 'ga' rer mos ldan gyi slob ma drung pa dge slong mchog ldan pa sogs la dge bskul bgyis nas/ ma Ni dung 'gyur brgyad
tsam len mi 'byung 'dug/ de nas a ma dran pa'i gdung shugs kyis bskul/ yang rnam rgyal du yum drung zhag lnga drug ngal bso bsten zhing/ dbang lung phran bu 'bul ba dang/
yid 'dres pa'i gleng mo sems tshim pa mang du byung rjes/ skye yul glo bo rang de/ sngon rgyal po ge sar gyis btul ba'i bdud gya rgyu'i yul yin par grags pa don la gnas
par 'dug/ dam pa'i chos la sol phye las gnag pa'i blo drag zhan yongs la che chung med par khyab 'dug pas/ chos khyad sgo btun sgrub mchod re tsam gyi zhabs tog 'jig rten
las snang gi 'gran dpe la dmigs sgrub pa ma gtogs lha chos gtsang ma 'dres med la snang phug kyang 'dren par mi nus 'dug pa nas/ yang dol phyogs kyi yul rnams su man bskul
la phyin/ 'tsho ba so so'i mi dpon rgan pa rnams la ster sbyin yang dag pas sems khrid de ma

Ni yul kun tu khyab pa'i 'khrul che ba blo yul las 'das pa'i dge tshogs 'bad med lhun grub spyi khyab tu byung zhing/ dung 'gyur yang ri khrod rang du chig sgril byas/ lce
thog nas 'don mi chos pa rnam dag dpag med byung nas yid bde bsam gyi mi khyab pa skyes/ phyogs der byung ba'i 'bul ba thams cad kyang ma Ni ba kho na'i phyogs su lhag ma
lus pa khyab par byas/ drung ba lung pa/ drung rnam grol ba/ drung pa 'bum ram pa/ drung pa rang 'byung sa dang bzhi la do dam bcol/ dol phyogs kyi ma Ni ba rnams la grangs
kyi gnas phra mo la yang som nyi med pa'i yid ches par yod/ de nas mon yul gyi kha thod bar bongs sa grags pa'i yul der phyin/ dbyar ngo dgon sar du bsdad nas/ chos don
gnyer gyi dge 'dun dad ldan sha stag la lam 'bras shin tu rgyas pa zhig gi dbu btsugs mtshams/ drung ba lung pa sku mched kyang byon byung/ sa der nyin mtshan dus drug
'khor mor chos kyi 'da' ba byung ste/ nged rang gis lam 'bras gzhung zhing du snga phyi thun gnyis su bshad pa'i chos thun shin tu ring ba/ bar bar la glo bur du 'ongs pa'i
bya bral gnas skor ba lam 'bras ma zin pa'i chos bsnyegs pa yul gyi rgan pa du ma la lam 'bras ring la ni gu lan bcu gcig tsam song/ nged dgos chos 'chad pa'i skabs/
zur chos la ba lung snying rje'i zla bas tshogs pa spyi khyab tu ma gcig ka so ma'i dbang le lhag brgyad ma dang bcas pa/ rnam grol bstan pa'i nyi mas bde mchog lU i pa'i
dbang lan grangs du ma/ padma bka'i thang yig gi lung/ 'bum ram pa tho rangs skar chen pas gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i dbang cha sbrel ma dang 'brel

bar gsang 'dus rnam bshad chen mo'i bshad lung/ bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang cha gnyis/ dar smyon he ru ka las phag mo khros nag gi dbang lung/ rang byung chos kyi rdo rjes
bde chen skor gsum sogs khong so sos kyang gcig tho gcig la ma phog par chos 'chad drag la yun ring ba gnang zhing/ skabs der 'bri khung mkhan rin po che mgon bzang pa dpon
slob/ songs pa sku mched kyi gtso mdzad/ lba lba sogs mon rgyal po'i mnga' zhabs nas 'ongs pa'i che dgu/ ras gos 'ba' zhig gyon pas lung pa'i stod smad thams cad ngang
dkar gyi khyus gangs pa ltar dkar por mthong ba/ khyad par bud med thams cad smad g.yogs ras khra bsul bsgrigs su byas pa'i sham thabs mdzes pas dkris/ skra'i tshogs ltag
par bcings pa lha mo'i rnam pa can rkang lag thams cad gser dngul gyi gdu bu dang/ g.yer khas rgyan te/ rgyang ring po nas kyang sil khrol gyi sgra snyan par sgrog pa/
dkyil 'khor pa'i rigs ma bcu drug kyang snang cha 'di lta bu yin no snyam pa'i yid spyod lhug par bskyed pa'i dad 'dus kyi skye bo dpag tu med pas dgon gnas kyi phyogs thams
cad khyab pa na/ yi ge drug pa las brtsams pa'i chos kyi sgo mdo sde za ma tog bkod pa'i rgyal po la bshad lung skad gnyis su sdebs nas skal bzang gi gdul bya rmad du
byung ba de dag gi rna ba'i khung bur zhag bdun gyi bar nyin re las nyin re chos thun je rgyas su spel ba'i chos kyi gtam rgya cher rnyed pas/ khong rang gi skad kyis 'grol
des yid lhag par rangs pa'i mgu ba thob/ bha Da gu ru/ mahA paNDi ta a tshe/ pha la pha la/ ces brjod cing/ shin tu gtsang sbra dang

ldan pa'i brtul zhugs 'chang ba de dag rang dbang med pa'i dad pa'i rlabs g.yos/ nged rang gi lham gtsug tu len pa sogs mi phyed pa'i dad pa dang rgyu 'bras la 'khrul med du
yid ches pa'i yang dag pa'i lta bas skal ba khyad par can gyi rnyed pa dang bcas/ yi ge drug ma'i sgra di ri ri/ tshong pa nor bu'i gling nas re ba'i bsam pa rdzogs pa
ltar/ slar rang gi yul ga la ba der log rjes/ 'bri khung mkhan rin po che dpon slob rnams la ni gu'i mgyogs khrid/ bde mchog dril nag gsum gyi dbang/ gzhan yang dgongs bzhed
ltar gyi 'dod chos lhug par phul/ mkhan chen pa nyid kyis chig rdzogs kyi gnas legs par bzhes/ thugs dad mos bcos ma ma yin pa sngar nas kyang 'dug cing/ slar yang 'phel
te gdung shugs kyi spyan chab ser phran drag po 'bab pa la 'gran du bzod pa'i rgyun nyin mtshan khor mor g.yo ba dang bcas 'bral bar mi phod pa'i ngang nas 'bri khung
gi gdan sa chen po nyid du phyags thegs/ lam 'bras sogs chos rnams kyang bar chad med par mthar phyin/ mon phyogs nas phul ba'i ras cha sngo dmar/ sman/ mkhar ba'i phor
gzhong/ shing 'bras/ khyad par zas mchog pos su sbyar ba lha'i zhal zas la bskrun par nus pa de rnams cung zad kyang ma 'bags par/ gzeb che ba gcig gi nang du bkur stir bgyis
nas bdag gir gzung/ gzhan 'bul ba longs spyod thams cad der 'dus kyi dge 'dun kun la sna cig kyang chud ma zos par sbyin gtong byas/ sa 'dir skya btsun khongs su ma
Ni dung 'gyur nyi shu rtsa lnga 'khrul med len mi byung ba rnams bla ma'i thugs dgongs rdzogs pa'i bsngo ba

dang smon lam gyis rgyas thobs par byas nas pha yul du log/ rnam rgyal du lam mi 'chag la yum gyi drung du phyin/ gzeb nang na yod pa'i dngos po phran bu de rnams phyag tu
thengs pa byas/ sngar yum rin mo che de nyid bzhes spro'i rnam pa gang yang ljags stengs su mi rig pa yin yang/ der nged la rten 'brel gyi gnad sgrig pa la dgongs pa 'dra/
rnam grangs du ma'i bzhes spro de rnams nas sne tshang re mchod pa gnang gi 'dug pa la/ 'bras bu ram sbrang rtsi sogs las grub pa sku srin la phog pa yong ma mchod pa drag
zhus pas/ bu chos rje rang yang tshogs 'khor gyi skabs zhal du ci gsol kyang mi gnod 'dug pa/ de dang khyad ci yod gsungs byung bas/ bza' ba rang bzhin gyis byin gyis
rlob nus pa'i mkha' 'gro mar go// bstab pa thams cad ga Na tsa kra'i pU dzar 'dug snyam pa'i nges shes skyes/ de lo ja shin tu dkon par 'dug pas/ bsam pa la ja bzang ba
dpus tshol byas/ dgun po 'di yum gyi zhal du thong nges byung na tshogs che bar 'dug ste snyam/ nga da lo dus chos kyi lam 'bras a ma dang thag nye bar 'dug pas/ byams gling
du mchod/ nyi shar la gsol ja re zhur gtong ba chab nu gnang ba'i bka' drin sob la dgongs nas cis kyang mchod dgos cing/ ja zho gang tsam 'di yang skabs dang bstun nas
bzhes pa zhu byas nas byams gling du phyin/ de nyin rang lam 'bras btsugs/ tshogs che zhing bshad pa mtha' chod zhib pa rang byung na'ang/ dpyid sos ma dang 'bral ba'i
zug rngu'i tsher ma rnon pos snying phug/ nyin mtshan khor mor a ma'i zhal ras sems la wal le ba dang/ da myur du mi rtag yid 'byung gi rang

mtshan de mthong yong snyam pa sha stag skam skam pa byung/ zur chos sogs dang dpe blta'i spros pa yang bcad/ thugs dam yang 'di yin rang med pa'i rgya yan byas su mi tshor
ba'i chod chod kho na'i ngang nas sa skya ra ma chag tsam re byas/ der lam 'bras grol/ bya lo zla ba dang po'i dgu mchod chen mo la chos grol ston dang lhan du tshogs pa
rnams la mar khu bre 'gyed kyis mtshon pa'i bsnyen bkur zab rgyas rang gi mar me brgya rtsa'i mchod pa bshams/ bde mchog bla mchod yid 'jur bar bgyis te/ sngar gyi rmi lam
gyi mtshan ma de dag la dpyad pas de las mi 'da' bar mthong nas/ de nub ma'i drung du phyin te bsdad/ de skabs yum sku khams shin tu dngas shing sku nyams che ba/ gzi
mdangs rgyas pa cig 'dug/ mjal la khad la dgun po de shin tu khams bzang zhing/ bu chos rje'i chos gaN rgyun mi 'chad thos pas yid bde bar byung/ ces shin tu dges pa'i rnam
pa ston gyi 'dug/ de'i srod la ja nyis sbrel tsam gyi rin 'phros gtam la/ nged rang byis pa'i dus yum rang gis bskyangs pa'i skabs smras pa'i gleng brjod rnams dang/ res
'ga' yum gyis thal cag re tsam gnang ba la shin brdzun yun ring po byas lugs/ nu ma slong ba la ngo 'tsho mkhas po yod lugs kyi gnas tshul rnams lhug par gsungs pas der
'tshogs thams cad bzhad mo dir dir byung ba'i ring/ sems la da tshe 'dir ma dang phrad/ gleng slang smra ba do nub kho na yin snyam blo 'dar phrug ge ba'i ngang nas/ bdag
byang chub snying po la mchis kyi bar 'gro ba gang gi lus su skye ba len na yang yum 'di ma dang/ nga bu kho nar gyur cig snyam pa'i smon

lam re re nas phreng ba la bcug pa'i 'khrul med du de ring rang la stong rwa can tsam song/ gral grol nas yab kyi gser 'bum drung nyal du phyin mtshams/ thun gtor sogs thugs
dam chag med rnams bgyis/ der gnyid gtan ma byung zhing/ bsam pa nges 'byung gis drangs pa'i sngar gyi smon lam de ka mtshan rangs vc: rang sa?ba btab/ nyi rtse la gzims
khang steng du bzhes spro gzab dgu bshams pa'i gdan gcig de gnang byung ba la/ mas lag bdar nas byin pa'i za ma'i jes ma 'di rang yin bsam dkon pa'i 'du shes kyis tshim
par bzas/ ja sbyo sbrel gyi rin/ mdang gi 'phros/ nges byis pa'i skabs kyi gleng blangs mang po gsungs pa'i mthar/ kho mo skal ba bzang/ de 'dra'i byis chung cig bskyangs
pa la/ da mig gis mthong bar sems can yongs kyi skyabs mgon chen po cig byung gsung spyan chab nyil mdzad byung bas/ re shig las snang gi 'char sgo 'gags pa'i dran med
lta bu cig byung rjes/ phyag gser zho gang yum gyi phyag tu phul nas/ phyag de nyid bdag rang gi snying gi thad du bzhag ste/ mdangs nub kyi smon lam gcig pu de lan gsum
snying thag pas btab/ de de bzhin du 'grub pa'i mtshan ma brtan po yang shar/ sdug bsngal yul phud/ skye 'chi'i 'tshang sdib/ sgyu ma lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin bzang po khong
du chud pa'i spobs pa khyad par can/ ma'i phyag snying la gtugs pa'i rten 'brel des byung/ tshe 'dir mjal ba'i rjes ma de rang la byas/ khams 'dus legs par grol ba'i ngang
nas brag stengs su lam mi 'chag la phyin/ chos rje 'dar pa dpon slob gra pho mo sum cu tsam/ gzhan dad 'dus bsgom

kho na gnyer bdun cu don 'dren la shangs chos rgyas pa rang zhig gi dbu de nyin ka btsugs/ rgyud sde lnga ras bris la brten pa'i dbang gi sta gon byas mtshams/ zla chos gcig
gi rin shin tu dmar ba/ chos nyan rin rgad mos brag phug bteg yong ba tsam gyi ngang la/ rtsa ba ni gu'i chos drug dang/ gdong po phyag rgya chen po gzhung khrid rdzogs
pa'i skabs der/ gnam gang gi nub tshogs kyi 'khor lo ma da na gtso bor gyur ba'i rgya che ba bsgrubs/ chos bro nyams mgur brjid chags pa/ spyir yang de skabs kyi tshogs
byung res la byas shing/ khyad par de nub yun rings spro zhing dang chags pa byas mtshams tshogs lhag dor/ byin pa phug 'og tu nyal du song/ rgyun ldan gyi dge slong rnam
pa la da dung rang re ja skol en tsam bzhugs byas/ ja shin tu bzang ba zhig bskol rin/ nged rang gis kyang ja khang du phyin pa'i 'phros gtam la/ khong rnam pa na re/ na
ning yum snyung skabs nas kha sang zla ba snga ma'i gnam gang la yum sras ma mjal bar/ nged rnam pa'i mthong snang la yang thugs skyo shas kyi rnam pa che zhing/ sngar dang
mi 'dra ba'i sku gzi mdangs ngan par 'dug pas/ lung bstan de'i steng du 'bab par 'dug snyam pa'i yid mi bde bar byung yang/ yum dang mjal man gyi zla chos gcig po 'di'i
rin sku gzi mdangs shin tu rgyas shing thugs spro ba'i tshul bstan byung ba 'dis da bar chad de bzlog pa yin nam snyam/ nged rnams blo gting nas bde ba'i bag phebs pa
byung zer gyi 'dug pa la/ ngas rmongs pa ha re long tsho/ ma drin can dang 'dral ba'i sdug bsngal gyi khrel gzhung dgos skal lo gcig hril khur ba khyed

rang chos shes pa de yin/ da sdug bsngal byas pas ci la phan/ khyed blo bde ba tsho la zhag bdun brgyad nas yang blo mi bde ba'i res 'bab las che/ de dus kha'i sdug bsngal
man na nged ma bu'i chos 'jig rten gyi dam tshig dang khrel bsam pa'i khur mi chung ba re'i go cha gyis byas rang shong gi spyil bur nyal du phyin/ tshes gcig man tshogs
pa byin gyis chos mtshams byas/ drung pa 'dar pa rang la chos bsham zhag bdun gyi ring dbang lung ma lus pa nyin mtshan kha bsgrags nas rdzogs par phul rjes/ zla ba gsum
pa'i tshes bzhi man yum rin po che snyan gong cung zad bsnyung ba'i tshul bstan nas tshes bdun gyi mtshan phyed tsam la/ dgung lo lnga bcu nga gsum stengdu rang gnas mkha'
la spyod pa'i gnas ga la ba der yongs su bzhud de/ bdag dang ma mjal na'ang/ sngar gyi smon lam de yi ger bris pa'i tho cig phul ba spyan gyis lan gsum gzigs/ thugs kar
stug stug pa lan gsum gnang rjes yi ge snyan gong du bcug sku gzhogs g.yas phab 'phral rang grongs 'dug pa brdzun med zhabs 'bring pa rnams kyis nges gsal du mthong/ de
sngar gyi bka' lung yod pas kun rig mi 'khrugs pa sogs kyi cho ga'i sgo nas sdig sbyong gi rnam pa ni mi dgos par thag chod/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i bsgrub mchod la brten
gsol 'debs kyi thugs dam bskul/ sngar de dang mjal stabs rnam rgyal kho nar bzhugs pa yin yang/ gshegs pa nged skyes pa'i pha khyim rnying pa der gnang 'dug pa/ kho bo rang
lo nyer lnga man skyes khyim gyi phyi them la gom pa mi 'jog pa'i dam bca' yod pas gdung mjal la ma phyin/ yum nyid kyi sku rgyan gser g.yu mu

tig byi ru spos shes sgam do nged yod sar khyer byung nas/ 'di dag la gzigs gshegs rdzongs sogs gang bab kyi bka' zhal gnang ba zhu zer ba la/ nga mig kyang mi blta/ nga la
ni zhe nas sa rdo dang khyad med/ sngar srol mi 'dug kyang/ a ma'i skye sa gu ge yin pas thog ma'i blo mchod kyi 'brel stabs bkra shis lhun por mang ja cig bskol/ nga la
a ma'i dran sor dbu skra sgam na 'dug zer ba de rnams bkur/ gzhan khyed rang tsho gros gyis la rjes na yod pa la gtam mi ngan cing/ yum rin po che'i sku yogs mi yong ba'i
dgongs rdzogs ci 'grub pa gyis byas nas/ dngos po bzang ngan sna cig la yang mthong thos reg gsum gyi dri mas ma gos pa'i dpang dri med gzigs pa'i spyan ldan rnams dang/
de dus kyi dgra gnyen grogs gsum thams cad la gsal mer yod/ de ltar dgung zhag ma rdzogs bar khong rnam pas kyang nged bsam pa'i dgongs rdzogs rang ngo bo shin tu snying
non sa bsgrubs shing/ sku gdung drung du/ drung pa chos rje pa'i phyag tshar gyi zhal slob gcig pu pa dge slong kun dga' mchog ldan pas gtso mdzad bzhi sde la bsnyen bskur
'bul ba thams cad dang rang gis byas/ lo mchod dus nged byang bkra dum du tsha rong chos rjes dbus gtsang 'khor nas 'bod mi rkang gtsugs gnang/ dpon slob mthar rgyas/
byang dgon tha dad nas 'dus pa'i tshogs sngar gyi lam 'bras dus kyi mi grangs gnyis sdoms pa tsam la lam 'bras rjes ma de 'chad kyi yod pas der bzhugs kyi tshogs pa thams
cad la mar khu bre 'gyed kyis mtshon pa'i bsnyen bskur/ chos rje rnam pa la bsngo rten gser zho re re/ tshogs pa byin la

nas 'gyed dang bcas bsgrubs shing/ skyes yul du yang mar zho bcu gnyis/ thud zho gang/ phyag gser srang gang sogs ma'i nub tshab la dmigs pa'i 'bul skyel yang dag pa btang/
dus mchod bzang dpe la 'khyer ba rang byung zhing/ mdor na da lta tshe 'di'i bskyed ma la yang drin lan du slad 'dod med pa'i sems can thams cad byang chub la 'god par zhal
gyis 'ches pa'i theg pa chen po pa rnams la bdag bcos ma ma yin pa'i zhe khrel gting nas skyes so//de ltar du bran thon pa dang lhan du lam 'bras kyang grol/ khyi lo
de nyiddrung pa chos rje bde bar gshegs nas/ lo bskor gcig song ba'i lo dus yin pas/ de la dmigs pa'i dge ba 'grub che ba gcig byung na snyam phu phag dgon par phyin/ sngar
gyi dkyil 'khor lnga'i steng du/ chos rje sku mched pas gtso mdzad/ shar phyogs nas byon pa'i dge bshes gsar pa sha stag rnams kyis bde bar gshegs pa brgyad kyi thugs
rje bskul ba sman bla'i mdo mchod/ nged rang gi rgyun ldan gyi grogs dge slong rnam pas mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu'i sgrub mchod dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor bdun zhal 'byed pa'i
chog bsgrigs phyag len 'dzub 'khrid rnams nan chags su byas rjes/ sa ga'i tshes bcu la dkyil 'khor so so'i thig btab nas nyer lnga'i bar dkyil 'khor re re'i mthar yang
gtsang zhing dag pa'i mar me lha bshos bzang zhing gya nom pa/ khyad par drung btsun pas gtso mdzad/ drung pa chos rje nyid kyi zhabs 'bring rgyun du bsten pa'i gzims gsol
rnying pa 'gas gdung rten drung mar me'i phreng ba rgya che ba gasto bor bshams pa'i mchod pa rnam grangs dpag med dus

gsum du go brje ba thun bzhir bcad pa'i bla ma mchod pa dang 'brel bar gser gyi maNDal 'bul ba nyid chig dril du gnang/ de skabs lha khang thams cad du nyin re bzhin rten gsum
yongs la byi dor sngon du 'gro ba'i mar me'i sdong bu gnya' shing gi khyon dang mnyam pa/ mtshan mo yang nyin mo ltar gsal bar byed pa'i mun bsel gyi mchod pa 'khor ma
rgyang ring po nas ngad ldang ba'i spos kyi dud sprin mtha' yas pa/ yon chab kha dog sna tshogs su bsgyur ba sogs/ de'i rin mchod pa'i shoms kho nas nyin mtshan 'da' bar
byas pas/ sha tsha'i nye sbyor ba 'ga' res 'di ltar/ dkyil 'khor kha grangs mang po dang/ lha khang thams cad du dkar me mdzad na mar gyis ma 'dang dogs mchis pas/ lha
khang rnams su 'bru mar 'bul ba gnang na legs zer/ mar khu mang po 'du byas 'dug pa la/ nga mchod yul bka' drin 'khor med kyi bla ma la byas/ dmigs yul drin can gyi ma la
bsam pa'i dge rtsa la nag mo 'bul ba rtog pa za byas/ lha khang ma lus pa'i srang ba do tshun snum gyis yongs su khyab pa'i phyi bdar nyin re bzhin lan gsum re dad long
rnams bskul nas bgyis shing/ de dus rna dpang ma nyams pa thams cad la brda 'phrod nges par/ lan gcig gnyis ma yin pa/ yab mes kyis bzhengs pa'i gnas 'di rnams la da lta
rang dbang thob dus zhabs tog 'di ltar 'bul/ des blo kha khegs/ mthar thug rgya gar rdo rje gdan mi rtag pa'i sar/ khra chal chil 'di kun kyang rtag pa dka' bo byas/ gyang
ris re re la 'dzub mo ma btsugs pa med na'ang/ gcer mthong du byung byung go mkhan mi 'dug/ skabs der rnam thar bstod

chen mtshan spel mi'i rtsom yang bla ma'i rjes dran la bgyis/ sa ga'i bcu bdun nyin tshogs su btsugs shing/ de nyin gang zag re res kyang dkar me lha bshos mi 'bul mkhan mi
'dug pas/ nang thams cad mchod pa'i yo byad kyis gang bar gyur to//de nas sa ga'i bcu bdun nub//yab rje dbyings su gshegs pa'i dus//rjes dran dge tshogs rab spel bas//thun
mongs slob mar bcas tshim tshe//skya rengs 'char kha'i snga logs su//mchog tu gsal ba'i sa ma dhiHrmi lam spangs pa'i mngon sum la//bzang po'i khri bcas mthon po'i stan//de
steng pha nyid bzhugs pa snyam//dkar 'jam dwangs pa'i rang bzhin gyis//legs byas g.yas pa'i zhabs brkyangs nas//bdag gi spyi bor rab bzhag te//mtshan 'dzin rtog pa
ma lus pa//zhi ba'i gnas la 'god par mdzad//sngar med dbang gi ye shes che//don chen gsang ba'i dbugs dbyung thob//byis pa rang nyams bzhin yengs pa//pha nyid dag pa'i dbyings
su bzhud//snang ba nam mkha'i 'ja' ltar yal//dbugs 'byin rnyed pa lnga pa'o//de ltar byin rlabs kyi mtshan ma khyad par can des yid lhag par drangs nas spro ba 'phel
te/ sngar thang skur bris pa/ lugs su blug pa/ tsan dan sogs shing brkos su bsgrubs pa'i skra lo re bzhin rgyun ma chad pa/ bzhengs pa'i mtha' bsten la dmigs/ gsum thog
gi ngos ma tshud tsam gyi rnam thar bris thang chen mo de nyid bzhengs shing/ mchod pa'i rgyur zangs stobs mi chung ba'i gzhi rten sbyar/ spyir yum la dmigs pa'i rdo rje
rnal 'byor ma'i bris thang bcu/ mkhan rin po che'i

[A:~150]thugs dgongs rdzogs thabs la bde mchog nag po pa'i gzab bris bcu/ rgya sgom ri khrod pa'i dgongs rdzogs la rgyud sde lnga'i dkyil thang khyad 'don bcu/ rang gi tshe
sgrub la dmigs tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dkyil thang bcu/ dkor sbyong la dmigs rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa'i dkyil thang bcu rnams bzhengs pa'i 'dun pa yod pa yang de los yongs
su rdzogs pa grub rjes/ rong nas 'khor te/ rong dugs la brten pa'i 'khru na 'chi nges pa cig byung skabs/ bsam pa la rgyu ngos rang snying non pa'i bya ba sgrub rgyu ma byung
yang/ lhag bsam dag pa'i dge ba lam du song 'dug/ bsags sbyang gi rnal 'byor skabs rmi lam du 'khru skyugs byung ba'i sdig pa zad pa'i rtags su byed na/ a la la snyam
sdug bsngal dang len gyi blo kha tsam min pa'i rjes dpag skyes/ gtong len gyi dmigs pa yid 'jur ba khril khril bas gcun pas rkyen thog tu blo khel pa'i nges shes lhug par
skyes shing/ gzhi nad phel che ba de rang gi so phyung nad khyer la song nas/ yang yang 'bod mi nan bskyed byung ba'i mdun ma dbu nas legs pa'i gnas ga la ba der zla ba
bcu pa'i bcu bdun mchod kyi nyan nas lam 'bras btsugs/ byang dgon tha dad nas 'dus pa'i dge 'dun bzhi brgya longs nges la bshad pa mtha' chod yang dag pa'i khur blangs
te nyin mtshan rgyun ma chad par gsung ngag rin po che nyid 'chad pa la chig dril du byas/ zur chos phran bu yang lam 'bras rang ma gtogs chos gzhan gyi rnam g.yengs rtsa
ba nas dor/ chos thun rgyun ring shing bshad lung babs chags pa'i ngang nas snang gsum legs par grub rjes/ sems bskyed la skye bo

dad can stong phrag tsam 'dus ba'i dbus su mar me gtso bor gyur pa'i mchod pa rgya chen po bshams/ sems bskyed kyi cho ga yang dag pa'i sgo nas der 'dus thams cad la thar pa'i
sa bon khyad par can skrun/ rgyu dbang yang chos brgyad dang 'brel ba'i dbang skrun don gnyer ma yin pa chos nyan pa sha stag la sbyangs gzhi sbyong byed legs par ngo
'phrod pa'i thabs mkhas kyi brda sbyor rang bzo dang ma 'dres par bgyis/ dbang skrun pa rnams la tshab zla ba gcig gi bar rnam rgyal 'joms kyis sna drangs/ dzaM la nor rgyun
mas mjug sten pa'i zur bka'i rjes gnang sum cu nyin re bzhin ma chag pa bsgrubs skabs/ dbu legs 'du khang du tshogs ma shong ba/ lha khang dang bla brang gi bar gyi
sa stong der byas pas brgyad brgya mi 'chad tsam byung/ de skabs tshogs chos kyi seng bar kun la/ dad pa can gyi sbyin bdag mtha' yas pa'i re ba skong ba'i tshe dbang/ kun
rig 'das pa lan dpag tu med pa chos ma grol bar de srid kho ra khor yug kho nar bgyid dgos pa byung zhing/ der tshogs thams cad kyis yi ge drug pa'i sgra rgyun mi 'chad
'grus pa'i dge ba brtan pa can gyis gzhi tshugs/ rang gzhan gyi sgo nas dung 'gyur len mi mang du byung ba/ snga phyi rnams sdom zhib rtsis byas pas brgya dang bcu gsum
lhag chad med pa 'grub 'dug pa la/ dung lnga kha skong du byas/ brgya rtsa brgyad po'i khas blangs grub pas yid gting nas bde/ der mchog dpal grogs mched glo bo nang du rkang
btsugs btang/ gser zho sum cu so gsum gyi ja shin tu bzang ba bsgrubs/ nged rang gi khar 'bru cig ma song ba byas/ srod

tho rangs dge 'dun tshogs pa'i steng nas nyi shu nyi shu la gsol ja grangs/ mi tshig mi 'dre'i ngag bcad kho na'i sher snying snga dgong gnyis ka lnga bcu nga 'dren re chag
med dang/ tshogs pa byin gyis mdo sum cu so 'dren thugs kyis longs pa kho na gnad nas/ bla ma dang dkon mchog gi thugs rjes der 'dus thams cad la so na ba cig kyang med
par chos mthar phyin pa'i chos kyi dga' ston la mang ja bsnyen bkur bzang ba'i steng der bzhugs kun la spyi 'gror zangs snod chung mtha' la yang nyag bcu las gtan mi chung
ba'i/ kha grangs brgya dgu bcu go lnga/ 'bras/ nas/ tshwa/ chu phye/ gos snam sogs dang/ dbu legs pa'i dgon bzhugs la dbyar gnas kyi dge rgyun la dmigs/ gser zho bcu bdun/
tshogs zangs che nges pa bzhi/ glo bo nang du mkhan rin po che'i gdung rten drung gser zho bcu gnyis/ byams gling du dbyar gnas kyi rgyur gser srang gang/ phu phag tu
bla ma rin po che'i mchod pa'i rten gser zho bcu gsum rnams phul ba bsngo bas rgyas thebs par byas nas/ nyin gcig ngal gso bsten te zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nyer gnyis la lo
chen drung du ma Ni dung phyur tshud pa'i bsngo ba zhu ba dang/ dus 'khor dbang brgyud sngar gsol ba btab pa nyid la rkang gtad/ gser zho sum cu so bdun gyi maNDal 'bul
rgyu khyer nas 'gro bar chas pa'i skabs/ drag zhan kun gyi da lo dgun so gsung chos babs can nyin mtshan med gnang/ gsol ba gtan ma song bas sku gzugs shin tu ngan par 'dug
pa/ da nam zla'i stabs ri klung thams cad gangs kyis chod pa 'di 'dra la phebs na sku tshe'i bar

chad du 'gyur nges pas/ lo chen pa la gser 'bul du rta pa gnyis sbrel dos chod brdzangs te/ re zhig sku ngal bsten/ sku mtshams dam pa rang gnang dgos zer/ tha dad nas gros
thon byed mi sha stag byung ba la gtan ma nyan par/ shi na yang de kas bsam pa rdzogs/ nga'i a ma drin can de la bzhugs dus sgyu lus kyi zhabs tog nyi ma gcig kyang ma 'grub/
dbyings su gshegs man dge ba 'dra byed blos byas kyang rgyu song gi sems tshim pa ma byung pa la/ da res zang zing gi dngos po cung zad dgra gnyen yongs kyi dpang thub
pa phyogs 'dir sbyin gtong gzigs gsal la phebs pa 'di yin cing/ gser gyi maNDal en tsam 'di/ da lta zhal bzhugs kyi bla ma rnams nas lo chen la nged rang gis yid brtas
par yod pas khong gi phyag tu thengs nas ma de'i don du bsngo bas rgyas thebs na snyam pa las/ 'dod pa log pa med/ dus 'khor sogs 'dod chos kun thob kyang sla/ ma thob
kyang ma la phan pa'i bya ba cig byung na snying des non byas mgo bsgril bas/ khong rnams kyang bden pa'i tshig des khrol/ don lo 'di nang du cis kyang phebs thub pa/ lo
chen drung man la mi phebs pa'i zhal bzhes gnang dgos ces mgrin gcig tu lab tu byung ba la/ spyir pha yul gyi phyogs 'dir sdod sa dang 'chi sa byed snyam pa med cing/ nga
rang la sa phyogs 'di lta bur 'gro don 'di 'dra yong/ mi tshe 'byed lugs 'di ltar bgyi gsung ba'i/ drung pa chos rjes lung bstan dngos dang rmi lam du 'khrul med byung ba'i
yid brtan yod/ 'on kyang kha ning labs pa bzhin brag steng sgrub phug tu shar ba'i rmi lam/ glo bo'i phyogs mtshams brgyad na

lcags kyi phur pa mi gang mda' tshad re 'gyel 'dug pas/ 'dzin pa'i yu ba shor ba'i mtshan ma gzigs gsal du nam phebs par skyes yul gyi sdug zhen la sdod rtsis yod/ da lo khyed
rnam pas bsam pa thag pas bsnyen bkur 'bul stegs yang dag pa la brten/ ma phyir du dge rtsa 'di rnams 'grub pa yin pas/ khrel ma srings na la yogs kyang yong/ nged zla
ba yang mi bcu bdun mchod pa'i nyi ma da lta nga rang 'gro ba'i grib tshod 'di rang la sleb nges byed smras pas/ bdag mos gtso mdzad thams cad de 'dra'i myur stabs rang
phebs thub pa dka' na'ang/ phebs pa zhal gyis bzhes pa rang gis bka' drin bskyangs/ da de ring nyi ma yang phyed 'dug/ rgongs phyogs gar yang mi phebs/ nang par snga bar
phebs pa drag/ gsol ja yang thon gyi yid zer ba'i tshig bsham rdzogs pa la/ gral der khag langs/'phral la zas 'tshol bya dang 'dra//gnas la nges med ri dwags 'dra//kag te
langs nas gzhi rdzogs pa'i//byar med 'di nyid kho bo'i gshis//byas lam sang phyin dus/ gzhung lam rnams kha bas chod/ ri brtsibs rang bskor nas byang rgyab la btol ste
nub dgon du sleb pas/ de na chos rje nub dgon pa'i dge rtsa'i dbu la bla ma rin po che mar lung pa spyan drangs 'dug pa/ khong pa rin po che rdo rje rgyal mtshan pa'i dngos
