dbang/ rta pod kyi pod lung rnams zhus/ gser zho gsum gyi maNDal phul zhing/ nged rang gis

kyang chos rje nub dgon pa/ chos rje chos skyabs dpal bzang pa dang chos rje mus sras pa vc: mus srad pa?zhang dbon gnyis kyi gtso mdzad/ 'ga' la de rin rnam sras rigs brgyad/
phyag rdor 'gro bzang/ dzaM la ser chen/ jaM la dmar po srog sgrub/ dzaM la 'brug zhon/ tshogs bdag chags pa rdo rje/ gnod sbyin a pa ra dzi ta sogs nor lha shin tu mang
ba'i byin rlabs rjes gnang rigs gtad rnams phul/ bla ma rin po ches gser zho gang/ rgya bum cig/ ras gon chen gcig rnams gnang ba dang/ chos rje nub dgon pas gser zho
drug/ chos rje mus srad pas src: mus sras pa?gser zho gang rnams gnang ba gcig ma blangs par bzhag nas/ slar yang bya dus btab snyeg pa ltar lam bsrangs phyin pas/ rtag
mkhar rdzong du sleb pa'i nub/ rmi lam na dar dkar po'i chas kyis klubs pa'i rta pa dkar po mdung dar dkar po khyer ba gnyis byung nas/ da lan ci nas kyang rgyal thang chu
bzang du phebs pa zhu zer ba'i ngang la gnyid sad/ wa brgyad cu'i la 'phrang la byas/ chu bzang gi dgon par rkang gtad phyin pas gnyag ston sangs rgyas kyi dus chen rang
dang thug/ bltad mo shin tu che bar byung/ de sku 'dra gser zhal ma dang/ mya ngan 'das sku gsung byon ma/ phyag rdor gyi sku gnam 'phur ma/ lha rgod rgyal thang gi zhal
'bag/ bla rdo/ srog 'khor sogs rten mjal zhib par bgyis nas bla ma pradznya bi dzA ya sku mched surya kirti gcung la gnyag ston sangs rgyas kyi rnam thar gyi pod lung/
lha rgyal thang gi srog gtad bka' bsgo mchod gzhung gi lung rnams nos/ gtor khang du gser pa thig zho long gcig rten du btsugs/ bsil ma zho gang mchod phran

du bgyis/ bla ma rnam pa la ka ra/ sman/ ras sngon yug gi 'bul ba sogs thugs mgu ba yang dag pa skyes te/ de nub sa mig tu nyal/ slar yang shin tu myur ba'i rtsol bas lam spyad
nas/ rta zla'i tshes bco lnga'i nub dpal ldan sman sdings su cog po phub nas nyal lo//de nas pha drung bsnyegs 'dod bu//don mthun bzhin du chas pa las//ngam ring zhes

kyang/ 'bul ba de bcu bdun bla ma'i dus chen rang la byung na snyam pa'i bsam pas gces su nyal/ gnas tshang ba rnams la khyed kyi phyogs 'di ni lo chen pa zer ba'i bla ma

thugs ni shin tu rtsub pa cig yod/ khong las kyang rtsub pa'i slob ma mnga' ris kyi sku drag pa yin zer ba cig na ning byon 'dug zer/ de skabs gsung chos mang po gnang
zer ba thos/ gzhan bug sgo bsdams sgrub pa rang la rtse gcig tu

bzhugs ces sleng slangs byung bas/ mnga' ris na yod zer ba'i rtsub po de nga ka yin/ 'di rnams cir 'dug byas/ gser rnams bstan nas dad pa la bkod de/ sang snga bar langs gtsang
kha nas g.yam leb mtho skor gcig maNDal du khyer nas sman sdings ri bo rgyas pa'i mgul bar 'dzegs te/ byin rlabs zil chen rgyas pa'i lo chen dang mjal 'phral/ rdo'i
maNDal gyi steng du gser zho sum cu so bdun bkod/ gang gi mchod rdzas ma'i gyer dang bcas phyag tu dengs par bgyis mtshams/ sngar yang yang du gsol ba btab cing yid la bcags
pa'i dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang rgyud 'grel man ngag dang bcas pa'i bka' drin yang skabs der nye bar thob te/ dus kyi 'khor lo'i sku gsung thugs yongs su rdzogs pa'i dkyil
'khor chen po'i zhal legs par phye nas/ byang sgor phung po khams kyi dri ma rags pa sbyangs nas sku rdo rje'i slad du chu dang cod pan gyi dbang/ lho sgor ngag gi dri
ma rags pa sbyangs te/ gsung rdo rje'i slad du dar dpyangs dang rdo rje dril bu'i dbang/ shar sgo yid kyi dri ma rags pa sbyangs te thugs rdo rje'i slad du brtul zhugs
dang ming gi dbang/ nub sgor 'pho ba'i dri ma rags pa sbyangs nas ye shes rdo rje'i slad du rjes gnang gi dbang 'dogs dang bcas pa ste byis pa 'jug pa'i dbang bdun stsal/
'og min gyi srid pa'i mthar thug pa 'jig rten pa'i dngos grub sgrub pa dang/ sems can thams cad kyi 'dren pa nyid kyis bsod nams dang ye shes kyi 'bras bu thob pa'i slad
du bdag gis lung bstan zhing/ rjes su gnang ngo zhes dus bsgo la mthar thug gi bar du legs par zhus nas/

slar lus kyi dkyil 'khor du gsang ba'i dbang/ kun rdzog byang chub sems kyi dkyil 'khor du shes rab ye shes kyi dbang dang 'jig rten pa'i bzhi pa/ don dam byang chub sems kyi
dkyil 'khor du jig rten las 'das pa'i dbang bzhi pa ste dbang bcu gnyis yongs su rdzogs pa dang/ gzhan don la lhag par mnga' bsgyur ba bdag po chen po'i dbang/ nges pa'i
bstan so so la bkod nas gong ma bzhi/ tshangs skud sogs sku gsung thugs kyi brda gsum byin pa nyid kyis rgyud ston pa po sogs su byed pa'i tshul rgyud 'grel las ji ltar
'byung ba'i cho ga dkyil 'khor gzhan gyis kha bskangs la cung zad kyang ma ltos par/ bdag slob ma'i nges pa dge slong gi rten gyis dbang las ye shes kyi phyag rgya la brten
te/ khyad par de dag dang ldan pa'i dbang bskur ba/ gang du shAkya seng ge mchog gi slob ma zla ba bzang po la sogs pa yongs su smin par mdzad pa'i bgyi ba ji lta yid
ches pa gsum dang ldan pa'i gdod ma'i rdo rje 'chang chen po'i gnas la bkod cing/ nam mkha'i rdo rje zhes brdar bzhag pa las rjes su rig pa'i mchog gi rdo rje bzhi'i rang
bzhin mgon po nyid kyis ma 'dres pa'i ye shes chen po'i ngo bor chub bzhin pa nyid du legs par khong du tshud nas/ ci byis pa'i slob dpon dag gis bcos ma'i dkyil 'khor
'ba' zhig tu brjod pa'i tshig tsam gyis sgra'i dbang bskur ba dang/ khyad par med pa nyid du ga la sems/ de'i phyir dbang bskur 'di lta bu thob pa las dkyil 'khor ma lus
par dbang bskur ba'i nges shes khyad par ba snying la skyes pa la yang the tshom gyis sbags

par ma gyur pa'i skal pa bzang po rjes su skyes pa'i mthar/ bsdus rgyud byang chub sems dpa'i 'grel pa skor gsum dang sbyar ba'i mtha' drug tshul bzhi ma lus pa phye ba'i ston
pa bzhi ldan gyi go ba'i 'tshang sgrib med du rtogs shing/ tsan dan dang tsan dan gyi dri ltar dbyer mi phyed pa'i rgyud 'grel gyi nges gnas nyid las byung ba'i sbyor
ba yan lag drug gi bsgom bya/ phyis 'byung gi bsre bslad sna tshogs su bsgyur ba'i tshong 'dus kyi 'o ma lta bu nyid dang 'dra bar mi spyod pa'i dbang bzhi pa'i don rang
gi de kho na nyid sngon du gyur nas de nyid gzhan la 'doms par mdzad pas/ zhal nas byung ba rna ba'i lam la brgyud/ gnyis su med pa'i ye shes gcig pu pa de'i ngo bor son
pa'i don rgyud snying la 'phos pa'i yid kyi re ba yongs su rdzogs par gyur te/sa la spyod pa'i 'og min gnas//sman sdings ri bo rgyas pa'i mgul//mgon po nyid kyi bsti gnas

mdzad pa'i khrid yig gi steng nas zhus/ snyan rgyud rdo rje'i tshig rkang/ tilli gzhung chung/ tilli pas gsungs pa'i bsam mi khyab gu'i do ha la lo chen nyid kyis mchan bu
gnang ba'i lung dang bcas/ mdor na mkhan chen rin po che chos grub seng ge la ji ltar gsan pa'i snyan rgyud rdzogs par thob cing/ lo chen nyid kyis sa bzang du mdzad pa'i
rim lnga'i khrid yig gi steng nas dmar khrid zung du sbyar ba'i gsang 'dus rim lnga/ kha che paN chen gyis sa paN la bstsal ba'i srol sal rdo rje'i nye lam gyi rlung sbyor
dmigs pa rnams la maNDal gser zho re re phul/ der nam zla'i stabs mar lam kyang sku 'o brgyal bar byung 'dug pas re zhig bzhugs pa gnang nas rgyud kyi lung sogs nged la
'dod chos 'ga' re dgos gsung nan bskyed dka' zhal lci bar phebs kyang/ tsan thabs su zhu phul te log nas gser zho gang gi me tog phul/ zhabs spyi bor blangs smon lam btab
te/ khas chad pa'i dus stengs su sleb la re'i blos bskul/ yar lam ngam rings su chos rgyal yab sras dang mjal ba tsam byas/ byang lam brgyud phyin pas lam kha ba che ba
sogs shin tu sbyong bar byung na'ang/ nyes skyon til tsam med par smras pa bzhin zla ba gnyis pa'i bcu bdun mchod pa'i nyin nyi tshod sor gang la snga phyi med par sleb/
dpyil bu de na mar 'gro dus pha ne ba gsum bsdad yod pa la/ bcu bdun nyin mchod pa gzobs la gshoms/ nga sleb gdong du ja me thongs pa gyis byas pa la/ pha nes yid gtan
byas/ bcu bdun gyi zhogs snga ba nas langs/ khang pa byi dor mchod gshom sogs byed pa'i skabs/ grogs rnams kyis khrel khrel byas/

da lo ri klungs med kha bas 'gags pa la tho na ngam ring tsam e phebs yin zer/ chos chod pa'i sgang ja dud bun tsam la sgo tsar sleb pa yin/ yar lam na yod pa'i 'brog pa rnams
kyis gser 'bul ba byung ba rnams la mig kyang ma bltas par rang dgar bzhag pas/ 'ga' res nan bskyed lag tu 'phangs byung dus slar kho rang la 'phangs/ de nas kyang lag
tu gtad byung ba kha phye ste dkon mchog mchod byas/ nam mkha' la gtor ba mang po byas pa'i gtam yongs na khyab yod cing/ dpyil bur sleb dus skol ja bzang ba nyeg drug
bdun tsam dang/ pha ne la byin rgyur gos cig ma gtogs/ dar kha gang ngam/ gser bse gcig med pa kun la gsal/ de nas dbu legs byams pa gling du zhag 'ga' ngal bsos te blo bo
vc: glo bonang du phyin/ de lo'ang sa ga'i dus chen la bsnyen bskur yang dag gi zhabs tog bgyis nas/ bar bong gi brag dmar chos sde'i lha khang gi rab gnas la 'bod mi rkang
btsugs byung bas phyin te rab gnas legs par bgyis/ der 'dus rnams la ni gu sogs 'dod chos kyi re ba rdzogs par byas skabs/ 'bul ba la byung ba'i zangs rnams lha khang
gi kun rar bsags pas mi gshong ba tsam zhig byung ba/ der 'tshogs pa'i dge 'dun rnams la ma'i don la ltos med du phul nas bsngo bas rgyas btab/ de dus dzo ki cig yod pa
snying ha las nas brgyal ba lta bu byung/ der dngos po so gcig ma 'dres pa byas nas slar log gnam stengs su bsdad/ dpyid sos nas dbyar smad bar sos dal cing bag phebs pa
rang byung dus der gong nas nam mkha' rin chen skyar skya rdzong du khri dmag dang bcas phebs byung ba'i phyag

phyir bkris/ shog gsung ba'i bka' stsal phebs byung na'ang/ char chu ches rkyen phran bu 'ga' la brten cung ma thon/ gong nas kyi chibs kha shar phyogs la bsgyur rjes/ rang
las kyi rtod phur ma'i mching ba ni grol/ gzhan ngo bsrung 'phreng cha ni shig tsam yang med pas/ lo chen dgongs dbyings sgrub pa dang/ bla ma 'ga' re dang mjal ba/ gnas
skor lhag ma rnams bgyid pa la zla ba dgu pa'i dgu mchod nyin dpon slob gsum gyis shar phyogs la yongs te/ thog mar rin chen dkon mchog dpal bzang pa'i drung dang mjal/
gser zho gang gi rnyed pa phul/ tshe rta bsgrags pa'i dbang bskur zhus/ phar yang grub rgyal ma'i tshe dbang zhig phul/ nub cig sa der nyal bas/ gsung las/ na ning nged rnam
pas phul ba'i gser ni gcig kyang ma bsnams/ da lo tshogs bsog byas pa'i rje drung rang gi sku skal yin gsung/ rten khabs bzang pa cig/ gser zho gsum/ phyag dril cig/
gsol dkar gcig rnams bstsal mtshams/ rim gyis brgyud nas ri bo che'i mdun du sleb pas/ rdo khral len mis mig thub byas/ nged dpon slob lnga la ras sngon bsgril ma gcig/ ting
shags cig/ dril bu gcig rnams sprad kyang gtong 'dod po rang ma byung ba'i lan/ yar lam bcwa ho zhus nas 'bru gcig kyang ma byin pas snying tshim par byung/ de nas ngam
rings chos kyi rgyal po'i mdun sar bde bar sleb/ rigs ldan mi'i dbang po yab sras/ dpon sa bdag chen ma yum sras rnams dang mjal te/ sman sdings su lo chen drung du sleb/
gser zho bcu gsum gyi maNDal/ bsil snyan bzang ba cig/ rgya bum gcig/

rten khebs zur bsgrigs sgo tshad ma gcig rnams phul/ nyi ma gsum zhabs drung du ngal bso bgyis te slar shar la 'ongs pas/ dpal rdor sngar shangs su khyung po'i bris thang chen
mo phal thog gnyis yod nges dang/ sor thog gi rgyud sde lnga'i bris thang thog tshad ma gnyis kyi dpe len la brdzangs pas/ mchog dpal rab rgyas grogs mched pas bzhengs
grub nas yar yongs pa dang phrad rjes khrag snar phyin pas/ rin po che 'phags chen dang mjal gser zho gsum gyi maNDal phul/ de dang slar log mon 'gro bsgrags par zhag bcu
bcag mal byas pa'i ring/ tshe dbang lha dgu/ sgyu lam/ lam zab phyi nang/ bla ma rin 'byung gi zhal shes khyad par can/ rigs lnga bla sgrub/ bir bsrungs rnal 'byor ma/
gces bsdus nas gsungs pa'i rtsa dbu ma lugs gnyis kyi dmigs pa/ mgon po lcam dral rnams zhus nas grwa tshang chen mor/ mes drang srong chen po'i drung du tshe dbang lha
dgu/ kun mkhyen chen po nam bsod pa'i bslab bya chen mo'i rtsa lung zhus/ nub gcig nyal bas dgyes pa rab kyi mthar phyin/ nged la khyed 'dra ba'i tsha bo 'byor pa shin tu
bzang na'ang/ bu dang tsha bo gnyis ka tsakra me'i 'khor lo thogs pa'i hur thum phaDa gnyis ka 'dug/ a pho rgan po'i gros la nyan na lo chen pas khrid bskyangs/ sku mdun
rgyud 'grel gyi bshad grwa zhig btsugs na/ nges don gyi bstan pa nyi ma shar ba lta bu'i bshad sgrub chu bo gnyis 'dus zhig yong ba 'dug ste/ sems can pa'i sku bsod la ci
srid dam gsung zhing thugs phab pa'i bslab bya bka' bkod du ma mdzad rjes/ o rgyan rdzong bar skyel mi gnang ba slar slog

nged rang dpon slob pas stag lung sna dkar du/ chos rje thogs med gsum pa'i drung du zhag gsum bsdad nas/ mthong smon du phyin/ thog mar pha rin po che trai bo dang mjal/ gser
srang gang gi phyag rten phul zhing/ dgyes pa'i zhal 'dzum yar ngo'i zla ba lta bu'i ngang nas/ bdag la khyed kyi yum brtse dungs can de thegs 'dug zer ba thos pas smon
lam yang dag par bgyis gsung ba'i bka' lung yid la 'bab pa lhug pa stsal/ rang yang sems ngo sprad pa'i drin can rje la yid brtas pa'i gus pas sngar bas kyang ches cher
'phel ba'i ngang nas karma pas sgar du 'bod mi gnang byung bas/ 'phral zhabs drung du phyin/ gser zho bdun maNDal du phul/ gdan gcig btings 'dug kyang sa brjen rang la
bsdad mtshams/ co 'dri mang du gnang gi 'dug pas/ de las 'ud che ba'i co 'dri mang ba zhig phul/ chos 'brel du ma Ni'i lung zhig zhus pas/ lus spyan ras gzigs su gsal ba/
ngag ma Nir gsal ba/ sems snying rjer gsal ba gyis gsung ba zhig thos/ sgar la sdod gsung ba'i bka' zhal du btab nas phyi phyag phul bas/ gser dngul las grub pa'i man skor
g.yu'i phra btab pa/ shin tu bzo khyad yod pa zhig gnang/ 'di'i nang na grub chen tilli pa nas kho bo'i yongs su 'dzin pa'i 'dren pa chen po sangs rgyas gnyan pa'i bar
gyi byin rlabs ma lus pa yod gsung ba'i bka' bstsal dngos su phebs/ de nas brtsed gdong du dpal sa skya pa ngag gi dbang po'i drung mjal ba la phyin/ gser zho gsum phyag
rten tu bgyis/ nged rang spyi 'gror 'jam dbyangs bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ chos rgyal ma'i lung

dang bcas pa/ gcig bu la tshe 'phel dkar po'i byin rlabs bka' 'grel du thugs rjes gzung zhing lam 'gor med par grwa thang gnas su sleb/ byams pa gling gi lha khang so so/ mchod
rten chen po/ tshogs byi rdzing pa'i phyag gi khyung po'i thugs sogs rten mjal zhib len byas/ rje dbon pad dkar ba la khong pa rang la phyag 'jal gser zho gang/ lo chen
rin po che'i drung gi dngul gdung gi dkar me gser zho gsum phul/ sgra mtshams sbyor tsam zhig btang nas slar log pha rin po che bsnyags mthong smon du sleb/ tshe rta
nag rgya phag gsum rnams kyi dbang bka'/ phag mo lha khrid/ ka dpe dang/ zab mo nang don rtsa 'grel gyi lung/ khyad par grub thob brgyad cu'i byin rlabs legs par thob pas/
bla ma grub thob de dag dang mjal yang/ gnang rgyu'i chos yi ge med pa snying po don gyi yas babs 'di nyid kho nar 'dug go snyam pa'i nges shes gting nas 'drongs/ der gser
zho gsum gyi maNDal/ mi dbang chos kyi rgyal po chen pos bstsal ba'i ja rduM/ dar yug/ spos chag/ kha btags rnams phul/ rje drung karma pa nyul rgyal khang na gdan chags
'dug pa'i drung/ kun spangs rin po che dang lhan du gser zho gang gi phyag rten khyer mjal du phyin pas/ byin dang mi mjal ba'i thugs dam ma grol gong zhabs drung du
'byor/ sngar dang mi 'dra bar bka' zhal 'grel chags yid la 'bab pa gnang zhing/ gsung chos 'dra'i bzhed yod kyang sngar gyi ma Ni'i lung de las ma thob/ mthong smon du sdod
rin zhabs drung kun spangs pas gtso mdzad/ mched po rnams dang/ sde pa'i gsol gzims/ sprul sku sman thang pa sogs du ma la

rgyud 'grel gyi lung/ skyes rab nang stag rgyud gsum gyi lung/ mchog mi 'gyur gyi bshad pa/ tshe dbang brgya rtsa lan grangs du ma/ rta mgrin yang gsang khros pa'i dbang/ beg
gdong gi rjes gnang/ gying lnga gza' gdong lcam dral gyi srog dbang/ bde mchog ldu vc: lU?dril nag gsum gyi dbang/ mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs sogs zur chos/ pha rin po
che'i thugs dam ma grol bar du 'jur bar bgyis te/ bka' 'grol zhus/ stag lung nas 'bod mi dang lhan du sna dkar du sleb/ zhag bco lnga tsam gyi ring nyin mtshan ngo mi shes
pa'i chos 'chad/ gtso bor rgyal sras chos rdzong pa nas brgyud pa'i bsnyung gnas dang/ blo sbyong bka' babs bzhi ldan nyid tshogs chos su bgyis/ zur du drung ras chen
pas gtso mdzad la grub thob brgyad bcu'i byin rlabs kyis mtshon pa'i dbang lung grangs las 'das pa/ nai gu'i mgyogs khrid bzlas pa tshar bdun tsam bgyis/ ne ser du drung
sher phyin ma la kar lugs gyi phag mo lha lnga'i dbang chos 'grel du phul zhing/ bdag gis kyang de nyid ka bka' 'grel du zhus/ bsam grub rtser pha rin po che'i zhabs la
btud bcag mal bgyis nas/ dpal snar thang gi mes dbon rnams dang mjal/ bde mchog nag po pa dbang 'ga' phul mtshams/ e waM du phyin chos rje gdan sa pa'i drung du/ bka'i 'grel
par bla ma gong ma'i dbang khang der tshe dbang lha dgu ma zhig zhus/ dar kha chen sum cu lhag tsam/ ras yug kha bco brgyad yod pa gcig gi sna drangs/ ras yug drug/ phyag
gser zho gang rnams phul/ dge sdings su dpal sa skya pa gzhi thog pa'i drung du tshe dbang lha dgu'i bka'

'grel zhus/ rin po che 'phags chen pa yang dag gdan chags 'dug pa la mgon po'i nang khrid/ chos rje spyan tshab pas zin bris mdzad pa de'i lung dang/ dkar bdud kyi rjes snang
vc: gnang tsam thob/ dpon slob gnyis ka'i drung gser zho re'i maNDal yang phul/ gdung brgyud rin po che'i zhabs drung nas shin tu thugs 'dre ba'i bka' drin bstsal zhing/
slar myur du 'khor shog gsung ba dang/ zhal mkhyen gyi rnam pas/ spos shel las grub pa'i thub pa'i sku gcig dang/ kha che/ gur gum/ khyi la wa ri khungs ma/ gzhan dzo
ki'i sman khyad par can ne tso dang bcas pa bsnams phebs dgos gsung/ mnyes mnyes dpag med mdzad cing/ slar bo dong e'i chos grwa mjal/ sa lung du phyin/ mkhan chen rin po
ches gtso mdzad/ zhal ngo rnams la tshe rta bsgrags ma'i dbang phul ba'i nub/ smyon med du rta mgo shin du gsal ba me long gi gzugs brnyan lta bu'i mtshan ma bzang po byung/
de mtshams dpal ldan 'bras spungs kyi dgon par paN chen rin po che'i drung du bsnyegs/ thogs mar tshe dbang rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor la brten pa'i dus kyi 'khor lo'i
dbang rdzogs pa/ 'khor lo sdom chen ras bris ma/ rdo rje shugs kyi rjes gnang/ khyung 'dra'i bsgom lung/ chos kyi rgyal po rnam rgyal grags bzang gis mdzad pa'i yig lung
mtha' dag zhu ba la zla phyed bsdad/ gser zho gang gi maNDal mtshon don du byas/ de las gzhan bka' dbang re re bzhin gos dar gan spos/ ras yug sogs 'bul ba sna ma chad
tsam phul/ bco lnga'i nyin dbang gi dngos gzhi thob pa'i nub gza' 'dzin ma grol bar/ khyung

'dra'i bzlas pa brtse vc: rtsegcig tu byas nas/ slar sman sdings ri bo rgyas pa'i mgul du phyin/ lo chen drung gis dgongs pa ltar rgyud lung dang ni gu'i dbu btsugs/ lhun sdings
kyi bar zhag bzhi bcu tsam gyi ring la/ ni gu'i dbang bka' nyer lnga/ spyan ras gzigs 'gro 'dul sogs bka' dbang mang bar phul/ nged rang gis dus 'khor dang/ gsang 'dus
kyi cho ga'i lhag/ rgya gzhung tha dad kyi lung/ sgron gsal gyi rgyan bdun sogs la zhib bshad/ grol thig/ yi ge bzhi pa/ khrid kha brgya rtsa'i kha bskongs bkra shis
grangs kyi mtha' bsten ming bkra bzang bar 'dug pas/ sems khrid yid bzhin nor bu zhus te/ 'di nyid lo chen drung gis bsgom gsan pa'i thog ma rang yin gsung ngo//dgon gsar
bla ma rtogs ldan pa nas/ snyan rgyud bde mchog gi dkyil thang dbang tsam g.yar nas/ dbang bka' rnams legs par thob pas/ sngar gyi ras chung snyan brgyud kha tshang ba'i
yid bde skyes/ zhu ban spyan gcig pa las bkra dum pa'i pha chos/ gzhan du btsal bas gtan ma rnyed pa'i rta mgrin dregs pa'i dbang lung/ tsaNDa'i srog dbang yang gnas de
kar zhus/ skabs der zla gcig la gdan gcig las ma g.yos pa'i tshogs 'khor bzhi bcu zhe lnga byung zhing chos bro dang mgur mas gzigs khang 'degs pa 'dra ba rgyun mar mdzad
kyang/ tshogs lhag gtong rgyu ni cher ma byung/ de rjes byin rlabs zil chen rgyas pa'i lo chen bka' drin 'khor med des/ brtse ba'i spyan chab g.yo ba dang bcas pa'i skyel
thung gnang/ zhabs dbang bdag gi skal bas bkar te thob pa'i las 'phro mi 'dug pa nas/ zhabs 'og gi sa brdul

cung zad mgo la bzhag/ lhag par 'khreng bzhin du/ 'phrabs byung du 'bod mi rkang gtad nan bskyed byung nas/ 'gro mi 'dod bzhin du phyin pas/ mgron gyis ma 'tsheng pa'i/ yar
lam gyi bskol ja la dmigs pa'i ja rdum che ba rang cig yod pa de bor/ des ma chog par sgro btags kyi ku cos lung pa bkangs/ des ma khegs par sdug gshis ngan par thag bcad
nas sku chags gang yod thams cad dus lan gcig la btol ba zhig byung/ de nub pho brang mjal nas khang gsar gyi bar spel nyal te/ rngod la brgyud nas/ rigs ldan chos kyi
rgyal po yab sras kyi drung du/ nges don rgya mtsho'i dbu zhabs ma lus pa la re re nas dris mal gnang ba'i lan/ rang blos gang spobs gsol rting ma'i ring la rdzogs par zhus
shing/ drung jo gdan pas dbu mdzad/ gong gi gsol gzims rags bsdus la bka' bzhin 'dod chos mang bar bgyis shing/ thub chen rab gnas sogs legs tshogs rgya cher spel ba'i
gnang sbyin/ dkar yol/ spos chag/ gser rnams lo chen drung 'bul mi brdzangs/ thub pa la dar yug gcig dang/ kha bcu bzhi dus 'khor la snyan dar phul rjes/ rgyu gzer chab
zhugs kyi phyag phyir bkris/ kun dril yab sras drung du zla gcig tsam bsdad nas skye yul la phyin pas/ sngar bshad pa'i rmi lam gyi mtshan ma bslu ba med pa bden don mngon
sum du gzigs gsal phebs 'dug cing/ rgyu gzer zlos gar gyi bstan bcos spel ba de/ ma 'ongs lung bstan du bsam shes kyis dpyad na mtshon pa zhig byung 'dug der zla ba dgu'i
ring rgyud man ngag bsgrags pa'i chos 'chad dang/ dbyar

rings ni gu bzlas pa lan bcu bdun tsam mi rtag skyo shas kyis bskul nas rang gzhan kun la smin par bgyis/ brag stengs su mtshams zhag bdun ma'i spyad cha shin tu dam pa'i ring/
sngar rang lo nyer gnyis pa la/ gnas de nyid du rnam sras rta bdag brgyad kyi mtshan ma gsal por mthong ba'i dus/ g.yon phyogs kyi stengs thad la 'dug pa'i gnod sbyin
a pa ra dzi ta'i gzugs shin du gsal ba rab kyi mthar phyin pa cig ja phor la byung ba yongs kyi mig lam la phebs/ slar log nas yongs dus rgyal thang chu bzangs su gtor
gsos rgyas pa/ snyan dar gser mchod rnams brdzangs/ zu lung du sngags gzhon gcig la gsol mchod kyi lag len bslabs shing spos shel sogs ster sbyin yang dag byas nas ngam rings
la brgyud/ dgun tsha'i jo bo'i drung na lo chen dpon slob bka' gyur ro cog gzigs tog gnang ba'i drung du sleb/ gser bsrang gang/ dar kha gsum sbrel/ do sbral/ kha rkyang
re re nged rang dpon slob kun gyis so so nas phyag mjal du bgyis nas dgon sar du paN chen rin po che'i drung yang mjal mtshams/ dpal ldan sa skyar gdung brgyud rin po
che'i thugs bzhed/ spos shel gyi thub pa/ dzo ki rdzas sna tshang/ gur gum/ ne tso sogs dgongs pa la 'byor pa'i dgyes pa bskyed/ spyir rten mjal che longs dang/ khyad par
rje btsun rin po che'i sku 'dra mdze thod ma la dgos pa'i khyad par gyis rten 'brel gyis dbang las snyan dar rnam lnga/ spos chag ma'i maNDal/ sgo rngum gyi mgon po'i
drung du snyan dar kha yig 'byar ba bcu gsum/ gser gyi mchod phran/ dge 'dun bcu phrag lhag pa'i gtor sgrub dang bcas phrin

las zhus/ de skabs bzhi thog tu gdung brgyud rin po che'i thugs dam bde mchog brgyud pa'i bris sku gzab bris rnams bzhugs pa'i sgam de'i kha 'byed mdzad/ drung pa rang gi phyag
gi gang zin cig thog mar gzigs pa zhu/ rten 'brel zhig blta gsung/ gcig blangs zhal phye bas nag po spyod pa'i sku byung ba/ thugs mtshar mtshar gnang gi 'dug/ dus der
bla brang shar du tshe dbang sogs yum sras lhan du phul/ phyag na yod pa'i bla ma gnam kha'u pa'i zhal gzigs kyi bris sku'i drung du bskang gso nub gcig byas/ ngor du
'gro mi 'dra 'dug pa la gser gyi yang chung zho gsum 'khor ba cig/ g.yu zho brgyad ri ba/ dar yug gcig rnams dang/ rin po che lha mchog seng ge'i drung gi nang rten la dkar
me'i thes dang/ ja shin tu bzang ba khal phyed dgu mchod la dmigs nas phul/ khro phu byams chen drung mar mi khur theg tshad gnyis kyi dkar me yang dag pa phul te lam
bsrangs/ de mtshams dben gnas dam pa na bza' brag phug tu sleb/ bde mchog lu dril nag gsum gyi dbang dang/ ni gu'i mgyogs khrid sogs bgyis shing/ gnas der snar thang nas
mes dbon drung gis 'bod mi rkang gtad nang byung bas dgongs pa bzhin 'ongs nas/ ni gu'i khrid sogs thugs kyi re ba skong ba'i legs lam rang gis ci shes bsgrubs/ byams pa'i
sku sogs la snyan dar yang mang bar phul nas/ khri khang du phyin/ tshe dbang brgya rtsas gtso byas pa'i dbang lung gi dgongs len gang yod byas/ 'phags pa'i sku 'dra phyag
nas ma la dar yug dmar po kha bcu drug yod pa/ ri phug gi bu ston rin po che'i gzim mal sku 'dra la snyan

dar kha grangs mang nges pa thes 'byar/ zha lu'i thugs rje chen po la snyan dar bkra shis kha btags dkar po zung dang/ dkar me spos 'bul rnams so sor bsgrubs rjes/ kun spangs
rin po che'i drung dang kha ru brag tu mjal/ pha rin po che'i drung du 'bul rgyu'i gser zho bdun gyi maNDal phyag tu bzhag nas dbus la lam bsrangs/ yar phyogs su zhag
'ga' bsdad rjes/ lha sar jo bo'i drung du snyan dar/ sngon gyi dar chen sman tshe kha chen bcu drug sbrel ba'i yug sne tshang/ jo bo bcu gcig zhal sogs la yang snyan dar
ma chad pa phul nas mda' skor byas/ glang thang du spyan snga rin po che'i drung du sleb/ gos chen ne ser kha sbrel/ gser zho gang rnams phyag rten du phul bas/ gson gshin
phrad pa lta bu'i yid bde yang 'di la zer gsung lhag par mnyes pa'i bka' zhal lhug par bstsal rjes/ na lendrar bdag chen chos kyi rje che ba'i drung du phyin/ gos lu haM
kha sbrel dang gser zho gang gi phyag mjal bgyis/ tshe dbang lha dgu ma cig gi bka' 'grel zhus/ thugs lhag par dgyes dgyes gnang zhing/ slar dkar yol/ dar yug ljang khu/
spos chag/ kha btags kyi gnang sbyin bstsal ba rnams spyan snga'i drung du phul zhing/ g.yas ru byang nas gnang ba'i gsol ja dpe bral de'i lhag nyeg bco lnga yang phul
bas/ phyis 'di las bzang ba'i ja ma myong gsung/ de nas spyang lung chos sdings su phyin/ rin po che'i drung du thog ma'i mjal rten bkra shis kha btags/ li sug/ ghi wang/
tsan dan dkar dmar/ gu gul/ se 'bru sogs bzang sman ka to ra gang/ srab chen gyi sku thabs shin du legs pa/ gser zho gang

rnams phul nas mjal nyin nas/ bdag rang gcig pu la lam 'bras 'dzugs pa gnang/ thog mar tshe dbang lha dgu zhig thob/ snang gsum skabs bsags sbyangs la rwa bsgreng skor du phyin/
ras mi khur gcig bshags nas dar cog/ dar thag/ jo bo 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i dngul gdungs che chung gnyis sogs la snyan dar so sor btags/ zhag gsum bsdad nas stag lung
thel gyi yang dben du 'ongs/ rten mjal zhib por byas/ chos rje sku mched drung du bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang yi ge drug ma'i lung zhus/ tshogs pa byin la rang rang gi bzhed
pa'i chos nyin mtshan rgyun mi chad par byas/ zhag bco lnga tsam la slar spyang lung gi dgon par sleb/ rin po che'i drung du kha btags ser khra bcu bdun/ dar yug ljang khu/
dkar yol bcu bdun rnams phul nas sngags lam rdzogs par nyan/ gzhan 'chag med rnams dang mgon po'i bka' sogs sngar ma thob pa ni gcig kyang ma byung yang/ paN chen rin
po che brgyud pa la yod pa'i 'dod chos yid tshims par mnos pa'i mthar/ stag lung du sprul pa'i sku dbon rin po che sku mched kyi rab byung bsnyen rdzogs kyi phyag phyir
bka' nan che ba'i 'bod mi byung nas skyar te phyin/ zla phyed tsam bsdad rin/ nyin rangs pa tshogs pa spyi'i dbang bka' rjes gnang kho nas sbrel/ mtshan mo mtshan ma phyed
par sprul pa'i sku nyid la ni gu'i dbang khrid/ thugs dam lha lnga/ dam can dregs drug/ 'jigs byed zhe dgu ma sogs dbang bka' byin rlabs rnam grangs mang ba/ khrid brgya'i
rkang grangs rdzogs tsam yang chos bdag po'i dper 'dug pas phul/ thugs rjes lhag par

bskyangs shing/ khong pa spyang lung pa chen po gzhon nu blo gros kyi sku skye zol dang brjod 'dogs min pa'i nges can du 'dug pa de'i byin rlabs yin pa 'dra/ de skabs nub gcig
stag lung mchod khang gi phyag bzhi pa dngul sku thog tshad ma de'i drung na lam dus zhig len pa'i ngang la/ dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i snang
ba shin tu gsal ba lha tshogs ma lus pa gcig gis gcig ma bsgribs pa mthong ba dri med khyad par can dang/ dpal sha wa ra yin snyam pa'i a tsa ra nag po hur bag can gcig dbang
gis brda sprad pa'i yid ches som nyi med par byung na'ang/ mchog gi sprul pa'i sku de nyid kyi thugs rje yin snyam pa'i gus pa kha tsam min par skyes so//der zla ba
bdun pa'i tshes bcu gcig la rje sku mched gnyis ka'i dge tshul gnang ba'i slob dpon dang/ bcu gnyis nyin rje drung dbon rin po che'i zhal snga nas bsnyen rdzogs mdzad pa'i
phyag phyi bsgrubs/ der byung ba'i rnyed pa rnams bdag chen chos kyi rje dpal ngag gi dbang po'i drung du/ dar kha brgya dgu cu go drug dkar yol bco brgyad/ spos chag bcu
khres bzhi rnams phul/ tshe dbang lha dgu ma zhig dang/ lha lnga ma cig zhus/ bsnyen rdzogs kyi las brjod pa tshar 'phral/ 'dod yon gang la yang ma zhen par/ de'i nyin
rang yong/ de nub 'jigs skyobs dgon par nyal/ sang spyang lung du sleb 'phral rin po che'i drung du/ dar chen dpus bsdus bgyis pa'i mdog tha dad pa mda' tshad nyer lnga/
ja dmar 'don kha lnga/ dkar yol shin tu legs pa bdun phul/ glang thang du 'bring dar kha grangs bzhi bcu zhe dgu 'bul du btang nas/ yer pa

dang jo mjal byas te rgyal chen gling gi pho brang ga la ba der phyin/ sde ba sku mched drung gi gtso mdzad la zab lam rdo rje'i rnal 'byor zhib pa gcig dang/ yum rin po che'i
phyag phyir lha lcam bkra shis pa la/ sgrol ma dkar mo'i tshe khrid gyis mtshon pa'i dbang lung mang du spel/ 'bral bar mi spobs pa'i thugs brtse bas bdag gir mdzad cing/
mkhan chen rin po che'i drung du tshe dpag med lha dgu ma'i tshe dbang zhus/ rnam sras dkar po'i tshe bsgrub slar phul nas/ sngar gyi gsal gnang de la sgro bskur spangs
pa'i phyir/ gong dkar du mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang zhu la cag mal zhag drug bgyis nas/ dpal sde la byas 'ongs pa'i lam rong rtse gsum du/ bya ba sprul sku rin po
che dang mjal te/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi bka' 'grel zhus/ rong gra smug tu gcung rin po che'i drung mjal ba la phyin/ spos shel lag rtse skor cig phul/ rgyal dbang bka'
'bum la bka' gtad gnang zhing/ de nub rje btsun rin mo vc: poche dang/ lcam sring drung gis gtso mdzad dpon slob drag bsdus bdun tsam la sgra mi snyan pa'i tshe sgrub/ mkha'
'gro ma dud pas sol ba'i rjes gnang yang bka' ma bzlog par phul rjes/ pho brang chen po gzhis ka rin chen spungs pa'i rtser/ mi dbang chos kyi rgyal po yab sras dang
mjal bas bka' drin yang dag pa'i thugs rjes gzung zhing/ rwa lnga rtser sde pa rgyal bu'i drung dang mjal/ rje rin po che rgya mkhar chos rdzong pa'i drung la tshe dpag med
lha mangs kyi dbang bskur zhus te/ dpal lhun sdings kyi mdun par bde bar phyin/ rigs ldan 'jam pa'i dbyangs dang/ lha sras padma dkar po'i spyan sngar phyin/ bde dgye

gsang gsum/ tshe dbang rigs bdun sogs blo lhag med pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi'i rnyed pa bsab par dka' ba'i bka' drin chen po'i bka' 'gog par ma nus pas/ rje btsun ma thugs rje'i
bdag mo'i drung dang lhan cig mi spobs bzhin du phul nas sman sdings bcu bdun mchod pa la ga Na tsakra'i pU dza btabs te phyir log/ chos grwa chen por rkang gtad nas
yongs/ chos du ma'i khar spel ba'i skabs/ sngar rgya sgom chen po'i dngos grub kyi pha phogs yong gsung bas de nyid yin nam snyam pa'i sku gdung yid bzhin gyi nor bu ring
bsrel gyi byur bur bstams shing/ dung g.yas 'khyil gyis rgyan pa'i byin rlabs rang babs su/ ni gu'i mgyogs khrid dngos bstan rang gis grangs su bgyis pa'i brgya dang lnga'i
thog tu phebs byung mod kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes gzigs pa mi log pas brgya rtsa brgyad song ba yin nam snyam zhing/ sngar rgya sgom rin po che dang ma mjal gong
gi ni gu rnam grangs su bgyis na/ grangs kyis gzhal bar mi nus pa lta bu yod la/ zab khrid anggi bzhag pa 'di rnams kyang/ dper na lam 'bras brgyud lugs mi 'dra ba nyer lnga
thob pa la/ zha ma lugs gud du phyungs/ nyer bzhi gcig tu bgyis pa dang/ ni gu lugs srol mi 'dra ba nyer lnga thob pa la/ thang stong ba'i lugs ma gtogs/ grangs gzhan
nyer gcig tu sdoms pa/ blo sbyong lugs bsrol mi 'dra ba lnga bcu tsam yang don bdun ma'i rgyas 'grel dpal yes ma dang/ legs bshad rgyan gnyis tsam du 'gril ba ltar/ rang
gi kha yod lag yod du da lata nam dgos blo nas 'chad thub pa'i dbang du byas nas brgya rtsa brgyad du ming smos pa go dgos

so// zhes bya ba 'di re zhig dbri bsnan med par yongs su grub pa'o//rab sbyang gzhung lugs kun gyi gnad don rig//mi mthun brtsod pa'i dbyangs rnams brag char go//gcig pur 'dug
kyang dga' ba'i ca co shor//sems kyi mdud grol mchog de 'di skad gleng//mang thos kun rtog bsam byung 'od brgya ba//rta bdun rkyen gyis gzhan dbang gling bzhir drangs//bcu
gnyis dga' ma'i khyim du bsgom pa'i mal//grol ba mchog gi gnas la dga' mgur bsten//kun gsal lang tshos rab dregs lus phra ma//gre 'gyur bye ba'i snyan ngag rgyud mang
sgras//mkhas rnams snying la dpyid kyi dga' ston chad//sna tshogs rang grol mchog la sbyor shes mod//deng dus byis pa kun la yul gyi skad//phal pa'i nga ros dga' ba bskyed
byed pa//rigs pa min la snang blo g.yo ba'i tshul//gnas 'dir grol mchog lhag par ngo mtshar gyur//sngon byon mkhas kun rig gnas gzhung brgya yi//dpag bsam lo ma'i dga'
ston chags nas//grub mchog rnams kyang don bzang 'bras bu yis//rang grol bcud len mchog la yid rton gyur//kyi hud gnyis 'thung dbang po'i kun spyod la//ma sbyangs ba lang
dga' ba gang la skye//ming tsam mtshungs kyang rang bzhin tha dad ces//grol mchog som nyi spangs te 'di skad smra//dpal ldan mkhas kun dga' ba'i bdud rtsi ni//rang grol
bsam pa'i bsnyim pas legs mnos te//gsung rab mchog la mi 'jigs spobs pa can//blo gsal rgya mtsho'i sde yis rnam par bkod//e ma kun rtog zhing sa la//nye bar 'khrungs

pa'i dga' bskyed gtam//bcings pa grol ltar don mtshon pa'i//mchog tu skal bzang bsti gnas nyid//'di na kun rtog me long la//rang dga'i bag chags gzugs brnyan tsam//'dzin pa
rang grol shar ba'i tshe//mchog dman yongs la gsal bar smras//cung zad bzlos par smos pa rnams//blo gros dman pas go phyir te//shin tu blun ngor brjod pa na//smra po ba
lang mtshon pa nyid//de skad brjod 'di snyoms las kyi//'dam byings gyur kyang dbang med du//bskul byed mang po'i nan tshig ngor//sdebs la mkhas rnams bzod par bzhes//'dir
'bad las byung dge ba'i cha//kun dga'i yid ches las skyes pas//'gro ba smin grol lam 'god pa'i//ded dpon mchog tu bdag gyur cig//ces pa 'di ni bod yul stod kyi cha// mnga'
ris kyi rgyud du byung ba'i dge slong thos pa 'dzin pa dpal ldan kun dga' grol mchog blo gsal rgya mtsho'i sde ces bya bas// bstan pa la dga' ba'i lha rnams kyis mngon
par bsrungs pas phyir rgol gzhan gyis klags blta bar dka' ba'i ljongs/ mi 'jigs pa skyabs kyis sbyin pas bde bar tsho ba'i zhing/ zong 'dod dgu 'byung ba'i tshong 'dus/
dpal khri gang gi yang rtse rnam par rgyal ba'i khang bzang mthon por sbyar ba las/ slar yang bsod nams chen po'i dpal gyis mngon par mtho ba'i mi dbang yab sras kyi bkas/
lhag ma lus pa'i gnas 'doms pa zhig ci nas kyang spel zhing nyer len gyi legs tshogs mtha' dag yang yang du bskul 'debs nan gyis mdzad de yongs su rdzogs par/ dpal snar
thang gi chos grwa chen po/ nag pa zla ba'i tshes gcig la grub pa'i yi ge pa ni/ shra dhaM pradznya ma ti dzo ki tsarya se na ces bya bas mos shing gus pa'i blos bgyis pa
phyogs dus thams cad du dge legs kyi rgyur gyur cig// //rnam thar skal bzang dad pa'i shing rta 'dren byed kyi 'phros zur 'debs mdzes rgyan/

shre ya se tu/dpal gyi 'byung gnas yid ches ldan pa'i rje//grol ba mchog gi thar lam ston mkhas pa//blo gsal rgya mtsho'i sde yi gtsug gi rgyan//brgyud ldan bla ma'i tshogs
la phyag bgyi'o//'di ltar lo zla'i zol gyis khrid pa'i mthar//skra dkar lcags kyu'i mtshon chas nyer bzung nas//lang tsho yol ba'i rgan po'i rang bzhin la//ngang gis 'jug
pa 'di ko ngo mtshar rmad//gzhon nu'i rang bzhin byis pa'i rang nyams kyis//chos brgyad zol la brten pa'i sgeg chos las//ring du son pa'i mang thos drang srong bdag//chag
med bas mtha'i gnas la yid rab 'phyo//brjod pa'i tshig gi dbu bas mi ngoms shing//thos pa'i mig dkyus g.yo ba'i yid drangs nas//tha snyad rtog pa'i lam la bgrod pa yi//ngal
ba 'di ko rang myong blun po'i gshis//don gyi khu bcud snying gi bum bzang du//nye bar len pa'i skal bzang grogs po dag//tshig gi na yar spyod pa'i sems bor

la//don bzhin 'doms la snying nas yid ches byos//e ma dam chos rin po che//bsams bzhin dka' bar ston pa'i tshul//mthar thug rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas nyid//ji ltar rnyed snyam
so nyer spyod//thos pa las gzhan lam med cing//bdag ni thos pa'i khur gyis bcings//thos bral mu cor smra ba ni//snying nas spyod par ma nus grang//bstan pa las lhag bkur
bsti'i gnas//gzhan du rdul tsam ma dmigs tshe//de nyid 'dzin dang spel ba'i phyir//thos pas mi ngoms nyid du gyur//thos bsgom spel mar bgyid pa'i sems//yid gnyis 'phyang
mor spyod na ko//dben gnas ri bo'i khrod nyid du//gnyug ma'i rang zhal blta bar smon//blta yul mthong bya'i gnas min pa'i//khyab gdal gnyug ma'i de nyid ni//grong dang
dben pa'i gnas dag tu'ang//ro mnyam nyid phyir 'bad pas ci//bdag blo thos pa'i bang mdzod 'dir//dbang lung gdams pa'i rin chen dag//dad pa'i zong gis nyer thob pa'i//gnas
tshul cha tsam yi ger spel//de yang rang gi las snang gi kun rtog ji lta ba'i gnas tshul sgrib med du bris pa'i yi ge snga ma de nyid dang rjes su 'brel ba'i brjod pa'i
sgor gyur ba yang/ rgya sgom sbas pa'i rnal 'byor bas dngos grub kyi pha phogs 'byung bar lung bstan pa'i gnas don mngon sum du mthong ba'i skabs/ yid bde mar ngo 'phel ba'i
ngang nas/ mi 'jigs pa skyabs kyis bde bar 'tsho ba'i zhing dpal khri khang gi yang rtse rnam par rgyal ba'i pho brang mthon por mi dbang yab sras kyi drung du/ paN chen
nags kyi rin chen nas brgyud pa'i tshe 'dzin

dkar po rgyal ba 'od snang gi byin rlabs chos kyi sgo 'byed sngon du 'gro ba can gyi padma tshe dpag med kyi 'chi med gnyug ma'i gzhung lam khyad par can la/ yi ge cha re re
nas dris mal gyis thugs kyi the tshom ma lus pa bsal te yid ches rnyed pa'i phyag khrid mdzub tshugs su phul mthar/ dpal shA wa ra 'chi med nas brgyud pa'i zab lam rdo
rje'i rnal 'byor rgya gar paN chen nags kyi rin chen gyi khyad chos de nyid kyi zhal lung chos rje chos kyi grags pa'i yig ris su mdzad pa'i dngos bstan las brtsams te/ rang
gi rgyud kyis bsdus pa'i myong ba cung zad kyi rjes su brgyan te zhib rgyas su phul bas/ rnam par dpyod pa'i mkhyen dgongs zhib mor 'byed pa'i dgongs pa'i dbyings su
yongs su byor zhing/ dad pa gsum stobs su gyur pa'i skal ba bzang po'i gnas bdag gir mdzad/ de las gzhan snga gong sa skya'i lo tsa ba chen po 'jam dbyangs gsar ma'i zhabs
kyi padmor mngon par dbang bskur phyin ci ma log par gsan pa'i dpal sdom pa rab 'jigs he ru ka bong bu'i zhal can gyi rdzogs rim phra thig gi rnal 'byor nai pA la'i paNDi
ta ma hA bo dhi nyid kyi thugs bcud nges brjod kyi rgyud bla na ma mchis pa de nyid dang/ tshe dbang brgya rtsa/ bde mchog lU i zhabs kyi dbang/ grub pa'i rgyal mo lha
mangs/ ye shes mgon po phyag bzhi pa'i bkas bsgo rjes gnang sogs 'bul ba'i skabs nyid du/ sngar smos pa'i rtogs brjod kyi rgya cher bshad pa nyid kyang bka' bskul nas legs
par sbyar zhing/ mtha' rgyas kyi bgyi ba cung zad dpal snar thang gi chos grwa chen po nyid du zhabs thogs par bgyi ba'i skabs/ chos grwa chen po de nyid na

bzhugs pa'i sa dge gnyis ka'i 'dus pa'i tshogs lhan cig pa'i dbus su bka' gdams glegs bam pha chos bu chos/ de dag dang 'brel ba'i thig le bcu drug gi dbang/ thig le'i bsgom
khrid rnams bshad pa 'doms che rang blos ci shes bla chos min pa bstan pa'i rgyun la bsal nas zhib rgyas su phul mthar/ dU ti'i 'bod mis yang yang bskul ba'i dbang las/
shul lam bde bar gting skyes mkhar chen du son zhing/ gnas de nyid du brag dkar nas mkhan chen rin po che spyan drangs nas/1mngon par rtogs pa'i rgyan 'grel pa dang bcas
pa'i dka' 'grel bzhed tshul rgya mtsho'i rlabs phreng/2lus dang yang lag rgyas par bshad pa lung don rgya mtsho/3sbyor Tika gnad kyi sgron ma/4rgyan gyi 'grel bshad 'jug
sgo gsum pa lung rig rol mtsho/5lung gi snying po/6mtshon byed dpe'i dge 'dun gyi zur 'debs ngag gi dbang po'i mdzes rgyan/7bsam gzugs kyi zur 'debs ngag gi dbang po'i do
shal/8rten 'brel gyi zur 'debs srid zhi'i gnas tshul 'char byed/9byams chos lnga'i nges don rab gsal/10byams chos kyi lam rim/11skabs lnga pa yan gyi thal phreng dbang
ba'i rdo rje/12tshad ma'i chos 'byung dpyod ldan dga' byed/13dka' 'grel rig pa'i snang ba/14kun bzang chos kyi rol mtsho/15rtog ge'i 'khrul 'joms chen mo/16rtog ge snying
po/17rtog ge'i de nyid bsdus pa/18sde bdun bang mdzod kyi lde mig/19dmigs rtag gi TIkka sems tsam gsal ba'i me long/20dbu ma'i byung tshul yid bzhin lhun po/21rtsa she'i
TIkka skal bzang gi 'jug ngogs/22'jug pa'i TIkka nges don gnad kyi TIkka/23dbu ma rnam nges lung dang rigs

pa'i rgya mtsho/24stong thun chung ba dbang po'i rdo rje/25rta khrid vc: lta khridchen mo tshangs pa'i rnga sgra/26-27byang chub sems 'grel dang chos dbyings bstod pa gnyis
kyi Twikka/28gzhan lugs kyi dbu ma nor pa brgya dang brgyad bgrangs pa nges don snyim pa'i me tog/29nges don bdud rtsi'i thigs pa/30stong nyid rab gsal/31lugs gnyis rnam
'byed rtsa 'grel/32'dul ba'i dka' 'grel nyi ma'i shing rta/33las chog gi dka' 'grel zla ba'i shing rta/34gzhi gsum cho ga bdud rtsi'i rol mtsho/35theg pa gsum gyi 'dul ba'i
bslab bya/36bslab bya bsdus pa las dang po pa'i gnas 'dul ba'i 'bel gtam rnam nges/37sdom gsum rab dbye'i kha skongs/38bsdus don/39spyi don/40thal phreng/41mngon pa kun
las btus kyi rnam bshad rnal 'byor spyod gzhung rgya mtsho'i rlabs phreng/42de'i grub mtha' bsdus pa/43mngon pa mdzod kyi mtha' chod bye brag tu bshad pa'i rgya mtsho
chen mo/44bka' 'gyur gyi dkar chag du ma/45chos grwa 'di nyid kyi byams chen gyi phyi nang gi dkar chag/46chos 'khor deb gter/47bca' yig tshan pa gnyis/48mol gtam rgyas bsdus
tshan pa bzhi dang/49bka' shog shin tu mang ba dang bcas pa'i lung shin tu 'jur ba nyin zhag gi gdan gcig skabs tsam ma gtogs lhag par 'grus pa'i brtson 'grus kyis mthar
phyin cing/ bsnyen bkur dang 'bul dngos kyis dge ba bskyed pa'i legs byas nyid sgrub bya'i gtso bor bgyis shing/ snga dgongs kyi cha/ sde pa yab yum drung du bka' dbang
ni gu'i mgyogs khrid sogs thugs kyi bzhed pa yongs su gang ba'i legs byas spel nas/ slar mang mkhar mu gu lung gi gnas la brgyud de byang phyogs chos kyi

rgyal po'i pho brang du phyin/ byang phyogs yab sras la dus kyi bka' dbang rgyu lam 'chag med kha gso/ tshe dbang brgya rtsa sogs 'bul ba'i skabs/ slar dpal stag lung gi gdan
sa chen po nas/ mchog gi sprul pa'i sku chen po'i bka' lung nan bskyed du/ sngar gyi chos kyi rnam grangs mtshan tsam thos pa'i legs byas kyi don de nyid slad nas zab
rgyas kyi bdud rtsi rjes su myang ba'i blo rings pa nyid du yod pa nas/ lam gyi dka' tshegs la ma ltos pa ci nas kyang myur bar/ sngon gyi dam tshig rjes su dgongs pa'i 'byon
lugs dgos gsung ba'i bka' bstsal ci bor blangs nas/ shul rings kyi ngal dub la khur du bzod pa'i ngang nyid nas/ thog mar dpal spyang lung gi ri khrod chen por rigs
'dzin 'chi med dbang po rgyal ba 'od snang gi ngo bor gyur pa'i dpal rin po che spyang lung pa'i zhabs drung du phyin te/ gser zho bcu gsum gyis sna drangs pa'i dngos po
rnam par dag pa lag na ci mchis pa thams cad yongs su dag pa'i sems kyis phyag gi padmor son par bgyis/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po nas brgyud pa'i lam 'bras cha lag yongs
su rdzogs pa'i bka' drin zhu ba'i snyan gsan btab/ zhag 'ga'i bar du lam gyis dub pa'i ngal bso'i yid bder ci bder 'khod cing/ de bar paN chen rin po che nas brgyud pa'i
grub pa'i rgyal mo'i tshe dbang khrid dang bcas pa zhus mtshams stag lung nas 'bod mi rim can du byung bas myur bar bskul te/ stag lung thang pa'i chos grags gcung rin
po che 'gro ba'i mgon po ras pa chen po'i zhal gyi dkyil 'khor nye bar mthong ba'i yid bdes drangs/ zhag gsum tsam bcag mal

bgyis nas/ sprul pa'i sku chen po nyid thang 'brog gi dben gnas na hor sogs mtha' 'khob kyi 'gro ba du ma'i don du chos kyi 'khor lo rmad du byung ba bskor zhing bzhugs pa'i
spyan sngar phyin/ dges pa rab kyi mthar gyur pa'i bka' bstsal gyi thog ma/ da lta 'di na nged la chos zhur 'tshogs pa'i bla ma khyung pos gtso byas bsgom chen sha stag
brgyad cu tsam 'dug pa/ 'di dag la chos kyi sgo 'byed du ming gi bkra bzang bar 'dug pa nas sems khrid yid bzhin gyi nor bu cig gnang ba zhu gsung ba'i bka' dang du blangs/
dgongs kha'i cha la 'gro mgon dung mtsho ras pa'i rnam thar zhib rgyas dang/ sngon byung skyes bu ye shes rdo rje'i rnam thar ma 'ongs lung bstan dang bcas pa yid ches
su sbyar ba'i chos kyi khog phub rnal 'byor bzhi gsum bcu gnyis nyid bshad bya'i ngo bor bkod pa'i zab khrid lag bcangs su zla chos cig gi bar bgyis shing/ zhabs drung
sprul pa'i sku nyid la thog mar skye bo mang po 'dus pa'i sku grib bsal ba sogs ched du dmigs pa'i rnam 'joms dzA li ma dkar po'i byabs bsrungs/ de nas rim bzhin rnam 'joms
bir lugs/ rnam 'joms ma Ni badzra rnams kyi dbang 'phags pa rin po che'i yig cha ltar bgyis/ rnam 'joms lha cig bum cig gi chab khrus btud mar zhag 'ga' phul mthar/ jo
