par 'dug zer nas phul/ dgun gyi reg bya dang/ dus chos sogs kyi dus btab la brten myur bar

lam spyad nas gting skyes kyi chos grwar dge 'dun bdun cu tsam la lam 'bras rdzogs par bshad cing/ khyad par sde pa rin po che nyid kyi drung du dgongs bzhed kyi gtso bor 'dug
pa nas bdag chen blo gros pa nas brgyud pa'i lam 'bras cha lag rdzogs par phul zhing/ brnyel bso'i zin tho sogs nan tan che ba rang gnang/ thun bzhi'i rnal 'byor phyag
bzhes su thebs pa'i ngo mtshar gyi dpal 'dzin par mdzad/ de skabs gnas de nyid du bdud rtsi ril bu sgrub pa'i mdun pa mngon du btang/ dge slong bzhi bsnyen sgrub la nan
tan gyi bskul cag ma rel ba'i gnad sbyor byas shing/ lam 'bras dang khong rnam pa'i bsnyen sgrub mthar phyin mtshams/ lam 'bras kyi chos yon rnams/ brag dkar nas mkhan chen
rin po che spyan drangs phyag tu dengs par byas/ bsngo bas rgyas 'debs zhus shing/ snga gong nas bka' nan yang yang gnang ba ltar/ mkhan chen drung du bde mchog lU dril
nag gsum gyi dbang/ ni gu'i byin rlabs dbang dang bcas pa zla phyed tsam phul/ nged rang gis kyang paN chen rin po che nas brgyud pa'i bsgrub thabs brgya rtsa/ rgya mtsho
rjes gnang rdzogs par zhus shing/ gser zho gsum dang bdun cha legs par cig gis sna drangs pa'i 'bul ba cha mthun yang bgyis/ de mtshams g.yas ru byang nas bdud rtsi ril
bu sgrub pa'i chas sman ltos che ba dang/ rje btsun grags pa/ chos rgyal 'phags pa sogs bla ma gong ma'i ril bu'i rta mtshan che ba gnang byung ba la gzhi blangs/ sa ga'i
nyer gsum nas nyer dgu'i bar gyi zhag bdun la brgyud pa'i phyag bzhes ma log pa'i bdud rtsi sman sgrub spel bas/ phyi nang gi

ltas me tog gi char dang/ dri bsung gi ngad/ ril bu 'phel stobs che ba sogs sgrib med du byung zhing/ ril bu sgrub pa'i skabs kyi ga Na tsakra'i dus gsum gyi pU dza sogs bzang
la gya nom pa yang dad pa gsum stobs su gyur pa'i mi dbang chen po yab yum gyis yang dag pa'i tshogs spel/ gnam gang la mtshams kyi bcad bya bkrol nas/ tshes gcig la
lam du zhugs te sman sdings ri bo rgyas pa'i mgul du lo chen snying gi thig le'i drung du ril bu'i phud dngos grub kyi skyes phul/ dgos dgur gyur ba'i bka'i shis brjod kyi
me tog rna ba'i rgyan du byas nas byang phyogs chos kyi rgyal ba'i pho brang ga la ba der phyin/ sngar gting skyes su bsdod pa'i skabs dang/ lam du'ang yar rgyab nas mchod
rten chen po'i rab gnas la 'bod mi rim can du byung yang mtshan ltas rtsub pas ma sleb cing/ ngam rings su sleb 'phral ti shri rin po che bzhugs 'dug pa'i drung du sbyong
rgyud kyi dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang zhus pa'i thog mar dar kha gsum sbrel/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dkyil 'khor drug la do sbrel/ 'jig rten pa'i dkyil 'khor drug
la kha yang re/ dbang grol rjes gser zho gsum dang bcas pa'i dbul ba brda mtshon tsam yang phul zhing/ de lo g.yas ru byang du phyag mo yang shin tu rtsub cing/ mnal ltas
sogs kyang lhag par rtser ba dang/ thugs dog che ba rang 'dug pa nas/ sku rim la dmigs pa'i drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog zhi ba las thams cad pa'i bsregs blugs btab pa sogs
rang blos ci mkhyud kyi legs tshogs spel bas mtshan ltas dge tsam dang/ chos rgyal mes dbon rnams kyi sku mdog legs par bsel kyang

mnga' thang la cung zad rtsub pa'i bar chad kyi sgo en tsam gyi 'char sgo sgrib med du byung pa nas/ rgyal po chen po sde bzhi'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor zhal phye/ chos
rgyal mes dbon rnams la dbang 'bul bar brtsams pa'i cho ga'i skabs bzlo skar chung ngu nas tsan thabs su phug ron sngo nag cig glo bur du 'phur nas dkyil 'khor gyi khar mchongs
byung ba la/ lag pas bsnyabs pas shog pa nas zin byung mtshams/ bsam pa la 'di phug ron rang brgyud pa ni ma yin/ bar chad rtsom pa'i dmigs bya der 'dug pas bsgral
lam snyam pa skad cig la/ ci bden pa la brdzun par sgrog pa'i ngan pa dag gi bla mas phug ron bsad zer ba la dgos pa mi 'dug snyam pa'i yid spyod skyes nas phyir skyel du
btang/ de mtshams rang dbang phul cing/ de man mnal lam rtsub pa sogs kyang 'gyur/ sku chags kyang nang khul du 'gyur nges pa'i mtshan ma gsal po gzigs gsal du phebs/ rang
yang yid bde snyam pa'i ngang nas lo dus kyi dus dbang rnams 'bul ba'i dbu btsugs/ rang gi yi dam du/ ka ya tha pa shraddhaM pradznyA ma ti rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sdes/
dpal dang po'i sangs rgyas kyi bsdus rgyud nyis bdag nyid du li khi taM gyi ngo mtshar bskrun pa dang/ sprul sku a lhun pa spun gyis rdo rje phreng ba'i dkyil 'khor 'bri
ba'i dbu btsugs/ ti shrI chen po'i drung tha skar la bskyod mtshams/ dbyar rings thog mar pan chen nags kyi rin chen nas brgyud pa'i sbyor drug/ o rgyan bsnyen bsgrub/
grol ba'i thig le sogs chos kyi rgyal po chen po nyid sku rkyang la smar khrid mdzub tshugs su phul zhing/ ji ltar phul ba'i gnad 'doms brnyel thor 'debs pa

gnang 'dug pa ni/ rang gis blo gros kyis 'bad de brtsams kyang sngo mi thogs par gyur zhing/ dpal mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho 'khor lo bcu gnyis rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen po
rang nyid gcig pu'i lag bris su dbang phul zhing/ 'di skabs chos rje dge bcu ba la kyai rdor bka' babs bzhi'i dbang/ bde mchog nag po pa/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa sogs kyi
dbang gnang/ gur sam gyi rgyud lung/ bka' gdams thig le bcu drug gi dbang skabs/ nam mkha' la 'ja' tshon ngo mtshar che snyam pa byung/ de skabs lho ri bo che nas rin
po che mang dkar ba dka' ba chen pos spyan drangs/ phreng ba skor gsum/ kRa ya'i kha skongs dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor zhe lngar dbang zhus pa'i/ dkyil 'khor chung mtha'
la dar kha gsum re/ de gong la dar kha lnga tsam dang bdun tsam spel ba sha stag dang/ dus 'khor chos dbyings gsung dbang/ 'jam dbyangs sku dra/ rdo rje dbyings sogs la dar
kha bcu gsum re/ bde legs dkyil 'khor gsum la kha thags dkar po lnga lnga/ dbang tshugs pa'i nyin sku chos srab chen legs pa gras grub/ rgya dril shin tu bzang ba/ rten
khebs bzang bsgrigs sgo tshad gcig/ dbang grol ba'i nyin/ gser zho lnga 'gor ba'i thig po cig gis sna drangs pa'i chos yon yang dag gis dges pa bskyed mtshams/ chos rje
pa de ring thogs pa'i gnangs nyin nged rang gis kyang nyi ma dbus kyi phyogs la btegs pa'i skabs/ chos rgyal chen pos gser zho sum cu so bdun gyi maNDal dang/ tsan dan dmar
po'i sdong po shin tu che bas mtshon pa'i gnang sbyin zla ma mchis pa bstsal/ zla ba dgu pa'i nyer lnga la byang

phyogs nas bteg pa'i bcu pa'i tshes lnga'i nub spyang lung chos sdings su 'byor/ dpal rin po che la gser sogs dpus dag gi phyag mjal btab/ rnal 'byor dam tshig gso ba'i lam
dbang zhus/ lhun grub rdzong la brgyud/ dpal stag lung gi thang chen por son pa na/ gcung rin po che 'gro ba'i mgon po ras pa chen pos gtso mdzad/ grwa nang gling gsum 'dus
pa'i dge 'dun gnam gyis sa bkab pa lta bus gdugs dang rgyal mtshan rol mo'i sgra dbyangs/ bdug spos kyi dud sprin sogs kyi rgyang ring po nas bsu ba'i bkod pa gya nom
pas mdun nas bsus te 'dus pa'i dbus su bdag gzigs tsam nyid nas 'gro mgon ras pa chen pos gus pa'i brkyangs phyag kyang btab par mdzad pa mthong ba tsam gyis sems rtsis
gtad med pa'i ngang nas zhal mjal legs par bgyis/ bkra shis pa'i dge mtshan yar dpe la bzhag pa'i ngang de nyid nas/ 'dus pa'i tshogs pa ma lus pa mchod khang chen mor gcung
rin po che'i phyag phyir bkris nas rno rjeng ba'i dbang gzab rgyas su phul cing/ na ning gi skabs ltar tshogs chos la chos drug/ phyag chen/ dbang lung phran tshegs zla
ba gnyis kyi ring rgyun chad med par chos kyi 'khor lo bskor rjes/ gling nang nas bsgom don gnyer kho na'i dad 'dus nyis brgya tsam dang lhan cig/ mchog gi sprul pa'i
sku bzhugs pa'i bsti gnas bse gling gi ri khrod du 'phos nas ri chos skor gsum zhib bshad bgyis/ mchog gi sprul pa'i sku chen po nyid kyi zhabs drung du rdo rje phreng ba'i
dbang 'bul ba dang/ snga gong gsan pa'i khrid thams cad pa'i brjed byang/ ngag las phyag bris su 'god pa

gang zhing/ bdag nyid kyang kha tsam min pa sprul pa'i sku nyid la yid ches pa'i dad pa bla lhag tu skyes shing/ mgon po shA wa ras byin gyis brlabs pa'i mtshan ma yang nyid
kyi mthu las byung ba'i yid gtan snying nas lhug par rnyed pa'i dbang las/ mar pa/ mi la/ sgam po ba/ phag mo gru pa/ bla ma zhang/ stag lung thang pa/ 'jig rten mgon po/
gling ras/ rgya ras/ rgod tshang pa rnams kyi bka' 'bum gyi lung/ 'brug skor gyi bcu gsum ma'i dbang/ rten 'brel/ ro snyoms/ bla sgrub/ bsre 'pho sogs nyid kyis 'brug
pa rin po che la gsan pa'i bka' rgyud rin po che'i bka' chos thams cad bum pa gang byor thob pas thos brgya'i sgro 'dogs lhag par chod pa byung/ de skabs yar rgyab phyogs
su zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i nang tsam la bya dka'i dbang gis yud tsam phyin skabs/ gzhung kre shing gi gdung brgyud pa spyan drangs nas/ rngog dkyil bdun gyi dbang/ rin chen
rgyan 'dra'i bshad lung/ bsre 'pho/ chos drug sras mkhar ma/ gdan bzhi dang ma hA mA ya'i rdzogs rim mtha' dag dang/ bka' bsrung du gsol ma'i dbang lung la thug gi bar
rdzogs par zhus/ 'bul ba dang zhabs tog cha mthun bsgrubs nas skyar log bgyis/ bse gling gi ri khrod nyid du zhabs kyi padmor son/ ji ltar thos pa'i chos rnams rdzogs par
phul rjes/ slar stag lung gi chos grwar chen por bgrod nas/ gcung ras chen pa'i drung du rngog dbang bdun sogs dgongs pa'i dbyings yongs su bskangs zhing/ slad ma dbon rin
po che bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung dbu skra bsil/ tshangs par spyod pa'i gnas yongs su bzhes par

mdzad cing/ 'bul ba rnam gzhag dpag med byung ba'i phud/ pha rin po che tre bo'i drung du ja sig kun nas bzang ba gsum/ gos phyi nang gnyis sogs dang/ mched grogs grwa pa rnams
la dar kha re'i 'gyed dang bcas pa'i mang ja gsum sbrel/ dpal rin po che spyang lung pa la ja sig gnyis/ gos phyi nang/ tshe dpag med kyi rgya sku/ gser gyi glegs bam/
rnam rgyal mchod rten/ rgya dril/ rten khebs sogs bcu gsum tshan/ rin po che gdan sa pa dang/ dbus smyon gdan sa pa la ja sdum/ dar yug/ gan spos/ rab dkar/ gos kha 'brel/
kga btags re re/ 'brug pa gcung rin po che'i drung du yang 'bul skad de mtshungs/ spyang lung tshogs su mang ja/ ja sig sdum gyi 'gyed/ 'di skabs paN chen rin po che
nas brgyud pa'i sbyor drug/ mkhas grub gzhon nu grub kyis mdzad pa'i phyag chen ga'u ma/ spyan snga lha gzigs ras pas mdzad pa'i phyag chen chos drug rnams zhus/ gdan sa
pas gtso mdzad tshogs la rdo rje phreng ba yang bgyis/ stag lung tshogs su ja sig bcu gnyis kyi 'gyed/ dpal sangs ne'u thog tu mang ja'i rgyur ja sig sbrel shin du bzang
ba/ dkar yol rtse rings brgya'i 'gyed rnams bsgrubs/ tshur lam sde pa brag dkar bas 'bod mi byung nas bkra shis ljongs su phyin/ zhag 'ga' ngal gso bgyis/ sde pa yab yum
drung du dgongs bzhed kyi dbang lung mang du phul zhing/ bo dong thams cad mkhyen pa'i tshems/ rnam rgyal mchod rten rang byon/ gser ljangs brdungs kyi ze'u lha khang dang
bcas pa/ de nyid 'dus chen brtsom dus kyi paN zhwa dar chen mi 'dra ba bcu drug gi 'dril lkogs dang

bcas pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi phyag dreg 'byar ba'i sbas don lhan thabs dang bcas pa'i glegs bam rnams bka' drin du bstsal rjes/ ma drin can gyi gtso byas 'grel pa
can 'ga'i don dang/ rang gi dkor sbyongs su dmigs/ lha sar jo bo rin po che la gser srang gang gi zhal gser/ gser zho gsum sku la ltos med du gtor zhing/ rgyun ldan du dar
chen gser mdog yug gi snyan dar sgron pa dang/ gzhan jo bo thugs rje chen po sogs snyan dar 'bul dgos nyer gnyis tsam dang/ zhal gser kyang thob bya kun la ma chad pa/
ra mo cher jo bo mi bkyod rdo rje sogs la'ang sku skal gya nom pa phul/ gser ston steng 'bul cha dkon gnyer chen mor ja sdum bzang nges/ gos phyi nang/ rab dkar rtsa rings/
spos chag/ kha btags/ zhal gser zhu mi la ja mgo spor/ dar yug/ gos kha 'brel/ rab dkar/ spos chag/ kha btags/ de 'og gsul la ja lha nyag bdun re/ gos kha re/ dkar yol/
spos chag/ kha btags re re/ de 'og lnga la ja lha nyag gsum gsum/ dar kha 'brel/ dkar yol/ kha btags re/ de 'og bcu la ja nyag re dang kha btags re/ dkon gnyer chung ba
bcu drug la dar kha re bgyis te/ gser ston yang dag pa'i dpe bzhag byung/ dge rtsa de dag gi bsngo rten pha lo chen drung du gsol ja bzang nges pa sig sbrel cig phul/ lha
sar sdod rin bde chen nas mchog gi sprul pa'i sku zhwa dmar cod pan 'dzin pa'i 'bod mi rim can du gnang ba'i bka' ma chogs par zhabs drung du phyin/ dgongs dbyings rin
po cher sbyar ba'i dbang rjes gnang mang du phul/ slad nas kyang

chos kyi sgo rab 'byams rjes su nod pa'i bka' lung yang yang gnang ba'i dgongs len gyi kha chad sne khrid du phul nas/ dbyar yar rgyab phyogs su dpon sa yum sras drung du 'bod
mi dos drag stag lung man rim can du gnang ba'i zhal ngo ma chogs par phyin/ tshogs dge 'dun sgang pa'i mkhan rin po che'i zhal snga nas dang/ zho ma mkhan chen/ mon
bu mkhan chen/ dar lung mkhan chen/ byams sdings mkhan chen/ mtshal mig mkhan chen/ dpal sdings mkhan chen/ rnam rgyal mkhan chen/ sde gling mkhan chen/ byams pa gling gi
zur chen/ chos 'khor sgangs la sogs drag bsdus zhal ngo gsum gyis gtso mdzad/ dbang cha gcig la/ sne gdong rtse nas dpon pa rin po che'i zhabs drung nas zhus pa'i paN chen
nags kyi rin chen nyid kyi thig rtsa gnang ba'i rdo rje phreng ba'i dkyil 'khor stengs nas dbang rdzogs par phul/ yar lam gong dkar rdo rje gdan du/ rin po che byams dbang
pa'i drung du sngar ma thob pa'i/ ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po la slob dpon padma dngos su gnang ba'i tshe dbang lha bcu bdun ma/ gu ru'i zlum po bzhi'i dbang/ rdo rje
phur pa sa lugs kyi stod byang chub sgrub lam dang/ smad drag po sgrol dbang rnams zhus shing/ chos kyi bka' drin gyis zho zhar ja sdum/ gos phyi nang shin tu bzang ba/
bkra shis kha btags rnams phul zhing/ 'brum bu la 'dzem stabs rong chen la brgyud/ ngur mig gi rje btsun sgrol ma'i drung du sngar mkhyud ltar snyan dar 'bul ba dang 'dod
don gsol btab bgyis/ 'brong rtser zhag 'ga' zung dbang lung gi 'brel pa tsam gyi rten 'byung yel

nas/ yang yang du yid bde lhag par bskrun pa'i bsti gnas mi 'jigs pa skyabs kyis 'tsho ba'i pho brang 'di nyid du/ rgyun gyi rgyal ba 'od snang gi tshe chog brgya rtsa dang
'brel bar/ rang myong gi bcud/ nyams len gyi mthil/ rtogs chos kyi ngo bo/ zab mo ni gu'i chos drug gi phyag khrid/ mgon dkar yid bzhin nor bus mtha' bsten pa'i legs lam
spel ba'i skabs 'di nyid do ces/re shig brjod pa'i sgor gyur pa yang de tsam de//dbri bsnan med pa'i sargar phye ba yang li khi taM//shes bya'i pha mtha' rjes dpog bya lam
'dra//rnam dpyod gshog pas bgrod tshe dka' ba ci//'di na sna tshogs grub mtha'i 'ja' ris la//bden par rtogs pa'i log shes byis pa'i blo//kye ho mig gyu'i chu la skom pa'i
bcud//gdung sems re ba'i 'grogs 'gro'i re dgas dag//rkang bang dgos med ngal ba 'di ko zhes//las snang sgyu ma'i mig 'phrul e ma mtshar//thos pa'i bdud rtsi bsil mngar
ldan pa'i ro//bsam byung lce yis myang tshe de lta'i tshul//bsgom pa yang dag don las gzhan min ces//snying gi rtag la lan brgyar 'char bar byos//chos tshul gang la'ang
sdang zhen ma mchis par//ci ste shAkya'i bka' nyid tshad mar gzung//rgyud sde'i nges gsang grub pa'i zhal lung la//dges dgur spyod la yi rang spel bar gyis//tshig 'bru yid
kyi glegs bur bris pa'i tshe//yig nag dpe tshogs khal rdo'i ngo bor go//don bzhin nang lta'i bsam gtan la dpyad pas//tshig gi sbu ba srang mtha'i rtsa bzhin shes//bstan
pa'i rtsa lag dam chos bdud rtsi'i sgo//rnam grangs bye bas yid dbang

ma tshim ste//da dung chos rgyun ting 'dzin ma thob par//thos pas ngom pa med 'di kho bo'i gshis//rtogs brjod lo zlas bcings pa'i rang blo'i zol//snyed pa chos la bgyis pa'i
bden pa'i gtam//dam pa'i tshogs las zhar nod bka' lung dag//gzhan la tshegs med 'doms pa'i mthu ldan su//dpyod ldan gzu gnas mdun du tshur byon dang//rang nyams blo gros
lang tsho'i dkyil 'khor dang//yon tan rgyan phreng ldan pa'i mig mchis na//yin min so sor 'byed tshe gsal bar rtogs//bdag ni 'di nas byang chub snying po'i bar//phyogs
re'i mig can chos spong khur len pa'i//bstan pa'i chos rkun nyid du ma gyur ces//dag pa'i smon lam snying nas 'debs pa lags//gang gi skye ba 'dzin tshe 'ang dag pa'i chos//de
nyid spel la blo yi mthu thob ste//yongs rdzogs thub pa'i bstan pa rin po che//rtsod pa'i dus 'dir slar yang rgyas byed shog//ces sngar brjod pa'i zur 'debs mdzes par
byed pa'i rgyan 'di yang/ mi dbang yab sras 'di gnyis kyis bskul ba'i ngor/ dge slong bsod snyoms spyod pa/ shrI wan a nanta mukti ba ra pu tsi tra sA ga ra se nas/ dpal
khri khang gi yang rtse chos rgyal pho brang du sbyar ba'i yi ger bkod pa'i bgyi ba po yang/ dad ldan shes rab blo gros rnal 'byor spyod pa'i sdes bgyis so// //rnam thar
yang rgyan nor bu'i phra bkod/

shrai ya pestu/'jam mgon ngag tshig grub pa'i dpa' bo ni//dpal ldan mkhas kun dga' ba'i rol rtsed mkhan//bsngags 'od smin grol mchog gi phrin las can//blo gsal rgya mtsho'i
sde zhes mngon sum gyur//yongs 'dzin mkhas mang zhal gyi bdud rtsi ni//dad mos bsam pa'i snyim pas legs mnos te//gcig tu gzhan la phan pa'i go cha las//nam yang rang gi
don las sred ma lags//sbyin pa'i g.yab mos dbul phongs phyogs kyi mgron//ma bos ngang gis mdun du nyer lhags tshe//gtong la rjes chags rab brtse'i spu long dag//'bad pa med
par lan brgyar g.yo ba nyid//sems kyi kun rtog ser sna'i mdud grol ba//bdag la mi sbyin bsam pa 'ga' yang med//ma chags dngos po srang mdo'i rtswa bzhin yang//yongs su
gtong la zhum pa ga la yod//lan la mi re grags pa don gnyer min//pha rol yid bde bdag sems rangs pa'i tshul//zol min snying nas lhag bsam dag pa yang//'di na dus gsum rgyal
bas mngon par

gzigs//chos sbyin bsam pas lha bcas 'gro ba'i yid//yongs su tshim pa'i sbyin pa zang zing med//bsod nams dpag yas gang des lus can rnams//thar pa'i 'jug ngogs bde bar bgrod
pa lags//tshogs mang 'dus pa'i dbus na mngon mtho ba//rgyu skar bye bas skor ba'i zla ba bzhin//smra mkhas 'dzum dkar g.yo ba'i bsil zer gyis//bskal bzang dad pa'i sku mud
rgyas par byas//e ma dus kyi mthar lhung bas//phyogs 'dzin tshub mas kun du bskyod//bzo gnas yid bde'i dpal 'dzin pa//u dum me tog lta bur snang//bstan la phyogs ris ma
mchis shing//bstan pa 'dzin la'ang nye ring ci//rang gzhan phyogs su 'dzin pa'i cha//rdul tsam yid la 'chang ma lags//pha ni yongs su gso ba'i phyed//ma dag bkum pa srid
min ltar//rang gi bstan pa spel ba'i phyir//gzhan gyi bstan pa ji ltar bshig//yongs la dag pa'i snang ba can//phyogs dang ris su ma chad pa'i//sangs rgyas bstan pa'i khol
po pa//yan pa blo bde kho nar bas//'di na 'ga' yi chas dgas shing//phal dang mthun par ma gyur kyang//lhag bsam dag pa'i rang babs la//rgyal ba sras bcas dgyes pa 'dzin//de
yang rang gi yongs su 'dzin pa'i dge ba'i bshes dpal rin po che spyang lung pa'i zhabs kyi padmor mngon par mchod de/ phyis nas zhal gyi dkyil 'khor mi mthong nges
pa'i yid shes skyo ba'i dbang las bka'i tha mar yang dga' ldan gyi lam mngon par 'thob pa'i 'pho ba 'od kyi 'ja' tshub ma dang

'brel ba'i snying po don gsum gyi man ngag zhus te 'bral bar mi spobs bzhin du/ chos 'khor dpal gyi lha sa la brgyud nas yar rgyab phyogs su dbyar ring bsdad/ don gnyer ba
'ga' dang 'ga' la dbang bskur rdo rje phreng ba bgyis pa'i skabs shig gi rmi lam du/ dpal rin po che spyang lung pa nyid/ sku gzi 'od mchog tu brjid cing sngar med pa'i spyan
ra nag po gsar pa zhig bzhes pa dang mjal bas zhal 'dzum mdzad cing kho bo ring por mi thogs par paN chen drung du 'gro zhes bka' bstsal pa'i ngang nyid la gnyid sad
pas/ bla ma rtsibs ri ba sogs la rang re'i dpal rin po che de nyid ring por mi thogs par zhing brje bar snang/ nged la rmi lam gyi 'char sgo 'di tar byung zhes smras la/
slar bdag cag rnams gtsang phyogs la yong ba'i ngur mig tu rje btsun ma sgrol ma dang mjal ba'i tho rangs yang sngar bzhin sku'i rnam pa de rang la khyad par phyogs shig
tu thebs pa'i rnam pas yid slong slong ba'i ngang la gnyid bsad pas/ bsams dus de ring gi tshes bcu 'di la bla ma dam pa de zhing bskyod pa min na rung snyam pa'i sems la
zug ngu che che yang byung yang gzhan la smras pa ni med/de nas rim gyis tshong 'dus su bgrod skabs rnam thar gyi zur 'debs mdzes rgyan de yang bris/de nas kyang snar thang
la bsgyur chu mig gi rje btsun gnyan sgrol byin rlabs can de dang yang mjal nas sgrol ma brgya tsam sku mdun du bton/ maNDal bzhi ba'i gsol 'debs byas nas/ stag la la
bgyis tsha shod kyi la nas chos rje 'bum ram pa'i 'bod mi gnang byung bas/ seng ge rtse dang nye ba'i bye lung zer ba'i dgon chung dpe'u can

zhig gnang ba der nyal zhing/ sang snga bar chos rje 'bum ram pa'i drung dang/ pu rangs chos mdzad pa cig/ gzhan grwa pa slob gnyer ba gsum bzhi zhig la/ tsA ri zil chen phug
tu slob dpon padmas ras chen dpal 'byor bzang po la dngos su gnang ba'i tshe dpag med lha bcu bdun ma'i tshe dbang de byas pas tshe mda' mtho gang tsam tshad byung bas/
lhag par rtog pa za zhing yid mi bde ba'i skabs de nyid du/ spyang lung nas 'dar pa rab 'byams pa dpal blo ba dang/ spyang lung pa'i gzhi grwa chos ldan du grags pa de
gnyis dpal rin po che chos dbyings ru gshegs pa'i tshul smra ba la sleb byung bas de ma thag der 'dus kun la rgyal sras gzhon nu ma'i sku bstod par ma skye nas thos mchod
byas rjes de nyid ka seng ge rtser rdzong dpon chos 'bod mi byung pas phyin/ seng ge rtse na bzhugs pa'i jo bo khar sa pa Ni tsan dan las grub pa'i drung du dkar me snyan
dar rgya cher phul nas dpal rin po che'i dgongs pa rdzogs pa'i bsngo ba smon lam bgyis/ der tshe dbang zhu mi rnam pa la da res dpal rin po che dga' ldan du gshegs pa'i
gtam 'dis tshe mda'i lhag chad 'di thub pa 'dra smras pa yin kyang/ de nas zla ba ma 'gyangs par tshe dbang zhu mi'i chos rje 'bum pa rang ma gtogs pu hrangs chos mdzad
dang grwa pa slob gnyer ba de kun 'brum pas dus gcig la gum snang ngo//de nas nged rang gi khal ma byin dang bla ma rtsibs ri ba sogs tsha shod nas byang zhabs drung du brdzangs
pas/ lag na 'bul rgyu'i dngos po ci yang mi 'dug pas spyang lung gi bang chen pa gnyis kyang nged rang dang lhan cig khrid nas gting skyes phyogs la phyin pa'i lam
gyi mgron

khang zhig tu dpal rin po che'i sku tshigs gcig byung bas zangs ma dang/ lcags slang sogs/ snod gang 'dug tu mar me phul bas/ de nub khyim de'i nang gi gdung rtsa tshun gsal
bar gyur/de nas gting skyes kyi dgon pa dga' ldan rtse brag dkar/ gser gling rnams su thos mchod kyi mang ja gzab rgyas dang/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas 'od zer ba'i drung
du bsngo rten ja thum sogs dpus gang dag phul rjes gser srang gang gi yig rten dang bcas spyang lung pa gnyis gting skyes nas phyir slog nas gting skyes su zhag bdun tsam
bsdad rjes rgyal sras dngul chu chos rdzong pa'i 'khrungs yul phul chung la byas/ lha sa rdzong du sde pa phyogs las pas 'bod mi gnang nas drung du phyin/ bka' chos kyi
'brel snga sor ngam ring du phebs dus gur zhal sogs kyi rjes gnang gsan pas slar yang phyag na rdo rje 'byung po kun 'dul gyi rjes gnang tsam gsan nas de dus ngor pa'i gnyer
chung kun dga' don grub pa yang 'dug pas khong la brgyud nas dpon mgon po ba sku rkyang la tshe dbang lha dgu bstud mar 'bul dgos pa'i skul 'debs yang yang gnang gi 'dug
pa la/ sde pa ma chen nas kyang tshe dbang gsan na legs sam/ tshe dbang 'di legs byas kyi rtsa ba yin pas gtan mi gsan pa 'di rten 'brel la cung mi shong snyam yang yang
smras/ yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan pa'i yi ge ji lta ba'i bdag chen blo gros rgyal mtshan nas brgyud pa'i gur lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang yab sras lhan cig gsan cing
gser srang gang sogs 'bul ba rnam gzhag brtse skyong dpag med mdzad nas byang phyogs su yongs/ chos rgyal yab sras dang mjal zhing

mkha' spyod bde ldan du zhag 'ga' ngal gsos rjes/ dbus kyi chu ngan pas lus la za bun cher 'dug pa'i nad 'don la rgyu tshe'i chu tshan la phyin/ der zhag bdun tsam gong nas
rin po ches kyang bdag dang lhan cig chab tshan mdzad/ bcu bdun mchod pa cig gi dus 'grig pas ga bur gyi dkar mo brgya skong 'bul ba gnang/de nas slar mkha' spyod bde ldan
du 'ongs nas bla ma rtsibs ri ba sogs la lam 'bras zhig gi dbu btsugs nas dgongs phyogs chos thun re bshad/ snga gong dbon po tshe brtan pa la ri chos kyi lung cig 'gro
byas shing/ lhag par chos skyong gi bskang gso brgya tshar zab rgyas rang zhig gi dbu btsugs nas nang mtshams dam par byas nas zla phyed tsam songs ba'i skabs/ nub gcig
gi rmi lam la dkar me'i skong bu chung nge ba shin du gsal dngas can zhig 'dug pa glo bur du rlung gis bsad song pa dang// chus gang ba'i shel bum dkar po zhig mi zhig gi
lag nas shor nas sa phyer song ba rmi bas sbyin pa'i bdag po la sku dog che ba yin nam snyam pa byung nas tshul 'bul ba la dge slong chos dpal btang bas de'i dgongs kha
lha sa rdzong nas zhabs drung tshor zhu yig zhib rgyas dang/ nged la yang sde pa phyogs las rnam rgyal ba gshegs tshul rgya dril cig gi thugs dam 'dogs rnams byung bas/
bka' zhal la mdangs kyi mnal lam de 'di la lta ba 'dra gsung ba byung/ de mthun gser mdog can nas o nga'i drung gi phyag rtags dang lhan cig sprul sku zhwa dmar pa'i bsnyen
rdzogs sgrub pa'i mkhan po la yong dgos pa'i nan bskyed/ dbon sa gong ma chen pos ched gnyer gnang nas sprul sku rin

po che dang gnyis ka'i bka'i shog yar rgyab du dbon sa chen mo la/ gnang ba bzhin ched gnyer gyi do dam khur bzhes mdzad nas phyag dam mtha' phugs bsed pa'i zhib 'khod dang
bcas phebs byung mtshams bsam dus/ kha sang gi rmi ltas dkar me mnal ba shel bum chag pa sogs 'di la blta bar snang bas/ da res phyin kyang phan thogs gtan mi yong nges
snyam/ chos rgyal chen po'i drung du yang mar mi 'gro ba'i rgyu mtshan phul bas/ sa skya gdung brgyud bsod nams rgyal mtshan pas bsnyen rdzogs ma 'grub pa la brten khams
phyogs su bstan pa'i rgyun la gnod pa'i phrin las khyab chung rang byung 'dug pa bzhin da res sprul sku zhwa dmar ba yul gnyan pa dang/ che sa gong ma'i yang bka' lung nges
gsal yar rgyab du gnang ba yin phyin ma phebs na gtan mi legs shing/ yar rgyab pa sogs la gong ma chen po'i dgongs 'khrungs sogs kyi rgyur song dgos yod gsung pa sems
la bzhag nas lam 'bras kyi snang gsum la chos mtshams byas nas/ bla ma brtsibs ri bas gtso byas grwa pa byin bzhag/ nang gtor dang rgya bsgom gyi gdung gi ched gnyer dge
slong chos dpal ba bkos nas/ dpon slob nyung bsdus rang gis dgun gyi reg bya la gdos nas shar phyogs la phyin/ mar lam o nga'i drung 'brum pa la 'dzem stabs chu bar chos
rdzong na bzhugs yod pa la mjal rtsis rang gi mdun pas phyin nas chu bar gyi mdar sleb nub rmi lam la sngar gyi dkar me ji lta ba gcig 'dug pa a tsA ra bzhin khros pas phus
mnal ba rmi bas/ de'i ltas o nga'i drung la sku tshe ring po mi yong bar go ba skyes nas/ 'brum bag ma snyad mjal

bar ma phyin par lam bsrangs/ brtsed du nyin thal byas/de nas rmi ltas la brnyad pa'i skor yang la/ yar rgyab tshor bang chen rdzangs/ nged rang dpon slob gsum tsam rang rtsed
pa'i nang du bsdad nas khong rang gi mi ngo/ phyogs kyi rtogs ldan pho mo sogs mang dag la ni gu'i khrid bka' cig btsugs/ gzhan yang tshe dbang brgya rtsa sogs dbang
rjes gnang 'ga' yang yang byas pa'i skabs/ nyer lnga'i nub byang sems ma nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i dbang gral du skyur gzi'i rnam pas ngu lab mang du byed kyin snang ba la yid
za bab tsam byung rjes/ dbang grol nas nyal ba'i tho rangs rmi lam la pu Ta bha tra sring mo gser gyi pu gri ma gsum mtsham sku'i dbyibs su mtsham zhing/ zhal ras zla
ba yar ngo ltar rgyas pa'i gzi 'od dang bcas nged rnam pas las byas yod pas sla rngan du btang rag thong zer byung bas/ gnyis sad byung 'phral dpal 'byor la smras shing/
de'i nub rnam rgyal la bslus byas pas ma song ba'i nub tu 'dug/ de mtshams nas ni gu'i khrid grol rjes 'brum bu'i bags vc: bags?gang chung gi ngos nas sku chas drel khal
gnyis tsam dang bcas lam la yang 'brum bag byung dogs tho rangs bshad nas chu bar chos rdzong du phyin pas nyi ma rgas khar o nga bzhugs pa'i gzims khang mthong mi mthong
gi ri snar sleb mtshams/ nged rang gi nyams la kha sang rmi lam du byung ba'i a tsA ra dkar me bsod mi de 'dra bzhis lam bkag nas ma yong zer mgo bsgril gyin 'dug pas/ de
ma thag rta kha sgyur log phyin pas dpal 'byor na re/ da nyi ma nye 'dir sleb nas log pas mi yong/ log kyang do dgongs gnas khang yang mi rnyed cis kyang mi

mjal na sku chas 'di pa 'bul ba la nga rang 'gro zer kyin 'dug pa la/ nga ni mi 'gro sku chas kyang sang nang par 'brum bag sogs byung na brjod pa che byas rta bkrab yongs
pas/ khong rnam pa yang blos mi long bzhin du rjes la byung nas srod khyer tsam la chu bar gyi gnas tshang bdag chen rin chen rgyal mtshan pa'i yul dang lhan cig byung zhing/
o nga yang de'i sang man 'brum pa bsnyung ba yin snang/de nas yang yar rgyab nas gting bskul dos drag byung bas mi 'dod bzhin du chas/ mar lam sprul sku sman thang pa'i
sras po sman tshe ba gshegs 'dug pa'i thugs bso la mjal tsam byas/ bal po rnams gser mdog can na yod pa la mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i sku bzo ba la yong dgos pa'i bka' lung
bsgyur byang dang/ dpon mo che la zhon rta gcig gnang yod pa'i rtsis sprad/ chos rje 'jam dbyangs pa paN chen gyi khri kha la bzhugs pa la dad mos skyes/ mjal tsam byas
nas lam bsrangs nas rong chen la phyin/ ngur mig tu sgrol ma'i drung du gsol btab byas pa'i rmi lam la/ sngar gyi shel bum de slar yang nged rang gi lag nas ma zin par
brdabs song ba rmi bas bsnyen rdzogs de go chod gtan mi yong bar 'dug pas thag sbad bcad pa'i yig lan bskur nas nub chos lung du mkhan chen rin po ches gtsos mdzad la rdo
rje phreng ba'i dbang gi dbu btsugs shing/ mkhan chen drung gi zhabs phyir dbon chen pa dang/ drung rab 'byams pa bkra shis pa la ni gu'i khrid cig kyang btsugs/ de dus
mkhan chen rin po che spyan rab rib kyi rnam pa cher sngon par 'dug pa la dag byed stong ra'i skabs sku khrus kha dog sna lnga'i rnam par yang yang 'khrus

pas/ spyan yang rab rib rang dag la song zhing thugs dad mos lhag par che ba byung/ de skabs o nga'i sku tshes ma zin lugs kyis rgyu tshan skyel mi rkang gtad dang/ rnam rgyal
gyi gnas tshul 'di ltar byung tshul snang mi brkos mkhan dpal ldan pa nyis sbrel cig sleb byung mtshams rang kun dga' dpal bzang gi 'brum pa ma thar pa nas blos ma phod
par khong bsnyegs 'ongs pas lha khud du 'phrad nas nged kyis shar lam byas/ khong dpon slob gser mdog can nas brgyud bsam grub rtse la byas nas khri khang du dus btab
pas 'phrad nyin nas skya nad thu bar sngon pa zhag gsum tsam byung rjes 'brum bu yang ba rang byung nas thar rjes/ 'brum pas na nas shi na phung po sogs skyur ba la las sla
bar 'dug snyam nas/ sngon gyi mkhas grub khyung po lhas pa gzhon bsod nams pa'i dgon gnas der byas pas legs par byung nas sems bde zhing/ de bzhin gyi rgyu mtshan 'bul
ba thugs dam gtor ma rnams rtser phul nas rtsibs ri ba sogs sogs 'bod pa la dpal dbang rdzangs 'brum bag stabs zhu lon las zhu yig sogs ni med/ dpal dbang sleb mtshams/
rtsibs ri ba sogs grwa pa rnam pa yang mar rdzong ba bka' drin bskyangs byung zhing/ bla ma rtsibs ri ba ngam rings su bsdod pa'i ring yang lhag par na ba yin par 'dug kyang/
'a pha kye'i sman sogs kyis dga' rab byung 'dug na'ang/ mar lam sngar gyi na ba'i steng du mgrin par rnag bsags pa'i skrangs po shin tu che ba/ lag pa la yang rma'i
rnam pa'i shu ba 'jigs pa/ lus kun la rnag dris mi bzod pas brtses/ ngu ba min pa med pa'i nyams thag tu

sleb byung ba'i khong nang par yong ba'i do nub rmi lam du mi nag rta nag po zhon pa zhig gis/ bdag la lag tu thag pa nag po phra sing ba gcig gtad nas 'dis dbu dkris zer ba
bzhin dkris lan gsum byas pa'i rjes la thag pa'i lhag ma en tsam byung ba de shangs su chug zer nas rna bug g.yon du bcug pas/ der sbrul nag khra gcig tu byas sna nas yar
khyur gyis zhugs byung pas 'jigs snyam nas gshed bskyed then pas sbrul de'i mgo chad snar lus/ gzhan lag tu sleb byung ba'i dngangs skrag gis gnyid sad byung bas/ de ma
thag gshed bskyed nas lag pas sna g.yas bkag nas bus pa lan gsum bzhi gcig la sna nas dngos su srod srod mtheb chung gi rtse tsam cig thon byung ba dkar me mi 'dug pas
ji ltar yod ni ma mthong/ spos me'i thal ba la kyungs/ de'i nang par khong sleb byung bas tshong 'dus lha rje shes rab la bstan dus mdze yin thag chod zer ba 'dug pas zhag
bdun sbrel lam zan re re dang/ bir bsrungs kyi sngags rang gi 'chil ma btab pas zhag bdun po rang la smen rjes tsam med par sangs drag nas ya mtshan par 'dug go//de dus
bdag pa dpon slob ma lus pa tshong 'dus khri khang rang du gzhi phab nas/ dus kyi tshe dbang brgya rtsa dang/ grub chen brgyad cu'i dris mal sogs dang/ kun dga' dpal bzang
pos/ sde pa ma chen drung du kAndhi ra'i sgra las drangs pa'i grub thob brgyad cu'i bstod pa'i gI ta yang nyin re ma chag pa'i bslab sbyangs phul/ bdag gis sde pa grwa
lnga drung la bcom ldan 'das ma ku ru kulle'i gsang khrid rjes gnang phyag bzhes khrigs bkod mthong brgyud ltar phul zhing brjed

sbyang gi rtsom pa yang bgyis nas/ slar bsam grub rtser gnyer chen rnam pa'i 'bod mi 'byung ba bzhin phyin/ tshe rta chos skyong gi bskang gso rjes gnang sogs ji ltar 'dod
bzhin pa bsgrubs/ zhol pa'i bde legs khang gsar ba dang/ sa phug pa sogs grangs bsdus mang po la yang tshe dbang/ chos skyong gi bka' bsgo sogs dang/ chos sde brag dmar nas
dbang cha gcig la gnas brtan sho brag pas gtso mdzad bka' bcu rab 'byams rang 'ba' zhig la/ zhwa lu pa'i lugs kyi phyag rdor gos sngon can gyi dbang bskur yang bde legs
khang gsar bar byas/ de dus chos sde brag dmar du chos rje gtsug nor bas nged khu tsha lhan cig ja la/ 'bod pa gnang ba'i dus/ khong pa'i mchod stegs kyi spos skya'i khris
na mkhan chen rin po che'i sku 'dra li las grub pa'i glo bor bzhengs pa zhig sa brjen la rang dga' gyi nar bzhag snang ba mthong bas yid lhag par skyo ba rang byung nas/
'di bdag la gnang na rung ngam zhus pas/ ci bder rnam mchog nged la drung chen chos skyong ba 'das dus byung ba yin gsung ba gnang gin 'dug/ der lag tu blangs nas mgor
bzhag bltas rjes phyag nas ma rang yin zer ba'i kha yig 'dug cing/ de nub thog mar khrus gsol yang dag byas nas zhal gser zhus/ nam bzas bran/ dkar me lha bshos sogs gzab
rgyas phul rjes re zhig phyag mchod kyi gtso bor bskur/ phyis yar rgyab tu sde pa rin po che'i drung bdag chen a tshe ba'i zhal snga nas bsngags pa yang yang dag dad mos
gnang ba'i spyan rgyugs kyi thugs lhag par mos gus ches che ba rang gnang ba 'dug pas dgos gsung ba'i bka'

lung byung nas blos longs par phul/ da lta byams pa gling gi nam mkha' mdzod kyi gzims khang gi mchod yul gyi rten gral la bzhugs shing/ na bza' dar zab kyis g.yogs pa mig
yul du phebs pas rje bka' drin can pa'i bka' drin cha tsam 'dis kyang 'khor snyam pa'i blo bde yang byung ngo//de nas snar thang la byas stag la brgyud nas 'dzad lha dbang
rtse'i rdzong rtser zhag gcig ngal gso bgyis pa'i dus/ zhi ba lha dang gnyis rdzong gi 'phyong rtse'i g.yabs der long gtam bgyis pas/ khos brag dkar sems dpa' chen po'i
zhal 'phros mang po smra yin snang bas brjed gsos nas gting skyes dbon chen pa'i gnas tshul dran pas yid 'byung nas khong la bstod pa'i zol du bsgrigs pa'i smre sngags yang
rang gi lag pas yi ger bris nas dpe cha'i zla la 'bral med byas pas/ de mthong res snying la gzer ba'i skyo shas thag chod yang yang byung nas rang gi blo'i bskul 'debs
su 'gro ba byung/ chos mdzad smin grol rgyal mtshan pas kyang zhal shus song/ khong gi go ba la ni ngas kun re bsgrigs par 'dug snyam pa 'dug/ nged ni zhe nas rang dam
pa'i mgon gyis ma zin pa'i las chad/ rang gzhan dmyal ba'i me dong du bsreg pa'i bsam sbyor 'di lta bu skye ba 'di dang tshe rabs gzhan du yang mi 'byung bar bya'o zhes
pa'i yid kyi gzer bu yin/ phyis ni khong gshegs zer thos pa'i thos mchod la 'od zhu bgyis/de nas brag sna la 'grim nas lo chen drung du mjal te ngam rings su sleb kyang/
sku ngo rnams kyis sku 'brum ma bzhes pas bag seng la rin chen gling du phyin/ 'di la rmi ltas en tsam gyi 'char sgo sngar byung zhing/

khang pa'i 'gram 'dings dus kyang bsam 'grub dga' ldan pa'i gnas brtan rnams kyis kyang gding ba'i khud du sa bsnoms nas las ka mdzad skabs/ der 'dus kun gyis mig shes la phebs
pa'i bya rgod dkar mo zhig gi sprul bsgyur dngos mthong snang na'ang/ phyis rang re yang bya ba gtad med dang/ hor 'jigs stabs rdzong las kyi spyan nyes brtsigs pa'i
dgos pa dor ba'i shing cha yang nged dbus la song shul dran nas/ lta gyeng ror song ba 'dir gda'/ sa gar bsdad pa la chu 'di rang lus la phan par 'dug cing/ nam yang mi
yong ba'i dge sbyor gyi sgang la gnyid 'dra ba'i 'od gsal la cham cham 'gro ba gzhan gyis sad dgos pa'i rnam pa gtud mar byung/ de skabs shug pa rkang gcig tu gur phug nas
der phyin/ bal po rnams kyis mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i spra bzo khyer byung ba la bgegs sprod dang gzhig mal byas dus/ chos rje byams pa gling pa'i bsgrub thabs ltar yum
zhabs brkyangs pa mdzad 'dug pa/ sa skya pa'i bzhed pa ltar byin pa gnyis kyis mkhyud par sgyur/ rin gling nas dge slong dpal skyabs drung pa snying rje'i rang gdangs can
ba lung pa dkon mchog bstan pa'i drung du zhu yig ja'i rten bcas bskur nas chos zhu ba la brdzangs/ der rin gling du zla phyed tsam bsdad rjes yul sa sper skyas nas der
chos rje dge bcu ba byams pa mang thos rab gsal ba'i drung dang/ lo bu gdan sa pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan pa/ drung buddha ba/ rang re'i dbon po kun dga' dpal bzang po rnams
la dbang rdo rje phreng ba bskur zhing/ chos rje rnam pa dpon slob la thog mar brtag gnyis gzhung rkyang lung du bar chad

bsel ba la bsgrags rjes/ rdo rje gur dang/ saM bhu Ti la bla ma gong ma'i mchan sa dpyad/ gur la gur rgyan dang/ saM bhu Ti la gnad kyi gsal byed/ rje btsun sku mched kyi yig
stengs nas zab bshad rang blos ci 'doms phul/ de skabs gur gyi zhabs na rdo rje slob dpon gyi sur bsdu ba yod pa'i tshig bkra 'gegs pa la gur nyid kyi nang gi las rgyas
pa'i tshe dpag med pas tshe spel byed ces pa'i tshig gis 'phros blangs nas tshe mdo'i rgyas bshad re byed pa phyag rgyun yin na'ang dpe gtan nas ma rnyed pas/ slob dpon
nas ras chen pa la brgyud pa'i tshe dbang de byas dus/ tshe mda' la chad mngon tsam byung ba rnams skyes bu chen po mang thos pa de nyid sku tshe ring po mi bzhugs pa'i
bltas su 'dug/ khong rnam pa'i bka' chos grol mtshams chos rgyal chen po'i drung dang mjal zhing bka' lung la nged phu chung la chab bzhugs la 'gro bas de bar lha lcam la
rgyun gyi thugs dam byed rgyu'i rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs cig gnang ba dang/ chu tshan nas 'gug dang bstun dus 'khor rtser phebs nas rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang cig nged
rang gcig pu la gnang dgos gsung ba'i bka' lung bzhin/ dpon sa lha lcam drung du thog mar smin byed yab bde mchog nag po pa'i lugs kyi mngon rtog vc: rtogs'brel pa'i dbang
dang/ de rjes yul rdo rje rnal 'byor ma nA ro mkha' spyod ma'i byin rlabs phul zhing de dus kun dga' dpal bzang po/ kun dga' rdo rje/ smin grol rgyal mtshan pa gsum la
yang dkyil 'khor de nyid du nag po pa'i dbang bskur nas/ bal po rnams la rgya sgom gyi gser sku mda' gang ma gcig bzo ba'i las dbu yang btsugs te/

shar phyogs nas chos rgyal chen po'i drung phebs nyin rang mkha' spyod bde ldan du spos nas gza' skar bzang ba la chos kyi rgyal po chen po sku rkyang rang la rdo rje phreng
ba'i dbang phul ba'i skabs/ nyin re bzhin du dkyil 'khor gang yin la phyi rol mchod pa dang 'brel bar sbyin sreg re nas ma chad pa 'bul ba sogs/ mchod bshoms dbang rdzas
cho ga dbang bshad 'di las rgyas pa nam du yang byed ma myong/ de dus chos rgyal chen po'i drung gi phyag gi dkyil thang rnams nas smon lam gnang dang gcig bzhes pa kha
phye bas bde mchog drug cu rtsa gnyis ma gtso bo zhal bzhi phyag bcu gnyis pa der snang bas/ 'di ci lags bka' phebs la/ slob dpon a bha ya'i lhag pa'i lha der rang yin zhus
