byas nas kha ton 'phel skabs mar lam chos rgyal chen po'i drung nas kyang ri khrod chen por phebs zhal mjal/de nas sngar yang yar lam phebs skabs

sgrub sder sgrub rgyags rgyun ldan gyi chos gzhis sbyor ba sogs bka' drin du mdzad cing/ de lo'i dus gzings skabs kyang sgrub pa mo rnam pa'i pha ma'i khyim ma lus pa la dar
'dzugs mdzad nas mi 'jigs pa'i skyabs kyi/ dril chen po bsgrags/ sgrub sde chen po'i bsreg mthud pa lta bu'i bka' drin mdzad cing/ sa skya gdung brgyud kyang de dus phebs
nas nag po gzhung drug gi lung nod pa gnang/ 'di skabs chos rgyal chen po nyid lha dbang rtser bzhugs dus/ gnas gsar ba rnam pa'i 'pho 'chug la brten pa'i bdag cag pas
zhu phod che ba'i zhu yig na rims/ brjod par mi spobs pa'i zhu lan nyin re bzhin dang/ lhag par chos rje rin po che mtshar sa/ chos rje mkhyen brtse ba dpon slob kyi zhu
ngag zhu don ji ltar ba'i yi ge lag ris ches rtsub pa rgyun mi 'chad kyi thugs g.yengs ba'i skabs yang yang bsnyan dbang rtser dgos pa byung/ de lo'i dgun 'khrid lhag par
'phel zhing khrid ston sngon med phye mar ri bo tsam dang/ 'brong sha ri ltar dpungs nas mi re'i dgos skal gyis kyang tshim pa thob pa'i blo 'das gong nas rin po ches bka'
drin du mdzad/ de lo'i dgun khrid grol mtshams labs skor 'dab skyes bzhengs pa'i ni gu'i brgyud pa'i rab gnas byas nas/ dgun chos stengs su chos sde chen po'i mkhan chen
pas gtso mdzad dpon slob rnams la dbang rdo rje phreng ba cig dbu btsugs pas/ 'jam rdor dang mi bskyod pa'i dbang gnyis grol rjes bya ba 'ga'i g.yengs bas 'phro bzhag
chos mtshams bgyis/ dbus la chas nas lam du zhugs te mar lam lha rtser mchog gi rdo rje slob dpon rab gsal zla ba

spyan drangs nas/ rje btsun ras chung pa nas brgyud pa'i dpal phyag na rdo rje gtum mo khyung nyer gcig ma'i dbang 'phan ne/ dpal 'byor bdag rang gsum pos zhus nas sa rims
dpyad/ snar thang tshong 'dus 'brong rtse sogs la brgyud nas rgyal rtser phyin/ mkhan rin po che'i drung dang mjal/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs/ mgon po stag zhon
gyi rjes gnang sogs bka' stsal bzhin phul/ 'phan ne dpal 'byor gnyis la chos rje zhal phu ba nas brgyud pa'i mgon po lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang de bka' 'brel du zhur bcug
der dpon sa mnga' ris rgyal mos chos 'brel med pa'i dus nyid nas phyag gi bkur bsti 'bul ba rnam gzhag rgya cher bstsal zhing/ dpon sa bde ba can mas mkhan chen rin po che'i
zhabs drung du phul ba'i bka' dbang rnams lhan du gsan/ gnang sbyin sogs yang dag mdzad/ de rjes chos rje rin po che gser gling pa sogs dang dpon drung gi sku ngo rnams
la dgongs bzhed ltar bka' chos mang du phul/ de dus sde pa rin po che gan pa rdzong na bzhugs pas de res ma mjal/ de mtshams spos khang du spos khang mkhan chen pas 'bod
mi gnang ba ltar phyin/ spos khang gi tshogs su grub rgyal ma'i tshe dbang/ mkhan chen drung/ chos rje kha'u ba/ chos rje brag bkras pa rnams la bde mchog nag po zhabs
lugs kyi dbang sogs dgongs pa ltar bgyis/de nas nya mo'i la la byas nub chos lung du mkhan chen rin po che dang mjal/ bka' chos phran bu 'bul ba dang ngal bso bsten/ 'phan
ne la rnam sras ser chen gyi rjes gnang zhig bka' 'brel du gnang ba'i gsol btab byas/ der ka

pad khyad 'phags sogs 'bul ba'i rnam gzhag thugs dad mos las 'ongs pa'i bka' drin yang dag pa bstsal nas/ slar yang lam myur bar dpyad gong dkar chos sder rgya ston byang chub
dbang rgyal dang mjal/ rgyun ldan gyi phyag mjal rten khebs bzang bsgrigs de phul nas yar rgyab tu sleb/ rim gyis bris sku rnams kyi dbu btsugs/ sde pa lho pa yang dpal
'byor rab brtan du yod ring phebs/ smon lam grol rjes mtshal min du zhag bcag mal bzhugs nas/ gong dkar gyi pho brang chen por dpon sa skyong chos kyi rgyal mo'i drung
du bka' dbang dgongs dbyings ltar du phul/ chos sder rgyal ston byang chub dbang rgyal ba'i drung du dpal mgon ma ning nag po'i srog dbang bdag cag 'phan dpal 'byor rnams
kyis lhan du zhus/ dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa gdong gnyan can dkar ser dmar ljang ste las bzhi mgon po'i rjes gnang rnams zhus/ bdag gis kyang 'grub rgyal ma'i tshe khrid 'bar
ra bas mdzad pa'i khrid lung phul/ de dus nang so gnyan po gnas pa la ho chal u rgyan zi'u ma/ rje tsong kha ba'i phyag dril rwa log rtse lnga khyad 'phags rnams dang/
dpon sa bdag mo'i bka' lung phyag dam zhib 'khod gnang bas/ sde pa rnam rgyal rab brtan pa'i phyag nas kun mkhyen chen po'i sku 'dra phyag na mdas bzang ma ti'i phyag bzo
sde pa sgar pa'i phyag nas dpon drung shag pa'i phyag tu brgyud pa'i grags can de yang gegs med par lag tu son/de nas chu shul/ ba de/ mtshar pa sna/ ljong sogs su bcag
mal re byas nas ba der 'bod mi gnang ba ltar gdung brgyud rin po che'i zhabs drung du 'byor/ yab yul lhan du rdo

rje phur pa'i stod las smad las sogs bka' dbang zab rgyas mang du phul rjes/ lha sar jo mjal byas nas gzhis ka brag dkar dang spyang lung brgyud nas stag lung du phyin/ tshogs
pa rnams la rgyud sde lnga'i dkyil 'khor chen por dbang yang yang dang/ zhabs drung sku 'bring pa'i phyag phyir sde pa lho pa'i drung bkra shis pa sogs la bsnyen rdzogs/
chos rje kun dga' bkra shis pa'i drung gi dge tshul mdzad nas slar log/ mkhar rtse la byas/ yar rgyab tu bris sku'i zhabs dril gyi gong lag tu gos gser ma'i ber thul
lu haM cig dang/ mtshal kha ri mo can sogs kyis zhabs thegs par byas/ zhal khebs sogs dpus gtsang dang rab gnas legs par bsgrubs skabs/ sde pa 'phyong rgyas pa dang rnam
sras gling pa sogs la'ang rgyal chen gling nyid du bka' chos 'brel pa dgongs bzhed ltar byas/ 'di skabs sde pa rin po ches mtshams sbyor bka' drin bskyangs nas dpon sa gong
ma chen po'i zhabs drung du jo nang gi bsrung yig gi 'jags yig khyad par can gyi bka' drin zhu ba'i zhu yig ri dwags kRaShNa swa ra'i pags pa sder bzhi dang rwa ma nyams
pa'i gdan bzhugs 'bul mi brdzangs pas/ re ba ji lta ba'i bka' bstsal yang dag thugs rjes bzung zhing/ rgya ston rin po che zhi bar gshegs pa'i thugs dam yun rings ma grol
bar zhabs 'bring pa gnyug mar gnas pa rnams blo rtser ba'i gros 'di la byung bas/ su kha si sogs mtshams ma bzhis zhu ba glus bskul ba'i snyan ngag yi ger bkod pa phul
bas thugs dam las bzhengs shing bla ma rin po che chos dbyings su gshegs 'phral thugs dam 'dogs su rdo rje phur pa'i bris sku

gcig dang bcas pa'i yi ger bskur byung skabs/ ja sig bzang pa/ gser thig po srang longs cig rnams phra la/ slar gdung rten bzhengs skabs 'phral byung gi gser thams cad ma zegs
par re re nas phul bas kun sdoms mgur mo nyer gcig tsam byung zer/ der yar rgyab nas mtshal min du 'ongs/ tshogs chos su jo nang ltar gyi sbyor drug gnad 'doms ngo sprod
'thems par byas/ kun mkhyen gyi bstod pa tshogs su btsugs/de nas gong dkar zhabs drung tshor yongs nas bka' lung bzhin gong ma 'gro ba'i mgon po rin po che'i sku gdung
gi rab gnas la bsdod gsung ba'i dgongs pa bgrubs nas dgun ngo bde chen chos 'khor du mtshams bcad bya shin tu dam pa byas pas kha ton dge sbyor 'phel ba byung zhing/ 'phan
ne sa skyo bar snang bas yar gtsang phyogs la brdzangs shing/ yar lam rgyal chen rnam sras kyi grub thob chos lung mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun grub pa'i drung du rnam sras
kyi rjes gnang ched kyis zhu ba'i khas bkod dang ja sig gi zhu yig rten dang bcas pa phul/ der mtshams ring la sne gdong nas che sa gong ma chen po'i bka' shog yang yang
gser srang re'i gnang sbyin dang bcas nas rab gnas gdung brgyud rin po che na rims gyis thugs dam rgyun bzhes yin dus bde mchog mai tri bcu gsum ma la brten pa dang/
rab gnas rang gi phyag bzhes kyang rje phag mo gru pa'i bka' 'bum nang gi dpe mdzod ma ltar las sa skya pa sogs kyi bsre slad med pa rang gi dbus gtsang dgos gsung ba'i bka'
phebs ltar du/ 'gro mgon rin po che dpal phag mo grub vc: grupa nyid kyi dpe mdzod ma ji lta'i phyag bzhes ma

'chugs pa'i rab gnas bar chad med par mthar phyin zhing/ dpon sa gdung brgyud rin po che'i drung du yang mjal ka 'phrod sbyor yum rin mo ches do dam gnang nas legs sbyor che
ba byung rjes/ rab gnas grol mtshams drang srong srin po ri'i bde mchog mjal ba dang re smon gyi smon lam 'debs pa la rkang btsugs snyan dar dar gos dbus gtsang gi kha
yig 'byar ba bcu gcig tsam phul/ bde chen chos 'khor du bsdod rin man du rje drung karma pa'i bod vc: 'bodmi lan mang du byung yang ma phyin/ dpon sa gong mas gnang ba'i
gser rnams phul ba'i lan gdan dmar gnang ba 'bral med byas/de nas yar rgyab tu yum ma las lhag pa'i bka' drin can ma'i sku khams dub pa'i dbu sngas su zla ba gcig tsam bsdad
phyag na rdo rje'i rjes gnang brgya tshar tsam bgyis/ der sku khams kyang cung zad bde mal sngon pa tsam byung rjes stag lung du rin po che'i drung khams phyogs la mi
phebs pa'i zhu 'bul la phyin pas/ dpon po dgur gyi shing mgo la phebs nas 'brog phyogs su 'gro phan mtha' yas pa'i dbang gis dbyar ring ma phebs par dgug bsdod gcig po la/
thog mar skyor mo lung du yab yum drung du ni gu phyag chen sogs khrid chos/ tshe dbang brgya tshar sogs dbang bka' bgrang yas 'bul ba la bsdad/ de skabs 'jam dbyangs
me tog gcig zhag bco lnga tsam gyi ring rgas pa med par bsam po le gnas pa byung ba de phyis gdung brgyud 'phel ba thob pa'i dge mtshan du snang/de nas sde pa lho pa'i drung
grag mig rtser skyor mo lung nas sku chas kyi rtse skyongs bka' drin bskyangs nas/ bdag gis spyang lung gi bla ma'i sku gdung

drung du rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs pa'i kyai rdo rje'i bdag 'jug gi dam tshig gso ba dang/ lhag par nyin re bzhin mchod pa gsar pa brje ba dang sgo bstun rgya sras
gzhon nu'i sku bstod sho lo ka bdun ma de brgya tshar re'i ring skor ba 'ba' zhig byas gsol ba snying nas btab cing zla phyed tsam blo phab nas bsdad/ de rjes kyang stag
lung rin po che'i phebs dgug rang la phyin tshogs pa rnam pa la dbang char dpyad pa'i dus 'khor gyi byis 'jug mngon rtogs sbrel ma nyin re bzhin dang/ rin po che sku mched
gnyis pos gtso mdzad la grub thob brgyad cu'i rjes gnang/ sbyor drug gi lung khrid tsam phul/ dor lho pa bdag po'i drung sa skyo ba'i thugs ma zug par nged la rgyang rtse'i
sa sne bar 'jigs sel la yong dgos gsung nas/ stag lung pa rnam pas mi gtong bzhin du yong ba'i the bcug nas phyin sna dkar rtse'i bar skyel ma byas/ de dus rje btsun
ma snyan grags bzang mo'i dbu thod dang mjal bas bdag gi lag tu bzung nas dum tsam bsdad pas nang nas bdud rtsi rang brdol brdzun med du khral la la byung bas der 'dus
kun ya mtshan che ba'i dad mos la bkod/de nas slar log yongs pas 'bras spungs pas/ rin po che 'bri khung pa'i sgar pa bcom pa'i dus zings pas lam bkag nas gong dkar du 'khyogs/
dpon sa rin po che'i drung du sangs rgyas kyi skyes rabs brgya rtsa'i lung dang/ sgrol ma nyer gcig gi rjes gnang phul/ sde pa srang mgo ba'i drung dang dpon sa dpon
drung la re mos su tshe dbang grangs btab phul/ der dpon sa rin mo che'i drung gis thugs dam dngul gyi mchod rten dang sgrol

dkar gyi dngul sku'i rab gnas bgyis/ de skabs kyi snang sbyin ja sig/ gos phyi nang/ dngul phor/ spos chag sogs byung ba rngog pa gdung brgyud pa'i phyag tu thengs pa byas/de
nas chu bo ri'i shan lam bgyis nas slad nas kyang skyor mo lung du phyin/ yab yum dgongs par yod pa'i bka' dbang 'ga' rim can du phul zhing/ de'i dus nub cig ma gcig gi
nam mkha' sgo 'byed kyi byin rlabs shig yab yum lhan cig phul bas/ dpon sa'i drung ye shes babs pa'i sku nyams chen po'i 'gyur ba snang cing dbyings rig ji lta ba'i dgongs
don 'grub pas bar chad kyi mtshan ma rang sar grol nas gdung brgyud lhums su zhugs pa sogs bkra shis kyi sgo phye ba'i legs byas 'bad rtsol gyis bsrung ba sogs kyi byed
pa la ma ltos par byung zhing/ spyir sngon gyi dus bdag gi bla ma rje btsun rin po che sbas pa'i sangs rgyas bzang po ba bzhugs thog tsam du gnang zhing/ der nub gcig
gi zhag sa dang/ rje btsun ma'i drung du bsnyung gnas kyi gug pa cig mdzad nas gtsang phyogs la phebs pas/ gser mdog can tshor paN chen dang mjal nas zhal 'phros la rgyu
mtshan phul pas/ paN chen rin po che'i gsung gis de rten 'brel lhag par ma yag der tshogs 'khor cig dgos rgyu yin pa la longs spyod kyi gangs stong sogs kyi rten 'brel yod/
da khyed rang mi sleb na yang nye 'brel lam slob ma 'dra bas rje btsun ma'i drung du tshogs 'khor cig phul na legs gsung ba rna bar yod pas snga phyir skyor mo lung du
bsdod ring sngas mgor 'bral med byas nas tshogs brgya tsam dang rjes 'brel du yang yang mgor blangs pa'i smon lam sems tshims

nges shugs bskyed nas btab cing/ slar rje btsun ma nyid kyi pho brang re gcig gi dgon par nub mo gcig phyed du nyal ba'i sngas mgor spyan drangs nas de nub ri bo dge ldan pa'i
gnas yin pas tshogs 'khor sogs la dgag dgos che bar snang yang dngos grub kyi gnas la re ba'i dung ba ches che ba'i dbang las 'jigs med kyi spobs pa bskyed de rje btsun
ma la dar kha mdog lnga'i snyan dar/ gser zho gang gi dkar me/ lhag par thod pa chang gis bkang pa cig phul/ rang gis kyang dpa' ma zhum par tshogs kyi zas la tshim par
longs spyad cing/ oM gsum ma brgya rtsa brgyad kyi zhal skyin blangs nas nyal rmi lam gyi 'char sgo ni ci yang ma byung ngo//snga rting du rje btsun ma la gser chab dang
na bza' yid ches pa yang nas yang du phul bas blo bde chen po'i tshim pa yang thob/de nas sga la la byas nas 'phan yul gyi shar 'bum pa mjal te stag lung du phyin pas rin
po che'i drung byang phyogs nas phebs pa dang sna thug tsam byung/ der gang legs kyi zhu ba snyan du btab nas skyar log byas/ skyor mo lung zhabs drung du yang ngal gso
tsam las skyid chags ma byas par lam bsrangs gong dkar zhabs drung tshor yang ma mjal bar gan pa la la byas ngur smrig mi sgrol ma la sngar rgyun gyi smon lam zhu ba sogs
dang phyag mjal snyan dar sgron pa rnams byas rjes/ g.yung la byas rgyal rtse la phyin sde pa yab yum sras bcas la bka' dbang mang du phul/ gzim gshegs gtsor yang de mthun
tshe dbang brgya rtsa sogs dang/ lhag par dpal 'khor lo bde chen bla brang dkar por mkhan rin po che'i zhal snga nas kyi thugs dam gsar bzhengs

rnams la rab gnas zab rgyas dang/ lam dus bso chog sgrol ma rnam par rgyal ma'i tshe sgrub lan gsum btud mar phul nas lam shar/ bsam grub rtse nas rgyal rtse'i 'bul ba rnams
gser mdog can du dgu chos kyi thug tshul la phul nas/ gang la yang ma 'grim par ri khrod chen por zla ba bcu pa'i tshes bcu la sleb/ der rim can du chos rgyal yab sras
rnams kyang phebs nas gzhi byes zhal rgyas pa'i bkra shis zhal dro thugs dgyes pa'i ngang kho nas 'da' ba byung/ der lo dus kyi dun khrid kyang btsugs/ chos rje nub dgon
pa byams pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa dpon slob phyogs nas byon pa rnams la shang chos rgyas pa rang gi thugs bzhed bsgrubs te/ snga gong du sbyor drug gi tshogs chos btsun
ma blun mo sgrub pa mor ming bzhag de kun gyis tshig gi zur tsam la yang go rtogs til 'bru gcig mi snang yang/ rigs ldan chos kyi rgyal po chen po nyid chos yun ring thung
ci byung la log nas snyan gtod pa gnang ba'i thugs kyi re ba rdzogs phyir du rgyud 'brel dpang bzhag gi bla ma brgyud pa'i byung tshul sngon 'gro'i spyi bshad dang/ khyad
par gyi khrid tshul rnams rgyas pa'i sgo nas legs par grub rjes/ mchog dbang la lho byang gi sku ngo lnga gdan 'dzom gyi gtso mdzad mi stong phrag gsum dang brgyad brgya
tsam la gong ma'i dbang bzhi cho ga ji lta ba'i spod chog bgyis nas/ sde pa lho pas gtso mdzad rnams dngos gzhi dam po'i bcad bya'i sku mtshams la bzhugs shing/ nub
dgon pa dpon slob pas gtso mdzad phyogs kyi rtogs ldan pho mo gsang sngags rnying ma ba dang ri bo dge ldan pa yang 'ga' re 'dus pa la shangs chos bshad pa rgyas shing

dmigs pa 'gril ba dang dbang byin rlabs la yang lhag chad med pa'i 'jur ba rang byin gyi mtshams ring tshul la ma chad par byas/ der sgrub pa mo rnams dang lhag par khrid gsar
pa'i skyes pho mo rnam pa'i sgom sran byed cing lta stangs sogs la chos rgyal chen po'i drung thugs ldan par dgyes pa'i gzengs bstod yang yang dang/ deng sang gangs can
gyi khrod na sgom sha ma kha yod lag yod dngos mthong 'di las lhag pa med nges shes gsung ba'i thag chod kyang gnang/ der sgom 'debs thebs gsum dang nyams lta gsum gyi
bsrang nas bston te slar ngo sprod kyi lam du 'dren pa'i tshe yang/ rang zhal lta ba rang bzhin rgyal ba'i rigs de yis/ sems kyi zhal mthong snying por brgyud la khyer pa'i
dus/ 'dris shing bsgom pas dka' thub skya bar chud pa'i dus/ yul de sngon du gyur bas mkhyen pa'i ye shes thob/ ces pa'i gnad gzung ste ngo sprod mthil phyin du btab
pas/ chos kyi rgyal po chen po pa de nyid kyi snga gong paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang las zab lam rdo rje'i rnal 'byor nyams khrid du bzhes pa dang/ rgyud pa nas brgyud pa'i
bka' babs pa'i mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas dus kyi 'khor mo'i chos skad grub mtha' ma lus pa thugs su chud pa'i dbang las/ dus 'khor rig gnas kyis rgyan pa'i smra
ba po ma lus pa'i sbyin pa'i zhing sa gshin pa nyid du snang zhing/ de skabs bdag cag la yang rang res ri khrod chen po'i gdan sa 'di la zhabs drung nyid nan ltar du gsol
ba btab pa la mdo don byung zhing/ nges don gyis bstan pa'i bsrog rtsa 'thud pa lta bu'i bka' drin zla med du bskyangs ces lan gcig lan gnyis min par

gsung gi sems la spro ba bskyed par mdzad cing/ thugs brel che bzhag chung bzhag nas ri khrod kyi dben gnas pa rdo ri brag brtsub pa nyi ma tsam yang dus su mi 'char ba dang
bskyod snga ba'i ma 'jen pa de la thugs sun mi gnang bar bzhugs par mdzad/ der khrid grol dang bstun nas chos kyi rgyal po chen po lha rtse 'phrul gyi pho brang ga la bar
gshegs/ spyir nged rang rim gro sogs kyi spros pa ye mi 'dod kyang rang re'i rta mgrin zhus pa'i bla ma byams pa dkon mchog dpal bzang pa'i zhal slob dam tshig can yin
pa'i mos zhen gyis chos rje nub dgon pa dpon slob rnam pas/ kun mkhyen dus gsum sangs rgyas kyi yang lhag pa'i lhar mdzad snang ba kun mkhyen gyi thugs dam bris sku'i rta
mgrin mdun du khong dpon slob rnam pas yang gsang khros pa'i gtor bzlog cig byed du bcug nas 'bul ba sogs kyang gzab par byas/ de mthun chos mdzad kun dga' legs grub pas
dbu skra bcad nas dge bsnyen gyi bslab pa nos pa'i rab ston rgya che spangs mtho ba rang gong nas rin po che'i bka' drin du mdzad/ der dgun khrid grol rjes mdog lor dge
sbyor kha ton dmar tsam yong la re'i 'dun pas phyin pa la smon 'gror sleb skabs/ bzang ldan chos sde chen po nas slob dpon rnam pas gsung ngag cig 'chad pa la yong dgos
pa'i yi ge sleb byung pas/ gong nas kyi bka' zhal la da res sku mtshams kyi bar chad yin nges shing phugs sku tshe'i bar chad du yang 'gyur srid pas da lan mdog lo'i gzim
phug gsar bzos rang du sku mtshams bcad bya dam pa gnang ba legs pa'i bka' nan ches che ba rang byon pa gnang ba la/ sngar

bdag cag skye yul gyi stabs ngor pa'i lam 'bras la sbyangs pa yin/ pha yul du lo re bzhin tshar re bshad dbus gtsang du ngor lugs ma cher gyi 'gro phan yang ma byung/ da res
bzang ldan pa rnams chos rje rin po che sangs rgyas rin chen pa'i rgyud 'dzin sha stag yin dus lam 'bras tshar gcig 'chad pa la 'gro ba yin byas nas sleb nyin nas chos
kyi dbu btsugs pas/ byang phyogs kyi bla ma slob dpon/ gzhan don gyi khur yod yongs 'dus nas chos rje rtse bas gtso mdzad dge bshes sbyangs pa sngon song rang da lta bla
ma slob dpon gyi ming bzhag nyi shu rtsa bdun tsam gyi dbu mdzad snang gsum la tshogs pa lhag par che zhing/ sngags lam man tshogs pa bzhi brgya lhag tsam la zla ba gsum
gyi ring snga chos dgongs chos gnyis ni tshod sor gang la yang snga phyi med pa'i tshogs chos spyi dang/ snga dgongs kyi bar lto thon 'phral po ti dmar chung sogs zur chos
gzhan don nus ldan gyi bla ma slob dpon rnam pa la gsol ja sbyor re'i ring zur du byas nas/ lam 'bras lam skor zhar byung gi gdams pa ma lus pa'i dbang byin rlabs la mthar
thug pa'i bar dang/ phyogs nas byon pa'i bla ma slob dpon rnams la sgrub pa lung sbyin la thug pa dang/ gzhung bshad kyang dang por gsungs pa'i a seng ma/ bar du gsungs
pa'i sras don ma/ mthar gsung pa'i gnyag ma/ gzhan dmar ma man ngag gi gter mdzod sogs lung rgyun rang re la yod dgu shog bu gcig ma chad par bklags shing/ chos skyong
gi phrin las sgrub pas chos bar chad med par mthar phyin cing rang re'i lag nas g.yu stong ri ba cig dang/ gser zho snga rting du bcu gnyis/ ja

sig gcig rnams dang/ gong nas rin po ches sa zhing stobs cher gnang bas lo dus kyi kyai rdo rje'i bsgrub mchod de yang chog mi dang zhag grangs spar ba'i sngar chos rje sangs
rgyas rin chen pas btsugs pa'i sgrub mchod la zhabs 'debs su dmigs nas byung zhing/ lhag par phrin las kyi snying por gyur pa btsun gsar bzhi brgya drug cu re lnga'i skra
bcad/ bslab pa phog cing ming gi thog mar bdag rang gi skra bcad kyi bla ma rje btsun kun dga' mchog grub kyi mtshan gyi thog ma kun dga' 'ba' zhig btags shing/ bsam
pa la yang bla ma rin po ches bdag gcig pu'i skra bcad pa'i bka' drin du mdzad pa'i drin bzor bdag gis da lo rang la kun dga'i ming can 'di tsam bskrun bsam pa'i dga' ba
dpag tu med pa yang byung/ der zla ba gsum lhag tsam du chos 'chad bskyangs rjes/ slar ngam rings su yongs rmi lam la gur mgon rtsub 'gyur gyi rnam 'phrul sna tshogs rang
'dug pas bskangs gso cung rgyun ring pa tsam cig sku rim du che ba zhus nas bskang gso zab rgyas rang brgya thar gsum btud/de nas dbyar chos stengs su na ning gi rdo rje
phreng ba'i dbang zhabs de mkhan slob rnams la 'bul thub na bsam de'i dgug sdod dang/ hor bzlog la dmigs pa'i rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi zhal 'bags mtshar du che ba zangs la
bsgrubs/ dbu rgyan sogs rin po che'i phra tshom dang/ spyan yang shel can du byas pa'i sngon med cig chos mdzad kun dga' bas 'phrul du byas/ dbyar chos ring chos sde chen
por skyas nas mkhan chen rin po che dbu mdzad slob dpon rnam pa gnyer bdun tsam la sngar gyi rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang zhabs

lus pa de slar sta gon nas skyar te phul/ tshogs chos la sgrub thabs rgya mtsho dang/ mkhan chen na rims sku tshe thung tsam du mngon pa'i gegs sel kho na la dmigs snang dmigs
thams cad rgyal ba tshe 'dzin dbang por gsal btab pa'i tshe khrid grub rgyal ma'i dmigs pa re phul/ gzhan pa dge ldan so so'i rang rang gi 'dod mos ltar dbang rjes gnang
grangs dang tshad du ma gzung bas nyin mtshan chad pa med par tshogs pa gsum stong mi tshad pa'i thugs kyi re ba yongs su bskangs te/ rang gi yang mi lus thob pa don
yod pa'i zang zing ma mchis pa'i chos kyi sbyin pa bla na med pa lhug par sbyin pa'i phrin las phul du byung ba'i gnas skabs 'di nyid do ces re zhig brjod pa'i sgor gyur
pa yang de tsam ste/ dbri bsnan med pa'i sargar phye ba'i li khi tam/sngon las bsags khyab nam mkha'i mtha' khyab pa/'di la brdzun bral rjes su dpogs pas shes/da lta'i las
snang yongs la dag pa'i sems/'di la'ang g.yo med rim gyis rjes su spyod/rgyal ba ston pa bstan pa 'ba' zhig gi/phyir zhing 'breng la phyogs cha'i nye ring spangs/chos bzhin
spyod las gzhan pa'i yid ches chad/rang rang phyag bzhes yin pas ci zhig go//rig byed gzhung lugs yig mangs bslab sbyangs mkhas/rtsa rlung gnad 'doms mu stegs rdzu 'phrul
che/sngags kyi bzlas brjod gting zab dka' thub brtson/de dag lam gol sangs rgyas bstan las 'byol/khrims gtsang thos pa'i spyan gsal sgrub ma gzhol/de 'dra'i skyes bu
gang na bzhugs kyang rung/gus pa'i thal sbyor ci nus mchod pa'i yul/mchog dman ma mchis gtsug tu thod bzhin len/deng sang

brtul zhugs mchog 'dzin ci chos mkhan/thos pa'i tshig 'bru rang blo'i lam du 'dren/sgom pa'i yid dpyod pho tshod yus po che/gang la bsams kyang mchi ma rnam par bkru/bdag blo
gti mug sbyangs pa'i gnas phra ba/chen po mgu ba'i rnam dpyod cang ma mchis/rang sems dpang bzhag grogs mkhar sbrang rtsi'i dpe/yun du sbyangs pa'i legs byas cung zhig
snang/tshig gi lam la 'bru len yid la bzhag/don gyi gnas la phra zhib ring du bsal/tshig don rab 'byor mi brjed gzungs su bsten/bslab sbyangs g.yel med bgyis pas 'gyod pa
bral/rang rang bla ma slob dpon gsung bgros tsam/rmongs dad snying la bzhag nas chos spong spangs/'gro ba'i bla ma rgyal mchog shAkya'i tog/de gsung dri med yid ches snying
por bzhag/mos yul gus pas zhabs la phyag bgyi'i gnas/chos kyis sbrel ba'i bla ma la gzhan su/gting mtha' mi mngon dal pa'i chos kyi gnad/gsung rab las gzhan smra po
gang gis ston/rang bzhed grub mtha'i nges gzung 'di'o ces/nan gyis bka' stsal de la chos rtags min/shes rab mig gis gzhung rgya bltas pa'i tshe/'khrul med ngo mtshar ltad
mo ring nas mthong/bde gshegs bka' yi bla mas bdag bskyangs pas/ma nor ma 'dres chos kyi gnad don rig/phan tshun chos tshul gnod pa'i sgor zhugs pa'i/bla ma'i tshogs la'ang
gus pas phyag bgyi'o//ces sngar bris pa'i rnam thar zur 'debs kyi yang rgyan du brjod pa 'di yang lha'i lcam gcig bde skyid dpal 'dzom gyis nan gyis yang dang yang du
bskul 'debs mdzad pa'i

zhal ngor/ mang du thos pa'i dge slong rnal 'byor spyod pa 'jam mgon grub pa'i dpa' bo dpal ldan kun dga' grol mchog blo gsal rgya mtsho'i sdes rgyal po'i pho brang byang ngam
rings kyi bya 'dabs chen por yi ger bkod pa'i bgyi ba po ni/ mos ldan smin grol rgyal mtshan zhes bya bas bgyis so//rnam thar spel rgyan nor bu'i do shal/

shre ya sestu/'jam des zhi dul mgon med yid bso'i gnyen//sgrub pa'i dpa' bo yongs la'ang dkon par snang//dpal ldan 'gro kun dga' ba'i smin grol mchog//blo gsal rgya mtsho'i
sde yis yun du sbyangs//yong dal dag pa'i rang snang ris med pa//kha tsam ma lags snying nas sems par bgyis//phyogs bral nye ring spangs pa'i phan bde'i blo//gzhan ngor
ma zad yin la lan brgyar bzhag//'di na pha rol phun tshogs la sdang bas//yid khro'i me chen 'bar ba'i kun rtog can//dag snang bud shing bsreg la brtson pa dag//bdag la brten
nas dmyal bar 'gyur ta re//kye ho ji ltar bgyis na bzlog par nus//ri gzar rbab dang cong rong chu rgyun ltar//gyen du 'dren pa'i thabs stobs 'bad pas ci//ngang gis ngan
'gro'i 'bab stegs gzhogs 'cha'i gnas//mngon shes mig nyams rmu thom long ba'i tshogs//gcig la gcig bsten gar 'gro'i lam ma dmigs//'ol tshod gom stags brdeg 'chos lag sbrel
nas//rab

dma'i mnar med khang par lhan cig song//snying rje'i dbang sgyur dman la rab chags pas//mgon med skyabs bral de dag 'dren pa'i ched//byams pa'i lcags kyus 'dzin la rjes phyogs
pa//shugs drag phan sems 'bad nas bgyid par smon//kye hud pha mar mi 'dzin khrel shor bu//phan btags lan du gnod pa'i bsam sbyor can//'di de ji bzhin dus mtha'i rang
bzhin gyis//yid klong sems kyi tsher ma zug ngu'i mtshon//e ma chos kyi bdud rtsi yi//rnyed pa'i lam du dug chu'i chag//dmod tshig mtshon rnon sbyin pa po//gdug pa'i slob
ma 'di re mtshar//bzo 'bras yon tan rgyan phreng ni//rnyed dka'i rnor bu'i do shal nyid//byang chub sems kyi lang tsho yi//bzhin ras mdzes pa'i dpal du gyur//bsam chung
tshe 'dis yid bskul nas//chos ltar ston la'ang yid chags pa//skal chad de dag mthong thos skabs//nges par 'byung zhing 'chi ma bkud//chos phyir snyan grags ring dor zhing//dka'
ba'i khur chen brgya phrag blangs//lhag bsam dag pas legs stsal na'ang//gzhan don mi 'gyur 'di re ko//rang sems spangs yin rang ched bral//gzhan phan ris med gzhan
don bsam//bstan pa'i khur khyer bstan pa'i rgyun//mi nyams 'dzin phyir mi lus blangs//sna tshogs chos tshul 'bum phrag gi//dbang lung gdams pa'i gnyer kha ba//gang la gang
'dod chos kyi sgo//'di na 'byed la rang dbang thob//de yang/ dpal ngam rings kyi chos grwa chen po'i 'dus pa'i dge

'dun la chos kyi sbyin pa zang zing ma mchis pa'i rnyed pas thugs kyi re ba yongs su bskangs zhing chos smra'i chos kyi khri chen po de nyid kyi gdan seng ge'i khri la chos
'chad kyi mtha' bsten du gyur pa'i tshig tu brjod pa yang/dpal ldan rigs brgya'i gtsug na rdo rje 'dzin//'gro kun dga' ba'i smin grol phrin las can//mchog gi 'dren pa blo
gsal rgya mtsho'i sdes//tshe rabs kun tu rjes su 'dzin gyur cig//ces shis brjod dang 'brel bar ma 'ongs pa'i skye ba dang tshe rabs rjes 'brel du mar yang 'di ltar dge
ba'i bshes kyi mdun bdar te/ dam pa'i chos ston par shog cig pa'i yid la smon lam thebs par byas nas/ re zhig phyogs de dag gi phrin las kyi 'jug sgo rdzogs pa'i brdar/ chos
kyi khri nas langs ma thag lam bsrangs te/ cang shes kyi bzhon pa la brten nas 'ongs pa'i skabs/ mkhan slob 'dus pa'i tshogs dang bcas pas skyel ma gnang ba la byon zhing/
der lus la gyon pa'i sngon dus kyi gos lu haM ri mo can gyi gong bsdus khyad 'phags dpe bral de yang lus nas bshus te ngam rings mkhan po'i drung gi sku la g.yogs/
chos kyi tshig 'bru ji bzhin du dgongs kyang/ don la yid kyis bdag gir mi len pa'i dge bshes skad du mtshan 'dogs pa rnams la snying rje yang rgya cher skye bzhin pa'i ngang
nas/ ngam rings kyi gnas khang du yongs nas zhag 'ga' ngal gso'i yid bde 'bad med thob rjes/ ston ser gong nas kun dga' rin chen pa sku mched rnam pa gnyis kyis yab mes
kyi phyag bzhes ltar chibs skyel la phebs shing shar phyogs la 'ong pas/ chos rgyal chen po rdzong dpal ldan lha rtse

na bzhugs pa'i drung du slebs/ zhag gsum tsam tshe dbang grangs btab 'bul ba'i bka' lung rjes su bsgrubs shing/ der gser mgur mo so bdun maNDal la bkod nas bstsal ba/ ngam
rings kyi dpyil chos rten la bzhag nas myur bar lam bcad phyin zhing/ gser mdog can du grwa pa rnams bsod snyoms la byon pa'i skabs mi nyung ba'i dus su 'dug pas sngon gyi
bag chags kyi rten mchod rnams la mjal 'dod skyes nas gsang thabs su lam mi 'chag la phyin kyang grwa pa rnams kyis kyang sa sa nas dgongs/ bsod snyoms pa rnams kyang nye
logs na 'dug pas g.yabs nas dge 'dun gsum brgya tsam gyi dbu la bla ma slob dpon rnam pas rgyan pa'i dge slong ma lus pa rnam sbyar gos dar las grub pa'i brjid chags gos
sku spyan 'dren bzhin sku la gsol/ gdugs rgyal mtshan sogs bkod pa khyad par 'phags pa'i bsu ba gya nom pa dang bcas rgya bar gyi tha/ sngar nged rang gser mdog can tshor
sdod skabs gung gser la rtsed mo'i ched yang yang nyul ba'i dben rtsa kha'i chu mig gi mdun ngogs de nas bsu ba mdzad de chos grwa chen po'i bsti gnas ga la ba der dal
gyis phebs pa'i tshe/ skyor mo lung gi chos sde nas paN chen rin po che la phul ba'i rnam sras ser chen rta bdag brgyad po'i 'char dar de rlung gis bskyod pa'i rkyen gyis
nged rang la lan gsum btud mar zhal phyogs byung bas de lo slar yang gser sogs rnyed pa rgya chen po rang yong nges par 'dug go snyam pa'i yid spyod sems la cher te byung
zhing/ der zhag lnga tsam gyi ring bsdad/ gtso bor sngon gyi rten rnams la zhib mjal byas pas rang re'i dmigs yul du

phebs pa'i rten mchod sul cha yang mi 'dug la/ byams khang gi nang ni sngon med pa'i gos dar gyi bla bre 'phan snyan dar sogs 'phel rgyas che ba rang byung 'dug cing/ der zhib
tu dpyad pas gsar bzhengs kyi sa paN gyi sku de sku 'dra yid bzhin gyi nor bu las dbu dpangs mtho bar 'dug pas/ paN chen rin po che dbu 'phangs dma' song bas rten 'brel
du mtshon par 'dug kyang grwa tshang nang gi brjod 'dogs su gsung dogs ngag sgo nas ma shor ba byas/ der bsdod rin 'du khang gsar par 'dus pa'i tshogs la 'jam dbyangs
a ra pa tsa na dkar po lha lnga'i dbang/ 'jam dkar dang mi g.yo ba dkar po'i rjes gnang gsum bgyis shing/ snye mo bye mkhar nas spyi bsod pa tshan cig byon byung pa la chos
'brel du/ rje btsun phyogs las rnam rgyal nas brgyud paN chen rin po che la bka' babs pa'i dbyangs can ma dkar mo'i rjes gnang/ bla brang du dbon po chos mdzad 'ba' zhig
la bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang cha gcig dang/ drung nas dpal mchog pa la dgos su sku rkyang la yab bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang bskur phul/ sngon slob gnyer skabs la lo
bslong du phyin nas ngo shes pa'i span gzhung ba'i rgan gsum mi dmangs dang bcas pa tshe dbang grub rgyal ma zhig kyang khrom chos su bgyis/ da res mang ja bskol ba sogs
ni ci yang ma byas/ mkhan slob sogs kyi gnang sbyin rnams kyang dar kha cig kyang ma khyer/ mnga' ris pa 'ga' res kha che gu gul 'dra phul ba khyer/ gzhan chos phyag kyang
sna gcig ma khyer/ yongs nyin bya rgod phung po'i chos khri'i stengs nas mkhan slob rnam pa lngas gtso mdzad/ dge

'dun span mi dmangs dang bcas pa der tshogs yongs la 'jam dpal mtshan brjod/ ltung bshags/ bzang spyod/ byams smon/ sgrol ma rnams kyi lung bgyis nas khul bu lung bar mkhan
slob rnams kyis gtso mdzad tshogs pa yongs kyis skyel ma gnang zhing/ de nub la'i mdun gyi grong tsho der nyal nas/ myang stod utpa la'i phreng ba kha che ba 'dra ba'i sa
phyogs der phyin/ thog mar shar rgyal po'i pho brang chen por sde bdag sras yum sku 'khor bcas la dbang chos kyi thugs kyi re ba yongs su gang bar byas nas/ de lo'i dgun
khrid jo nang gi chos brgyud 'dzin pa'i myang stod rtse chen gyi chos sder bgyis te/ ri khrod dga' ldan gyi sgrub dpon dang bcas pa'i sgrub pa po kun kyang byon/ skyid
mkhar sogs sngon jo nang pa'i chos lugs la dad pa'i sa phyogs tha dad nas khrid zhu la snyog mi dang/ lhag par bu bu mo khrid la yongs pa'i chos skyel du pha ma ming po sogs
yong ba yang/ chos kyi sgra thos pas slar yid drangs nas khrid rwa nyid du dad mos kyis zhugs pa yang grangs med byung zhing/ rtsa chen nang gi dge 'dun gyi steng du
phyogs pa'i dge 'dun bla ma slob dpon rnams dang/ dpon skya che chung dpag med 'dus pa'i brtse chen gyi 'du khang gi nang du mi shong ba tsam la zab lam gyi sngon 'gro 'thebs
par bkrol zhing/ mkhan po che'i zhabs phyir rin po che gser gling pa dang/ chos rje bse pa'i drung rnams la logs su dbang rdo rje phreng ba dang/ nA ro ni gu'i khrid
byin rlabs rnams kyang nyin re bzhin phul/ mchog dbang skabs mi mangs nas 'du khang du ma shong par seng ge kha'i stengs dang/ lha khang gi sgo khang rnams su yang

dbang mi bsdod dgos pa byung zhing/ khrid kyi dam po ma byed bcings bsten mi grangs btab bzhi brgya bdun cu don lnga tsam grangs 'khrul med byung zhing/ mchog dbang gi nyin
tshos kyi dbur mkhan rin po che yang phebs pa'i ye shes chen po'i gzigs ngor steng gi nam mkhar brgyud pa'i bla ma la lus pa khrom tshogs su bzhugs pa'i nang nas mtshungs
med nya dbon phyag na glegs bam 'od zer sna lnga 'phro ba 'dzin pa'i 'od kyi rtse ma lus pa bdag dbang gi rdo rje slob dpon gyi chas zhugs bal po sanggA shrIs chos rje
sa skya paNDi ta la phul ba'i rgyun drug sde pa shar kha ba'i gan mdzod na bzhugs pa de gyon pa'i rgyan drug gi cha shas so so la reg cing thim pa'i cho 'phrul dang/ bgegs
sprod skabs las can mang po'i mig mthun par bdag nyid rkang pa sa la mi reg par gar bsgyur bar mthon bas yid bskul nas khong rang dag kyang rtsis btab med par lus 'phar
g.yo'i gzhan dbang lhur len pa dang/ 'ga' res bdag nyid khro bo'i dbang po dpal ldan shugs dngos su mthong nas yid ches pa'i dad pas snying brlan par gyur cing/ dbang dngos
kyi skabs dus 'khor dpa' bo lhan cig skyes pa 'od zer brgya stong 'phro ba'i skur dbu mdzad chen mo bas gsal bar gzigs zhes gsung zhing/ rang gi yid la yang sngar dang
mi 'dra ba'i ye shes chen po'i snang ba rab 'byams 'bad med lhun grub tu byung ba yang/ bdag gis sbyor drug gi khrid dbu tshugs nyin nas bzung ji srid khrid kyi bka' rgya
ma grol ring la tshogs su khrid chos 'chad du 'gro gong rtse chen bla brang shar cher na bzhugs pa'i 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang po'i sku gdung drung du nyin

re bzhin bkra shis kha dag cig gis sna grangs pa'i dar chen dpus grus kha dog so so'i snyan dar re re/ spos mar me lha shos maNDal so bdun ma yan lag bdun pa dang sbrel ba'i
phyag mchod smon lam bgyis pa'i thugs rje nyid du mngon zhing/ de mthun grub chen kun dga' blo gros pa'i sku gdung sho ma ri chung na bzhugs pa'i drung du yang snyan dar
dkar me sogs yang yang phul/ snying nas smon lam dang gsol btab bgyis so//de dus mchog dbang yan la gser mgur mo so bdun 'grig pa dang ras yug po bdun rnams gser mdog can
du dgun chos kyi thug tshul la phul bas sngon med kyi thug tshul byung skad cing/ mchog dbang phyin nas sbyor drug nam grol ring la byung ba'i gser rnams la zho so bdun
byung ba chos kyi grol ston dang bsngo ba'i rgyas 'debs rten du zab lam rdo rje'i rnal 'byor gyi ting nge 'dzin 'khrul med ye shes chen po dngos su gzigs pa'i mkhan rin
po che'i drung du phul zhing/ khrid pa rnams kyang gegs med ye shes kyi lha mig rnam par dag pa'i skal ba mchog gi las can 'ba' zhig tu gyur la/ dad mos kyi 'bul 'degs kyang
blo'i yul 'das rang byung ba dag kyang gang la gang 'os kyi sbyin pa'i zhing dag la ser sna med par sbyin la/ de dus khrid de ring grol rgyu'i tho rangs bdag gi sngas
mgor mkha' 'gro ma shing lo'i gos can zhig gis khyod kyi nges don zab mo'i bstan pa spel ba'i legs dar du byung shambha la'i pho brang gi ma la ya'i bskyed tshal nas khyer
yongs pa yin zhes a ru ra rlon pa yongs su smin pa'i 'bras bu ro dro ba'i mchog bdud rtsi bsil dngar dang bcas pa gcig dngos

su bstsal ba bdag gi lag tu lon dus ni rgya kham smin shos ltar nyor mo la/ phyogs shig nas khu bcud brdol la khad snang ba la khas 'jib pas sngon chad lces ma myog ba'i mngar
la dwangs pa'i bcud kyi rgyal po bre gang tsam zhig gi btung ba khog tu song mthar/ bdag gi lag pa gnyis kyis snyim pa'i nang du 'dus pa tsam la bzo mdog a ru ra gser
mdog mchog gi bzo dbyibs dang mdog tu snang zhing/ der mi su la yang ma bstan par tshags byas chos grol nas gnas rnying du 'bod mi byung nas phyin/ slar rgyal rtser sde
pa rin po che la rdo rje phur pa'i stod las smad las kyi dbang dang mgon po'i me 'bar ma'i lung/ chos skyong gi bka' bsgo nang khrid sogs phul nas dgun dus drang reg khyad
du bsad de stag lung gi dngul sku bde mchog thub chen sogs kyi rab gnas la shar phyogs la rta kha bsgyur nas/ shar lam snang dkar rtse sde pa sku mched drung du tshe dbang
chos skyong che chung gi rjes gnang sogs dgongs pa ltar phul/ bsam sdings nas rje la ye shes lus can mas gdan bzhugs gnang byung ba'i lan dus tig sogs 'bul ba bgyis nas
lam bsrangs/ zhabs drung skyor mo lung du zhag 'ga' bsdad rjes rab gnas rang la rkang gtad stag lung du phyin nas gtsug lag khang gsar bzhengs nyid du rten mchog gsar
bzhengs gnang ba kun bsgrigs te/ rab gnas rten gyi dkyil 'khor bde mchog nag po pa la brten dkyil 'khor rdul tshon du bzhengs shing/ sngar mkha' 'gro mas mngon sum du bstsal
ba'i a ru ra'i rgyal po sman mchog dpe bral de nyid kyang bde mchog dngul sku'i mgrin par bzhugs su gsol dgos

pa yin zhing/ da lta gzhan gyis byad kha la brten chos rje sku mched gsung 'dzer ba'i gsum 'byed kyi byad 'grol dang/ dus rnyigs pas sems can kun kyang gre gag sogs nad mang
pos gzir ba'i nad sel gyi rten 'brel rmad byung du yang blos dmigs pa'i dad mdun cher yod na'ang/ nged slob gong du bde mchog gi gzer rnams bsdams tshar nas re ba ma rdzogs
shing rten 'brel de dag gi sgo yang ma 'grig la 'on kyang rang las la rang mi'i dper byas nas rab gnas kyi bkra shis rdzas brgyad kyang bil ba byis pa'i mgo tsam dang/
de dang mnyam pa'i shing gi sar bu gsum la gser gyis rgyan bkod byas pa'i nang du/ nyung kar/ ghi haM/ li khri/ rgya gar gyi rdza ma bzo khyad can khra mo'i nang du zho/
dur ba sbom khra zheng la sor bzhi bdal ba dang/ ring thung rkang gang pa tshigs gsum yod pa'i blo 'das kyi mgo mjug dngul gyis bstums nas gser gyi za ra tshags byas pa/
me long yang mtho gang sgor mo la 'od zer pa tra'i ri mo 'phul 'bur dod gser chus byugs pa/ dung dkar la yang bkra shis rtags brgyad gzab nas brkos dngul shog gser gyi
padma'i kha rgyan can rnams dang/ phub chen sgor mo gnyis la mar gyis tshon gyur byas pa'i 'khor lo dang nor bu legs par bcos nas yon bdag kham gzugs skye sgo can rigs gtsang
gnyis kyis phrag pa la khur ba dang/ btsun mo rin po che lha zhal gzab legs dang rgya gar gyi rgyal mo'i gzugs bsgyur/ blon po yang lha 'bag thod can rgya'i nang blon
gzugs la kha spu ring po'i gzugs bsgyur dang/ glang po glang gdong lus sogs ras khrug la bsgrubs shing/ mche ba'i

gzugs 'jam shing las 'khrul byas/ zangs gser las gdong rgyan dang drwa phyed/ dril bu g.yer kha yang bsnyims pa kha sbyar tsam gyi brjid bag bcos pa dang/ rta mchog chibs dngos
mdog sngon po zhig la sga chas gzab pa rang gi bkod pa khyad du 'phags pa la kong gzugs kyi gzhogs lha phrug 'dra ba'i sna khrid dang/ dmag dpon skyes bu lus rtsal yod
pa'i khrab rmog gi ya lad can ral gri 'dzin bzhin pa dang bcas sna tshogs rol mo dang rgya gling sogs kyis sna drangs pa'i mngal dbul gzab par byas la/ gzhan yang zhal
dro'i rgyas pa'i sbyin bsreg dang gar gyi mchod 'bul rnams bgyis pa'i mthar/ kho bo nyid kyi lus la gos mtshal kha 'jam byus la gos nal ser ri mo can gyi mtha' chag dang
me long byas pa'i chos gos thang rkyang cig gyon/ gos gser ma'i sgom zhu thel lugs brjid chags shig gyon nas rang nyid kyi chos las skyes pa'i sras kyi mthu bo/ ngo mtshar
mchog gi sprul pa'i sku ngag dbang bkra shis rnam rgyal grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po mched bcas 'dus pa'i dge 'dun dang bcas pa'i me tog gi phreng ba'i bsil mas
lhag gnas kyi mnga' gsol rgyas par phul nas/ rab ston sogs la zhag bcu gnyis bsdad rjes/ byang lam la byas snye mo brgyud nas dus btab steng du myur bar lam bcad de yar
lam bye mkhar du 'bod mi byung pa ltar phyin/ kun mkhyen 'dzam gling pa rang gi gtso mdzad tshogs pas bsu ba sogs srid zhu phun tshogs gnang/ rje nyid kyis gtso mdzad tshogs
pa yongs la chos 'brel du rje btsun phyogs las rnam rgyal ba'i thugs dam lha lnga'i rjes gnang bgyis shing/ mang ja/ tshogs pa'i

mi re la dar ngos skal re'i kha 'gyed dang/ chos rje'i drung du 'bul ba rgya chen po'i bsngo rten dpus dag kyang byas nas nyes skyon med par zla ba gsum pa'i tshes bcu bzhi
la smon gror slebs shing/ de ngam rings kyi chos sder ja sig brgyad/ bzang ldan du bzhi/ gser mdog can du tshes lnga la dmigs pa'i ja sig bzhi/ lo chen drung du ja sig sbrel
dang kha btags dkar po brgya rtsa brgyad/ rin po che thugs rje dpal ba la rten khebs cig/ mchog gi rdo rje slob dpon rab gsal zla ba mgon po la dngul skyogs dang/ dung
gi rta chas legs pa/ ja bzang ba sig gcig/ jo nang du ja tshab nas je bre'i khal lnga brgya'i sgrub rgyags bkye zhing/ de nas byang du bka' lung bzhin phyin mtshams zla
ba bzhi pa'i tshes brgyad dang dgu la bde mchog nag po pa'i ras bris la brten pa'i dbang dang/ tshes bcu la rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sindhu ra'i byin rlabs gsan pas de nub
kyi tshogs grol rjes bsnyung ba'i tshul bstan nas/ sa ga'i tshes bcu bdun gyi srod chen la dpon pa lha lcam de nyid rang gnas mkha' spyod kyi gnas la bzhud de/ de 'phral
du lha sar jo bo rin po che la dkar me'i rgyur gser ga chung ngu gcig dang/ gos lu nyig gi snam sbyar smon lam gyi yi ges brgyan pa/ drang srong rin po ri dang re sag
gi jo mo gnyis la yang snyan dar yig sbyar/ sta lung vc: stag lungdu rten bzhengs rgyu la gser zho brgya dang/ gser mdog can du gser sa thig mgur zho nyi shu rtsa bzhi 'gor
pa dang/ bya rgod gshongs su bsil ma zho nyi shu rtsa bzhi rnams mang ja'i rgyur phul zhing/ sku gdung chas 'jug dang rjes 'brel du cho ga bkod nas rdo rje rnal 'byor
mar

bskyed de mchod yul du bzhugs pa'i spyan sngar rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i cho ga rgyun mi 'chad dang bcas oM gsum ma nyin khri mtshan khri dgung zhag ma rdzogs bar byas/ rjes
su yang dus dran bar cho ga chag med dang/ dgung zhag ring ma rdzogs bar sgo spel nas yod pa'i chos rje mkhas mchog pas gtso mdzad la mang ja sbyor gsum ma sogs 'phral dang
spun gyi bsnyen bskur 'bul ba gzab rgyas bgyis/ na bza' 'bul gyi nyin 'ja' sprin ngo mtshar ba dang/ me tog gtso bor nas khang rang gi steng du 'bab phul che ba byung/
'ja' sprin kha dog sna lnga yang nas khang rang gi steng du 'khor ba mthong zhing/ dgung zhag grol nas kyang zla ba brgyad pa'i tshes bcu'i bar/ bdag gis sngar rgyun las
ma g.yos pa'i cho ga'i rgyun dang/ oM gsum ma'i bzlas pa sngar ltar ma chag pa byas rjes zla ba de nyid kyi tshes bcu gcig la sta gon dang/ bcu gnyis kyi nyin dngos gzhi
byas pa'i dge bcu pa dpon slob bcu gsum gyi lu hi pa dang/ lo phu ba dpon slob bcu gsum gyis dril bu pa zhig dgon pa dpon slob bcu gsum gyis nag po pa'i dkyil 'khor zhal
phye nas lta bu dril nag gsum gyi bsgrub mchod mdzad pa'i yon du chos rje rnam pa gsum po re re la bkra shis kha btags re/ rab dkar chag med re/ dngul gzang re/ sked rags
ser po dang dngos gtsang re/ zhwa mo re/ spos chag re/ rgya dril spus dag re/ dngul gyi ka pa la kha gcod dang bcas pa re/ gser zho re/ dge ldun mi re la spen 'dab re re
rnams phul/ de'i nub bdag gis me chog byas nas a ka ru

nag po dang/ tsan dan dkar po'i bud shing gis sku gdung yongs su sbyangs shing/ de nub nam mkha' la sprin dmar po'i dbyibs kyis rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sku ri bo tsam gsal
bar bstan rjes/ nam mkha'i khyon sindhu ra'i mdog tu 'gyur ba'i 'od kyis ngam ring spyi mtsho yang bsgyur ba byung la/ gdung thal rnams de nub rang mtshor sbyangs shing/
sku gdung dang lhag par thugs lan du mar skyar nas me mchod phul kyang ma tshig par slar mchod pa'i rten du bzhag cing/ dgung zhag rnams la 'ja' 'od dang me tog gi char gsal
bar byung zhing/ gdung tshangs yang rnal 'byor ma'i sa tshar bsgrubs/ grang gser gyis byugs/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i bris sku thog tshad cig 'phral du bsgrubs shing/
gzhan rnal 'byor ma stong sku'i bris thang bcu dang/ kun dril rnal 'byor ma'i dris sku che chung 'dres pa brgya rtsa tsam dang/ tsha rten gyi dbu skra la mang re tsag jo
mo'i 'dra len gyi shing sku dngos byon bzhengs shing/ dus dran gyi bcu bdun mchod la'ang ngam rings byams chen drung du zhal gser la mgur mo sum cu so bdun gyi grang gser
spus dag rang dang/ snyan dar sman tshe dkar khra ser khra yug sne tshang/ ling yug gi 'phan dang/ ngam rings mkhan po la 'bul ba'i bsngo rten gos phyi nang/ ja sig/ rten
khebs gser ma sgo tshad sogs dang/ dge 'dun sum brgya la ras yug sne tshang spus bsgrubs re re phyag tu 'bul ba dang/ gser mdog can du spos shel phreng ba'i thug tshul
gyi rgyu sogs bgyis/ 'di skabs myang stod la yul tsam phyin zhing/ dgun khrid grol rjes rang la stag lung gi 'bul skyel ba byung ba'i stengs nas jo nang du

bre'i sgrub rgyags stong rwa dang/ bde chen/ sangs rgyas gling/ brag ram gsum du nas khal brgya brgya'i dge mthud byas rjes/ ja sig brgya dang gos dar yug lnga bcu phul nas/
byang nas chos gzhi chos lung byang rtse skor dang lus kyi mthongs kyi skor rnams gnang zhing/ chos lung byang rtse'i gzhir yod btsun ma rnams gnas spos shing sgrub sde
gsar 'dzugs kyi lugs byas/ nged rang gis rtag rtse sgal tsam gyi yar phyogs la phyin nas 'phral du log nas yong pa'i mar lam lha chu dus min la gdong du bsu ba'i tshul du
byung ba nas chu phud dkar yol gang btungs shing/ der zhabs drung skyor mo lung gi skor gyi skad bya tshor bas yid 'byung nas chos lung byang rtser zhag 'ga' yid 'pham
pa'i ngang nas mtshams se yod skabs su/ gzims spyil dkar por srin lag g.yon nas khrag gi rgyun brdol bas dbang bskur cig byas rjes/ lho'i mtsho sgo phyogs la 'bod mi'i bya
ma rta zhig gi rkyen sbyar nas phyin pa'i yar lam mang dkar la byas/ rab gsal zla ba mgon po la yang gser srang phyed dang gsol ja bzang ba'i 'bul ba byas nas rje btsun
gyi sgrub gnas cha lung gi gnas skabs bgyis te mtsho sgo'i mdun gyi chu bo che'i rba klongs la mi nyi shu tsam gyis 'dol li la bteg nas phyin pas ya nga la g.yang za'i ngang
nyid nas pha rol du son/ der yang ni gu'i mgyogs khrid dang/ lhag par chos 'khor lhun po nas rje lha btsun pa'i drung la dgos bzhed ltar bka' gdams glegs bam tshang
ba/ thig le'i khrid dang rjes 'brel thig le bcu drug gi dbang/ bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang/ nag po gzhung drug gi lung/ mgon po

gdong bzhi pa'i rjes gnang/ rgyud sde lnga chen mo'i dbang sogs bstan pa'i rgyun la bsam nas phul zhing/ slar yang mtsho sgo nyi nas shar du yong/ drung 'bum ram pa dang mjal/
khong nyid kun mkhyen rin po che'i gdan sar bzhugs pa dang/ skyes yul gyi zhen stabs byas gos phel mtshal kha ri mo can zhig kyang 'bul ba byas shing/ de nas mnga' bdag
rgyal mo dgongs pa'i dbyings ltar rjes su bsgrubs nas lce lung gi rdzong la rab gnas la phyin/ der rgyal rtse nas sde pa'i bka' shog 'bod mi gnang byung zhing/ blo bde
nas kyang sde pa mgon chen pa bsnyung ba thu mo sku srog gi dgag bya la thug pa yod pa'i nan bskyed kyi gsung shog byung yang/ da lta nged lce lung nas gting skyes rang
la lam mi 'chag la 'gro zhing/ da res sde pa mgon chen pa mi gshegs pa'i khag len nged rang gis byed pa'i zhu yig phul ba la/ snyung ba thu ba rang gi sgang yin pas der yid
ches ma byas na'ang/ rjes su de thog tu khel pas slar dad mos 'phel ba byung 'dug/de nas gting skyes mkhar chen gyi gzims khang gsar 'debs rang du zla ba gsum gyi ring
la dga' ldan rtse pa'i gzhi gra dpus gtsang gang yod kyi steng du dgon 'og gi grwa pa dpus sgrugs byas pa'i grwa pa rang brgya dang bdun cu don lnga tsam la lam 'bras smin
pa'i mthar thug pa'i gzhung rkyang rdzogs par bshad cing/ sde pa yab sras kyi gtso mdzad la shin tu spros med kyi zab khrid lag bcangs su bsgril ba dang/ lce lung rdzong
gi mkha' spyod pa'i gdan sa ba la bka' bsdams vc: gdamsglegs bam tshang ba'i dbang lung khrid chos/ la stod lho phyogs nas byon pa'i rtogs ldan chos sku nam mkha'i ming

can sogs khong dpon slob rnams la shangs chos rdzogs pa dang/ gzhan yang bde kyai sogs kyi dbang lung phran tshegs khong rang rnam pa'i zhe 'dod gang yod kyang lhug par byas/
gzims khang gsar pa la rab gnas kyang gzab rgyas bgyis shing/ lam 'bras kyi sems bskyed skabs/ gting skyes nas sde pa rin po che'i drung gis der 'dus kyi dge 'dun skye
bo'i tshogs dang bcas pa la nas 'gyed dang/ rang re la yang bsngo rten du gting skyes bre chen gyi nas dpus gtsang stong rwa gcig gi 'bul ba byung ba la gzhi blangs nas/
dge 'dun nyis brgyas zla ba gnyis kyi ring tal por kha che paN chen gyi lung bstan sgrol ma'i drung du sgrol ma 'bum gter bcu gnyis rgyun cig la gnang bas rang gzhan gyi
bar chad du ma'i sgo gsal ba'i legs tshogs yid ches pa rang byung zhing/ der gting skyes kyi lam 'bras zab rgyas bcu bdun la gral ba'i bco brgyad la shar phyogs la phyin
nas/ thog mar rgyal rtse'i rtse rgyal rang du zhag sbrel tsam ngal gsos nas rtse chen phu'i gad ser dgon par zla ba gnyis nang mtshams bsdams pa'i ring/ mkhan rin po ches
bkas bskul nas paN chen gyi rnam thar rgyas par spel ba'i rtsom pa bgyis shing/ de nyid gser yig tu sgrub pa'i bka' drin yang mkhan rin po che nyid kyis gnang/ de mtshams
rtse chen du zla phyed tsam gyi ring sngar gyi sbyor drug gi zhabs dang ni gu'i dbang khrid sogs mang du bshad nas/ rgyal rtse nas bdag chen che sa rin po che'i bka' bskul
yang yang byung ba ltar gzims khang mngon dgar zla ba gsum gyi ring la thog mar sku mched yab sras kyi gtso mdzad la dbang bskur rdo rje phreng ba dbang

gi mtha' rgyas legs par phul rjes/ gsung ngag cha lag rdzogs pa'i slob bshad dang/ gzhan yang dbang lung rjes gnang dpag tu med pas dgos pa'i dbyings gang bar bgyis shing/
mnga' bdag rgyal mo'i drung gi gtso mdzad la yang ni gu'i dbang khrid rdzogs par bgyis mtshams/ lho mon phyogs kyi phag ri rin chen sgang nas lha pa'i drung gi 'bod mi nan
bskyed yang yang byung ba bzhin/ shing 'bras 'dra za ba dang/ bso yang bsod par 'dug snyam sang 'degs gnang 'degs rang la/ gong nas bka' drin can gyis rtse lnga ye shes
rdzong gi lha khang gsar bzhengs kyi rab gnas la shog gsung pa'i bka' shog phebs pa la bka' drin bsab par dka' ba'i yus kyis yongs nas/ rab gnas kyang bcu bdun mchod stengs
rgyal phur 'dzoms pa'i dus stengs su legs par grub pa'i skabs 'di nyid du/ dbus nas zhabs drung dpon pa khri lcam drung phebs byung ba'i phebs bsu la ri khrod jo nang
du slar log nas/ sku'i dub pa gang bsos kyi dgongs len mtha' dag dang/ tshe dbang brgya rtsa sogs bka' drin rjes dran bgyis shing/ 'di skabs/ lha rtser byang nas chos rgyal
mes dbon rnams kyi drung du mjal ba la phyin/ zhag lnga tsam gyi ring la gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang dang tshe dbang brgya rtsa rnams phul/ slar jo nang du 'khor rjes/
chos rje dar ma ba'i drung dang mkhas mchog grags bzang pa la ni gu'i khrid dang/ gong nas kyi gtso mdzad la rtsa dbu ma'i khrid/ dpon sa bdag mo'i drung du slar yang tshe
dbang brgya tshar/ gzhan yang/ sde pa lha sa rdzong pa la phur pa'i stod las smad las kyi dbang rnams byas

rjes/ nyer bzhi'i rgyal phur 'dzom pa'i 'grub sbyor la/ yang yang bka' tho byung ba bzhin gzhis ka rin chen spungs par phyin/ mar lam gser mdog can tshor mkhas slob rnam pa
lngas gtso mdzad la/ paN chen bzhugs khri'i steng nas rang res brtsams pa'i paN chen rnam thar gyi lung bklags nas ma myur bar bcad de/ tshes gsum la pho brang rin chen
spungs par legs par btol pa'i nyin man lha rdzas me tog dkar po'i char chen nyin re bzhin rgyun ma chad par 'bab pa zhag bdun byung zhing/ sa skyongs mi'i dbang po sde pa
rin po che'i zhabs drung nying du dgongs dbyings bzhin dus 'khor bde mchog gshed dmar sogs dbang grangs mang/ tshe dbang lha dgu/ grub rgyal ma/ tshe rta sbrags ma rnams
kyi dbang brgya tshar gsum/ chos skyong ris mang po'i bka' bsgo/ phyag chen ngo sprod sogs phul zhing/ sde pa rgyal bu'i drung du yang de mthun tshe dbang rnams dang/ gu
ru'i zlum po'i bzhi'i dbang/ rwa lngar dpon su yum chen mo'i drung du yod/ sbyor drug ngo sprod sogs dgos zhes kyi dbang chos phul/ slar ri khrod chen por bar chad kyi mtshan
ma med par slebs mtshams/ gnas rnying rje'i drung du dbang rdor phreng/ sgrub thabs rgya mtsho/ sgrol ma gnyer gcig dang/ dgongs pa'i bzhed rang du snang bas shangs
chos yongs rdzogs sogs dbang 'ong man ngag gis thugs kyi re ba mchog tu bskangs pa'i skabs 'di nyid do//zhes re zhig brjod pa'i sgor gyur pa de tsam de dbri bsnan med pa'i
sargar phye ba'i li khi taM/yid dbang chog shes bral ba'i rlom pa can//nam

yang bde ba'i mal du mnal mi srid//gang byung cis kyang chog pa'i gu yangs po//'char kha'i snang bas bsad par nus ma yin//bslab sbyang 'bad pas rngo thogs bgyis pa'i chos//grog
mkhar sbrang rtsi ji bzhin phra mo'i chad//ma 'dres yongs su brtsegs pa'i thos pa'i nor//dal 'byor don yod bgyis par mtshon dpe'o//zang zing 'byor pas dbul ba'i bsod
snyoms pa//rgya chen thos pas phyug pa'i mdzod ldan bdag//rnam thos dzam lha'i dpal la'ang mi smon pa'i//'phags nor bdun gyis yid kyi dbul ba bsal//'dir snang yud tsam mdang
nub rmi lam bzhin//'phrul shes bden par 'dzin pa'i khrims yod dam//tshe rabs skyid pa'i legs smon dam pa'i chos//gang la'ang thos pa'i bag chags bzhag 'di'o//yang yang
srid pa'i gnas 'dir bdag 'khyams mod//kun tu dge ba'i bshes la brten pa dang//las dkar chos kyi bya bas ma phongs pa'i//mtshams sbyor bzang pos nam du'ang ma btang lags//deng
nas bzung te byang chub bar du yang//rgya chen thos pa'i bya bas mi zhum zhing//zhi ba'i dbyings la ci nas mi sred pa'i//nam yang 'gro ba'i dor la rjes phyogs gyur//gson
yang bya rgyu bstan dang sems can ched//gum par gyur kyang las smon de nyid de//mdor na lus ngag yid kyi bgyi ba'i tshogs//bstan dang sems can don phyir bsngo ba
yin//bskyid par gyur na'ang dkon mchog thugs rje'i mthus//sdug kyang snga ma'i las mdzad yid spro'i ngang//skyid sdug sngang bas lha chos mi 'gog pa//yi dam 'di la nam yang
'gyur ba ci//deng sang

dus kyi mthar lhung khrel bor bas//shes ldan yongs kyang ngan g.yo'i las ma 'jug//ma lus 'gro ba'i bde skyid 'joms byed pa'i//mi zad sdig pa'i las stobs e ma mtshar//blo mig
gsal na las 'bras me long ltos//dkar nag ma 'dres bde sdug 'dren ma'i gzugs//mtho ris ngan 'gro'i gnas bkod ji lta'i tshul//mthong tshe dran pa'i ngang der the le rgyob//kha
drag dpung che nga rgyal ri bo'i spo//cher rlom phal cher dmyal ba'i dngos rgyur mthong//yud tsam mi rtag rtag 'dzin 'khor ba'i gshis//smyon pa'i snang blo'i dpe 'dra
a re sdug//mi rtag mthong yang mi rtag ma dran pa//bdag 'dras gdams ngag brgya phrag bsgoms kyang 'chal//tshe 'di'i bya bas nges par yid skyo ba//de tshe bdag gis bsags
pa don dang ldan//mdor na srid dang zhi la mi gnas pa'i//mtha' bral dbyings der rang sems ngal bsos nas//yang yang mar gyur drangs med sems can tshogs//ris med phan bde'i
dpal la 'god gyur cig//ces sngar bris pa'i rnam thar yang rgyan gyi spel rgyan du brjod pa'i yang// dad ldan 'gas bskul 'debs su bgyis pa'i ngor dge slong rnal 'byor spyod
pa pa// 'jam mgon grub pa'i dpa' bo dpal ldan kun dga' grol mchog blo gsal rgya mtsho'i sdes jo nang gzim spyil du yi ger bkod pa'i bgyi ba po ni mos ldan smin grol
rgyal mtshan zhes bya bas bgyis so// //rnam thar mtshar rgyan/

shrai ya sestu/'jam mnyen mgon gyur grub pa'i dpa' bo ni//dpal ldan 'gro kun rab dga'i smin grol mchog//zab cing rgya che'i chos kyi 'khor lo yang//blo gsal rgya mtsho'i sde
yis rnam par skor//srid pa'i dpal gyis myos pa'i dbang ldan kun//rab dka'i chos kyi snang bas grol ba mchog//rang rang skal pa'i cha shas gyur pa ni//blo gsal rgya mtsho'i
sde yis yang yang sbyin//kun la snyoms pa'i yid dga'i phan sems tsam//rang grol mchog gi sems la bzhag byas te//phyogs su ma chad bde ba'i dbus gang du//chos sbyin zang
zing med pa'i phan bde spel//gang yang gzhan la rab mkhu'i khong khro'i yid//yid kyi khang bu rang snang la mchel dag//dag pa'i snang ba rgya che'i skal dman rnams//rnam
grangs du ma'i snying rje'i gnas su mthong//chos tshul kun snang dwangs pa'i yid kyi mtsho//ma 'dres gsal ba'i gzugs brnyan bye ba brgya//'gal med dad mos snang ba'i rang
babs ni//dpyod ldan mig gi gzigs mor rnam par bkra//'di na snga ma'i las 'phro las//nye bar rnyed pa'i dal 'byor mchog//rnam kun don yod gyur pa yis//bdag yid lan brgyar
tshim par gyur//bka' drin

khur gyis lci ba yis//yongs 'dzin yid bzhin nor bu rnams//chos dbyings rgya mtshor thim gyur nas//srid zhu'i yul gyur skal pa phra//sku brnyan tsam gyi cha shas la//rjes dad
mig chu g.yo bzhin yang//bla mas nor ba'i dus dag la//rjes dran bskul phyed mchod la brtson//gang dag nyi 'od mdun dag tu//srin bu'i me khyer snang 'dzin ltar//dngos nyid
las gzhan 'dra 'bag dag//'bad pa lhur len byis blo'i tshul//bdag ni bsags pa'i mthar lhung pas//yul mchog dngos mthong las gzhan pa'i//rmi lam rol par mjal tsam la//dga'
ba sems 'di tha chad do//e ma dam pa'i mgon gang gi//gsung gi dbyangs snyan rnar len zhing//zhabs pad gus pa'i gtsug rten rnams//dga' ba rgya chen sgom par rigs//de yang
dpal jo mo nang gi ri khrod chen por dus khrid dang rjes 'brel zab lam rdo rje'i rnal 'byor gyi skal bzang ye shes kyi mig can du bsgrub par bgyis pa'i rjes thogs nyid
der jo mda'i 'dom pa'i stod tsam gyi dar zam de la thon nas rgya mkhar brgyud nas de nub smon 'gror nyal/ sang smon 'gro'i phu'i dgon chung gi la la byas chos lung byang
rtser phyin pas la mtshams kyi phag mo dur khrod kyi padma brag khung gi thad der mdze pho thar pa bas stod res dmar po shin tu legs pa kha gsum sbrel cig phul byung bas
kho la mdze byung ba min cing ming la mdze por btags par snang bas bsam dus/ ming grwa la dpags na dam tshig gi sal sel en tsam gyi brda' chos dang/ phugs rje rnal 'byor

mas rjes su 'dzin pa'i rten 'brel du ras dmar dri mas ma gos pa 'od chags 'dir 'dug bsam pa byung nas gzims spyil dkar por oM gsum ma'i bzlas pa ci mang dang/ lho na chos sku

'dug pa la tshe dbang grangs btab mang ba dang/ gtor bzlos sogs sgo du mas da res bsnyung ba dwangs bskyed yod pa byung skabs/ chos sder mkhan rin po che'i sku gdung
gshed dmar la brten pa'i 'od bzhur phul/ nang rten byams pa'i sku la rgyur gser zho bzhi bcu/ dpal 'byor gyi gcig dang zhe gcig phul nas/ pa nams su

dpon sa a khrid kyi mtshan byang bsreg pa'i cho ga lam ston byas/ gzhis kar zhabs drung du do ha skor gsum gyi rnam bshad par phu ba blo gros seng ge'i Tikka'i steng nas zhib
bshad dang/ rje mkhyen brtse rtsom yig zhal len gnang ba'i bsnyel tho gzab rgyas kyang 'bri ba mdzad cing/ rgyal ba'i skyes rabs dpag bsam 'khri shing gi mdo bkod gzab
bris rnams la rab gnas legs par bsgrubs gsung ba'i bka' lung ltar cho ga mthar phyin bgyis nas stag lung la phyin/ sa ga zla ba'i bcu bdun dus chen la stag lung gi chos
grwar sleb/ zla ba de'i gnam gang la rje zla ba mgon po rmi lam du lhag par gsal bar byung bas rkyen byas nas/ mos dungs glo bur ba 'dra bas blo bskul te/ dge 'dun gzhir
bzhugs dpus sgrugs dngos gtsang rang rgya dang/ chos phug dbon chen/ nang so gro lung pa/ chos rje rig 'dzin pa sogs rang re'i rgyun sde brgyad tsam la dbang bskur rdo rje
phreng ba gzab rgyas rang zhig byas shing/ de dus gtso bor dkyil 'khor gang dang gang gi gtso bo bla mar gsal lhag par btab pa'i dbang len pa rang la nan chags lhur len
pa'i rang gdangs blo la 'gag med shar ba cig byung ba rjes su bsams pas/ de'i gnam gang la rje rab gsal zla mgon pa gshegs par 'dug pa la/ dus zings pas nged la lon cha

ldan gzhan la yang dbang bskur ba'i 'gro phan ngang gi bla ma'i dgongs pa rdzogs pa skal pa che 'dug snyam pa rjes la

brgyud kyi dbang lung khrid rnams phul zhing/ lcang lungvc: i.e. spyang lung nas rje dbon gdan sa pa theg chen chos rgyal nas brgyud pa'i lcang lung pa rang gi pha chos
su gyur pa'i lam 'bras gsan pa la rkang gtad dpon slob drag bsdus 'ga' zhig byon byung pa la/ bstan pa'i rgyun la bsam nas dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i phyag bzhes ji lta
ba la ngor pa'i 'dres ma shor ba byas pa'i lam rdzogs par bshad dus/ stag lung sprul pa'i sku chen pos kyang gsan/ de skabs zla ba byung ngo cog gi nyer dgu la drug cu
pa re rgyun ldan yod pa'i bdun pa'i nyer dgu'i drug cu pa'i nub rtsub 'gyur bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ba phyis sku rim dmigs su mon pa'i dge bltas su mngon pa byung zhing/
gzhis ka nas dngul sku'i sku 'dra dran pa'i gsal 'debs su mtshan thogs pa de'i rab gnas kyang stag lung rang du zhur gnas byung ba bzhin bsgrubs/ stag lung du yod rin
zhabs drung skyor mo lung gis 'bod mi brag kha nas gnang ba dang/ de bzhin du gong dkar/ brag dkar/ yar rgyab sogs tha dad nas bstud mar byung yang khas len tsam yang med
pa'i sne cha rang la bzhag rjes/ lhun grub rdzong du sprul pa'i sku rin po che rnam pa'i yab sde pa'i drung lnga pa'i gnas la thugs dbyings phyogs pa'i spyan sngar yul
mchog dam pa'i bskyed rtsa gnang bas mos dungs kyis phyin nas mjal 'phrad dang/ dbang bskur gyi gshes skyel mtshon par byas zhag gsum tsam bsdad nas slar log pas/ de 'phral

rang sku tshe'i 'du byed btang pa'i tshogs dbu yang sku mched rnam pa'i bka' ma phyogs par byas/ de dus sku 'bum thang gi dbus su bsngo ba'i skabs 'bum pa gnang ba la zhabs

gzhis kar sleb pas zhabs drung khu dbon ni gang yang ma bzhugs 'dug/ khra ma nas kyis phebs bsu gzhi len yang dag gnang zhing/ zhag gnyis nas pa nams nas khu dbon mgyogs
bshad gnang nas phebs pa dang mjal byas rjes/ tshogs pa'i mkhan po'i bkod ja zhu ba la chos rje kun bzang rgyal po dang 'ber nag gnyis brdzangs shing/ chos lung nas dbon
chen pas mkhan rin po che'i dgongs rdzogs bsngo rten du 'jam dbyangs rgya sku/ dngul rkyan/ dngul ti/ rdo rje bzang lam ma'i bla bre/ ding phon/ rten khebs bzang bsgrigs/
thub pa gnas bcu rnams byung ba'i gnas bcu de grwa tshang chen mor phul/ dngul bcad rnams nas su bsgyur nas dge ba'i dmigs thes su bzhag nas/ rwa lngar dbon sa yum chen

tshugs cig 'chi khar byed rang bsam yang byed dbang ma byung pas lus ma sgyur yang sems sgyur nas phyi ma lha chos kyi

las skrun par 'dug/ rnam par grags tshod dbon sras lha dbang kun dga'i sras mor brtags pa de yin cing/ gang na'ang mngal skyes kyi mkha' 'gro ma dngos lags dus tha snyad

snga rting gnyis tsam yang bde spyod gtan nas ma gnang bar des gtsos pa'i 'bul ba rnam grangs 'ga' zhig mdzad/ nged kyi lag pa la phyag gis bzung nas thugs kyi mi brnyel
ba zhu zhu gsung ba'i bka' nan kyang 'byon pa'i yid lhag par phreng ba'i ngang nas lam bsrangs/ lha rtser gong nas sku mched rnam pa gnyis kyi sngo lo bdag po chen pos

bris sku thod tshad/ mda' dar bcu/ khrab rmog gri gsum/ gtor gur gser ma/ stag gzig gung gsum gyi pags pa/ phyag mtshan/ rus rgyan/ khra ma nas kyi rten thugs chen mo rnams

dge sgyur phul nas byang du sde pa dzaM la'i drung gi sku gdung drung du dbyar rings cho ga ma chag pa la/ bu sgrub chen rnam grol seng ge dpal bzang po la 'dod chos
gang yod dang/ dbyar smad dbon po kun dga' dpal bzang po dang/ slob dpon khar sgo ba rnams la lam 'bras sngar gyi chos lhag/ 'phags pa'i bka' 'bum yongs rdzogs/ ni gu'i
khrid sogs dang/ gong nas dzaM la'i spur bzhu dang nang rten sman bla byams pa'i nang bzhugs rab gnas tshar 'phral shar phyogs la 'ongs chos lung du yud tsam bsdad rjes/
gting skyes brgyud rgyal rtser sde pa chos rjes dbu mdzad la lam 'bras/ chos sder sa dge'i 'dus pa gnyis tshogs la bka' gdams glegs bam pha chos bu chos thig le bcu drug
gi dbang khrid rnams dang/ ni gu'i khrid/ dbang rjes gnang rnam grangs dpag med/ lam 'bras pa gang yod la 'phags pa'i spyi chung ljon chung dag chung sa dpyad 'phags 'chan
rnams kyi steng nas brtag gnyis kyi mgyogs bshad tshar gcig rnams grub 'phral byams chen nas chos rje shar chen pa 'bod pa la byon byung pa dang lhan cig byams chen du
'ongs nas/ chos rje rin po che 'bras yul nas dbu mdzad slob dpon rnam pa so so dang bcas pa'i drag bsdus rang la lam 'bras yig sna drug cus rgyan pa'i cha lag dang bcas pa'i
zhib bshad chos yun ring zhing bshad babs 'gril ba'i 'doms gang che'i rgyu dbang grol mtshams/ gzhis kar

gos sku'i rab gnas la dpon slob lhan du phebs skabs/ skyid grong nas zhabs drung khu dbon gyis chibs bsu dang bcas/ pho brang chen po rin chen spungs pa nyid du bkra shis kyi
sa chags pa'i ser phreng/ gar 'chams/ rnga bshon dang bcas pa'i mdun bdar ste/ dge mtshan gyi them skas la legs par 'dzegs nas/ mchod yon zhal 'dzom bsod nams chen po'i
dpal gyis mngon par mtho ba'i bzhugs khri so sor 'khod pa gnang zhing/ rab gnas kyi cho ga'i bya ba mtha' rgyas zhal lu vc: zha lunas rje mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug dpon
slob rags bsdus dang lhan gcig/ rgyud sde nas ji skad bshad pa'i legs byas ma lus pa bsgrub cing/ sbyin bdag bsgo ba'i skabs khu dbon yab yum sras dang bcas pa la bkra
shis phyag stod/ mnga' gsol shis brjod kyi me tog 'bul ba'i bar dge bar bgyis nas/ rtsa ru'i ston mo rgya che yangs mtho/ 'bul ba'i rnam gzhag blo 'das kyi dpyod ldan yongs
kyi re ba yid bzhin du gang ste/ chos dang srid zhi'i dpal yongs su rgyas pa'i ngang nyid nas/ slar yang byams gnas bde chen yangs pa'i gtsug lag khang nyid du slar log
nas sngags lam gyi dbu btsugs/ lam 'bras zhabs rdzogs pa dang sde pa rgyal bu'i drung dang rje mkhyen brtse'i drung gi thugs bzhed kyi chos phran rnams kyang grub/ shar
phyogs nas pha rin po che'i sprul sku dpon slob rnams phebs byung pa la zhabs tog bsnyen bskur gang bcogs dang/ tshe dbang dgung grangs ma/ nag rgya phag gsum gyi dbang/
chos drug rlung sems dbyer med/ phag mo lha khrid/ sku gsum ngo sprod/ grub brgya'i byin rlabs

sogs bka' chos thob gang che'i thugs kyi re ba rdzogs par byas/ grags par gzims khang gi bkra shis gzhi 'dings la phyin skabs/ snye mo nas chos rje'i drung phebs byung zhing/
mchod yon lhan du nag po spyod pa sogs kyi skyes rabs rnams kyi lung phul yar lam rwa lngar zhal ngo gdan 'dzom bkra shis zhal rgyas stengs su tshe rta/ dmar po skor gsum
sogs rgyun gyi legs spel gyi dbang chos rnams dge bar 'phul nas/ gser mdog can du mkhan slob rnam pa'i dgongs bzhed ltar 'ongs nas lam 'bras gtso bor bzhag pa'i dag ljon
skor gsum/ spros med/ ra khrid/ ni gu sogs kyi khrid dang/ bde kye gsang gsum sogs kyi zur bka' rnams grangs mang ba/ lhag par srin lag gi khrag rang rdol byams chen
du byung ba de yar khyer yongs nas nag po pa'i dbang cha brgyad 'grel mar byas zhing/ gzhan lha phran so so'i rjes gnang/ rnam gur sogs chos skyong so so'i bka' bsgo'i bar
nyin mtshan khor yug tu 'da' ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bar chad med par mthar phyin/ de skabs nged rang gi lag nas nas khal lnga brgya'i phogs 'bul/ khri khang
nas nas ras dpus dag rang gi khal 'gyed/ sku mdun zhing gis tsha 'gyed rnams tshogs pa lnga brgya longs pa la bsgrubs shing/ nged rang gi dam bca' byas pa'i cha nas mang
ja ma bkol/ gzhan so so nas mang ja bzang la mang ba thugs la btags byung zhing/ gser mdog can nas bsam sdings su sngar gyi ni gu'i lhag/ ga'u ma'i 'khrid cig dpon sa yum
mad kyi gtso mdzad la byas/ gzhan lU nag dril gsum gyi rdzogs rim/ chos phran brgya rtsa'i lung sogs rnam

grangs 'ga' re byas nas tshur lam khri khang du tshe dbang tsam phul rjes/ snar thang tshogs su bka' gdams pha chos bu chos/ thig le bcu drug gi dbang/ jo bo rje nas brgyud
pa'i sgrol ma nyer gcig gi rjes gnang/ sde pa yab sras la tshe dbang brgya rtsa/ tshe khrid/ dril bu lus dkyil/ rim lnga'i khrid sogs dgongs par yod pa'i bka' chos rnams
phul zhing/ tshogs snga rting du mang ja gsum/ kha thags gsum brgya'i tshogs 'gyed/ byang chen du'ang mang ja 'gyed chas/ sdod ring byams pa sgrol ma rnams la snyan dar
dang/ lha khang pa so sor dkar me rgya cher rgyun ldan phul nas slar khri khang gi skyid tshal yid bde rnam par rol pa'i dga' tshal nyid du zhal ngo gdan 'dzom la bkra shis
sku tshe'i dpal bskyed tshe dbang brgya rtsa/ rim bzhi'i khrid/ phag dkar shes rab gsal byed la sogs pa'i bdud rtsis/ dad gus yangs pa'i shel snod gangs bar bgyis te/
lha chen tshogs kyi bdag po'i mdun sa rang gnas nor bu'i gling gi yangs rtse bsam gtan gong 'phel gyi gnas nyid du nye bar son pa'i skabs 'di nyid do ces legs par bris pa'i
li khi taM//dpal ldan bde dge kun gyi dga' tshal ni//rnam grol mchog gi bcos blo'i skyed tshal las//blo gsal rgya mtsho'i sde snod 'dzin pa'i tshogs//dges bskyed ngang
gis mgron du bos pa bzhin//kun tu srid pa'i dpal 'byor mtha' dag la//nges 'byung chen po'i dga' gdung rang grol mchog//yang yang yid la sems pa'i rnam rtog phreng//nam du'ang
chad pa med la yid rang byos//kun nas bag yod khrel gzhung la//ngang gi dga' spror gyur pa

ni//sems kyi mdud grol mchog lags te//gzigs shig gzhan la med pa'i chos//yongs la dag snang ris med pa'i//kun spyod sor bcu sbyor ba'i tshul//dga' ba rgyas pa'i mig dkyus dag//rang
grol mchog gi rgyang ring bltas//mkhas grub kun gyi bzhed srol rnams//ma 'dres yid dga'i rnam rol du//legs rtogs sems kyi mching grol mchog//'di na rang babs lhug
par skyong//gang yang rnam mang chos tshul yongs la sdang sems med pa'i lhag bsam can//gang yang bstan 'dzin skyes bu kun la phyogs cha med pa'i mos gdungs can//gang yang
mkha' khyab bstan pa kun la nye ring med pa'i phan sems can//gang yang sngon bsags smon lam gyis grub 'bad pa med pa'i phrin las can//gang gang legs smon 'di de bzhin//yang
yang phan bde'i dge 'bras dag//de de de bzhin rang gzhan la//'bad 'bad mi dgos lhun grub shog//skye ba du mar bsags khyab mthar phyin pas//tshe 'dir ji lta'i re smon
yongs gang ba//'di de dkon mchog thugs rje'i mthu nyid dang//brgyud ldan bla ma'i byin rlabs las byung bas//da dung nad med yun du 'tsho ba dang//zang zing g.yengs ba'i
bdud kyis ma khyer bar//lha bsgom sngags bzla bka' bsrungs mchog rten pa'i//bsam pa lhun gyis grub pa'i rgyur gyur cig//ces rnam thar mtshar rgyan 'di yang gang la dad pa'i
gdung shugs skyo bsun mi mnga' zhing/ mos gdungs kyi dpal 'dzin pa'i skal bzang mi yi dbang pos nan gyis bskul ba'i ngor brjed ngas dang le lo'i bgyid skyur spangs te/
ji snyed kyi don ji lta'i yi ger bkod pa 'di yang/ dpal ldan kun dga' grol mchog blo gsal rgya mtsho'i sde'i blo gros kyi rgya mtsho las so// //
